Chapter 1730: The Spiderweb Splits and Changes

Li Fan revealed his plan: to use 'Return to Truth' to derive a version of the 'Manual of Mountains and Seas Changes' from before the Primordial Immortal Realm's disappearance and compare it with the current version to deduce secrets concerning the True Emperor. The Saints, focused on the upcoming reconnection and the Void Realm threat, discussed the strategic importance of the thirty thousand years of Void Realm ahead. Saint Lianshan explained that certain segments of Mountains and Seas were critical junctures, vital points that the Void Realm sought to control.

The Void Realm had intercepted the Three Saints because the mountains and seas ahead were strategically vital. Lianshan explained that Mountains and Seas, though constantly changing, had an overall, immutable trend of decline towards doom. However, certain critical junctures, like the one ahead, could alter this trend. These junctures were hidden, even from ordinary Saints.

Guihai magnified a segment of the Mountains and Seas view, focusing on a cultivator named Qiu Tianhui, who hesitated before transcendence, contemplating a more perfect method. His inner thoughts revealed his dissatisfaction with the limitations of transcendence and his search for a new path. He ultimately used himself as bait in the "Mountains and Seas Fishing Ground" to attract the Mountains and Seas Angler, hoping to escape or find a new way.

The Angler, a Saint-level existence, easily captured Qiu Tianhui. However, the Fishing Pond exploded, and Qiu Tianhui reappeared, having found another way—"Mountains and Seas Together." He explained this method involved using the continuous momentum of Mountains and Seas to extend one's life, eventually occupying a significant portion of Mountains and Seas. He believed the current decline of Mountains and Seas offered an opportunity.

The Saints were perplexed. Shou Qiu revealed that Qiu Tianhui and Shao Zidai were not directly present but had influenced the evolution of beings in Mountains and Seas, creating descendants like Li Tianhui and Zhang Tianhui, who embodied their Dao. These descendants, not ordinary blood relatives, were born through borrowing Mountains and Seas' power. Saint Guihai confirmed this, explaining Qiu Tianhui and Shao Zidai had intertwined their power with the Dao of Beings. Saint Lianshan noted their descendants covered the entire Mountains and Seas, demonstrating the continuity of their method.

Li Fan connected this to Qiu Xinhui, the Last Saint, who emerged from a withered Great Dao of Mountains and Seas. He theorized Qiu Tianhui's method, culminating at the end of Mountains and Seas, created a powerful being like Qiu Xinhui. The Three Saints acknowledged the couple's talent but noted their fear of the Void Realm and their subsequent hiding. They planned to track them through their influence on beings, using reincarnation as a potential connection point. Li Fan, however, stated his inability to protect Mountains and Seas, fearing his strength was insufficient against subsequent Void Realm attacks.

Chapter 1731: Devour Mountains and Seas

Like plucking at lute strings, Li Fan attempted to touch and alter the rules of this world with his twin fingers.

"Using the power of Devouring Mountains and Seas, weave a giant net. Evolve it into a world, forcing the creatures that enter to fight desperately with all their might..."

"When a creature perishes within the net, it will instinctively absorb them."

Li Fan looked again at the combatants locked in mortal combat.

As if after their demise, one glowing orb after another floated out. Each represented a life on the battlefield, containing the principles and creations they mastered in life.

Perhaps not all, but certainly the most essential essences, brought forth by desperate life-or-death struggles that unleashed their full potential.

On the mountain of corpses and sea of blood created by the great battle, countless glowing orbs of varying sizes rose, drifting into the [Net] hanging in the sky. This scene was indescribably bizarre.

Li Fan seemed mesmerized, flicking his fingers several times, trying to alter the direction of the glowing orbs.

He failed repeatedly but never gave up.

By the time the great battle ended, although Li Fan had not succeeded even once, a sense of confidence gradually bloomed in his eyes.

As per usual, he did not collect anything for himself.

He only took back what was divided amongst the enlightened beings after their desperate battles.

The remaining enlightened beings did not express excessive gratitude towards Li Fan. They merely seized every opportunity to recover and strengthen themselves.

As indigenous inhabitants of this world, they clearly understood that the battles to come would inevitably be more brutal than the last, until they were completely annihilated.

However, the instinct for survival did not allow them to give up.

Even with only a sliver of hope, they would continue to fight!

"These are the attributes bestowed upon them by the Net of [Tether]. It has nothing to do with my incitement. This conveniently suits me."

The enlightened beings had not fully recovered when the next wave of enemies descended.

"According to the formation, resist the enemy!"

Li Fan's spiritual sense rippled outwards.

In the minds of the enlightened beings, a profound formation simultaneously materialized.

Although its principles were difficult to comprehend, it did not prevent them from entering the formation in order.

With Li Fan as the core center of the formation, all the enlightened beings were connected as one.

Killing intent condensed, forming blood-red clouds that shot up to the sky, obscuring the heavens.

This formation was created by Li Fan, based on the 'Concentric Unity' characteristic of the Xuanji Ring.

Under the enhancement of the great formation, the enlightened beings shared their senses, as if they were a single entity.

Although there was no increase in their strength or realm, it transformed countless desperate fighters into an integrated whole.

They no longer had to worry about attacks from behind, and their companions' support always arrived in the most timely manner.

From fighting individually, they automatically differentiated into countless small groups to efficiently encircle and annihilate the enemy.

The battlefield situation instantly shifted.

What was originally a balanced, intense battle, turned into a one-sided slaughter due to the emergence of this formation.

Li Fan had anticipated this outcome and his attention remained focused on the sky of this world.

"Many thanks to our elder for bestowing this method!"

Only when the battle was won and the enlightened beings shouted in unison did he slightly shift his gaze.

"There are defeated remnants, you may devour them."

Li Fan pointed at the blood-soaked battlefield and said indifferently.

The enlightened beings were all slightly stunned.

But they were created to be disposable combat constructs, so they didn't overthink it.

Upon hearing Li Fan's command, they immediately began to feast.

Soon, the messy battlefield was cleaned up.

The battlefield remnants, apart from slightly filling their stomachs, seemed to have no other significant use.

For the vast majority of the enlightened beings, this was the case.

Yet, there were a few exceptions.

"You, you, you."

"Come here."

Li Fan singled them out, and three or five figures quickly flew before him.

They knelt respectfully.

Although Li Fan's cultivation level still appeared mortal on the surface, the subtle aura emanating from him instinctively made them tremble with submission.

They dared not act presumptuously in the slightest.

"So that's how it is."

After observing for a long time, it was unclear what Li Fan saw, but he suddenly uttered this sentence.

A moment later, one of the kneeling figures, without any warning, suddenly exploded, shattering into pieces of flesh and blood.

"You all consume this."

Li Fan commanded the remaining figures.

Their bodies trembled slightly. Without hesitation, they began to swallow the remains greedily.

However, this time, as they fed, Li Fan's fingers repeatedly drew slow arcs in the void.

As if touching, and as if playing an instrument.

As the flesh and blood entered their bodies, these kneeling figures were all strengthened to varying degrees.

And at this moment, the next wave of enemies arrived.

"Kill."

Without further words, Li Fan simply gave the order, and the created beings clashed with the beasts of the net once more.

This time, Li Fan did not gain an advantage. The strength of the newly evolved creatures, taking into account the enhancement of the 'Concentric Unity' formation, was more than a notch stronger than the previous wave of enemies.

However, this did not include the slight reinforcement the enlightened beings gained from devouring the flesh and blood earlier.

This resulted in Li Fan's side still holding a slight advantage in the situation.

And...

As the battle raged, Li Fan's consciousness continued to echo.

The enlightened beings were astonished to discover that as the enemies fell, wisps of indescribable and unfathomable power were captured and absorbed by them.

Some merely had a simple effect of increasing their blood energy and cultivation, while others contained fleeting memories of insights into divine abilities and great daos!

Although initially ignorant and lacking consciousness, the enlightened beings, as Li Fan's enlightenment was completed, their intellect grew day by day. They were also naturally adept at divine abilities and combat.

Without Li Fan needing to actively teach them, many among them instantly comprehended the memories.

Even if a few remained ignorant, through shared insights, they quickly grasped the profound mysteries from their companions.

The battle transitioned from a mere contest of strength and blood energy to one where divine abilities began to manifest.

The battle was swiftly concluded.

If the initial situation was only a slight advantage, then after the enlightened beings began to comprehend and manifest divine abilities, it became a crushing victory again.

The enlightened beings, having gained benefits, became like hungry wolves, scrambling for the remaining scraps on the battlefield.

But there was too little meat and too many wolves, not enough to go around.

Thus, unprecedentedly, they began to anticipate the next wave of approaching enemies even more!

A peculiar emotion and atmosphere began to breed within their hearts.

After the initial confusion, they quickly understood. This was the fortune Li Fan had brought them.

So, they all knelt respectfully, expressing their reverence and submission.

"Rise."

"I do not need your kneeling. What I need is..."

"To tear apart this sky with me!"

Li Fan pointed at the net-like sky and said indifferently.

There seemed to be an unresolvable emotion building in his heart. After a moment of dead silence, the created beings roared towards the sky in unison.

At that instant, their voices shook the cosmos and resounded through the heavens.

Simultaneously, in the sky, a shadow seemed to flash past.

Then, boundless dark clouds began to gather.

Strong winds rose, thunder rumbled.

This was the net's response.

The legion of enlightened beings had indeed made significant progress in strength, but as long as they did not exceed the net's carrying capacity, the net could always create enemies that matched their strength.

The next wave of evolved malevolent creatures was indeed much stronger than the previous one.

This made the recently reinforced enlightened beings almost feel as if they hadn't grown stronger at all.

Without Li Fan's guidance, they spontaneously began to exert all their efforts to absorb and strengthen themselves amidst the fight.

And in Li Fan's eyes, within this vast net of this world, another smaller net seemed to be weaving and converging.

"Still not enough."

Li Fan said after observing for a long time, suddenly.

So, he increased the stakes again.

"Your nature is chaotic and ignorant. Thus, you can only kill enemies based on instinct, which will ultimately be your downfall."

"I have a method that I can impart to all beings."

"Absorb the essence of heaven and earth to gather your energy. Utilize the wonders of heaven and earth to build your Dao foundation..."

As Li Fan spoke each word, the countless enlightened beings present, their gazes towards the surrounding net-world subtly changed.

It was as if they saw the remains of the previous battlefield,

everywhere emanating fragrance, appearing delicious and alluring.

This world was created by [Net] in imitation of its past devouring of the Primordial Immortal Realm. Truly, every place held exotic treasures, and every patch of ground was a divine treasure.

However, they all transformed into sustenance for the enlightened beings' cultivation.

"Devouring Mountains and Seas..."

"Who can't do that?"

"If things don't change again, even with the foundation of the Primordial Immortal Realm, it will only end up like the previous Xuanhuang Realm."

Li Fan looked on with cold eyes.

Although he borrowed the name of the [Devouring Mountains and Seas] method from the past, it was not the same cultivation method.

The reason why the enlightened beings could truly devour this world was none other than Li Fan's deconstruction of the [Net] before him.

The essence of the net was another manifestation of [Net]'s past devouring of Mountains and Seas.

Li Fan held the [True Revelation Manual], having witnessed countless changes in the substance and illusion of Mountains and Seas.

Especially with the augmentation of Shou Qiu and Dao De's 'Concentric Unity,' his comprehension of the transformation of truth and falsehood, while not yet at its peak, could be considered a preliminary success.

After all, Shou Qiu had once, with a single thought, erased the virtual embodiments of countless Saints, and he himself could achieve Sainthood through the illusory forms of Mountains and Seas.

This world, originating from Mountains and Seas, made it not so difficult for Li Fan to deconstruct it.

What was difficult was finding [Net] hidden behind the scenes.

So Li Fan had been waiting for [Net] to rewrite the rules again.

Change begets flaws.

From only being able to devour evolved malevolent creatures, it had ascended to being able to devour the world itself.

The meaning behind this leap was significant.

[Net], who possessed the ability to Devour Mountains and Seas, naturally understood this principle.

As Li Fan said, if they continued to not change the rules and allowed these enlightened beings to run amok, this net would soon fall apart.

Representing the will of [Net], a drastic change occurred in the world.

Myriad bolts of lightning simultaneously appeared, illuminating the dim heavens in an instant.

The lightning did not vanish in a flash but seemed frozen, gradually filling the sky.

Like cracks, and like threads.

Dense and numerous, spread across the sky.

A moment later, infinite beings gushed forth from these cracks.

Their target was none other than Li Fan and his army of enlightened creations!

Even though they had no concept of fear, the net-evolved creatures, witnessing this scene, instinctively stiffened.

Just as their elder had said, the sky had been torn open by them.

But...

The number of enemies appearing simultaneously was simply too great!

Faced with such a terrifying disparity in numbers, no matter how they struggled, they would likely be easily crushed into fragments.

"At this point, what use is there?"

"It's merely a desperate struggle. Killing one is enough, killing two is a bonus."

While their minds were shaken, Li Fan's voice echoed in their hearts again.

This allowed them to barely regain their senses.

They retreated, forming a defensive line, gathering at one point, to face the surging enemy together.

However, the power disparity between the two sides was too immense.

The legion of enlightened creatures collapsed upon the first contact!

This was no longer the normal process of the net forcing a desperate struggle and then absorbing; it had turned into a complete purge.

Li Fan ignored the enlightened beings who were rapidly disappearing around him,

and even ignored the net beasts that were about to attack him.

"Finally found you!"

A cold glint appeared in his eyes. His movements were identical to what Saint Tai Wei had done previously.

He stretched out his hands and tore forcefully.

But it was not merely imitating the Saint Emperor's actions.

The Saint Emperor's desperate blow only exposed [Net] hidden behind the scenes.

Li Fan's true objective, however, was to carve off a piece of flesh from Him!

Not for Mountains and Seas, but solely for himself.

"First Saint of Mountains and Seas, I wonder how your path differs from the present!"

"Devouring Mountains and Seas, this Dao suits me perfectly!"

Separated by the Void Realm, connected only by the脉络 of Mountains and Seas.

The Saints in the Xuanji Ring on the Other Shore could only see the images transmitted by Li Fan. Li Fan, therefore, did not fear exposing his secrets.

With a single thought, truth and falsehood transformed.

"Since you've come, don't leave."

Li Fan's mortal body, amidst the tide of countless monsters and beasts, was so minuscule and insignificant.

But without him making any obvious move, all the monsters that approached instantly vanished.

As if they were invisibly wiped away.

Without exception.

And as Li Fan slowly strode, ascending the heavens step by step,

amidst the dark clouds of monsters, a long, vast chasm appeared along with his steps.

Even though the [Net] evolved creatures were programmed to fearlessly rush to their deaths, witnessing such a bizarre scene, they instinctively felt a sense of resistance, an unwillingness to rush forward to their deaths in vain.

Apart from the momentary shock caused by the instantaneous erasure of truth and falsehood, the fundamental reason was their creator.

[Net], was also experiencing a trace of fear.

Even with the ability to Devour Mountains and Seas, in the face of the transformation of truth and falsehood, dissipation was only a matter of moments.

[Net], a top predator, was also extremely cautious.

Facing Li Fan, whose origins were unknown yet wielded unimaginable divine abilities,

it made a decision almost instantly.

Retreat!

This segment of Mountains and Seas could no longer be stayed.

Even with heavy losses, it was better than perishing.

As if time itself had frozen and then resumed, the lightning bolts previously frozen in the sky of this world slowly dissipated.

The world began to crumble, and the shadow hidden behind the scenes seemed to be moving away.

As for those evolved beasts...

They had already become a feast for the remaining enlightened beings.

"Our elder's divine abilities are peerless, his words are true. He has indeed led us to tear apart this sky!"

They were extremely excited in their hearts, doing their utmost to hunt the surrounding evolved creatures.

Some of these evolved creatures were even stronger than them.

But at this moment, they seemed to have lost their purpose, standing dazed and immobile.

Allowing them to be slaughtered and then devoured.

"Indeed, following the right person is very important."

A naive thought began to sprout in the minds of the enlightened beings.

Chapter 1732: Treat the person's body also

In truth, with [Net]'s true strength, if it had truly fought with all its might, it would not have collapsed so quickly.

Firstly, Li Fan's attack using the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood was truly astonishing in its execution.

[Net]'s carefully laid out web of devouring was instantly shattered before Li Fan, unable to offer the slightest resistance. The gap between them was as vast as the difference between heaven and earth. Unfamiliarity and fear filled its mind, and [Net] could not muster the slightest fighting spirit.

Secondly, [Net] was not a native being of this segment of Mountains and Seas. It had merely come to hunt the "Great Dao of Mountain and Sea Beings." Even if the hunt failed, it suffered no substantial loss. However, if it were to truly fight with Li Fan, this unfathomable and ferocious being...

Stealing Opportunity, Oracle Prediction, Perspective, Vastness, Li Fan...

Those who entered this net this time came one after another, all prepared. Even if it defeated Li Fan, perhaps even stronger beings would come.

Moreover, its existence had been exposed, and this was no longer a place to linger.

With all these reasons piled up, [Net] only cared about escaping and had no intention of fighting further.

It actually allowed Li Fan to rampage through the net at will, as if entering an uninhabited land.

The Primordial Immortal Realm that [Net] had painstakingly woven mostly became nourishment for Li Fan and his enlightened creations to comprehend their Dao.

The process of using "Truth is Falsehood" to erase the traces of the net was also Li Fan's process of comprehending its essence.

Normally, Mountains and Seas are guarded by many Saints. Even if Li Fan wanted to unleash his "Truth is Falsehood" abilities at will to test his comprehension, there was no suitable opportunity. But now, Li Fan could unleash his powers without restraint, enjoying himself to the fullest.

The Primordial Immortal Realm, though merely an illusion evolved by [Net] after devouring the primordial state of the Mountains and Seas, was still as real as the current Mountains and Seas.

As "Truth is Falsehood" continuously erased the surrounding scenery, wondrous insights continuously surged into Li Fan's mind.

It was like a grand feast after a long period of starvation, an unprecedented sense of satisfaction overwhelming Li Fan.

"As the saying goes, what is learned from books is shallow; to truly know something, one must personally experience it."

"Simply knowing versus truly experiencing it firsthand. Indeed, there is a significant difference."

"Even the shared memory of 'Concentric Unity' cannot completely replace my personal involvement. I once experienced erasing the virtual images of countless Saints from Shou Qiu's perspective, but the feeling was far less exhilarating than it is now..."

Since his reincarnation, this was the first time Li Fan had unleashed the power of "Truth is Falsehood" to his heart's content. While displaying his ultimate techniques, he did not forget his goal.

The net hiding in the shadows was gradually shattering. [Net], the first Saint of Mountains and Seas, finally revealed its true form.

In reality, it was not "human-shaped" but a massive aggregation of swirling circular shadows.

Innumerable small black tentacles coiled around its body, occasionally displaying and flashing images of Mountains and Seas that had been devoured by it.

Looking at its appearance, it was like a giant spider made purely of black shadow, lurking above the Mountains and Seas!

Upon seeing it, Li Fan's heart instinctively felt discomfort.

It was as if the black shadow, upon contact with his gaze, had infiltrated his body and begun attempting erosion.

Li Fan let out a cold snort and, using the transformation of truth and falsehood, instantly erased the influence brought by [Net].

"From [Heart Change]," [Stealing Opportunity] on the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood panel, enveloped in seven-colored splendor, instantly lost its color, becoming plain black and white, its profound essence gone.

And in the real Mountains and Seas, Li Fan, in this instant, transformed from the Saint of [Universe Cycle] into the Saint of [Stealing Opportunity]!

He looked at the figure of [Net] that was gradually fading and said coldly, "You stole my Great Dao, and now you want to leave?"

"What you took from me... you will return!"

One of [Net]'s myriad swirling shadowy tentacles suddenly exploded without warning.

It transformed from ink black into the same chilling gray.

Then, as if losing control, it surged into the other tentacles, greedily plundering!

[Net] possessed the ability to Devour Mountains and Seas, but under the sudden onslaught of this gray anomaly, it was somewhat unable to resist!

It could only watch helplessly as the other party plundered a portion of its accumulated essence.

Although both were forms of devouring on the surface, their underlying principles were fundamentally different.

[Net]'s devouring of Mountains and Seas was like a hunter preying on its prey, a form of forceful seizure.

But this grayish, cold aura...

Taking without permission, is called stealing!

This out-of-control gray aura within [Net]'s body was precisely the portion of the Great Dao's origin that it had previously snatched from the Saint of Stealing Opportunity.

It had already been swallowed whole and transformed into a part of its own power.

However, under the pressure of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, as [Net] attempted to flee.

Under the manipulation of Li Fan, who had transformed into the Saint of [Stealing Opportunity], this wisp of origin instantly became uncontrollable.

It returned to Li Fan's embrace, and then, in turn, began to frantically steal the essence of [Net].

Within [Net]'s body lay its accumulation of countless years of hard work in devouring Mountains and Seas.

It was an undeniable treasure trove.

Under normal circumstances, even the true Saint of Stealing Opportunity would not find it so easy to steal the Great Dao within.

But coincidentally, the thief had now entered the treasure vault! The most stringent defenses at the periphery were no longer a concern. The remaining task was to plunder as much as possible before the treasure vault was moved!

Although there were myriad treasures within the vault, Li Fan deeply understood that the most valuable among them was not the Great Dao [Net] had devoured over the years.

But the vault itself!

It contained the fundamental structure that constituted [Net]'s ability to Devour Mountains and Seas, the reason for [Net]'s attainment of Dao!

"Such an opportunity, once in a thousand years!"

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, feeling a torrent of power slowly transferring from [Net] to himself.

Besides [Net]'s accumulations, Dao cultivation, and innate talent, there was also its luck, its fate...

The total sum of its existence was being meticulously stripped away by Li Fan, as if by a sleight of hand, and taken away!

"Bastard!"

[Net], this nascent Saint of Mountains and Seas, finally let out an enraged roar!

Its voice was piercingly sharp, not human-like, but rather like the shrieking screams of myriad insects.

The black shadows vibrated violently, as if driven into a frenzy by the theft of its treasure vault.

"What? You can steal, and others cannot?"

Li Fan remained indifferent, his sleight of hand unabated.

He even taunted it from time to time.

"You..." [Net]'s dimming figure seemed to regain its ink-black color.

But upon thinking of something, it ultimately did not choose to continue fighting Li Fan.

It chose to flee as quickly as possible, minimizing its losses.

Before departing, it did not forget to utter a vicious threat.

Its resentful voice echoed through this world that was on the verge of shattering.

"Stealing Opportunity... very well! I have noted you down!"

The ink blackness completely receded.

The treasure vault gradually became illusory, as if vanishing from this Mountains and Seas. Li Fan could only snatch less and less.

In the end, he could only watch as [Net]'s trace disappeared.

Li Fan sighed with lingering dissatisfaction: "The Great Dao of Stealing Opportunity is indeed extraordinary. It could even touch and sense the existence of [Returning to Truth] within my True Spirit back then."

This small trial run now made him understand its profound magic even more. No wonder that at that time, despite being as cautious as Stealing Opportunity, he was willing to abandon everything and fight for his life. Besides his inherent nature, it was also because of his absolute confidence in the Dao he wielded."

"It's a pity. If Returning to Truth hadn't been unwilling, perhaps he might have even succeeded then."

Li Fan, in the guise of the Saint of Stealing Opportunity, managed to strip a layer of skin from [Net].

In the Hall of Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, a new line of text was added because of this.

Although currently just a fleeting phantom image, it already displayed its uniqueness.

Instead of being enveloped in colorful radiance, it was covered in a simple, ancient gray aura.

Exuding an indescribable sense of ancientness.

Besides "ancient," there was also a peculiar charm intertwined with it.

As Li Fan observed closely, he could faintly discern something.

It was the word "forbidden"!

As if disallowed by Mountains and Seas, and disallowed by this Hall of Great Dao.

Unlike other Great Daos of Mountains and Seas that Li Fan had previously encountered and absorbed, which stayed obediently once integrated,

this one was constantly restless, with a desire to break free and escape.

Although suppressed by the [Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood], its struggles were destined to be futile.

But this "rebelliousness" already revealed the uniqueness of [Net]'s Dao.

Li Fan mused: "The Three Saints once said that [Net], which always hid in the shadows, would be affected accordingly once exposed. It is a backlash from pushing its own Dao to its limit, transcending Mountains and Seas."

"Now, from the wisp of aura I stole from the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, [Net]'s Dao indeed shows signs of breaking the limits of Mountains and Seas."

Without time to savor his gains, and without [Net]'s support, the evolved Primordial Immortal Realm before him was about to shatter piece by piece. Li Fan, abruptly, shed the guise of [Stealing Opportunity].

He transformed back into his original appearance as [Universe Cycle].

"Esteemed Master, save us!"

Suddenly, cries for help echoed into Li Fan's ears.

They came from the enlightened beings Li Fan had created.

After the tribulation of the world's destruction, they were now less than one in a thousand.

However, those who survived had gained immensely.

Li Fan considered for a moment and casually collected them.

He wasn't afraid of them leaking secrets.

The transformation of truth and falsehood, how could ordinary beings understand it?

Let alone them, even if the Saints on the Other Shore came in person, they would only see through the battle between Li Fan and [Net] with confusion and incomprehension.

With the net shattered, Li Fan reappeared in the true Mountains and Seas.

In an instant, he fell into the previous segment of Mountains and Seas, into the sight of the Saints.

Li Fan's expression remained unchanged. As wisps of power enveloped him, they guided him towards the Xuanji Ring.

Looking around, this segment of Mountains and Seas was far less lively than the one Li Fan was in.

It even seemed rather desolate.

Not to mention the Saints who had achieved Sainthood later, only six of the original nine Saints of the Other Shore remained.

It seemed the Void Realm and [Net] had indeed put immense pressure on their survival.

"May I ask, fellow Daoist, from whence do you come?" Saint Guihai asked with a solemn expression.

Li Fan recounted the entire ordeal, one by one.

He only concealed the matter of him transforming into the Saint of [Stealing Opportunity] and feasting.

"Is that so?"

Upon learning that reinforcements from the later segment of Mountains and Seas were coming, and that their strength was so formidable, even the Three Saints were somewhat taken aback and revealed expressions of joy.

"Fellow Daoist Fan's ability of True Spirit Infusion is truly a great fortune for Mountains and Seas!"

Li Fan replied, "The current priority is to quickly reconnect the fragmented Mountains and Seas and build defenses together."

"Although the Void Realm's encirclement this time was magnificent, it is definitely no match for our combined might!"

Saying this, Li Fan looked towards where his main body was located.

...

In fact, the moment [Net]'s web collapsed and Li Fan's avatar officially entered the front segment of Mountains and Seas.

The Xuanji Ring on the Other Shore had already vaguely revealed the blurry scene.

However, because Li Fan's transmitted images had suddenly disappeared at the critical moment, the Saints were still in a state of shock and doubt.

"I observed that Fellow Daoist Fan's everything was going smoothly and was about to break the deadlock. What happened?"

Li Fan frowned, sensed for a moment, and then slowly said, "The脈络 of the beings of Mountains and Seas were affected, and I couldn't sense what was happening within the net."

"However, at the last moment, I sensed the signs of that world about to collapse. For us, this should be a good thing."

The Saints remained silent.

Originally, Li Fan was only meant to delay, but unexpectedly, he had actually broken the net.

Although, in reality, eight parts of the credit belonged to Saint Tai Wei's earlier revelation of [Net]'s hidden presence.

However, this action was still beyond the expectations of the Saints.

The Three Saints looked towards the front segment of Mountains and Seas, and after a moment, nodded slightly. "The power of [Net] covering Mountains and Seas is indeed disappearing. It is leaving."

With the confirmation from the Three Saints, the other Saints within the Xuanji Ring breathed a collective sigh of relief.

"Without [Net]'s covetous gaze, we only need to face the threat of the Void Realm from now on."

"Although its pressure is immense, we have, after all, slowly grown accustomed to it."

Compared to the Void Realm's Dao Annihilation, the Saints found the existence from the primordial beginning of Mountains and Seas to be more troublesome.

This was not to say that the primordial beings of Mountains and Seas were stronger than the Void Realm.

But rather, while the Void Realm's tribulation was terrifying, it lacked so many variables.

Everything was laid bare on the table.

Conversely, beings like [Net], the primordial Saint of Mountains and Seas, possessed unfathomable strength and unpredictable thoughts and actions.

For example, its decision to risk coming to the later stages of Mountains and Seas completely surprised the Saints.

Regardless of the outcome, it always added variables.

If it were just a game of chess between the two sides, it would be fine; it would be a matter of responding to moves.

But they also had to face the greatest threat, the Void Realm, simultaneously.

With these two troubles at the same time, even the Three Saints felt some difficulty.

However, with [Net]'s departure this time, the clouds had finally cleared.

With Li Fan's avatar as the link, the two segments of Mountains and Seas quickly reached a consensus.

On the surface, both sides would maintain a non-aggression stance, to avoid provoking a fierce reaction from the Void Realm.

In secret, Li Fan's avatar would use the True Spirit Infusion technique to create as many new Saints as possible.

Then, the Saints of the latter segment of Mountains and Seas would slowly, through the脉络 of Mountains and Seas, secretly transport their avatars to the front.

Once all preparations were sufficient, both sides would strike simultaneously.

The front segment of Mountains and Seas would attract the Void Realm's attention, while the Saints of the latter segment would emerge, doing their best to quickly reconnect Mountains and Seas.

Once the reconnection was successful, the Void Realm's siege would be broken!

"Originally, it was almost a dead end. Unexpectedly, the situation is now looking very promising!"

"Fellow Daoist Fan's True Spirit Infusion divine ability is indispensable!"

"Alas, without Saint Tai Wei, we were still worrying about how to break the net."

...

As the Saints chatted, the atmosphere on the Other Shore gradually became more relaxed.

Only Stealing Opportunity discreetly transmitted to Li Fan privately.

"May I ask Fellow Daoist Fan, did you encounter anything unusual when [Net] retreated?"

Li Fan asked with some confusion, "Why do you say that, Fellow Daoist Stealing Opportunity?"

"The Primordial Immortal Realm shattered, and chaos ensued. I could only strive for self-preservation and did not notice anything unusual."

"Or rather..."

Li Fan suddenly paused, "When [Net] left, it seemed extremely furious. Not just because of its retreat."

Stealing Opportunity pondered and said.

Chapter 1733: The Year of Mountains and Seas

"Fellow Daoist Stealing Opportunity, did you perceive something amiss?" Li Fan asked knowingly, feigning ignorance.

"Indeed, there are some peculiarities. In that instant, I... felt as if another [Stealing Opportunity] Saint had descended upon Mountains and Seas." After hesitating for a moment, Saint Stealing Opportunity quietly said.

"Two Daos appearing in Mountains and Seas on the same day. I felt my foundation shaking, as if it were about to be taken away. At the same time, my heart was filled with both fear and greed..."

"That feeling was unprecedented!" Stealing Opportunity said with a worried expression.

"Hmm? Such a thing happened?" Li Fan exclaimed in surprise.

Then he frowned deeply. "How is this possible? You achieved Sainthood through [Stealing], and one Dao cannot have two masters. How could there be a second one in Mountains and Seas... Hmm?"

As he spoke, Li Fan seemed to suddenly recall something, and his words abruptly stopped.

Stealing Opportunity immediately noticed Li Fan's anomaly and hurriedly asked, "Fellow Daoist, have you remembered something?"

Li Fan hesitated several times before speaking hesitantly, "The strange phenomenon that occurred to you indeed has a traceable origin. However..."

Glancing at Shou Qiu Gong beside him, Li Fan slowly said, "It concerns another's secrets, so it is not appropriate to speak directly. Fellow Daoist, please do not be anxious. Let me ask first."

"Then I thank you in advance, Fellow Daoist!" Stealing Opportunity's expression became solemn.

After some pretense of communication, Li Fan transmitted to Stealing Opportunity after a while, elaborating:

"Fellow Daoist must know that Shou Qiu Gong achieved Sainthood through fragments of the Great Dao of [Longevity]..."

Stealing Opportunity, being intelligent, immediately understood after Li Fan's hint.

"Are you saying that Shou Qiu Gong had the same feeling as I did?"

"Even more severe than yours. Shou Qiu once said that he is not the true master of Longevity, but merely obtained a fragment by chance. However, the true master of Longevity does not exist in Shou Qiu's contemporary segment of Mountains and Seas. They exist only at the beginning of Mountains and Seas, much like the powerful beings of that era."

"They, to avoid the calamity of Dao Annihilation, used the divine ability of [Severing the Future], thus achieving eternal existence in the past. Under normal circumstances, they would never set foot in the middle or later stages of Mountains and Seas. Since [Net] originated from the beginning of Mountains and Seas and hastily retreated after exposure..."

"Before leaving, it seemed rushed and angry. Coupled with your perception of another aura of Stealing Opportunity."

Combining these factors, Li Fan provided an answer: "Could it be that the one who descended at that time was the ancient Saint of Stealing Opportunity from the beginning of Mountains and Seas?"

Without Li Fan needing to say so, Stealing Opportunity's body trembled, and he thought of this point.

He instinctively felt it was unbelievable, but his fleeting feeling was definitely not wrong.

"In Mountains and Seas, there is truly another being who controls [Stealing Opportunity]?"

"I have not yet fully mastered the Great Dao of Stealing Opportunity?"

"Born at the beginning of Mountains and Seas, its foundation must be deeper than mine. Coupled with the active emotions that arose in my heart at that time..."

"Could it be that this person's fortune surpasses mine?"

Stealing Opportunity fell into deep self-doubt.

Subsequently, Stealing Opportunity appeared somewhat disoriented.

Only after successfully differentiating another thought and having it reside within a lucky native being of Mountains and Seas did he finally regain his composure.

Once again, through the脉络 of Mountains and Seas, he saw the Saints assembled.

There were the six Saints of the front segment of Mountains and Seas, such as Lian Shan, Gui Hai, Tai Yi, Gui Ming, Duan Chan, and Shou Qiu.

And more than ten figures, like Stealing Opportunity, who, though seemingly not Saints on the surface, were actually avatars of Saints from the latter segment of Mountains and Seas.

Stealing Opportunity, already in a state of mental turmoil, was now even more shaken to see his own seat in the front segment of Mountains and Seas empty!

Although he had already learned from Li Fan about the tragic battle situation in the front segment of Mountains and Seas, where only six Saints remained, Stealing Opportunity, confident in his own strength, firmly believed he was among the six surviving Saints.

Unexpectedly, upon arriving here, he found his original seat empty!

This further unsettled him: "Those whose strength is far inferior to mine have also survived. Does this not indicate something in the unseen realms?"

Fortunately, these were merely mortal avatars that had forcefully crossed through the脉络 of Mountains and Seas. The other Saints did not notice Stealing Opportunity's inner turmoil for the time being.

They were merely discussing the grand plan of reconnecting Mountains and Seas.

"Fellow Daoist Universe Cycle is already searching all over Mountains and Seas for potential talents. The later generations are abundant with talent, but this era is exceptionally barren. Moreover, the Void Realm's aggression is becoming more ferocious..."

"Although I have now reunited, we must not be careless!" Saint Gui Hai sighed, saying.

It was unknown what cruel battles they had endured, but the Three Saints of this segment, lacking their previous arrogance, now possessed a cautious foresight and carefulness.

Before the Mountains and Seas were officially reconnected, although they were the same person, their different experiences had led to slightly different personalities.

The avatars of the Three Saints' consciousness did not overstep their bounds, remaining core to the Three Saints of the current timeline.

All nodded in agreement.

The atmosphere in the hall became somewhat solemn. Saint Lian Shan continued, "Fortunately, as long as we survive this tribulation, the Mountains and Seas ahead, as far as the eye can see, will be a smooth path! If this reconnection is successful, for the next thirty million years of Mountains and Seas, no one will be able to stop us."

Upon hearing this, the Saints couldn't help but feel their spirits lift.

After several reconnections, they already knew the benefits involved.

And the combined time of several fragmented segments of Mountains and Seas was less than a million years.

Now, Saint Lian Shan was claiming that there were thirty million years of long time ahead, waiting for them.

If they were to connect them one by one, how much would their strength inflate?

The Saints couldn't help but fall into reverie.

Even the somewhat dazed Stealing Opportunity felt his spirits lift upon hearing this.

"Indeed. He hid at the beginning of Mountains and Seas, and his strength was already fixed. But I traveled upstream, merging all my past selves. The true belonging of Stealing Opportunity is still unknown!"

...

Li Fan suddenly spoke, asking, "May I ask the Three Saints, how many years ago was the so-called beginning of Mountains and Seas? And how long will such a reconnection continue?"

Upon hearing this, the Xuanji Ring fell silent.

Not to mention the Saints present, even transcendent cultivators within Mountains and Seas knew that the years of Mountains and Seas were incredibly long.

Measuring it step by step seemed romantic, but in reality...

Furthermore, the separation by Dao Annihilation and the Void Realm at each segment.

The phrase "extremely difficult" could hardly encompass it.

In the past, the Three Saints did not mention specific years, merely vaguely referring to them.

Affected by the Xuanji Ring and the deliberate avoidance of the Saints, they chose to turn a blind eye to this question.

Now that Li Fan had pointed it out, all the Saints present had to face it.

How long had the life of Mountains and Seas truly spanned?

Apart from the Three Saints, no one present knew the answer.

Shou Qiu, who managed Longevity, was already the longest-lived among the Saints.

However, in front of the Three Saints, he could only see himself as a junior.

Even Shou Qiu had no accurate answer to this question.

The Saints could only turn their gaze to the Three Saints.

It was evident that the Three Saints genuinely did not wish to answer this question.

A long silence ensued in the Xuanji Ring.

It was the divine sense avatar from the later generation that finally broke the silence.

"Fellow Daoist Universe Cycle, since you ask, then let us speak."

"We did not mention the past because we feared it would hinder everyone's will to reconnect. However, after several successful reconnections of Mountains and Seas, I believe everyone now possesses sufficient resilience."

Saint Lian Shan heard his other self speak and finally nodded.

"Knowing earlier has its benefits. Since that is the case..."

The Three Saints simultaneously waved their hands, displaying an image of the continuous Mountains and Seas before everyone.

They had seen a miniature panorama of Mountains and Seas before, but the Saints actually had no precise sense of which segment of Mountains and Seas they were currently in.

"The merging of Mountains and Seas leaves traces."

"Like tree rings, every inch deeper is called a [Year]."

"One year of Mountains and Seas, in our more familiar chronology..."

"Is approximately a hundred million years of time."

As the words were spoken, the Saints' expressions were still relatively natural.

The number [hundred million] sounded terrifying, but after all, some of the Saints present had lived for that long.

Thus, they could still accept it for the moment.

Glancing at the emotions of everyone present, Lian Shan continued slowly, "Since Mountains and Seas merged and we obtained memory, Mountains and Seas have already existed for nearly a thousand years."

As if imbued with the aura of prolonged ages, the Lian Shan Saint in the Saints' eyes seemed to grow somewhat aged in that instant.

A silence fell upon the Xuanji Ring.

One year equals one hundred million years.

A thousand years of Mountains and Seas meant one hundred billion years.

At first glance, it did not seem like an incredibly long duration.

However, all the Saints present had personally measured and reconnected segments of Mountains and Seas.

Their several arduous efforts had only restored a million years of time.

And now, a journey of hundreds of billions of years awaited them...

Even with the mindset of Saints, upon realizing this, they couldn't help but feel dizzy for a moment.

Even with the thirty million years of smooth sailing ahead that Saint Lian Shan mentioned, they had only covered one ten-thousandth of the path!

Could they truly finish it?

This thought suddenly emerged in the minds of the Saints.

In the Xuanji Ring, the main bodies of the six Saints were fine.

With the reinforcement of the Three Saints' 'Concentric Unity,' even after knowing the truth, they still possessed a faint glimmer of hope, barely holding on.

But the divine sense avatars of the other Saints, who had forcibly crossed over through the脉络 of Mountains and Seas, were plunged into mental storms of varying degrees.

If reaching a hundred miles means reaching ninety, then what they were doing now was far from even starting.

That they did not collapse on the spot after realizing the arduousness of their mission was a testament to their Saintly disposition.

Li Fan, like the other Saints, wore an expression of profound shock.

In truth, he had already estimated this.

After all, others could only roughly infer the scale of Mountains and Seas through the illusory projections of Mountains and Seas periodically displayed by the Three Saints. However, Li Fan had obtained the [Outline of Mountains and Seas Changes] recorded in [Returning to Truth].

What it recorded was not the Mountains and Seas of a single era,

but the entirety of Mountains and Seas.

Even with Li Fan's resilient spirit, he had almost lost himself when witnessing such a vast amount of data back then. It was no wonder that [Returning to Truth] had always kept this option hidden, only revealing it when Li Fan had grown to a certain level.

After fully imprinting Mountains and Seas with infinite spirituality and achieving Sainthood as a Saint of Mountains and Seas,

Li Fan began to deeply doubt the matter of reconnection.

The past years of Mountains and Seas were simply too long.

The reconnection efforts of the Saints were truly like ants crawling.

Furthermore, not to mention the obstruction by the Void Realm...

With Li Fan's appearance and True Spirit Infusion assistance, they had successfully reconnected several segments of Mountains and Seas.

What if Li Fan did not exist in Mountains and Seas?

Could Mountains and Seas truly be reconnected?

The matter of reconnecting Mountains and Seas originated from the end of Mountains and Seas and was passed down by the Walker of Mountains and Seas.

With the strategies and disposition of the Three Saints, they actually agreed and acted upon it.

Admittedly, from a theoretical standpoint, if one could succeed in one instance, one could succeed in a hundred. Even redoing it a thousand or ten thousand times was merely a matter of routine effort.

There was indeed a possibility of reconnecting Mountains and Seas.

But this was predicated on the premise that everything in the Void Realm was calm and peaceful.

However, reversing merely a million years, Li Fan had encountered Void Realm avatars and the ancient Saint weaving a net, and many other variables.

It was truly unimaginable how many more twists and turns awaited them on the path ahead.

Li Fan already felt that his life thus far was long enough.

But compared to the scale of hundreds of billions of years, he was truly like an infant in swaddling clothes.

Under this immense disparity, doubt arose within Li Fan.

This question had been hidden in his heart for a long time, but there had never been a suitable opportunity to voice it.

Now that it was finally asked, Li Fan felt a sense of relief.

This question was not merely intended to provoke or doubt.

But rather, it genuinely carried a sense of seeking counsel.

Even Shou Qiu, who embodied Longevity, could not resolve Li Fan's doubts.

He could only place his hopes on the Three Saints.

Seeing everyone in the hall seeming lost, Saint Lian Shan smiled and shook his head slightly, "It was precisely because we foresaw this scene that we were unwilling to reveal the true age of Mountains and Seas."

"From the perspective of ordinary beings, seeing the true and immense length of Mountains and Seas would indeed cause profound confusion."

"However..."

"Since we are willing to carry out the plan to reconnect Mountains and Seas, it means this plan is definitely feasible!"

"Hundreds of billions of years, though seemingly long, are merely the path we have already traveled."

"If everyone is willing, you can truly experience the past hundreds of billions of years of Mountains and Seas within my mind."

"I believe that once you have personally experienced it, the confusion in your hearts will naturally dissipate."

Saint Lian Shan's voice echoed throughout the Xuanji Ring, causing a faint white light to ripple.

The Saints' hearts were stirred with excitement, and their fighting spirit was somewhat rekindled.

Li Fan also began to understand.

On the scale of ordinary life, one would naturally be terrified by the terrifying magnitude of hundreds of billions.

But the Three Saints could be said to be the embodiment of Mountains and Seas.

As they said, hundreds of billions were merely the path they had already traveled.

Retracing it now, even with added hardships,

was it not within the realm of possibility?

"It is precisely because we have experienced it that we believe," Li Fan mused.

He was also the first to speak, "I dare to borrow the memories of the Three Saints to traverse the vast distance of Mountains and Seas."

"It is like a prophecy of reconnection."

"Otherwise, I fear I may not be able to truly persevere."

Li Fan's emotions seemed somewhat low.

The other Saints remained silent, but most of them felt the same way in their hearts.

The reasoning was sound.

But whether one had personally experienced it or was merely supporting it with vague belief, it was entirely different.

The Three Saints exchanged glances, as if after careful consideration.

They then nodded in agreement.

"A hundred billion years of time is indeed long."

"I will lead you through the experience, but you may not be able to persevere through the entire journey."

"Do not force yourselves; just do your best."

"Using mere intent avatars would be insufficient. It must be done with your main bodies."

The speaker was the intent avatar of Lian Shan.

Returning to the scene where Li Fan's main body was located, within the Xuanji Ring of the current Mountains and Seas.

The bodies of the Three Saints began to emit a hazy radiance.

As if containing immeasurable light and immeasurable scenes.

The Three Saints asked one final question, and after receiving affirmative nods from all the Saints,

the radiance intensified, completely engulfing the figures of all the Saints!

Chapter 1734: A History of a Hundred Billion Years

Lian Shan, the civilization of Mountains and Seas.

Gui Hai, the beings of Mountains and Seas.

Tai Yi, the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas.

The Three Saints could roughly represent Mountains and Seas itself.

Under Li Fan's guidance, the Three Saints guided all the Saints within the Xuanji Ring into their own long memories.

It did not begin from the time of Mountains and Seas splitting its spirit.

But from the time the Primordial Immortal Realm disintegrated and Mountains and Seas gradually merged.

As it was an experience of memories, no real individual entities were differentiated.

All Saints appeared as green light dots gathered together.

What the Three Saints saw and heard were displayed on three light screens, arranged before the Saints.

Although it was merely "viewing," the Three Saints, with their unfathomable power, imposed a sense of "being present" upon them.

It was virtually indistinguishable from experiencing it firsthand.

Through the eyes of the Three Saints, they vaguely glimpsed a corner of the true Primordial Immortal Realm. What was previously just an empty concept gradually became concrete and clear.

The Primordial Immortal Realm was born and evolved after Mountains and Seas split its spirit, at the time of Mountains and Seas' initial creation.

Perhaps because the [True God] was immeasurable and Mountains and Seas could not consume it all. Or perhaps during the True God's fall, Mountains and Seas did not obtain all of it.

In any case, within the Primordial Immortal Realm, there were numerous peculiar beings born naturally, some even feeding on Dao. Beings fought each other, and some coveted the rare opportunity of Mountains and Seas devouring.

All things competed, and life flourished.

No boundaries, no restraints, no taboos.

Who lived and who died.

All depended on one's own abilities.

The Primordial Immortal Realm existed for an unknown duration. But since Mountains and Seas could not last forever, it was destined to meet its end today.

Innumerable small black holes appeared in various corners of the Primordial Immortal Realm.

Like terrifying vortices, they devoured everything around them.

The foundational principles that constituted the Primordial Immortal Realm vanished into them in an instant.

Beings scrambled to survive, no longer caring about their conflicts.

Green light dots flickered incessantly, the intentions of the Saints intertwined.

"The Primordial Immortal Realm, what a magnificent and majestic existence, nurturing countless Great Daos and beings, yet it fell apart in an instant under the merging of Mountains and Seas!"

"No matter how extraordinary, it was merely an experiment of Mountains and Seas. When Mountains and Seas understood its destiny, which was to merge, it was naturally abandoned."

"Born from a single thought of Mountains and Seas, and extinguished by a single thought of Mountains and Seas..."

"Unexpectedly, even the Three Saints held fear in their hearts."

"This scene strongly resembles our struggle before the descent of Dao Annihilation. Everything we experienced, we did not expect that our predecessors from a billion years ago had already gone through it. In this way, Mountains and Seas are like a colossal cycle."

The disintegration of the Primordial Immortal Realm was like a storm, mercilessly sweeping away the surviving beings within it. Even beings as powerful as the Three Saints could only flutter their wings like ants in the wind, desperately trying to maintain their survival, unable to resist this grand trend of Mountains and Seas.

The Saints, who had been discussing amongst themselves just moments ago, now, as time flowed by, were suddenly caught in the storm of Mountains and Seas' disintegration, gradually losing the ability to speak.

Only now did they realize what a stroke of luck it was to have been protected by the Primordial Immortal Realm.

Similar to the tribulation of Dao Annihilation that annihilated everything, yet different in substance.

This storm was the shedding of the excess by Mountains and Seas, the elimination of foreign elements.

All the essences that originated from the Gods, which they had not absorbed earlier, were now to be completely reclaimed.

Nothing existed beyond Mountains and Seas.

No transcendent beings, no one standing above Mountains and Seas.

To survive the storm, one could only become a part of Mountains and Seas.

The storm lasted for tens of millions of years before finally subsiding.

If they were merely observing within the Three Saints' memories, rather than personally experiencing it, perhaps only one in ten Saints would have survived this catastrophe.

As if having absorbed all the essence derived from the Gods, Mountains and Seas finally revealed its form.

The Infinite Sea, nurturing all possibilities.

Without the concept of time, starlight flickered, cycles of birth and death, all constantly evolving and dissipating within it.

Above, the Majestic Mountain stood tall. Though formless and intangible, it represented eternal energy and foundation. Like a pillar, it was precisely because of the existence of the Majestic Mountain that the infinite possibilities within the Infinite Sea could continue.

Mountains and Seas relied on each other. They seemed independent, yet interdependent.

"Everyone, this primordial Mountains and Seas... seems vastly different from what we see later?"

"The so-called infinite possibilities in later Mountains and Seas still exist within the constraints of the river of time, like myriad great rivers flowing concurrently. But at this time, Mountains and Seas..."

"Possibilities are like ripples on a placid pond, appearing and disappearing, yet not affecting the Infinite Sea itself. Compared to the current Mountains and Seas, the state of the primordial Mountains and Seas is undoubtedly more stable. Why force merging?" Doubts arose in the hearts of the Saints.

However, their inner thoughts could only be revealed to onlookers. For those truly within the situation, the focus was solely on one thing.

That was to survive!

Compared to the previously unrestricted paradise, the formed Mountains and Seas had extremely strict rules.

Even somewhat cruel.

Regardless of one's strength, one could not live forever. One could only be like the infinite possibilities constantly born and extinguished within the Infinite Sea, life and death beyond one's control.

Even those who once roamed freely in the Primordial Immortal Realm could only perish silently now.

The new rules of Mountains and Seas were cruelly incompatible with the beings of the past. However, they forged a new, sufficiently stable order.

Between the birth and extinction of possibilities, it seemed to follow some unfathomable law. Although starlight flickered within the pond, the pond water remained calm.

The Majestic Mountain above stood like a pillar beside the pond.

Mountains and Seas relied on each other, balanced and harmonious.

Most of their former companions had perished. The Three Saints either went dormant within Mountains and Seas, or merged with Mountains and Seas, or waited for their chance.

The primordial Mountains and Seas were exceptionally peaceful.

The possibilities evolved within were also extremely simple.

There were not even beings in the strict sense, only simple life forms like algae.

However, as the starlight flickered differently within the Infinite Sea.

The forms of evolved possibilities gradually became richer.

In some possibilities, intelligent life began to appear.

The Three Saints, struggling to survive under the harsh rules of Mountains and Seas, took the opportunity to escape into them, seeking respite.

Compared to the nascent beings of newly formed possibilities, the Three Saints, originating from the Primordial Immortal Realm, were undoubtedly true "Saints."

But the Three Saints did not attempt any intervention, merely observing silently.

When they sensed that a possibility was about to vanish, they timely withdrew and sought survival again within the Infinite Sea.

An unknown amount of time passed like this.

If there were no accidents, Mountains and Seas might have remained peaceful forever.

On this day, the Infinite Sea, without warning, began to boil and churn.

The sea of stars shimmered like a mirror, seeming to reflect scenes from outside Mountains and Seas.

The Three Saints looked up, trying to seize the opportunity to peek.

However, they only saw fragmented glimpses, but instantly understood the reason for Mountains and Seas' turmoil!

After devouring the Gods, Mountains and Seas sought to maintain a state of "eternity" without the passage of time.

Without beginning or end, it could naturally last forever.

It seemed to have succeeded.

But...

At this moment, outside Mountains and Seas, time was still quietly flowing!

At a time when Mountains and Seas were completely unaware!

It was as if a pair of eyes had been coldly watching them from the very beginning.

Chapter 1735: The Evolution of the Mountains and Seas

Not only the Saints immersed in memory, but even Mountains and Seas itself, were shocked and trembled at this discovery, unable to stop.

The Infinite Sea instantly churned with countless ripples. The number of possibilities appearing simultaneously in this moment was greater than all possibilities that had appeared in the past hundred million years combined.

The Majestic Mountain towering above also seemed to suffer an invisible impact, trembling incessantly.

After devouring the Gods, Mountains and Seas thought all things in the world belonged to Mountains and Seas.

Harmony and interdependence, forging an eternal world.

However, the discovery at this moment dashed Mountains and Seas' long-held hopes.

Thus, change was born.

...

"Where does that gaze from outside Mountains and Seas originate? Could that be the so-called [Stars]?"

"If this gaze did not exist, perhaps Mountains and Seas could have maintained this so-called eternity. Possibilities are born and die, but it does not affect Mountains and Seas itself. Time has meaning for the irregularly emerging possibilities within the Infinite Sea, but for Mountains and Seas itself, it has no meaning. But with this gaze from outside Mountains and Seas... everything has become different!"

"Mountains and Seas transformed from an eternal creator and sustainer to an observed entity. No longer transcendent, no longer eternally unchanging."

"This inexplicable gaze is likely the root cause of Mountains and Seas falling into its current predicament. Precisely..."

After the initial fear, numerous questions arose in the minds of the surrounding Saints.

But since Mountains and Seas itself could not find the answer, let alone the Saints present.

They could only continue watching with bewilderment.

In the past, without knowing of the gaze upon Mountains and Seas, Mountains and Seas might have maintained its balance independently.

But since sensing that wisp of gaze from outside Mountains and Seas, Mountains and Seas could no longer maintain its former tranquility.

As more and more ripples appeared simultaneously in the Infinite Sea, a pond could not indefinitely contain them.

As if a great wind was constantly blowing, carrying the pond water outside the pond.

Causing Mountains and Seas to merge, breaking the stillness.

Time quietly began to flow over Mountains and Seas.

After devouring the Gods, the situation where Mountains and Seas sought to condense itself into a single point did not last long before it was shattered.

Perhaps this signified some inevitability.

The merging of Mountains and Seas was destined to be a calamity for Mountains and Seas.

But for the beings within the possibilities of Mountains and Seas, it was undoubtedly a great fortune.

Some beings, amidst the upheaval of Mountains and Seas, glimpsed the Majestic Mountain towering above within the Infinite Sea.

Thus, they began attempts to ascend.

Although most ended in failure, they persevered, never knowing what it meant to give up.

As if driven by some inexplicable force.

Although beings were born from Mountains and Seas. The ambition to scale mountains and cross seas was their innate instinct!

Time was like an engraving knife, altering the original shape of Mountains and Seas.

The water in the pond slowly flowed outwards.

From a trickling stream, it became myriad rivers flowing concurrently.

The wind and water eroded, causing the Majestic Mountain, which originally stood by the pond, to also suffer erosion.

Slowly merging into the great rivers.

As time passed, the process of merging Mountains and Seas accelerated.

Perhaps it was an inescapable fate for Mountains and Seas, or perhaps it was some attempt by Mountains and Seas itself.

From the ancient Mountains and Seas, where Mountains and Seas stood side-by-side, maintaining eternity, to the current state of Mountains and Seas.

A vast period of one hundred and fifty billion years had passed.

Possibilities no longer appeared and then disappeared, but instead, along with Mountains and Seas, flowed endlessly forward with time.

The great waves washed over the sand.

As the life cycles were continuously prolonged, the upper limit of strength for newly born beings in Mountains and Seas was constantly raised.

Finally, one day, a being leaped from the Infinite Sea and touched the boundary of the Majestic Mountain.

Although it perished shortly after,

its impact on Mountains and Seas was undoubtedly immense.

Like a giant stone thrown into the Infinite Sea, creating countless splashes.

More and more beings began to emulate and repeat the attempt to ascend.

Perhaps it seemed unreasonable, yet also very reasonable.

Because the Majestic Mountain was right there.

Another hundred billion years passed.

The limit that beings of Mountains and Seas could touch grew higher and higher.

Even with the name "Infinite," the Majestic Mountain was destined to be conquered one day.

Over these years, Saint Lian Shan, having witnessed numerous attempts to ascend, felt inspired.

He also joined the continuous stream of people, embarking on the journey.

Finally, one day, leaving everyone behind,

he reached the summit of the Majestic Mountain.

The gaze of the Saints shifted along with Saint Lian Shan's memories.

While the experiences of the Three Saints were presented in parallel before, the scenes from Saint Lian Shan's perspective forcefully overshadowed the other two Saints.

Standing at the peak of Mountains and Seas, Lian Shan did not survey the entire Mountains and Seas.

Instead, he instinctively recalled the feeling of that gaze from outside Mountains and Seas from many years ago.

So, he could not help but look up, attempting to gaze outwards.

In just an instant, Saint Lian Shan felt the existence of that gaze!

Even though he was now the strongest being apart from Mountains and Seas, in that moment, he could not withstand it. His form and spirit were shattered.

However, Saint Lian Shan did not return empty-handed.

In that instant, he clearly felt that after hundreds of billions of years, that gaze from outside Mountains and Seas.

Had seemingly drawn closer!

It was a feeling akin to "hearing the Dao in the morning and being able to die in the evening," Saint Lian Shan felt no regret for his impulsive decision that led to his demise.

Even as he was about to perish, he remained immersed in the shock brought by that gaze.

However, as the first being to ascend the peak of Mountains and Seas, Saint Lian Shan was destined not to perish just like that.

In his fading moments, the scenes he had witnessed in the past, the countless beings in Mountains and Seas striving fearlessly to explore and ascend the Majestic Mountain, reappeared in his mind.

"Mountains and Seas are majestic, and the beings of Mountains and Seas are no less so."

"Mountains and Seas are infinite, yet with the limited steps of the beings of Mountains and Seas, they can still measure it."

All sorts of realizations flashed through Lian Shan's mind like sparks.

In the final moments before his demise, Lian Shan once again proved his Dao.

Using himself as a bridge, he paved a smooth road for all beings to ascend the peak of the mountain.

"My past self would not have possessed such enlightenment to gain such insights at the brink of death."

"It is because of..."

"That gaze."

Saint Lian Shan descended into the world.

Mountains and Seas changed again.

Mountains and Seas were, in essence, independent existences.

The beings, civilization, and Great Dao of Mountains and Seas.

Were all unrelated to Mountains and Seas itself.

However, since the appearance of Saint Lian Shan, Mountains and Seas itself had developed an increasingly intricate connection with everything within it.

Subsequently, Saint Gui Hai and Saint Tai Yi were born.

The Three Saints acted as catalysts, leading to the emergence of more and more beings that could rival Mountains and Seas.

It was like a hundred flowers blooming and all trees vying for spring.

Mountains and Seas entered an unprecedented era of prosperity, as if the merging of Mountains and Seas was a beneficial event with no drawbacks.

The prosperity of Mountains and Seas lasted for over three hundred billion years.

During this period, countless possibilities evolved freely.

But under the unseen guidance of the Three Saints, they all ultimately pointed towards the path of Lian Shan crossing seas, utilizing the power of Mountains and Seas.

The Three Saints were products of the civilization of Mountains and Seas, and in turn, they influenced the beings of Mountains and Seas.

Chapter 1736: Secretly Borrowing Momentum

Like catalysts, the sentient beings of Mountains and Seas further accelerated the process of merging.

Prosperity reached its peak, and calamity finally arrived.

From where did the first wave of Dao Annihilation originate? Even the Three Saints, who had attained Dao, could not perceive it.

It was as if it sprang from nowhere, suddenly appearing.

However, the Mountains and Seas were still in their prime. The disappearance of a few possibilities was akin to humans shedding hair; it did not truly signify anything.

Until the tide of Dao Annihilation, with the passage of time, persistently accompanied Mountains and Seas.

Eventually, it grew powerful enough.

Unbeknownst to them, it had grown to a point where it could contend with Mountains and Seas. Like a phantom, it suddenly emerged, confronting Mountains and Seas.

Wherever it passed, possibilities collapsed, and Great Daos ceased to exist.

Mountains and Seas were severed.

What was originally a continuous whole was forcibly cut into countless pieces.

Mountains and Seas could still maintain a tenuous connection through their internal脈络.

But beings born within Mountains and Seas were fractured into shattered individuals across different temporal layers.

Not only was their strength greatly diminished!

Some even had their memories affected, becoming distorted and incomplete.

The Saints, looking back at the past hundred billion years of Mountains and Seas through the perspective of the Three Saints, often encountered memory fragments that seemed covered in a layer of gray.

These were parts that had been broken and lost due to the severing of Mountains and Seas, later re-created by the self-contemplation of the Three Saints.

In the sensory perception of the Three Saints' memory, five hundred billion years had passed since the first appearance of Dao Annihilation until now.

It was an incredibly long time.

Furthermore, the consciousness of the Three Saints was not that of mere individuals. They had manifested countless avatars, spread across almost all possibilities.

This included the vast majority of civilizations, Saintly beings, and Great Daos within Mountains and Seas.

The sheer volume of data was unimaginable. If the Three Saints had intentionally blurred it, this torrent of five hundred billion years of memory would have been sufficient to wash away, distort, and rewrite the personalities of the observing Saints to some extent.

Although it was a virtual leap, it did not prevent the Saints from truly experiencing the journey the Three Saints had once taken.

However, they did not focus on the countless possibilities within Mountains and Seas but instead centered on the overall temporal experience of Mountains and Seas.

The Saints saw that the initial calamity of Dao Annihilation was indeed negligible.

The possibilities lost to Dao Annihilation were less than even one ten-thousandth of those lost through the natural evolution and demise of Mountains and Seas itself.

However, in the struggle of Great Daos, one's rise meant another's fall.

Once a trend of collapse was born, if not stopped, it was destined to grow infinitely.

Even the smallest variable, accumulated over hundreds of billions of years, would become a number of astronomical proportions.

By now, the Void Realms formed by the erosion of Dao Annihilation could already contend with Mountains and Seas.

Even in the more distant future, the demise of Mountains and Seas seemed to be a foregone conclusion.

A long journey was slowly approaching its end.

After withdrawing from the memories of the Three Saints, it took the Saints a long time for their gazms to regain clarity.

"Although it is the path we have traveled before, the thought of having to retrace it makes my scalp tingle."

"This path is simply too long and too difficult." Bai Xiao exhaled, filled with emotion.

"From an outsider's perspective, the birth of Dao Annihilation seems utterly unreasonable. Outside of Mountains and Seas, there was no Void Realm to begin with. Apart from that direct gaze, there was nothing else. Yet, as Mountains and Seas evolved, Dao Annihilation inexplicably arose, eroding Mountains and Seas..."

"Could it be that the Void Realm originated from the gaze upon Mountains and Seas?"

After the initial sigh, the Saints refocused on the peculiarities within the memories of the Three Saints.

"As far as I can see, it is unlikely. Even with the current state of collapse in Mountains and Seas, the Void Realm is merely on par with Mountains and Seas. It is only through the accumulation of erosion over a vast expanse of time that this final decay has occurred. But that gaze..." Stealing Opportunity said, looking towards Saint Lianshan.

"If Saint Lianshan's perception at that time was not mistaken... the pressure brought by that gaze was absolutely beyond that of Mountains and Seas!"

The other Saints deeply agreed after recalling.

"Saint Lianshan's attainment of Dao actually places him on par with Mountains and Seas. Yet, before that gaze, he could not endure for even an instant. For Mountains and Seas to be altered because of it, is only natural."

Upon reaching this point, the Saints collectively fell into an eerie silence.

Since the gaze from outside Mountains and Seas was mentioned, its origin was unavoidable.

The answer seemed obvious.

Yet, it was so inconceivable that the Saints hesitated to be the first to speak it.

It was Li Fan, unburdened by any taboo, who directly voiced their unspoken question.

"It seems the doubts in everyone's hearts are the same as mine."

"With such power, a single glance that alters Mountains and Seas. Could this gaze be from the [Gods]?"

This seemed to be the only plausible answer.

The Saints, unable to answer Li Fan’s question, all looked towards Saint Lianshan, the only one who had truly seen that gaze.

"I also do not know..." After a long silence, Saint Lianshan could only offer a rare wry smile.

"No one has seen the true form of the Gods, besides their fragmented forms within Mountains and Seas. I have not seen the Gods, nor do I know their shape. Even if it were possible to meet their gaze, how could I be certain?"

"However, if we deduce by normal reasoning... your guesses are likely not wrong," Lianshan continued.

Tai Yi shook his head, "The Gods transcend Mountains and Seas, so they are naturally difficult to infer with ordinary logic. Our various guesses and deductions are unlikely to yield the correct result."

"However, one point is certain. Even if that gaze does not belong to the Gods, it originates from an existence higher than Mountains and Seas. Comparable to the Stars."

"Perhaps it is a remnant that Mountains and Seas, in its fragmented form, did not fully devour. Or perhaps it comes from an unfathomable, unknown place, an equal to the Gods. All the changes in Mountains and Seas since its eternal state are due to it," Gui Hai summarized.

A warmth surged into the hearts of the Saints with Gui Hai's words.

It diluted the sense of ancient desolation from witnessing hundreds of billions of years of memory, and at the same time, it gradually dispelled the invisible influence brought by that gaze.

Lianshan looked at Li Fan, "Fellow Daoist Universe Cycle, how do you feel? Do you still have any doubts?"

Li Fan first nodded, then shook his head, "Even though I have experienced it once, and will retrace the path, it still feels incredibly difficult. I lack the wisdom, courage, and perseverance of the Three Saints. However..."

"Even ants cling to life. As Saints, besides the path of rejoining and saving Mountains and Seas, there seems to be no other method to survive. We can only try our best for survival."

Li Fan's forthrightness surprised the Saints present.

However, it was indeed true. The Saints all nodded slightly.

"A journey of a thousand years begins with a single step. Let us first overcome the mountain before us." Li Fan smiled.

What Li Fan spoke of, naturally, was the segment of Mountains and Seas ahead, heavily besieged by the Void Realm.
