The Saints, having reorganized their spirits, refocused their attention on the fragmented bodies of themselves in the front segment of Mountains and Seas.

From the perspective of the Three Saints in the previous epoch, they began explaining the situation.

"Compared to the crisis of being surrounded and attacked by Void Realm avatars before, the situation is not worse."

"The reason the situation has deteriorated to this point is still due to excessive Dao Annihilation. Even with our protection, Mountains and Seas are bound to gradually dissipate," Saint Lianshan said, pointing at the waves of energy blowing in from outside Mountains and Seas.

The warm white light of the Xuanji Ring enveloped the entire segment of Mountains and Seas.

But visibly, it was constantly twisting and vibrating.

As if being manipulated by an invisible hand, its shape was constantly changing.

The Xuanji Ring itself, and the Mountains and Seas it protected, were truly like fragile bubbles, precarious and on the verge of shattering at any moment.

"The severity of Dao Annihilation is indeed extremely rare."

"Even in Saint Lianshan's memory of billions of years, such a concentration of Dao Annihilation is very uncommon. No wonder they say that after passing this hurdle, the path ahead will be smooth sailing."

"In this Dao Annihilation, if we only seek self-preservation, it might not be difficult. However, to protect Mountains and Seas simultaneously..."

For the first time, the Saints felt the immense pressure from outside Mountains and Seas. They each frowned and pondered their strategies.

"The pressure of Dao Annihilation is as mighty as Mountains and Seas. Only Saints, who can stand shoulder to shoulder with Mountains and Seas, can resist it. Previously, when facing despair, the number of Saints had dwindled. However, now..."

"With my True Spirit Infusion divine ability, as long as Mountains and Seas can be sustained, we can always create enough Saints. With each additional Saint, the pressure of the Dao Annihilation tide will lessen. When the number of Saints is sufficient, this calamity will naturally dissipate without us needing to act," Li Fan said softly.

Then, he changed the subject, "However, this can only be a last resort. Firstly, although True Spirit Infusion has the power to defy fate, it also requires suitable candidates. The number of cultivators at the cusp of transcendence, one step away from Sainthood..."

"Is actually not that large. Secondly, time is likely not on our side."

Saint Lianshan nodded slightly, "Fellow Daoist Universe Cycle's perception is indeed sharp. Perhaps sensing [Stealing Opportunity]'s departure, the pressure from the Void Realm outside Mountains and Seas has intensified. The waves of Dao Annihilation are growing stronger, and soon we will reach their peak. We do not have that much time to slowly create Saints."

As if to confirm Saint Lianshan's words, the white light outside the Xuanji Ring suddenly distorted violently.

Even the Saints seated within the Ring felt a sudden jolt.

Looking up, within the pitch-black Void Realm, figures seemed to be descending in layers.

Like an army advancing, their blades pointed forward.

"Void Realm avatars..."

The Three Saints frowned simultaneously.

Previously, to intercept Li Fan and his reinforcements, the Void Realm was willing to deploy over a dozen avatars.

Now, to completely conquer this segment of Mountains and Seas where the Great Dao of Life resided, the Void Realm would naturally mobilize more forces.

Especially after [Stealing Opportunity] was forced to retreat by Li Fan.

Even the formidable tide of Dao Annihilation was difficult to resist.

Now, coupled with so many Void Realm avatars...

"What is the plan?"

For a moment, all the Saints felt somewhat troubled.

"I have a plan, not sure if it is feasible," it was Shou Qiu Gong who spoke.

Of course, it represented Li Fan's thoughts through the principle of Concentric Unity.

"Shou Qiu, please speak freely."

"From the memories of the Three Saints in the previous epoch, we witnessed how Mountains and Seas changed according to circumstances. And this place is the central node supporting the life脉络 of Mountains and Seas..."

"Perhaps we can unleash the power of Mountains and Seas itself to counter the trend of Dao Annihilation!" Shou Qiu said calmly.

The Saints remained silent, seemingly contemplating.

Shou Qiu continued on his own, "Mountains and Seas may seem weak and precarious, needing our salvation. But after observing the Three Saints' billion-year memories, I have gained new insights."

"The civilization of Mountains and Seas, the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, the beings of Mountains and Seas - are they truly Mountains and Seas?"

"They are merely derivatives after Mountains and Seas evolved according to circumstances! In the very beginning, when Mountains and Seas coexisted and endured eternally, that was the form Mountains and Seas should have had."

"In other words, all these things, from Mountains and Seas' perspective, are merely external elements. Like a person's clothes!"

"Not Mountains and Seas itself!"

Shou Qiu's words were earth-shattering.

The Saints now knew that the civilization, beings, and Great Dao of Mountains and Seas were largely derived from the Three Saints.

Now Shou Qiu uttered an astonishing statement: the Three Saints could not represent Mountains and Seas.

Within the Xuanji Ring, there was a deathly silence.

The Saints observed their own noses and noses their hearts, neither agreeing nor disagreeing, but waiting to see the reaction of the Three Saints.

"Shou Qiu has observed Mountains and Seas for countless years, and after gaining our memories, has indeed gained deeper insight into the mysteries of Mountains and Seas."

"In a certain sense, what you say is correct."

"Everything attached to Mountains and Seas cannot represent Mountains and Seas itself."

"Since the first beings were created, and were stained with innate malevolence, Mountains and Seas had no choice but to destroy them. The perfect state Mountains and Seas envisioned was the eternal state after the destruction of the Primordial Immortal Realm."

"Possibilities would rise and fall like ripples, and beings would multiply and perish within them, without affecting Mountains and Seas in the slightest."

"Mountains and Seas were eternally independent, lasting through all ages. Unfortunately..."

"This attempt failed."

"Mountains and Seas and the civilizations it spawned became entangled, their connection deepening. However, in the final analysis, their essence remained different," Lianshan did not deny Shou Qiu's conjecture.

The Saints fell into contemplation upon hearing Lianshan's words.

"In a sense, our appearance is ultimately detrimental to Mountains and Seas."

"The fragmentation of Mountains and Seas, and the subsequent merging into a new God, was the ideal outcome. Even if not, maintaining the eternal state from the beginning would still be the best option. But..."

Li Fan recalled the scene he had witnessed in the past, of the lone star appearing and devouring everything, and slowly said, "Any so-called being, civilization, or Great Dao within Mountains and Seas is merely a manifestation of Mountains and Seas' fundamental power, representing a loss of its strength..."

"The stronger the civilization, the beings, and the Great Daos of Mountains and Seas, the weaker Mountains and Seas itself becomes."

In an instant, Li Fan thought of something, and his words suddenly stopped.

He had a guess, but it was too unbelievable to speak rashly.

He continued to recall the scenes from the appearance of the lone star.

"Outline of Mountains and Seas Changes, Stellar Rhythm Law..."

Saint Lianshan, seemingly unaware of Li Fan's inner turmoil, continued, "Shou Qiu's idea is indeed excellent. Mountains and Seas are in a standoff with the Void Realm. Now that the Void Realm army is pressing in, Mountains and Seas can naturally mobilize its forces to fight back. The key issue is..."

"How can it be done?"

"Behind the Void Realm, there is a will directing its forces. But Mountains and Seas..."

Saint Lianshan shook his head slightly, "Since the decay of Mountains and Seas' eternity, it has been a long time since we felt its true will. Even if we can occasionally sense it, it is merely instinct."

"Unconscious instinct, perhaps, can strive to contend with crises, but it cannot mobilize troops and strategically guide forces like the Void Realm. This is perhaps the most crucial reason why Mountains and Seas has fallen behind."

Chapter 1737: A Trance Sees the Future

"Even we, who are called Lianshan and Guihai, cannot truly gather the power of Mountains and Seas in one place."

"Moreover, offensives can be freely directed, but how can defense be arbitrarily changed? Under the backdrop of Dao Annihilation's erosion, every part of Mountains and Seas is almost at its limit of tolerance. If we draw power from Mountains and Seas here, the other segments will likely be swallowed by the Void Realm immediately."

"We are blocked by the Void Realm's gaze, unable to survey all of Mountains and Seas. Even if we could control the power of Mountains and Seas, we cannot outmaneuver the entity behind the Void Realm," the Three Saints concluded.

Li Fan pondered for a moment, and with a sigh, said, "I was perhaps being too optimistic. However, with the current critical situation, Mountains and Seas possess ample power yet cannot utilize it. To be preyed upon by the Void Realm without resistance is truly vexing."

"If there were Saints whose sight could span from beginning to end, and whose strength could move mountains and seas... wouldn't the crisis be resolved instantly?"

The Saints present were all rendered speechless.

"I actually think Fellow Daoist Universe Cycle's previous idea might not be entirely infeasible," Stealing Opportunity suddenly said during the silence, capturing the attention of all the Saints.

"As the saying goes, embracing death leads to survival. In times of life and death, extraordinary power is bound to emerge. Although we cannot actively mobilize the power of Mountains and Seas now, perhaps we can force it."

The memories of hundreds of billions of years had swept away the gloom in Stealing Opportunity's heart.

He had regained his former confidence and said slowly, "Not only pushing Mountains and Seas to unleash its own power, but also involving the couple, Qiu Tianhui and Shao Zidai!"

"At such a crucial central node of the life脉络 of Mountains and Seas, I refuse to believe they would leave no protective measures. After all, the Great Dao of beings is dependent on Mountains and Seas. If this segment of Mountains and Seas is destroyed, regardless of their schemes or where they are hiding, they will surely be affected!"

Stealing Opportunity's analysis, though to the point, was somewhat bordering on dangerous.

While the Saints were pondering the feasibility of his suggestion, only the Three Saints and Li Fan noticed the deeper implications of Stealing Opportunity's words.

"Forcing Mountains and Seas... Stealing Opportunity's idea is somewhat risky."

"Interesting. If it were the usual Stealing Opportunity influenced by the Xuanji Ring's Concentric Unity, he wouldn't have had such a thought. It's more like the natural thought of Stealing Opportunity freed from constraints and returning to his original nature. Could it be..." Li Fan observed calmly, subtly gauging everyone.

"After billions of years, even [Concentric Unity] has faded somewhat. The situation with me, Shou Qiu, and Dao De is relatively good, as it's a unified trinity of sharing and close connection."

"But the other Saints in the Xuanji Ring... seem to show signs of losing control."

"Although it's very faint, it should not be overlooked."

If Li Fan noticed, the Three Saints had naturally also perceived it.

However, they did not expose it, and the Xuanji Ring emitted a faint, almost imperceptible flash of white light.

Whether they had lost control or not was a separate matter from the feasibility of their suggestion.

After some deduction, the Three Saints acknowledged that Stealing Opportunity's plan did indeed have some chance of success.

However, it was not considered the best course of action and could only be used as a backup plan if absolutely necessary.

"Let us first accumulate strength and engage in battle."

"Although the Void Realm is powerful, we need not be afraid before the fight. Not to mention ourselves, the scene of Shou Qiu and Universe Cycle repelling numerous Void Realm avatars is still vivid in our minds!" Tai Yi looked towards the outside of the Void Realm, a cold glint flashing in his calm eyes.

The strength gained from repeatedly reconnecting Mountains and Seas had gradually brought the Three Saints closer to their original temperaments.

As the wielder of the All-Beings Staff, who had devoured and assimilated all five primal chaos, Tai Yi was certainly not one to surrender easily.

In response to Tai Yi's praise, Li Fan and the other two simply smiled without excessive reply.

As the holder of the [True Spirit Infusion] divine ability, Li Fan was the most crucial source of reserve strength for rejoining Mountains and Seas. Unless absolutely necessary, the Saints would not send him into battle.

Unless he voluntarily offered.

However, this time, Li Fan had already made up his mind to observe the unfolding events.

Therefore, for the next period, Li Fan spent his days journeying through Mountains and Seas, searching for potential talents and guiding them towards Sainthood.

Hundreds of thousands of years had passed from the time he was familiar with.

Mountains and Seas had produced countless talented individuals.

Selecting them successfully was no easy feat.

This time, Li Fan also proactively contacted Saint Tai Wei. He selected promising candidates from the Tai Wei Holy Dynasty.

In the past, when choosing reserve Saints, the focus was mainly on nameless cultivators at the transcendence realm.

However, the Holy Dynasty had a unique situation, a world governed by a single ruler. Despite billions of subjects, the highest cultivation level besides the Tai Wei Holy Emperor was only True Immortal.

Even if they met all the requirements for resources and talent to ascend to Sainthood, it would take an extremely long time. They truly could not afford to wait.

However, this time, Li Fan had a premonition that the battle for the front segment of Mountains and Seas might be a protracted war.

The countless citizens of the Holy Dynasty could not be overlooked.

Li Fan's appearance greatly alleviated the Tai Wei Holy Emperor's burden of alchemy, thus he held considerable goodwill towards Li Fan and naturally agreed to his request.

Not only were all the beings in the vast Holy Dynasty made available for Li Fan to choose from,

but the Emperor even personally recommended several individuals.

"These few individuals may not have cultivated yet, but their character and innate talent are top-notch. Among the entire Holy Dynasty, they are among the very best. All they lack is the corresponding opportunity."

After his battle with [Stealing Opportunity], Emperor Tai Wei seemed to have undergone another transformation.

Previously, he was purely a noble and supreme Holy Emperor, residing in lofty heights.

Now, a transcendent and ethereal aura occasionally emanated from him.

Li Fan glanced at him with slight interest, and asked curiously, "Fellow Daoist Tai Wei seems to have gained new enlightenment?"

Emperor Tai Wei did not conceal anything, "I used to believe that as an Emperor ruling a Holy Dynasty, I should govern all my people and perceive everything. However, after observing the memories of the Three Saints' billion-year journey through Mountains and Seas, and realizing that even Mountains and Seas could not maintain eternity, my thoughts began to change."

"To be omnipresent and omniscient is indeed good. But perhaps..."

"To be hidden within heaven and earth, yet not be there, allowing the populace to be unaware, to grow accustomed and forget. This might be superior."

Li Fan frowned slightly, not expressing agreement.

Emperor Tai Wei smiled, "It's merely an experiment. Fellow Daoist Universe Cycle need not worry too much."

"The Holy Dynasty is, after all, my Holy Dynasty."

"Even if there are cataclysmic changes, returning to a stable state is within my thought."

"Fellow Daoist Tai Wei is truly domineering!" Li Fan praised.

He paused slightly, then Li Fan suddenly raised an unrelated question, "Fellow Daoist Tai Wei also crossed paths with [Stealing Opportunity] before. I wonder..."

"How did it feel?"

Emperor Tai Wei, seeing Li Fan's expression, understood his intent. He answered frankly, "Merely so."

"If the beings of the so-called Primordial Immortal Realm are all of such caliber."

"The Tai Wei Holy Dynasty might have been able to expand its territory at the dawn of Mountains and Seas!"

Emperor Tai Wei’s implication aligned perfectly with Li Fan’s thoughts.

Li Fan simply exchanged a knowing smile and then moved on.

After traveling for eighteen years in the Holy Dynasty, Li Fan selected three suitable candidates.

Two of them were recommended by the Holy Emperor.

One was a lecturer in the Holy Dynasty, whose life should have been dedicated to spreading the Holy Emperor's words to all people. However, this person did not believe what he taught. Within the Holy Dynasty, this was naturally an act of extreme treason. However, he hid it well, and was never discovered by those around him.

If it were only for this, the Holy Emperor would never have valued him so highly.

The most interesting point was that as a lecturer, this person was familiar with various classics. He knew the greatness of the Holy Emperor he served. Therefore, he was well aware that his little "rebellion" could never be hidden from the great Holy Emperor.

"Supreme Holy Emperor, like heaven and earth, encompasses all things. How could he not tolerate my minor heresy?"

Although harboring rebellious thoughts, he also understood the importance of proportion and discretion.

The Holy Dynasty was the Holy Emperor's foundation of cultivation, and he would certainly not allow anyone to damage it. Though he did not believe in the Holy Emperor, he did not spread his rebellious thoughts to others. Instead, he was absolutely loyal to the task of spreading the Dao.

Diligently and without any slack.

"This person is truly contradictory," Li Fan remarked with a smile upon learning of his background.

"The Emperor sees it not as a contradiction. It is merely seeking a possibility to break free from the Holy Dynasty. Since he wishes it, why not grant it?"

"Moreover, his cultivation will certainly not disgrace the prestige of the Holy Dynasty," Emperor Tai Wei said calmly.

The lecturer's name was Su Shaozhong, an ordinary name, yet perhaps hinting at deeper meaning.

The other person recommended by the Holy Emperor was a martial artist of the Holy Dynasty, Hong Qianquan.

Within the cultivation system permitted by the Holy Dynasty, he effortlessly reached the pinnacle. Truly like a celestial being, worthy of use.

As for the third person among the trio, he was personally chosen by Li Fan.

Compared to Su Shaozhong and Hong Qianquan, he was utterly ordinary.

Even Emperor Tai Wei was somewhat perplexed by Li Fan's choice.

However, the Holy Emperor did not probe further, and Li Fan offered no explanation.

The reason for choosing him was that Li Fan sensed a familiar aura from this person.

The familiarity was not from this world, nor from any previous life Li Fan had experienced.

It was...

From instinct.

Previously, when Li Fan underwent the endless cycles of reincarnation woven by the Great Dao of Universe Cycle, he had doubted his own sharp intuition.

The so-called intuition was merely the memory of past experiences after countless cycles of reincarnation.

Whether this guess was true or false, he would set it aside for now.

Now, Li Fan felt a sense of familiarity from a mortal of the Holy Dynasty, as if he had met them several times.

How could he not take this seriously?

Li Fan silently observed this mortal named Mo Yongge.

Attempting to find a clue in his intuitive memories.

All past experiences seemed to have faded completely.

No matter how much he searched, he could not find its trace.

But this time, Li Fan was very patient.

The three were taken along to cultivate, continuing to search for potential Saints in Mountains and Seas.

Adding the Three Saints might help the current situation,

but their contribution would be limited.

Li Fan still needed to continue his search.

More than a hundred years passed, and the situation in Mountains and Seas grew increasingly dire.

Indeed, with the assistance from the later segment of Mountains and Seas, the pressure from the Void Realm was temporarily held back.

But soon the Void Realm also sensed this external force.

Without hesitation, they chose to escalate.

Like dark clouds obscuring the sun, the accumulated might of the Void Realm surpassed previous levels.

Under the heavy obstruction of the Void Realm, even the gaze of the Three Saints could no longer penetrate.

They were completely confined within their limited scope.

Fortunately, their foundation remained, and they were not easily breached for the time being.

Under the combined efforts of Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Dao De, they even repelled several Void Realm avatar attacks.

"But it won't hold for much longer."

"At most another five hundred years."

Li Fan was content to only intervene during critical moments.

He continued to search for promising candidates while observing Mo Yongge.

It was as if piecing together fragments.

The past that had been lost was slowly resurfacing.

"If I'm not mistaken..."

"The time period is roughly the same as now. However, the experiences encountered were completely different."

"The Holy Emperor perished, scattering his fortune amongst the people before his death, leading to a surge of emergent powers."

"Mo Yongge was one of them. He reached the Saint realm, and was even someone I was 'Concentric Unity' with before."

"Just like Dao De and Shou Qiu."

Li Fan slowly closed his eyes, hiding his immense inner turmoil.

Even witnessing the destruction of Mountains and Seas would not have caused him such distress.

Perhaps only the shock he felt at the appearance of the lone star could compare.

"The more I recall, the clearer it becomes. It's as if I personally experienced it."

"It's definitely not just imagination."

"But the key is, when was this?"

Li Fan knew the crux of the matter was not Mo Yongge, but himself.

Once again, Li Fan traced back all his memories since his transmigration.

He even enlisted the help of Shou Qiu Gong and Dao De to review everything.

To ensure nothing was missed.

Finally, he was certain that he had never experienced such a lifetime.

"Fellow Daoist Universe Cycle, have you noticed that the Mountains and Seas in this memory are vastly different from ours?"

"The demise of Emperor Tai Wei is something you have never experienced in your many reincarnations."

"It's as if..."

"It exists in another Mountains and Seas."

Shou Qiu's words plunged Li Fan into deep contemplation.

"Another Mountains and Seas."

These five words seemed to have triggered something.

Combined with his previous efforts to piece together lost memories,

another segment of Li Fan's lost memories began to surface slowly.

It was at the end of time.

The Void Realm was about to devour everything, and even though the Last Saint Qiu XinHui fought with all her might, she could not change the situation.

"Heh heh. Fellow Daoist Fan, why haven't you made a move yet?" Afterwards, he said this to Li Fan.

Then, Li Fan vaguely lost control of his body.

He even lost his memories of that time, only vaguely recalling the scene of Mountains and Seas perishing and the lone star appearing.

At this moment, these lost memories were slowly reappearing in Li Fan's mind.

"One finger can make the stars appear and then return."

"It can block the stars for a moment, but not for a lifetime."

"I am also seeking this answer."

"If I had not seen it before, where would my [Return to Truth] come from?"

...

Scenes, like thunderbolts, continuously illuminated Li Fan's mind.

Ignoring the searing pain in his mind, Li Fan desperately maintained his composure, analyzing everything he had suddenly learned.

"Did I say these words, or did Return to Truth say them?"

"No, it must have been Return to Truth's words. Otherwise, why mention 'my [Return to Truth]'?"

Previously, Li Fan had only thought that when he lost his memory, his body had been controlled by Return to Truth.

Now it seemed...

It was likely not the case.

Chapter 1738: The Ordinary Person is Truly a Perfect Man

"It is more likely that these were my own personal experiences."

"But I lost the memories of that time, so they only appeared as vague intuition."

At this moment, Li Fan couldn't help but doubt if he was still in a simulation by [Return to Truth].

But having reached the Saint realm, Li Fan's state of mind was already far beyond what it used to be.

After a brief shock, he quickly calmed down.

"Such doubts are meaningless."

"Truth is false, and false is truth. The so-called true Mountains and Seas were also re-evolved from absolute void swallowed by the Stars, as interpreted by Return to Truth. The key is my past."

"If my guess is correct, then my perceived first life might not be the true first life."

"What is my Return to Truth? What is Return to Truth?"

Li Fan, at the end of Mountains and Seas, had witnessed the divine abilities of the Saints.

The arts of False is True, foretelling the future, traversing the river of time, and inheriting by Heavenly Selection.

Originally, Li Fan had already harbored suspicions.

Coupled with the sudden recovery of memories, and the words he spoke, "If I had not seen it before, where would my [Return to Truth] come from?"

The answer seemed to be on the tip of his tongue.

However, precisely because of this, Li Fan felt it even more inconceivable.

"Could it be that Return to Truth is a fusion of True is False, False is True, and the Great Daos wielded by various Saints?"

"Then... who is that consciousness hidden deep within Return to Truth?"

Return to Truth possessed its own independent consciousness.

This was undeniable.

Whether it was the feeling of hunger and devouring when encountering something useful to itself, or the guidance it provided to Li Fan at critical moments.

All unequivocally proved this point.

Then the question arose: if Return to Truth were merely a collection of Great Daos, a pure tool, it should not possess its own consciousness.

Could it be that the Great Daos aggregated within Return to Truth gave rise to an independent will?

Or perhaps...

Recalling another self that suddenly appeared at the end of time, during the annihilation of Mountains and Seas,

a shocking thought suddenly arose in Li Fan's mind.

Once it appeared, it was like a breaching dam, gushing forth uncontrollably.

It filled Li Fan's mind, making him instinctively crave to verify the correctness of this guess immediately.

"Return to Truth is me?"

"I am Return to Truth?"

As this thought arose, the Mountains and Seas shifted, and all things perished.

In these past few years, Mo Yongge and the three others who had followed him and achieved Sainthood, vanished without a trace.

Shou Qiu Gong and Dao De, who sat beside him in the Xuanji Ring and shared Concentric Unity, also suddenly disappeared.

Even the Saints on the Other Shore, the entire segment of Mountains and Seas.

All seemed to vanish in an instant.

As if an unfathomable, mysterious power had completely and utterly isolated Li Fan from the outside world.

Besides Li Fan, there seemed to be nothing else in existence.

Then, a figure emerged from the void.

His form and appearance were identical to Li Fan's.

However, his demeanor and temperament were vastly different!

The moment Li Fan saw the other "Li Fan," his heart skipped a beat.

He felt both immensely familiar and extremely estranged.

With just a glance, he knew the reason for this estrangement.

The "Li Fan" opposite him stood there quietly. Even without speaking, he instilled a sense of innate peace and security in hearts.

As if everything could be entrusted to him.

And he would never betray that trust.

Utterly sincere, purely noble, supremely righteous.

Kindness like Su Bai, Virtue like Shou Qiu.

He was the savior of Mountains and Seas, like a perfect being in the world.

...

"You... are me?" Li Fan was utterly shocked.

The "Li Fan" opposite him offered no explanation.

As Li Fan spoke, it was as if ice melting and snow thawing.

Unimaginably vast memories flashed from the darkness, like countless shining stars, flooding in.

Not long ago, Li Fan had experienced, through the perspective of the Three Saints, a thousand billion years of time from the dawn of Mountains and Seas to its current mid-to-late stage.

While the path of a thousand billion years in Mountains and Seas was long, with Li Fan's current strength, he could barely endure it.

But now, Li Fan was about to be annihilated and destroyed by his own past memories.

Like an ant compared to the vast ocean, falling into it instantly, it was impossible to see its entirety.

He could only vaguely glimpse the past from the countless overlapping raindrops in his surroundings.

A thousand billion years, a significant portion of Mountains and Seas' lifespan.

But now, in Li Fan's sea of memories, it was merely a droplet condensed from a single cycle of reincarnation.

In the vast ocean, how many water droplets were there, more than trillions?

That was the path the past "Li Fan" had walked.

Countless reincarnations, countless attempts.

All for the purpose of saving Mountains and Seas from the Stars.

However, as "Li Fan" had said.

"It can block the stars for a moment, but not for a lifetime."

The ultimate outcome of all final reincarnations was the descent of the lone star, devouring everything.

Mountains and Seas could not be saved in the end.

...

Compared to the other self hidden within Return to Truth, the current Li Fan was truly pathetic.

He could observe and accept the memories of one or ten reincarnations,

but gradually, with hundreds and thousands, he began to falter.

It was as if he had fallen into the abyss of the sea; the pressure from all around was immense, almost crushing Li Fan's soul completely.

"It's not time yet."

"Go back for now."

Just as Li Fan was about to be completely engulfed by the surrounding darkness, a voice appeared, rescuing him in time.

The darkness receded, and the vast past memories, like bubbles, vanished before Li Fan's eyes.

The two looked at each other.

Combined with the clues gleaned from the previous memories, Li Fan finally pieced together the truth.

The Li Fan of the past had repeatedly attempted to save Mountains and Seas from the [Stars].

But like the countless beings struggling within Mountains and Seas, all attempts were futile.

He tried countless times, but each time failed to truly prevent the descent of the Stars.

One failure after another, with no hope of success in sight.

Yet, he never gave up.

In the very end, he decided to make a change.

This change was the origin of the current Li Fan.

Li Fan finally understood why "Return to Truth" had been so resistant to interacting with him from the very beginning.

Besides the vast difference in their scale, where the other party could engulf Li Fan with a mere thought,

more importantly, it was to preserve the independence of the current Li Fan.

To prevent him from being influenced by the past, and to act according to his own instincts.

After all, they originated from the same source. If the two had close contact, the result would be as Li Fan had just experienced.

In an instant, falling into the abyss, consumed by his own past memories.

His soul was shattered.

"Save the world..."

"Save myself first."

Only the last voice echoed in Li Fan's heart.

The veil isolating him from the outside world abruptly dissipated.

As if suddenly surfacing from underwater, Li Fan instinctively gasped for air.

Even though he had finally found the answer he had desperately sought, Li Fan did not feel a sense of sudden enlightenment.

Instead, various emotions, difficult to suppress, began to arise in his heart.

"The only thing worth celebrating is..."

"The past me is likely truly dead."

Chapter 1739: United Hearts To Solve Doubts

"Whether the past me was incredibly powerful or not, the moment he decided to make a 'change,' he ceased to exist conceptually."

"What is currently sealed within Return to Truth is not true consciousness."

"But 'experience' built upon an unimaginably vast amount of memory data."

"The owner of this memory originally belonged to Li Fan."

"Therefore, upon initial contact, it could not be stopped and converged towards Li Fan's mind."

"But precisely because the past Li Fan had become impossibly powerful, even though his existence had perished, those memories of countless cycles of life within Mountains and Seas could still react to external situations like a true will."

"When encountering useful Great Daos, it would feel hunger and devour."

"When encountering fatal crises, it would warn."

"Even when encountering old friends who fought alongside him, it would come out to say hello."

"But he ultimately no longer existed."

"Only the instinctive reactions based on his vast memories remained."

"Therefore, upon realizing that the current Li Fan was not yet strong enough to fully accept his past experiences, he decisively severed the connection."

Thus, Li Fan returned to reality.

"Fellow Daoist Fan, are you alright? You seem a bit absent-minded."

"What happened?"

Almost instantly, Li Fan’s mind was filled with concerned greetings from Shou Qiu Gong and Dao De.

Only then did Li Fan realize with surprise that even under the influence of the Xuanji Ring's 'Concentric Unity,' his encounter with his past self's memories had gone unnoticed by others.

"This indicates that the past Li Fan's strength was far beyond that of the Three Saints. Even if only Memory Stacks remained, they could ignore the rules of the Xuanji Ring."

Li Fan was not particularly surprised by this.

After all, no matter how strong the Three Saints were, even at their peak before the fragmentation of Mountains and Seas, they only cultivated within Mountains and Seas. Li Fan, however, had the accumulation of countless cycles of Mountains and Seas reincarnation.

"They say Concentric Unity, but I can now unilaterally shield certain memories."

"I can deceive others, but others cannot deceive me. Isn't that an inherent advantage?"

In an instant, Li Fan narrowed his eyes, realizing this point.

"However, in this situation, there's no need to hide anything from Shou Qiu and Dao De."

After a moment of thought, Li Fan decided to share his recent experience with them.

A short while later...

Shou Qiu marveled, "Originally, I thought Fellow Daoist Fan carrying Return to Truth and re-experiencing multiple times was already extraordinary. I never imagined there would be an even more convoluted past."

"So Mountains and Seas have already been destroyed and recreated countless times."

"With Fellow Daoist Fan here, it is truly the fortune of Mountains and Seas!"

Dao De was also momentarily overcome with emotion, "To be able to share Concentric Unity with Fellow Daoist Fan, we are without regret even in death."

Li Fan snorted, "I don't think it's that great. If he had truly succeeded in saving Mountains and Seas, then any praise would be deserved. But failing every time and repeating the same thing countless times, what's the difference?"

Shou Qiu and Dao De smiled wryly, unsure how to answer for a moment.

"Alright, let's put the past aside for now. I truly need your help to judge something."

"There are a few questions that still linger in my heart."

"First, even though I am absolutely certain, I still have doubts. Has the past me truly perished? Or is it some imposed thought process? Could he have left behind some contingency plan? Perhaps after I successfully save Mountains and Seas, he will make a move to counter me?"

"Second, the origin of my sharp intuition has finally been answered. However, the source of infinite spirituality remains unknown. I only vaguely feel that the past me did not doubt this matter, and therefore did not enlighten me. Is infinite spirituality truly infinite? Or is it the accumulation from his countless reincarnations?"

"As for the third point? Save the world by saving yourself. What is the meaning of these five words?"

Li Fan spoke fluently, expressing all his doubts in one go.

His demeanor was open and honest, without any unusual expression.

This was his way. Even facing his past self, no matter how great, noble, or divine the latter appeared, he would never blindly trust. He would doubt what needed to be doubted.

Under the rule of Concentric Unity, Shou Qiu Gong and Dao De, already familiar with Li Fan's character, were not surprised. They began to ponder seriously.

After a long silence, Shou Qiu Gong slowly spoke, "Regarding the first point, my judgment is consistent with Dao De's. The past Fellow Daoist Fan should indeed no longer exist."

"Having exhausted all possibilities without finding a way out, he could only stake everything, severing his past self to create a new life. It was like recreating the heavens and earth, thus creating a sliver of possibility. If there were still some hidden means left behind..."

"Causing failure at a critical moment, rendering all past efforts in vain. Wouldn't that be a wasted effort? Given Fellow Daoist Fan's foresight and character in the past, he would never engage in such a meaningless act."

Li Fan nodded slightly.

Of course, he didn't entirely believe Shou Qiu's words. He himself harbored doubts, so how could Shou Qiu not be influenced? He could be influenced by the past Li Fan; could the Concentric Unity of Shou Qiu not be?

However, for now, it was a small comfort.

Shou Qiu naturally understood this and quickly moved on, focusing on Li Fan's second question: "Regarding the origin of infinite spirituality, I have two hypotheses."

"First, it is an innate quality that accompanied your transmigration. It is precisely because of this characteristic that the past Fellow Daoist Fan could have had such admirable experiences. Otherwise, for beings born within Mountains and Seas, to jump out of the cycle of Mountains and Seas... even the Three Saints might not have been able to achieve it."

"As for the second hypothesis... it stems from what you said, that the past you had no doubts about the origin of infinite spirituality. If it came from transmigration, he would naturally be puzzled. Unless he knew certain memories that you are unaware of. From witnessing the origin of infinite spirituality during transmigration. Given his character, he would never conceal such an important matter from you. Since he did not mention it, we can only assume it was not mentioned. Therefore, we can only infer that infinite spirituality might come from the accumulation of his countless reincarnations."

Shou Qiu seemed to envision Li Fan countless times striving to save Mountains and Seas, and then regrouping after every failure.

He couldn't help but gaze with admiration, and then with longing.

"It is not solely his own accumulation. Or perhaps, it also includes the entire Mountains and Seas," Dao De added.

"Oh? What do you mean?" Li Fan asked.

"When Mountains and Seas were annihilated, residual True Spirits were left behind. When Mountains and Seas were recreated from nothingness by the Great Dao of True and False, how this residual True Spirit was formed is still unknown. If Mountains and Seas were recreated, then this guess would not hold true. If Mountains and Seas reappeared, not relying on the past True Spirit..."

"Then it might explain the origin of the infinite True Spirit within you."

"It is the remnants of the previous Mountains and Seas accumulated through countless cycles of reincarnation," Dao De said word by word.

Chapter 1740: Enlightenment Saves the World

"After the destruction of Mountains and Seas, only residual True Spirits remained in the Void Realm. When we traversed against the current, we all witnessed the vast and boundless quantity of these True Spirits."

"This is only a minuscule part of the True Spirits accumulated during one long cycle of Mountains and Seas' lifespan. What about hundreds or thousands, or even tens of thousands of cycles?"

"It is likely unimaginable, akin to infinity!" Dao De slowly explained his guess.

Li Fan immediately thought of the previous life, when he remained conscious for a period after activating Return to Truth. He then realized that his own infinite spirituality seemed to be constantly consumed during this process. He instinctively retorted, "Mountains and Seas were recreated, requiring True Spirits as a medium. The residual True Spirits were likely used to reshape Mountains and Seas after the activation of Return to Truth. My previous experience is the best proof of this!"

Facing Li Fan's confident words, Shou Qiu and Dao De fell silent and pondered for a while, then seemed to reach the same conclusion and smiled silently.

"Why are you two laughing?" Li Fan was initially puzzled, but after sensing their thoughts, his expression also became somewhat strange.

Disregarding that Li Fan already knew, Shou Qiu still shook his head and said, "Fellow Daoist Fan, the reason you feel your True Spirit is being depleted is because you are growing weary during the crossing."

"Is it possible..."

"Besides the depletion caused by extraction, absorbing a large amount of residual True Spirits from Mountains and Seas, exceeding your body's limit, could also produce a similar feeling?" Shou Qiu and Dao De both stared at Li Fan.

"Otherwise, with your infinite True Spirit foundation, how could it be so easily restored if it were truly depleted?"

"Moreover, with the Great Dao of True and False and supreme divine abilities, why would reshaping Mountains and Seas require the so-called residual True Spirits?"

"The descent of the lone Star would surely engulf all things. Even the Void Realm and residual True Spirits are no exception. The process of Return to Truth activating and traversing to the end of time also involved collecting True Spirits along the way. With your current strength, it would be difficult to bear such a quantity of True Spirits absorbed imperceptibly in a short period."

Li Fan instinctively frowned and retorted, "Absurd! How can I not distinguish between overeating and starvation! As for the Great Dao of True and False..."

He paused, and found that what the other party said actually made some sense.

However, due to his naturally suspicious nature, Li Fan quickly dismissed this hint of agreement.

Squinting, he observed Shou Qiu and Dao De, and Li Fan vaguely realized something. Because the past Li Fan and he were essentially the same person, Shou Qiu and Dao De, who shared Concentric Unity, did not treat him as an "outsider."

Coupled with the noble image he projected, Shou Qiu and Dao De tended to interpret all of the past Li Fan's actions with ultimate benevolence and compassion.

This was completely contrary to Li Fan's perspective.

Having realized this, Li Fan did not choose to continue arguing.

"This matter is not difficult to verify. The next time I activate Return to Truth, I will watch with wide eyes."

"Having been tempered by the Three Saints' billions of years in this life, and having witnessed numerous cycles of Mountains and Seas, my endurance has improved. I will no longer be muddled as in my previous life," Li Fan said solemnly.

Shou Qiu and Dao De both nodded.

The three tacitly moved on, no longer dwelling on the matter.

"Let's talk about saving the world by saving oneself."

These five words were clearly conveyed from the past Li Fan to the present self.

And they held no profound mystery, simply the literal meaning.

To save Mountains and Seas, one must first save oneself.

"In the past, Fellow Daoist Fan's heart was always with Mountains and Seas. To save the world, you often had to make choices between yourself and Mountains and Seas, and you would lean more towards Mountains and Seas."

"As the saying goes, nature is hard to change. With his noble character, even after countless reincarnations, some things would never be done. This might be why, after countless cycles of Mountains and Seas, not all possibilities have been explored. Perhaps the chance for survival lies with the current Fellow Daoist Fan!" Shou Qiu Gong commented.

"No matter how he struggled to turn the tide, he could not ultimately prevent the descent of the lone Star. To save Mountains and Seas, one must contend with the Stars, or even defeat them."

"But..."

After a long period of thought and silence, Dao De continued.

"To contend with the Stars while maintaining the existence of Mountains and Seas might itself be an impossible task."

"Mountains and Seas fragment, and then merge with the Stars. We cultivators originate from Mountains and Seas. To transcend our own origins, to save Mountains and Seas while contending with the Stars. Perhaps even the True Gods of that era could not achieve this."

Dao De's words inspired Li Fan.

Like a bolt of lightning, his mind cleared. "Mountains and Seas and the Stars are in opposition, diminishing each other. To prevent Mountains and Seas from merging with the Stars, one must either return to the beginning of fragmentation and take its place. Or..."

"Before the Stars devour Mountains and Seas, take the lead and incorporate Mountains and Seas."

"Mountains and Seas are no more, but I exist. And then I face the Stars."

"Is this what is meant by saving the world by saving oneself?" A peculiar glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

Shou Qiu and Dao De seemed to glimpse the fleeting images in Li Fan's mind and the surging emotions in his heart. They remained silent, neither agreeing nor objecting.

Setting aside whether he could truly contend with the Stars even after devouring Mountains and Seas.

Even if Li Fan succeeded...

What kind of being would Li Fan become after devouring Mountains and Seas and defeating the lone Star? It was beyond imagination.

How could they be sure that he would ultimately still choose to 'save the world'?

Uncalculable, unknowable.

Inevitably so.

But it was the only option left after countless failed attempts in reincarnation.

At this moment, Shou Qiu and Dao De could vaguely feel the struggle Li Fan experienced when making such a decision.

Li Fan naturally sensed the thoughts of the other two.

He chuckled, "You two are thinking further ahead than I am. Devouring Mountains and Seas, snatching food from the Stars' jaws, is not that easy."

"Let alone the Stars. The Three Saints, and even the Saints from the dawn of Mountains and Seas, I cannot overcome them yet. Am I to assume that if I claim to be saving the world by devouring it, they will readily accept? Is it only Li Fan who can act, while others cannot?"

"In the end, it still comes down to cultivation."

There was no doubt that Li Fan's words were highly rational.

Shou Qiu and Dao De pondered carefully and came to a realization, sighing, "It is precisely because we have witnessed the past actions of Fellow Daoist Fan that our hearts spontaneously recognized Fellow Daoist Fan as the sole savior of Mountains and Seas. We would support you unconditionally, even if you intended to devour Mountains and Seas."

"As for others, they would not be like us."

"Unless..."

"Incorporate all sentient beings of Mountains and Seas into the Xuanji Ring, sharing the principle of Concentric Unity!" Shou Qiu suddenly blurted out.

Even Li Fan's heart skipped a beat upon hearing this.

Given his nature, he would never share his innermost thoughts with others.

However, by chance, he had tried it once.

Having tasted the benefits and realized there was no harm, he had repeatedly done so.

However, the Concentric Unity of the Three was the limit of his current acceptance.

The idea of Shou Qiu opening his heart to all beings in Mountains and Seas was something he had never even considered.

"Fellow Daoist Shou Qiu, isn't that a bit extreme?"

"There are billions of beings, too many variables," Li Fan mumbled.

However, Shou Qiu did not abandon his idea. The more he thought about it, the brighter his eyes became.

"The nobler the character, the more one can feel the greatness of the past Fellow Daoist Fan. I believe that even ordinary beings in Mountains and Seas, after experiencing what happened in the past of Mountains and Seas, would make the right choice. As for those stubborn ones..."

"They cannot obstruct the general trend!"

Dao De added forcefully, "Upon careful consideration, it indeed seems feasible!"

Shou Qiu then said, "If it were not for the constraints of the Three Saints' Xuanji Ring, how could the Saints of Mountains and Seas unite in heart? Our plan is merely to emulate the story of the Three Saints. However, the Concentric Ring we wish to create will be far grander than the Xuanji Ring. Our reliance will also be far greater than that of the Three Saints!"

"If there were no greater Concentric Ring encompassing Mountains and Seas, how would the beings of Mountains and Seas unite for their own survival?"

Shou Qiu and Dao De looked at Li Fan with fervent eyes.

Their eyes were filled with undisguised fervor.

Li Fan naturally knew that this fervor was not directed at him.

But under the effect of Concentric Unity, it was directed at the past savior Saint.

"In a sense, the past me was infinitely close to the ideal self of Shou Qiu and Dao De. Though unattainable, the heart yearns for it. Under the Xuanji Ring's influence, they have experienced it firsthand, thus gaining infinite recognition."

The rapid and dramatic transformation of Shou Qiu and Dao De was, in reality, understandable.

Fundamentally, the past Li Fan was simply too powerful. His actions were too legendary. Even after his death and the dissipation of his consciousness, his past deeds alone could command and influence the Saints.

"But so what?"

"Saving Mountains and Seas now still relies on me," Li Fan snorted inwardly.

"Upon reflection, Shou Qiu and Dao De's plan might indeed be feasible."

"However, it requires long-term planning."

"The Hall of Great Dao of True and False, Stealing Opportunity, Stellar Fortune..."

Countless thoughts raced through Li Fan's mind, deducing potential changes.

The Saints were cooperating wholeheartedly, striving to reconnect and save Mountains and Seas from the Void Realm's encroaching army.

Unbeknownst to them, within their own ranks, the Three Saints, who were crucial, had already undergone subtle changes.

Although he had a vague plan, Li Fan dared not reveal any hint of it.

He knew very well that if he did not expose his innermost thoughts through Concentric Unity, he would immediately become an enemy of all Mountains and Seas!

The countless memories of his past self would also become treasures in the eyes of others.

His strength was still insufficient to execute his plan; he needed to continue to lie low.

"However, perhaps it's time to consider adding more candidates for Concentric Unity."

After witnessing the transformations of Shou Qiu and Dao De, Li Fan looked at Mo Yongge, who was yet to become a Saint, standing beside him, with a thoughtful expression.

"Choosing candidates must be done with utmost care."

"Like Shou Qiu and Dao De, their spontaneous concern for Mountains and Seas is the minimum requirement."

"Preferably, they would be those who fought alongside my past self and whose character has been verified."

From all aspects, Mo Yongge was undoubtedly a highly suitable candidate.

The fact that he could leave vague memories for Li Fan meant he was no ordinary person.

He was likely a loyal follower and comrade of the past Li Fan, inseparable through life and death.

Achieving Dao through the [Song], his faint melody echoed through the shattered Mountains and Seas, inspiring and encouraging the Dao hearts, enabling the Saints to persevere and fight even in despair.

Although Mo Yongge had not yet become a Saint, with Li Fan's assistance, it was a certainty.

"The only trouble is that the principle of Concentric Unity originates from the Three Saints' Xuanji Ring."

"The truly concentric ones are only the first Three Saints seated there. Others who came later were merely influenced subtly."

"The Three Saints can be one entity. But there is a natural gap between them and other beings in Mountains and Seas, making true Concentric Unity impossible. But I am different."

"To ensure it is foolproof, the chosen candidate must be truly concentric with me!"

A cold glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

"The Xuanji Ring is profoundly mysterious. Cracking it was already an arduous task. To further modify it now..."

"It cannot be done without understanding its principles."

Li Fan was not muddled by his past self.

He still had a very clear understanding of his own strength.

"With my current comprehension of the Xuanji Ring, even with the addition of Shou Qiu and Dao De, we might not be able to add another person to the Xuanji Ring."

"The one who tied the knot must untie it. To achieve the goal, we must still rely on the Three Saints."

"But how to subtly influence them?"

Li Fan looked at the increasingly perilous situation of Mountains and Seas, shrouded in the Void Realm's dark clouds, and a general idea began to form in his mind.

"However, we must not be hasty, lest we reveal our intentions."

"Compared to my past self, the number of reincarnations I have experienced is negligible. We can proceed slowly."

Now that he understood the truth of Return to Truth, his worry about it leaving him at any moment had vanished.

He could plan everything more cautiously.

Action follows knowledge.

What Li Fan did was in line with his thoughts.

He continued to search for potential Saints in Mountains and Seas, and guide them.

Besides the three from the Holy Dynasty, he found two more suitable candidates.

Without hesitation, he generously poured his True Spirit into them, doing his utmost to infuse them.

Compared to his perfunctory efforts in the past, Li Fan was now more diligent and attentive.

In his view, these newly ascended Saints would likely be his allies in the future.

While infusing True Spirit, Li Fan was also comprehending the True Spirits he was mobilizing.

With the memories of his past self, his understanding of them was subtly changing.

"Residual True Spirits are the remnants after the destruction of Mountains and Seas."

"And Mountains and Seas originated from the Gods."

"In a sense, this is the fundamental reason why beings can become Immortals and Saints."

"The residual True Spirits are essentially no different from the True Spirits inherent in beings."

"This means that the calamity of Dao Annihilation in the Void Realm has no impact on [True Spirit] itself."

"Only the appearance of the lone Star can erase them."

"But, is it erasure, or absorption?"

Li Fan recalled the scene he had witnessed back then and pondered secretly.

Previously, he had considered releasing all the True Spirits within himself.

Return to Truth immediately showed an unprecedented warning upon sensing it.

"Theoretically speaking, even if Mountains and Seas collapse, it can be restored with the change of True and False through a single thought."

"This means..."

"The torrent of True Spirits can even influence the reshaping of Mountains and Seas by Return to Truth?"

Chapter 1741: When the Three Saints Fell Together

"To reshape Mountains and Seas, it relies on the change of truth and falsehood. The change of truth and falsehood is not just one Great Dao, but the saying 'when truth becomes falsehood, falsehood also becomes truth.' True is False, erases the influence of the Stars. False is True, recreates Mountains and Seas from a realm of broken void."

"Birth and death, reality and illusion, existence and extinction. All depends on a single thought..."

Li Fan’s thoughts churned in his mind, and with a wave of his consciousness, a phantom form suddenly materialized before him. It was an empty silhouette, its features indistinct.

"With my current comprehension of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, creating life from nothing might still be difficult. But if it's just a lifeless object..."

Li Fan waved his hand, and the phantom of the unfinished creation dissipated, replaced by an ordinary-looking twig. It radiated no special energy, a mere piece of common wood. Yet, because Li Fan had created it from nothing, it possessed a certain extraordinary significance.

Li Fan had been able to create objects from nothing using False is True long ago. For instance, he had once created the 'Ancient Primordial Vastness' to allow Emperor San Mo to leap possibilities. However, creations born from False is True were highly unstable and could not persist for long. As Li Fan's comprehension of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood deepened, the duration of existence for his False is True creations also increased. This twig, if undisturbed by external forces, could now endure for a hundred years.

The twig repeatedly appeared and vanished. Li Fan continuously contemplated the process of transformation between truth and falsehood. After a long while, he finally confirmed one point: "This process truly does not involve the consumption of True Spirits."

"Then what connection does reshaping Mountains and Seas have with True Spirits?" Li Fan looked into the distance, his gaze seemingly piercing through countless illusory realms, reaching the very end of Mountains and Seas. He recalled all the segments of Mountains and Seas and illusory realms he had encountered on his journey.

"If the torrent of True Spirits were to pour out from me, the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood would naturally not be affected. The only thing that might change because of it would be..."

"The Stars." Li Fan suddenly had an epiphany.

"Even the corpses left behind from the countless cycles of Mountains and Seas could still be devoured by the Stars, becoming their energy. My past self has fallen, yet the Stars might grow stronger because of it. One diminishes as the other grows." In his mind's eye, Li Fan saw an image of the lone Star suddenly leaping out of the darkness, its destructive radiance even more dazzling than before. Li Fan’s heart skipped a beat. He vaguely understood the true meaning of that phrase, "It can block the stars for a moment, but not for a lifetime."

"Not only must I save people, but I must also deal with the aftermath. Being a savior of the world is truly no easy task." Frankly speaking, Li Fan had no interest in becoming the savior of Mountains and Seas. But he was very interested in devouring Mountains and Seas and achieving supreme power. As for whether the unconstrained Li Fan, after achieving his goal, would still be willing to save Mountains and Seas, even with a casual effort... that would depend on his mood.

...

While searching for ordinary talented individuals, Li Fan also participated in several battles between the Saints of Mountains and Seas and the armies of the Void Realm. Even so, the Saints' side inevitably began to fall into a disadvantage.

As they had analyzed earlier, the Void Realm could endlessly draw power from other time periods. With the power to encircle and kill a complete Mountains and Seas, it could naturally suppress a single, fragmented Mountains and Seas with ease. Not to mention the increasing number of Void Realm avatars, eventually reaching thirty-six. The constantly overlapping clouds of Dao Annihilation, after prolonged accumulation, seemed to have reached a qualitative change. Mountains and Seas, though not yet devoured by Dao Annihilation, seemed to have suddenly been cast under a shadow. Colors began to fade in Mountains and Seas, and the once vibrant world gradually turned black and white.

"What happened? Why do I feel as if everything around me has become ethereal?" The spiritual sense avatar of Bai Xiao, who had traversed to provide support, flickered incessantly, its radiance growing dimmer like a book whose pages were being torn out one by one, leaving only a thin cover. It wasn't just Bai Xiao; the other Saints' spiritual sense avatars, including the Three Saints, were also undergoing the same change.

"This feeling... it’s as if we are within the Void Realm, not in Mountains and Seas. Our very existence is melting away like ice and snow." "Although the Void Realm has not yet completed its erosion of Mountains and Seas, the encirclement’s intensity has caused the power of that void to penetrate prematurely. If this continues, Mountains and Seas will not be able to hold on for long!" "In that single moment, the Void Realm's accumulated power outside Mountains and Seas surged again—doubled. Dark and profound, it swallowed everything. Perhaps even the light of the Three Saints would struggle to illuminate it."

The Saints felt the changes in Mountains and Seas, their expressions exceedingly solemn. They looked towards the Three Saints, awaiting their decision.

"Strange, the Void Realm's reaction..." "Something is not right." Whether it was the Saint Gui Hai from the current timeline or the spiritual sense avatars who had traversed from later periods of Mountains and Seas, they frowned. They looked towards the sky, and countless images seemed to appear before their eyes. Even with the Void Realm's obstruction, their deductions could not be stopped. The flashing images became the only color in the black and white Mountains and Seas.

"Something has happened at the beginning of Mountains and Seas." "Saints have fallen, chaos has ensued, upheaval." "The resistance forces of Mountains and Seas have been greatly weakened, allowing the Void Realm to draw more power here." Gui Hai's deduction took much longer than before, and perhaps due to the Void Realm's obstruction, the consumption was extremely high. A single white hair appeared on Saint Gui Hai’s head. However, he paid no mind to it, attempting to continue his deduction. Saints Lian Shan and Tai Yi also joined in with great tacit understanding.

The Three Saints sat, their seven-colored radiance flickering, revealing some clearer images. Though fleeting, the Saints could clearly see who the Sage who had fallen at the beginning of Mountains and Seas was. It was precisely the [Lock] who had just retreated from this segment of Mountains and Seas!

"He is dead?" The Saints were all astonished. And at this moment, as if sensing the Three Saints’ probe across spacetime, dozens of malicious gazes simultaneously came from within the light and shadow. Like ravenous beasts seeing edible lambs! The Three Saints reacted with extreme speed, ceasing their deduction before the gazes could spread. Despite this, strands of malevolence followed the unseen connections, scattering throughout the Xuanji Ring. They took form. "Roar!" Some resembled ferocious beasts, some like ghostly spirits, and some like laughing skulls. Though their strength was far inferior to the Saints present, they still lunged towards the Saints with immense ferocity, roaring. The outcome was obvious; they were easily annihilated by the Saints. However, the Saints' expressions did not relax in the slightest. Instead, they grew even more solemn. Especially the Three Saints.

"We just felt dozens of gazes, but none of our own." "We are no longer in the Primordial Immortal Realm," Saint Lian Shan said with a grave expression. "Could it be that the Three Saints have also fallen?" Li Fan asked in surprise. "Not so. Not only us, but some old friends have also vanished without a trace. It seems..." "The time for separation has come." After the Three Saints finished speaking, they exchanged glances. Then, as if by unspoken agreement, their figures transformed into streams of light and faded away. In an instant, they perished on the spot, leaving behind dumbfounded onlookers!

Chapter 1742: The True Nature of All Saints

The sudden turn of events was too swift! Even Li Fan could not react in time. The leaders of the Saints, the commanders of uniting Mountains and Seas, the Three Saints Lian Shan, Gui Hai, and Tai Yi, had perished without any warning. And they had done so voluntarily!

"How... how could this be?" Not only the Three Saints of the current segment of Mountains and Seas, but even the Three Saints in Li Fan's original later segment of Mountains and Seas also chose to self-destruct after sensing the anomaly.

As the controllers of the Xuanji Ring passed away, the white light dimmed, and the expressions of the Saints gradually underwent subtle changes. In the world beyond the shore, the atmosphere began to become peculiar.

"Concentric Unity!" Li Fan immediately ordered Shou Qiu and Dao De to act. Before the Saints could be overtaken by their original natures, Li Fan and the other two occupied the positions originally held by the Three Saints. The Xuanji Ring's radiance brightened again, and the gradually deepening gloom instantly dispersed. The Saints were once again influenced by Concentric Unity.

However, Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Dao De were ultimately not Lian Shan, Gui Hai, and Tai Yi. The temperaments of the Saints had already begun to change.

"Well done, Three Saints. They claimed to be uniting and saving Mountains and Seas, but when it mattered, they ran faster than anyone."

"It cannot be called running; it is merely adding a bargaining chip for Mountains and Seas' detachment."

Although the events were bizarre, the Saints had witnessed too much. They had all reacted and understood. In the Primordial Immortal Realm, the Saints were absent. The time for detachment had arrived. It was likely that the Saints at the beginning of Mountains and Seas were all participating in that grand spectacle of Mountains and Seas' detachment.

Moreover, the Three Saints possessed the divine ability of [Primordial Immutality]. One entity, eternal and indestructible. If all three Saints across all time and space perished, with only one surviving, then this last surviving Saint would return to their peak state. To gain an advantage in this battle, the Three Saints decisively chose to perish in the other time segments, gathering all their power at the beginning of Mountains and Seas.

"Alas, Mountains and Seas' detachment. We are unfortunately unable to witness such an exciting event. Moreover..." Bai Xiao sighed and looked outside of Mountains and Seas.

The existence of the Three Saints was the cornerstone of Mountains and Seas. Now that they had suddenly vanished, the already precarious situation of Mountains and Seas became even more fragile. In various parts of Mountains and Seas, many possibilities were frozen, losing their vitality, and entering a state of static stillness, as if they could shatter into countless pieces at any moment. The remaining worlds also seemed to be slowed down a thousandfold, and everything within them became extremely sluggish. This was a sign of further existential decay. Their fundamental existence was no longer sufficient to support further evolution, like a dried-up stream at the headwaters, slowly desiccating.

"If Mountains and Seas perish, under the encirclement of the Void Realm, we will likely have nowhere to escape." Without the Three Saints' gaze piercing the Void Realm, pointing the correct direction, and without the Three Saints standing tall like lighthouses, guiding the way forward. Even with Li Fan's True Spirit infusion continuously replenishing them, the Saints would likely be unable to escape the layers of the Void Realm. The Saints all understood this clearly.

After Bai Xiao spoke, no one objected.

"What does it matter if the Three Saints are gone?"

"If we work together, we might still carve out a path to survival!"

The future was dark and uncertain. At this moment, Li Fan suddenly spoke. His words were bold, and he showed no signs of panic.

"Fellow Daoist Universe Cycle, do you have a good plan?" Influenced by Concentric Unity, and due to Li Fan's constant True Spirit infusion to the Saints, his perceived importance had risen. In the hearts of the Saints, Li Fan's status, though not as weighty as the Three Saints, was definitely that of a linchpin.

Li Fan's eyes narrowed, and his gaze flickered as he said, "Since Mountains and Seas have changed, our plan must also change. The previous priority was to reunite and save Mountains and Seas. But now..."

"We have only three words."

"Survive!"

Compared to the mission of saving Mountains and Seas imposed by the Three Saints, the goal of survival was obviously more in line with the original nature of the Saints. Li Fan's proposal at this moment was not refuted by any of the Saints; they all nodded in agreement.

"All beings can be used, Mountains and Seas can be used, everything can be used!" The situation was critical. Li Fan spoke concisely, directly sharing the plan with all the Saints. It was precisely the plan previously proposed by Shou Qiu. To rely on the life脉络 of Mountains and Seas to stimulate internal potential.

"As things stand, we can no longer afford to be too concerned about trivial matters!"

"The Three Saints went to participate in the detachment feast. We have no luck to witness it, but we cannot let them profit for nothing!"

"Speak, how do we proceed!" The Saints had no hesitation and all agreed to Li Fan's plan.

"Mountains and Seas remained indifferent to the threat of the Void Realm because, after all, the Void Realm only devoured the Mountains and Seas of the current timeline, not the entirety of Mountains and Seas."

"Given the vastness of Mountains and Seas, it could naturally remain indifferent to such losses. However..."

"What if we spread the crisis of Mountains and Seas' destruction to all parts of Mountains and Seas?" Li Fan's words made the Saints pause. They had been immersed in the idea of saving Mountains and Seas for too long, and almost never had such a brilliant idea occurred to them. Facing Li Fan's question, their minds were blank for a moment.

It was Li Fan who then pointed out the path.

"Everyone! Don't forget, we previously crossed the Void Realm and traversed Mountains and Seas by virtue of the life脉络 of Mountains and Seas. Similarly, we can now use this脉络 to go to other Mountains and Seas!"

"Of course, what we will do is not just to leave ourselves, but to bring the Void Realm's erosion with us to various places!" Li Fan and the three led the contingent on the Other Shore, and their execution was extremely efficient. Before his words had even finished, an extremely brilliant radiance erupted from the Xuanji Ring, enveloping the entirety of the fragile current Mountains and Seas.

At this moment, all the offspring derived from Qiu Tianhui's Great Dao of Beings were marked. The divine senses of the Saints poured into them. Moments later, myriad stars rose from the paper-thin Mountains and Seas, following the hidden脉络 of Mountains and Seas, heading towards the past and future.

And, as Li Fan had requested. This time, the Saints were not merely attaching their divine senses, but also acting as 'guides,' emitting their own radiance and pointing the direction for the Void Realm. The hidden脉络 of Mountains and Seas were like hidden tunnels all over Mountains and Seas. Although the Void Realm devoured Mountains and Seas, it was unaware of their existence. But now... new lights shone and rose within the脉络 of Mountains and Seas. And they quickly transferred and traversed between different Mountains and Seas. The Void Realm could hardly avoid noticing!

Without hesitation, the Void Realm immediately adjusted its offensive deployment. The heavy clouds of Dao Annihilation no longer universally devoured every part of Mountains and Seas. Instead, they primarily followed the flaws left by the Saints, along the脉络 of Mountains and Seas, and began to penetrate everywhere. With the Dao Annihilation being diverted, even the formidable invasion of Dao Annihilation reduced the pressure on Li Fan and the others within the Xuanji Ring.

Chapter 1743: The Mountains and Seas Enter the Painting

"Refreshing! So refreshing!"

"In the past, it was we who protected Mountains and Seas, but now Mountains and Seas has become our cover! Truly, karma cycles, and retribution is inevitable!"

Amidst the roaring laughter of the Saints, Mountains and Seas were shattered by the torrent of Dao Annihilation. According to common sense, Mountains and Seas, having suffered such damage, should have ceased to exist. But by some hidden force, it was being resisted from the Void Realm's erosion, and countless fragments of Mountains and Seas were being forcibly reassembled in one place, making Mountains and Seas still appear "complete."

Li Fan's divine sense swept across Mountains and Seas, and he instantly identified the source of this sustaining force. As expected, it was the divine sense left behind by the couple Qiu Tianhui. As the focal point of the Great Dao of Beings in Mountains and Seas, the intermediary node from the beginning of Mountains and Seas to the end of time, this pair of divine senses manifested as a couple was not truly a living being but a personification of concepts. Normally, they were unaware of this themselves.

Now, facing the existential crisis of Mountains and Seas, the couple instinctively looked up at the sky. Their expressions gradually became vacant. Their figures seemed to be rapidly vibrating, and with each fluctuation, a shadow of a being detached, turning into a point of light and drifting towards the sky. These points of light did not give birth to beings but flew to various parts of the impending destruction of Mountains and Seas, like nourishing supplements. After Mountains and Seas absorbed them, the tendency of fragmentation instantly slowed down.

"The Qiu Tianhui couple indeed left a contingency!"

"This is using the power of beings to nourish Mountains and Seas. It is like a potent medicine for a dying person, perhaps a final flicker of life, but it ultimately cannot save Mountains and Seas!"

The Saints saw through this clearly and remained bystanders. At the same time, most of their attention remained focused on the hidden脉络 of Mountains and Seas. As the torrent of Dao Annihilation continued to erode, Mountains and Seas' instinctive reaction finally arrived. And its intensity exceeded the Saints' imagination.

In various parts of Mountains and Seas, it was as if a great wind had suddenly risen. Those remaining possibilities that could barely withstand the impact of Dao Annihilation were instantly engulfed in terrifying vortices as this wind swept through Mountains and Seas. Countless possibilities were annihilated, turning into the purest power of Mountains and Seas. Beings, civilizations, possibilities, and Great Daos—everything existing within Mountains and Seas returned to nothingness in this immense storm. What remained was only Mountains and Seas itself. Utterly pure, and immensely powerful. As if returning to the state after the initial detachment, Mountains and Seas was merely Mountains and Seas.

Boom boom boom!

Loud collisions echoed from all over Mountains and Seas. Several torrents rushed into the sky, clearly the streams of Dao Annihilation that had previously entered the脉络 of Mountains and Seas, now being forcibly repelled by the mighty power of Mountains and Seas. The enemy retreated, and we advanced. An indescribable and immense vitality flowed from the脉络 of Mountains and Seas. The shattered Mountains and Seas slowly began to recondense.

Perhaps sensing the specific crisis conditions from the outside world, the newly formed Mountains and Seas no longer evolved numerous possibilities. Nor did it manifest the rumored form of the Primordial Immortal Realm. Instead, it resembled a stone carving. All phenomena of Mountains and Seas were imprinted upon it. Having lost the concept of "change," it exuded a solemn and majestic aura.

The Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas appeared, and everything within Mountains and Seas seemed to be enveloped by its power, losing its vitality and becoming part of the carving on the tablet. Even the Saints within the Xuanji Ring could not escape. The white light around the Xuanji Ring froze, becoming still. The irresistible power of petrification continued to erode inward.

"Go!"

Li Fan saw that the situation was unfavorable and decisively chose to manipulate the Xuanji Ring with the Saints and escape into the Void Realm. What could have been an instant journey was now making them inch forward in the petrified Mountains and Seas. Their intuition told the Saints that if they remained any longer, their fate would be the same as Mountains and Seas itself: petrified and carved into a tablet.

At the brink of life and death, they all unleashed their full potential. All sorts of Great Dao radiance flickered, illuminating the Xuanji Ring with vibrant colors. They forcefully broke through the blockade of the petrified Mountains and Seas and successfully escaped into the Void Realm. All that remained of the Xuanji Ring was a long line drawn by its outer light, lingering in the solidified Mountains and Seas.

Hiding in the Void Realm, the Saints, still recovering from their shock, looked back. Ironically, in the past, everyone avoided the Void Realm and Dao Annihilation. But now, compared to the surging Void Realm, the petrified Mountains and Seas seemed even more dangerous. At the very least, with their strength, no matter how fierce the Dao Annihilation, they could still cling to survival for a while. But facing this petrification of Mountains and Seas... If the Saints did not flee, their fate would be the same as everything else within Mountains and Seas: petrified and carved.

Faintly, through the patterns on the stone tablet, they could see the last scene within Mountains and Seas. But now there was no vitality, no future. Mountains and Seas had forever stopped at this moment.

"Fellow Daoist Tai Wei!"

Amidst the Saints' stunned silence, Shou Qiu exclaimed, causing their hearts to skip a beat again. Following Shou Qiu's gaze, they saw the majestic figure of Emperor Tai Wei carved onto the sky of Mountains and Seas. Like a blazing sun, he had stood before protecting the Holy Dynasty's populace, attempting to resist this sudden catastrophe of Mountains and Seas' anomaly. Although Emperor Tai Wei was petrified, his expression was still clearly visible. He stood with his hands behind his back, looking up at the sky, fearless. It was a pity that the strength of a Saint was not enough to withstand this calamity of petrified Mountains and Seas. Not only did he fail to save the citizens of the Holy Dynasty, but he was also buried along with them.

"How foolish!"

"Why didn't Fellow Daoist Tai Wei flee?"

"It was not inability, but unwillingness. Tai Wei's entire foundation was in the vast Holy Dynasty. Now that the Holy Dynasty is gone, and its people are gone, even if he could barely escape, his strength would be less than a tenth of what it was. Rather than become sustenance for others, it was better to end it himself."

"Fellow Daoist Gui Ming, what do you mean by that?"

"Heh heh..."
