The petrification of Mountains and Seas, the demise of Tai Wei, and all these stimuli caused the Saints to move closer to their original natures. Li Fan, however, did not pay much attention. He and Shou Qiu and Dao De had formed a Concentric Alliance, and could easily suppress the other Saints. At this moment, his gaze was fixed on the stone tablet of Mountains and Seas before him. This stone tablet gave him a feeling identical to that of the [Monument of Boundless Mountains and Seas]. The Monument of Boundless Mountains and Seas was inscribed with traces of various Great Daos, and the raised lines on the Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas also corresponded to the various principles within Mountains and Seas!

"If I could absorb this stone tablet, it would be like swallowing all the Great Daos of Mountains and Seas!"

The thought suddenly arose in Li Fan's mind. However, after witnessing the scene after the collision between the Void Realm and the petrified Mountains and Seas, he instantly abandoned this idea. He saw that the Dao Annihilation power that had lurked into the脉络 of Mountains and Seas had not only been repelled but also, the Void Realm that had already devoured Mountains and Seas, had its gains returned to Mountains and Seas' control as the petrification progressed. The Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas did not display a fragmented piece eroded by the Void Realm, but a complete picture. At the cost of sacrificing its own vitality, it forced the Void Realm's countless years of accumulated invasion to be rendered useless in an instant! And facing the Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas, the waves of Dao Annihilation, and even the Void Realm avatars, all wanted to invade again. But the stone tablet was like one entity, standing firm and motionless. While connecting the fragmented Mountains and Seas in a peculiar way, it also completely hid the脉络 of Mountains and Seas.

Chapter 1744: Seas and Mountains Can No Longer Exist

"The petrification of Mountains and Seas is like drinking poison to quench thirst. Although it temporarily cuts off the possibility of Dao Annihilation's invasion, it also means that this segment of Mountains and Seas..." Li Fan gazed at the petrified Mountains and Seas before him, feeling as if he were facing an ancient tomb. Ancient and solemn, filled with deathly silence. It blocked the Void Realm's attack but also cut off its own future.

"This is Mountains and Seas' strategy of procrastination. Dao Annihilation invades through the脉络 of Mountains and Seas, like poison entering the bloodstream. Although Mountains and Seas actively petrifies itself, it can avoid short-term poison, but it is ultimately harmful to the overall Mountains and Seas.

In fact, its harm is no less than being devoured by the Void Realm. Otherwise, facing the massive invasion of Dao Annihilation, Mountains and Seas could have chosen to petrify itself entirely long ago..." Li Fan's divine sense swept over the petrified Mountains and Seas, and various thoughts arose. He keenly sensed that the Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas was slowly expanding its range as time passed. Although the speed was slow, it was incredibly resolute. He then understood: 'This process is irreversible. Once initiated, all of Mountains and Seas will eventually become a stone tablet. It can repel the Void Realm's attack, but it still cannot prevent the arrival of the Stars. The day Mountains and Seas completes its transformation into stone will be the day the solitary Star appears.'

'Ultimately, the detachment of Mountains and Seas was to inherit the power of the Gods. But this Stone Tablet...'

'Although it contains all the Great Daos of Mountains and Seas, it is not qualified to be called a [God].'

Shou Qiu sensed Li Fan's thoughts and transmitted with great emotion, "In the past, I sat and watched the sea, deeply feeling my own insignificance against the vastness of Mountains and Seas, thus gaining various insights. However, facing this petrified Mountains and Seas now, I have no new insights. Although its domain is vast and its Dao is profound, it is ultimately of no benefit to sentient beings."

Dao De also agreed, "Even we can sense this, so Mountains and Seas must know. Using a future of despair, only to delay for a moment. It seems that at the beginning of Mountains and Seas, a major upheaval occurred!"

"The Three Saints previously mentioned 'the time for detachment has come,' not 'Mountains and Seas' detachment.' This undoubtedly means that the Saints at the beginning of Mountains and Seas were contending with Mountains and Seas for the creation of detachment. If the detachment in that year was not by Mountains and Seas, then Mountains and Seas would not exist now. Everything concerning the evolution of Mountains and Seas, and thus they had to fight desperately. Mountains and Seas' actions were likely also out of necessity. They had to face the gluttonous Saints while also preserving themselves under the fierce assault of Dao Annihilation..."

Li Fan chuckled coldly. "The Saints and Mountains and Seas fighting for detachment. It sounds exciting, but unfortunately, we have no part in this feast. However, Fellow Daoist Fan, why didn't you witness this upheaval in your previous lives?" Dao De asked.

"The origin of this upheaval probably relates to [Lock]," Li Fan said, looking at the ancient characters on the Great Dao Hall that were no longer struggling. "After I devoured part of its essence with the Great Dao of Stealing Opportunity, Lock's strength must have greatly diminished. The Primordial Immortal Realm is full of dangerous beings. If Lock's abnormality is discovered by others, it might become a meal for them."

"Perhaps it was the fuse for detachment." Li Fan frowned, trying to deduce something. However, he knew too little about the Primordial Immortal Realm. He gained nothing. "However, it can be inferred that the Saints at the beginning of Mountains and Seas were only one step away from detaching. With a little help, they could cross that invisible limit."

The three communicated secretly. Meanwhile, the Void Realm, after witnessing the petrification of Mountains and Seas, withdrew its heavy encirclement. Although it was still pitch black, in the eyes of Li Fan and the others, it had become much brighter. This segment of Mountains and Seas no longer had any value for them to devour, and the crisis was resolved. This turn of events was something they had never anticipated. The act of diverting disaster had triggered an unexpected reaction from Mountains and Seas, achieving the same ultimate effect.

"The petrification of Mountains and Seas is like a massive stone blocking the way. The effort to reconnect has also become meaningless." Li Fan and the others returned to the later segment of Mountains and Seas, which was still normal, and sat within the Xuanji Ring. The other Saints, having lost their long-term goal, were momentarily lost.

"We are now like a small boat on a river. Whether the boat sinks or not depends entirely on others. Our fate is not in our own hands... it's truly frustrating," Bai Xiao sighed.

"If it were still about Mountains and Seas' detachment, then it would be fine. But what if another Saint occupied Mountains and Seas' original path? We are all born from Mountains and Seas. If Mountains and Seas did not exist from the beginning, wouldn't we also perish?" Gui Ming's concern was not unfounded. Since the departure of the Three Saints, a sense of unease had begun to well up in all the Saints' hearts. They had initially attributed it to the Void Realm's erosion, but now, as the tide of Dao Annihilation receded, this unease not only failed to disappear but intensified. It was as if a great disaster was imminent, a calamity was about to arrive. Yet, the Saints could do nothing but wait for their fate.

"Even ants cling to life, are we just going to wait for death?" Stealing Opportunity's eyes were filled with unwillingness. "If only we had been a little faster at the beginning of Mountains and Seas!"

Just as the Saints' minds were in turmoil, Li Fan suddenly spoke, "I have a plan that might allow you all to escape this calamity. However, I cannot guarantee its success."

"Fellow Daoist Universe Cycle, please speak freely!"

"The outcome of detachment determines our fate. To escape its influence, the only way is to step beyond Mountains and Seas. We Saints, though said to stand shoulder to shoulder with Mountains and Seas, are far from being truly independent of it," Li Fan said slowly.

"That is true. But we have little time left. The outcome of detachment will be revealed soon. How can we step beyond Mountains and Seas before then?" The Saints were puzzled.

"Since Mountains and Seas can no longer accommodate us, let us return to the Void Realm." Li Fan pointed to the darkness outside of Mountains and Seas. "These past years, I have continuously infused True Spirits. Accumulating True Spirits, burying them deep within the Void Realm. After years of calling out, I seem to have developed a certain inexplicable connection with the Void Realm. However, in the past, our goal was to reunite Mountains and Seas, so it was inconvenient to reveal this. Now that the times have changed, it is not a problem to tell you."

The Saints, who had been battling the Void Realm and Dao Annihilation for so long, had developed it into an instinct. At first, they were startled upon hearing this. However, considering their current predicament, their stern and vigilant expressions gradually faded.

"Returning to the Void Realm? Fellow Daoist Universe Cycle, have you truly tried it?"

"In the Void Realm, all existence disappears. If we return there, what will become of us?" Although they did not object, the Saints' doubts remained.

Li Fan's face remained unperturbed, "Although I have never truly tested it, I believe there is a high probability of success. Don't you see the Void Realm avatars that besieged Mountains and Seas before? Their forms were identical to true Saints."

"If they can accommodate avatars, why can't they accommodate true Saints?" Li Fan said sternly, "We only need to try. With disaster looming, do you all have a better method?"

Despite his words, it was not yet the most critical moment. The Saints still harbored doubts. Until... Mountains and Seas suddenly became illusory and ephemeral.

Chapter 1745: A New God Descends Upon the World

This void was ethereal, fundamentally different from being consumed by the Void Realm.

Dao Annihilation devoured, yet Mountains and Seas as a whole remained. Fragmented, like a tree gnawed through and riddled with holes. As long as the great tree did not collapse, the Saints who could move freely within Mountains and Seas could each use their abilities to avoid the falling areas, still maintaining their own survival.

But the current ethereal state of Mountains and Seas was like a great fire starting from the roots of the tree. The raging flames consumed all of Mountains and Seas from start to finish, and nothing could escape.

Even if the Saints hid in the Void Realm, they would merely change their location. Their connection with Mountains and Seas would remain. The formless fire would then follow this hidden connection, burying the Saints together!

"The competition for the divided god, and Mountains and Seas actually lost?"

While shocked, the Saints also instinctively felt a great fear.

This was a precursor to their own impending demise.

Mountains and Seas perished, and the New God was crowned. All that Mountains and Seas had gained from the Gods, and all that sentient beings had gained from Mountains and Seas, had to return.

As long as one did not escape from Mountains and Seas, and their temporal node was after the divided god, they could not escape this calamity.

The Saints gazed from afar towards the other end of Mountains and Seas. The myriad things of hundreds of billions of years seemed to transform into points of light, flowing and converging towards the beginning of Mountains and Seas.

At first, it was silent, then as the light gathered,

it gradually formed a mighty torrent.

Even though Void Realms occasionally intervened, the giant waves merely brushed past them with a gentle pat, easily traversing them.

In the face of this unstoppable tide, the Saints also felt a sense of belonging, like a destination, from the beginning of Mountains and Seas. Although they could still maintain their footing for the moment, their bodies had already begun to lose bits and pieces uncontrollably.

Not only the sentient beings of Mountains and Seas.

Even the Void Realm could not escape this change.

In the darkness, shadows seemed to churn and surge. Threads of dim light flew out from the Void Realm, heading rapidly towards the beginning of Mountains and Seas.

As if being forcibly segmented and extracted, a deafening roar and a piercing screech arose together.

"Even what was once swallowed by the Void Realm cannot escape. This..."

"Who is the Saint who divided the god?"

At this moment of great change, Li Fan's attention was more focused on the Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas.

The petrified Mountains and Seas, compared to its normal state, had a stronger resistance to this regression.

But not much.

It persisted for about twice as long, but ultimately could not escape the fate of returning to the god.

Like gusts of wind sharp as knives, they gradually smoothed out the raised patterns on the stone tablet. All the Daos that Li Fan had comprehended on the Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas were swept away by the torrent, heading towards the New God at the beginning of Mountains and Seas.

Finally, the so-called hard stone tablet also slowly turned into countless grains of sand, disappearing without a trace.

"Fellow Daoist Universe Cycle, I am willing to try what you just said about returning to the Void Realm." At this time of crisis, Duan Chan was the first to speak.

The trend of returning to the god grew more intense.

During the time the Saints were hesitating, not only had they lost nearly a tenth of their existence, but their forms could no longer maintain stability. Like a disturbed ink blot, they flowed uncontrollably towards the beginning of Mountains and Seas.

Even the influence the Saints could exert on the outside world was greatly dissipating. Specifically, the Saints' transmissions became intermittent, as weak as mosquito chirps.

If it weren't for Li Fan still being in his prime, one might overlook him amidst this grand spectacle of Mountains and Seas returning to the god.

The Saints were in distress, yet Li Fan could still maintain his peak strength.

This was because the moment Li Fan perceived the anomaly, he enveloped himself with the transformation of True and False.

With himself positioned between true and false, even facing the surging tide of returning to the god, he could sit unmoving and move freely.

If the current Mountains and Seas were a great river surging towards the East Sea, then Li Fan, Shou Qiu, and Dao De, the alliance they formed, was a small boat on the river.

Although they could not stop the river's flow, they could temporarily protect themselves.

Li Fan did not immediately respond to the Saints' calls, but instead frowned and asked, "What do you think of this New God, Shou Qiu?"

"Although it has reaped the fruits of Mountains and Seas' divided god..."

"It is likely not a true god. At best, it is merely a new cycle of Mountains and Seas," Shou Qiu said precisely.

Li Fan could not help but smile, "At the very least, in the Hall of Great Dao of True and False, all Daos remain unmoved. At the very least, our transformation of True and False remains as steady as Mount Tai."

"We are like this, and I believe there are still similar beings in Mountains and Seas. Compared to that true god, it is still lacking," Dao De also nodded in agreement.

"Even the Void Realm. Although the Void Realm was forced to spit out Mountains and Seas after devouring it, the Void Realm itself has not dissipated. Not to mention the [Stars]. This new god will inevitably clash with the Void Realm. I see it as just another cycle restarting, ultimately leading to the same outcome of the solitary star descending."

"However..." Shou Qiu's expression suddenly turned solemn, as if foreseeing something.

"Compared to Mountains and Seas, this New God will likely not sit idly by. After it finishes dealing with the old Mountains and Seas, it will probably absorb us remaining remnants."

"No matter. Let him taste the power of Returning to Truth then!" Li Fan chuckled lightly.

Having awakened some of his past self's memories, Li Fan had no doubt that Returning to Truth could suppress this New God.

In countless past cycles, scenes like this had occurred.

But in the end, Returning to Truth always reset everything.

"Since Returning to Truth can return to the stars with a single thought, it can naturally shed the god with a single thought."

"Let us go with the flow and observe the true face of the New God up close," Li Fan squinted and said.

Shou Qiu and Dao De naturally agreed.

"As for the other Saints..."

In the torrent of returning to the god, the Saints could no longer maintain their forms.

Only distorted afterimages remained, their faces unrecognizable, still shouting something at Li Fan.

However, their connection to reality was becoming weaker and weaker, and even Li Fan could not hear them clearly anymore.

"But the foundation of the Dao still remains."

"Rather than benefit the New God, it is better to benefit me."

"Let's enter the Hall of Great Dao of True and False!" Li Fan said.

Originally, the talk of returning to the Void Realm was just a deception to stall for time. Now that the Saints had lost all power to resist, Li Fan no longer hid his intentions and revealed his sharp fangs.

With a wave of his large sleeve, he captured all the struggling afterimages of the Saints into his grasp.

Stealing Opportunity, Querying Fate, Duan Chan, Karma Judge, Star Raft...

Lines of text silently appeared on the Returning to Truth panel.

Some were already there, becoming clearer after this absorption. Others were newly added, contributing to the Hall of Great Dao of True and False.

As for the perplexed feelings of the Saints, Li Fan naturally did not care.

While savoring the essence of the Saints, he sped towards the beginning of Mountains and Seas along the torrent of returning to the god.

Without the obstruction of the Void Realm and going with the powerful momentum, their speed was extremely fast. In the blink of an eye, they had traversed one-fifth to one-sixth of the hundred billion years of time.

However, as they drew closer to the New God, the sense of returning to their destined fate became even more intense.

Even with the protection of the Transformation of True and False, his own existence and Dao foundation were gradually becoming unstable.

He could only huddle together with Shou Qiu and Dao De for warmth.

"The New God is being gestured. Even without seeing its face, judging by this momentum, it is extraordinary," Dao De and Shou Qiu both exclaimed.

The three in one, in a flash, traversed another fifty billion years.

They moved closer to the beginning of Mountains and Seas, where the New God was located.

With Li Fan's current understanding of the Transformation of True and False, he could no longer maintain the Great Dao of Universe Cycle against the New God. The wind of returning to the god distorted and warped the Transformation of True and False, as if it would break at any moment.

"At this point, the outer garment of Universe Cycle is useless to me."

Li Fan no longer forced himself and decisively abandoned the Great Dao of Universe Cycle.

Golden lights scattered into the surrounding torrent. Li Fan, having shed his outer garment, immediately felt much less pressure.

The Transformation of True and False no longer needed to maintain external objects, only to protect Li Fan's consciousness.

Dao De followed suit.

Only Shou Qiu could still persist.

As the helmsman of this small boat, he continued to lead them towards the New God.

"I see Fellow Daoist Fan seems to be looking for something along the way. Could it be the two white dots hidden within Mountains and Seas that you saw back then?" Shou Qiu asked while steering.

Li Fan nodded, "At the end of time, Mountains and Seas were lost to the Void Realm. Everything ceased to exist, only two white dots leaped out, facing the erosion of the Void Realm with a tenacity even greater than that of the entire Mountains and Seas. This shows the strength of these two white dots."

"However, they are hidden very deeply. Apart from the ultimate end when the solitary star descends, I have never seen their faces in other circumstances. Now that Mountains and Seas are returning to the god, the Void Realm has been swept clean. This is the best time to observe them. However..."

Li Fan frowned slightly, "Having traveled more than half of Mountains and Seas' lifespan, I still haven't seen any trace of them. Strange..."

"At this moment, Mountains and Seas has not yet completely vanished. They might still be able to hide. Let's observe further."

The closer they got to the beginning of Mountains and Seas, the faster their return speed became.

Only ten billion years of journey remained to the New God.

Even Shou Qiu had to abandon his own Dao path.

The three were left with only the shared consciousness of Concentric Unity, riding on the small boat named Transformation of True and False.

"The true Lord of Longevity must have perished in the battle of the divided god."

"For a period in the past, I alone enjoyed the Great Dao of Longevity."

"Compared to before, there are indeed different insights. I just don't know if I can contend for the position of Lord of Longevity."

Shou Qiu suddenly spoke.

"Hmm?" Li Fan heard this and felt a bit strange.

Because in the state of Concentric Unity, he had not sensed Shou Qiu's enlightenment at all.

After a moment, he understood.

Not only were their Dao paths diverging, but even the effect of [Concentric Unity] was gradually disappearing as they got closer to the beginning of Mountains and Seas.

Even though they knew each other so well and had gone through so much.

A sense of vigilance instinctively arose in Li Fan's heart.

Concentric Unity had not completely failed, so Li Fan's thoughts were naturally perceived by Shou Qiu and Dao De.

They both smiled wryly, "Fellow Daoist Fan, you are truly... cautious."

"It seems only with Concentric Unity can you truly feel at ease."

"However, caution is never wrong."

Li Fan did not feel embarrassed by their teasing.

"With Shou Qiu's potential, the mere Lord of Longevity will surely be within his grasp."

"Moreover, in this battle of the divided god, we might not be able to..."

Li Fan stopped abruptly as he was speaking.

In that instant, during the rapid journey with the current, he caught a fleeting glimpse of a solitary figure standing tall.

The small boat where Li Fan and the three were located, along with the great trend of returning to the god, sped towards the beginning of Mountains and Seas.

And that figure seemed able to stand still in the torrent.

The two sides passed each other in an instant, and Li Fan could only vaguely see its general appearance.

"Just now..."

"It was one of the two white dots," Li Fan stated with certainty.

Appearance and form could be disguised, only that unique aura could not be changed.

"But it was not the one I encountered at the bottom of the Infinite Sea."

"Their strength was equally unfathomable."

Li Fan, currently in the torrent of returning to the god, clearly understood how terrifying the devouring power of the New God was at this moment.

But the figure just now still carried an air of effortless grace.

For Li Fan, a passerby who passed by, it seemed to feel a hint of surprise. But it did not follow up to investigate.

Instead, it continued to choose to lie dormant and observe.

"Did Shou Qiu see the details of the other party clearly?" Because the effect of Concentric Unity had weakened again, Li Fan actively asked.

Shou Qiu pondered for a moment and shook his head slightly.

"With all Daos returning to the god now, all Dao paths within Mountains and Seas should be unavoidable. But that figure was able to avoid the influence? Truly strange. And..."

"It neither goes nor stays, it neither approaches nor retreats. It seems to be waiting for something."

"Waiting? Could it be..." Li Fan felt something and suddenly looked up towards the front.

The last ten billion years of time passed in a flash.

Upon reaching this point, the speed suddenly slowed down.

Like a confluence of a hundred rivers, the essence of life from various periods of Mountains and Seas all converged here, forming a brilliant and bizarre vortex.

Stillness, rotation.

Devouring, emitting.

Convergence, bursting forth.

...

Numerous contradictions filled the space, but because of the existence at the center of the vortex, all mutually exclusive existences could coexist.

God.

Not actively observing.

But in the instant of seeing this giant vortex, the figure of the god leaped into view.

Then his consciousness was churned and shattered like waves crashing against the shore.

All other consciousnesses ceased to exist, only the figure of the god echoed endlessly.

Li Fan never expected that even a New God, merely replacing Mountains and Seas, even one still in gestation, would possess such terrifying power.

Even with the protection of the Transformation of True and False, and the support of the Three Saints acting in unison.

Under the reflection of the God's shadow, his consciousness was easily shattered.

With almost no power to resist.

A small boat capsized, falling into the giant vortex.

Following the myriad things of Mountains and Seas, it slowly converged towards the New God in the center.

After an unknown amount of time passed without consciousness, Li Fan gradually regained clarity.

In a daze, he recalled what had just happened, and looking at his current situation, he was utterly shocked.

Although it felt like he had slept for a long time, he hadn't gotten any closer to the god.

The speed at which the New God was digesting the essence of the entire Mountains and Seas did not seem particularly fast.

Li Fan had only moved a little closer within the vortex.

The reason he woke up...

Was because Dao De sacrificed himself, using his remaining consciousness as nourishment. Coupled with Shou Qiu's continued nurturing, this awakened Li Fan.

"Fellow Daoist Fan, look at the New God ahead."

"Its state seems somewhat off."

Shou Qiu's weak voice came, and Li Fan's heart stirred. He couldn't help but look in that direction.

Chapter 1746: Fortune Seizes the Heart

Even though they were on the verge of the vortex, almost within a step of the New God's supposed location, they still couldn't see its true form.

They only observed a colossal shadowy figure standing within the vortex, silently absorbing the brilliance of countless energies.

It seemed to be in a deep slumber, with no trace of outward fluctuation. If one didn't look, its existence would be imperceptible.

This was drastically different from the overbearing divine shadow that had appeared in Li Fan’s consciousness just moments ago, knocking him unconscious.

"Fellow Daoist Shou Qiu, what exactly happened?"

"Why do I feel..." Li Fan asked, his voice filled with doubt.

"It seems I'm not the only one experiencing this illusion. The New God truly is dead," Shou Qiu said, panting heavily, appearing extremely weak.

"The New God is dead."

Li Fan, feeling a confirmation of his vague sense, stared blankly ahead.

His perception of the scene changed.

The divine shadow still stood, majestic and imposing, yet unreachable. But within it, there was no spark of will or consciousness, as expected. It was like an empty shell, mechanically fulfilling the New God's mission of devouring everything.

Li Fan concentrated his gaze for a moment, only to be startled by the sensation of the colossal figure before him solidifying within his mind. He immediately shut his eyes, refusing to look any further.

Only after the divine shadow in his mind completely vanished did he manage to breathe a sigh of relief.

"Even if it's merely the corpse of a god, it's not something we, in our injured state, can covet," Shou Qiu advised, his voice filled with a rare weakness. Even without the augmentation of Concentric Unity, Shou Qiu instantly understood Li Fan's thoughts. "Even with our full strength from before, we could at best only protect ourselves."

Though reluctant, Li Fan tried again and had to admit Shou Qiu was right. The return of Mountains and Seas to godhood was a complete reshuffling of all power in the world. All things had lost, and the only winner was this newly born god before them. Under the immense torrent, even the Saints could only perish like ants, swept away by the wind. Li Fan and Shou Qiu had managed to persist until now only thanks to the protection of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood. Looking around, all things within Mountains and Seas had been extinguished and erased. Only pure energy brilliance remained, continuing to flow into the silent vortex towards the divine figure at its center. When the vortex was completely absorbed by the god, it would signify the true descent of the New God. But who knew what unforeseen event had transpired? The New God had fallen before it could even be established!

"The Saints of the early days of Mountains and Seas, who sacrificed their lives to fight for the fragmentation of the god, could never have imagined that becoming a god would only take moments, only to end in such a fashion." As the vortex slowly drifted, Li Fan, still unwilling to let go, occasionally opened his eyes to observe the appearance of the god's corpse. He had also attempted to comprehend and absorb the surrounding brilliance, but it was neither the Great Dao, nor Mountains and Seas, nor anything he had encountered in his past reincarnations. It seemed to be nourishment exclusively for shaping the New God. After trying various methods, even the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, he could not utilize it even in the slightest. He could only focus all his attention on the god's corpse. Li Fan suddenly remembered the figure he had glimpsed in the torrent of the god’s return. A thought sparked in his mind: "Could it be that He was waiting for the fall of the New God? Did He foresee this long ago? If so..." With a thought, the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood once again enveloped him. He was completely hidden within the infinite brilliance of the vortex, not revealing the slightest trace. "I hope that person can arrive sooner." Li Fan silently calculated the remaining time before he was fully engulfed by the divine shadow, and waited. Time flowed by. Li Fan was already halfway into the vortex. Even without looking, the influence of the divine shadow could still penetrate the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, taking shape in Li Fan’s mind. Then, it began to occupy his thoughts. The sense of crisis in his heart was difficult to suppress. Li Fan forcibly stopped himself from engaging with the divine shadow, wanting to observe further changes. "He should be here soon." At this moment, outside the vortex, no more points of light were flying in. The divine shadow seemed to have finished absorbing all of Mountains and Seas. Mountains and Seas no longer existed. Within the outermost light ring of the vortex lay the only remaining existence in the world: the god's nourishment. "Why is the Void Realm so slow to act? Or perhaps, from within the vortex, I cannot perceive things outside that light ring?" "Besides me, are there any other existences hidden here?" The divine figure already occupied a significant portion of his thoughts. Li Fan tried his best to ignore it, resisting the invasion of the divine shadow with thought. Compared to these questions, the memories of his countless past reincarnations seemed more suitable as a defense. As he began to recall past events, the divine figure imperceptibly dimmed. As if grasping a lifeline, Li Fan plunged into the torrent of past memories. Although still blurry, he could observe more than he could under normal circumstances. "In the past, I did indeed encounter the New God's descent. And it was reset." "But an experience like mine, where the New God is born and then quickly perishes... has never happened before." "Why did the New God perish?" Under the dual protection of the memory torrent and the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, Li Fan drew closer and closer to the divine shadow, to the point where he could almost glimpse its secret. At this very moment, the figure Li Fan had been waiting for finally appeared. A dazzling white light shattered the outer light ring of the vortex and brutally entered the god's nourishment. As if anticipating the scene within the vortex, it immediately shot towards the divine shadow at the center without hesitation. The once calm brilliance of nourishment instantly stirred into a tempest, intending to engulf this blasphemous intruder. The wrath of a god was indeed unbearable for mortals. Even though the white light was one of the few survivors after the great tribulation of Mountains and Seas’ return to godhood, under the devouring embrace of the surrounding brilliance, it rapidly dimmed by half. Yet, its thunderous momentum never ceased. In an instant, it tore open a corner of the vortex, reaching the edge of the divine shadow. It seemed as if, in the next moment, it would enter the god's corpse itself. To seize the god’s fortune! Li Fan, observing from the shadows, felt his heart momentarily stop. Instinctively, he wanted to obstruct it, to fight for it. Fortunately, he was powerless. Coupled with Shou Qiu’s calm dissuasion, he abandoned the suicidal thought. However, other hidden existences chose not to wait any longer. Within the turbulent vortex, just as the white light was about to collide with the god’s corpse, three different glows suddenly erupted. One white, one purple, one cyan. This other white light was precisely the existence Li Fan had sensed in the boundless seabed. Now that they met again, circumstances had changed. Li Fan remained hidden, while the other party was exposed. Witnessing the other party again, scenes rapidly flashed through Li Fan’s mind. "Fellow Daoist Fan, have we met before?" The willow-thin figure in white asked politely. Li Fan simply remained silent. Outside of them, the roaring tide of Dao Annihilation was vaguely visible. Without dwelling on the question, the two joined hands and together resisted the disaster. ... "This is the fourth time I've asked you this question, Fellow Daoist Fan, yet you still choose not to answer?" It was still the voice of the willow-thin figure. However, the surrounding environment of Mountains and Seas had undergone drastic changes. The initially bright and vibrant background was now dark and silent. And the two who had once fought side-by-side as companions now stood opposed, swords drawn. Facing the willow-thin figure's question, Li Fan still chose silence. "Hmph." "If you won't answer..." "Then die." Billions of dazzling white lights simultaneously surged upwards, dispersing the darkness for a moment. Each ray of light was like a sharp sword, radiating killing intent. It directly targeted Li Fan. ... "Fellow Daoist Fan, have we before..." "Met?" It was another scene that felt familiar. This time, the willow-thin figure asked again. However, his expression, compared to the previous scenes from countless reincarnations, seemed to have subtly changed. Li Fan still chose to respond with silence. However, the cultivator figure did not get angry because of this. Instead, he showed a thoughtful expression. "When truth becomes falsehood..." "Falsehood also becomes truth." Even after countless reincarnations, Li Fan could grasp every subtle change. Extremely keenly sensing the anomaly in the willow-thin figure, he did not hesitate. He directly activated the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, resetting Mountains and Seas. "Countless heroes in Mountains and Seas, how can they all be deceived..." A long sigh echoed. ... Boom! Boom! Boom! The fierce collisions stirred up immense ripples that jolted Li Fan awake from his past memories. He had no time to ponder their meaning, only looking at the changes on the field. The white, purple, and cyan glows, arriving after the initial white light, actually managed to block the first glow that came from outside the vortex. With the four points of light gathered together, Li Fan could finally distinguish the differences between the two white lights. The willow-thin figure, hidden within the god’s nourishment vortex and presumably an old acquaintance of Li Fan, was a silvery white, like a star. The glow that came from the outside world, the one Li Fan had brushed past earlier, was a deathly pale white. Though seemingly similar, their paths represented entirely different doctrines. As for the purple and cyan colors... Li Fan had no time to ponder before another change occurred on the field. The pale white light, the instigator of the commotion, after being blocked by the other three glows, paused for only a moment before retreating in the opposite direction. It swiftly retreated, and a thread of white light tore through the vortex again. It had come and gone! "Is it a strategic retreat due to difficulty, or..." What made Li Fan feel a chill was that it wasn't just the pale white light. The other three glows, after a moment's pause, also scattered in different directions. They intended to escape the massive vortex. "Bang! Bang!" Li Fan's heart inexplicably pounded violently. The outermost light ring of the vortex suddenly dimmed. The turbulent nourishment vortex instantly fell into absolute stillness. And then... The divine corpse in the center, which Li Fan thought was dead, suddenly opened its eyes. The four beams of light vanished into the divine being’s gaze. The divine figure stood tall, disappearing from Li Fan’s observation. What followed was the disappearance of the cyan light point, which had been closest to the divine shadow. It vanished soundlessly, without even causing a ripple. Seeing this, the remaining two white lights and one purple light accelerated their pace, scattering. The pale white light collided with the outermost vortex ring. However, escaping was more difficult than entering. That dim white ring was no longer easily pierced as before. Under the fierce collision, the pale white light instantly shrank by a fraction. However, it managed to create a gap. Flickering a few times, the pale white light successfully escaped. The silver-white point, representing the willow-thin figure, followed in the pale white light's footsteps, also escaping before the encirclement closed in. As for the purple light, it was not so fortunate. Like a mosquito, it was easily crushed by an invisible hand. The purple light point was instantly erased. Having easily dealt with two hidden pests, the god did not reveal itself. Nor did it choose to pursue the two white lights. The nourishment vortex remained still. The light ring at the outermost edge of the vortex flickered erratically. It was as if the god's gaze was constantly scanning within the vortex. As if searching for something. Li Fan held his breath, doing his best to maintain his illusionary state. He now understood. There was no divine fall! It was all a trap laid by this newly ascended god. Crude, but effective. After all, no one had ever witnessed the scene of successfully seizing a god's fortune. When faced with a god's corpse that offered no resistance and countless pure nourishment, even remaining Saints would find it difficult to resist such temptation. They had come precisely to fight for the fragmented godhood. Even if someone might have foreseen it was a trap, when other Saints made their move, others would inevitably be unable to resist. To seize godhood, to hesitate even a step was to hand over the fortune to others! Even knowing it was a trap, they had to fight. It was a trap, and an open scheme. "Having attained godhood, it is as easy for it to crush other Saints as it is to crush ants. Yet it still resorts to such underhanded tactics." "Who is it?" The god scanned, its gaze becoming more frequent. It seemed convinced that there were still pests hidden within the vortex. It persevered, repeating its scan. Li Fan's unease grew with each passing moment, feeling as though he might be discovered at any second. But he dared not rashly activate his True Return. After all, under the god's scrutiny, his consciousness would likely instantly become blank. He wouldn't even have time to activate True Return. "Fellow Daoist Fan, act according to the situation." "Allow me to face this so-called god." Shou Qiu's voice slowly transmitted. Then, a majestic figure leaped into the divine vortex. Where his steps landed, the brilliance parted. Shou Qiu revealed his original form, his hair and beard flowing, confronting the god. "After becoming a god, you have become unrecognizable?" "You possess a familiar aura, yet I cannot discern who you are." Shou Qiu's voice boomed, seemingly intended for Li Fan’s ears. The god remained unmoved. The turbulent vortex dimmed once more. It seemed as though Shou Qiu would be crushed to death at any moment. But... "When truth becomes falsehood..." "Falsehood also becomes truth." Shou Qiu slowly chanted, his long robe fluttering as if in a windless environment. His figure suddenly became ethereal and indistinct. Outside of him, a pair of giant hands seemed to flash by, grasping at emptiness. "I once sat and watched the sea..." "Now Mountains and Seas are no more." "I shall stand and annihilate the god!" As if blown by a fierce wind, Shou Qiu's robes billowed. He exhausted his understanding of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, pointing lightly towards the unseen god beyond. Ripples gently spread within the nourishment vortex. It was as if something had changed, yet also as if nothing had changed. "True Return!" Seizing this opportunity, Li Fan roared in his heart.

Chapter 1747: True and False at the Divine Front

Familiar white mist slowly emerged from the nourishment vortex, silently. At the same time, Shou Qiu's standing figure seemed to be frozen in time. His facial expression was fixed, frozen in the moment he had pointed towards the god. An invisible ripple spread outwards, and Shou Qiu's figure shattered inch by inch.

Compared to the purple and cyan light points, Shou Qiu’s demise caused a slightly larger commotion. It wasn't as if he was silently crushed like an insect; it had even stirred up a few ripples within the nourishment vortex. But that was all. Irresistibly, he drifted away with the wind.

However, Shou Qiu, amplified by the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, had undoubtedly stood at the pinnacle of Sainthood. His final strike, aimed at the void, had ultimately brought some minor influence to the god, creating a tiny crack in the impenetrable nourishment vortex, the birthplace of the god.

The white mist of True Return, thanks to this opening, enfolded Li Fan at its core, providing him with a foundation and a source of power. The white mist no longer feared the god’s brilliance, rolling forth immensely from the void, blocking all external threats. The god's oppressive pressure seemed to have vanished. The world, apart from the white mist and Li Fan within it, became utterly silent, so silent it was almost suffocating.

"True Return was successful?" Li Fan wondered, a lingering fear in his heart.

At this moment, the white mist violently trembled. It was as if countless fists from the outside were relentlessly pounding it. With each impact, the thick white mist became more transparent. Soon, the space outside the white mist, which had previously vanished, became faintly visible again.

Then...

A colossal, cold, and emotionless eye appeared at the edge of the white mist. Its gaze, indifferent and fixed, stared intently at Li Fan huddled within the mist.

At this moment, Li Fan felt as if his heart had been squeezed. He trembled with pain from extreme fear, his mind going completely blank. Without him as the anchor, the white mist began to break down even faster, showing signs of gradual dissipation.

"No! It hasn't discovered me!"

On the brink of life and death, after a brief moment of paralysis, Li Fan's survival instinct kicked in, and his thoughts began to function again. In an instant, his mind raced, his thoughts sharper than ever.

"When I previously entered the New God's sight, my divine sense felt like it was struck, and I passed out completely."

"That was when the New God was still disguised as a corpse. Now, the New God's eye is so close, yet I only had a brief moment of blankness?"

"The blankness was due to my own fear, not an external influence from the New God."

In an instant, Li Fan understood. Due to the concealment of the True Return white mist, despite how close the New God's eye was, it still hadn't discovered him within. It wasn't that the god had seen him. It was that he had seen the god.

"So, I haven't been discovered." With this realization, his fear vanished. The white mist instantly thickened again. The situation had a quick turnaround.

And as Li Fan's mindset changed, the True Return white mist correspondingly transformed, which he naturally noticed.

"So that's how the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood works."

With a newfound understanding, Li Fan sat down, ignoring the blazing sun-like, solitary eye of the god. He tried his best to recall his glorious deeds from the past.

"The Saints of Mountains and Seas, and even the New God, all bowed to my will in my past reincarnations."

"Regardless of who seized godhood this time..."

"It still cannot escape this fate."

"Truth is Falsehood!"

Li Fan's eyes were calm, all fear vanished. Only absolute confidence remained. The mist moved with his thoughts. More and more white mist emerged from the void, surging forward with ever-increasing speed. For a time, it sounded like the howling wind and rumbling thunder. Layer upon layer, they superimposed.

The god's solitary eye, finally, could see no more. The last thing the divine eye saw before it disappeared was a flicker of anger in its usually serene eyes. Then, a faint roar seemed to come from outside the white mist.

"It's done!"

Feeling the danger recede and having narrowly escaped, Li Fan couldn't help but breathe a sigh of relief. Unexpectedly, a wave of weakness washed over him. He felt dizzy and utterly exhausted, as if all his strength had been drained, leaving him powerless to do anything but be carried along by the white mist.

"The consumption is this immense?" Li Fan's head felt heavy, his eyelids like weights. His plan to observe the subtle changes in True Return before and after was thwarted. He could only fall unconscious.

...

Anchored 1 year. The initial anchor point. When Li Fan next regained consciousness, it was as if he hadn't fully escaped the peril of his previous life. His body felt as though he had undergone rigorous training, aching all over. This pain seemed ingrained in his soul, as if congenital. Even after Li Fan quickly cultivated to the Dao Integration realm, this soreness did not disappear, only lessened slightly.

Li Fan didn't rush to ascend to immortality again or choose his True Return inheritance. Instead, he reviewed his experiences from the previous life.

"Truly, pulling one hair moves the whole body."

"I never expected that my casual plucking of [Lock]'s essence would lead to the outcome of the god fragmentation battle in the early days of Mountains and Seas."

"Mountains and Seas return, and a New God is established. What a grand scene!"

Even recalling the torrent of godhood return, Li Fan still felt a sense of shock.

"Vast and boundless, obliterating all. The Saints of Mountains and Seas were like ants. The power of this torrent itself was not much inferior to the New God. If I hadn't been protected by the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, I would have likely perished on the spot, just like the other Saints."

His thoughts seemed to follow the torrent of godhood return, back to the early days of Mountains and Seas. Two white lights, one purple, one cyan, and the New God, all converged in that massive nourishment vortex.

"That white point..." Li Fan's gaze sharpened. Recalling his memories again, the past resurfaced.

"Fellow Daoist Fan, have we met before?"

"There are countless heroes in Mountains and Seas, how can they all be deceived!"

Li Fan savored these two sentences, his eyes narrowing slightly.

"This white point, like Saintess Qiu XinHui at the end of Mountains and Seas, vaguely sensed the truth of Mountains and Seas being repeatedly reset."

"After meeting me again, it developed a sense of vague familiarity, thus constantly questioning. Although I never answered, after another reincarnation, this white point's intuition grew even stronger..."

"It was unstoppable. Thus, the sentiment that the heroes of Mountains and Seas could not be deceived arose."

"Hmph, still too pedantic. From the beginning, one should have found any excuse to concoct a story. Remaining silent only makes it seem like a guilty conscience."

"If they cannot bebe deceived, then either kill them to suppress them, or unite in heart. Instead, it was allowed to grow unchecked..."

Li Fan was quite dismissive of his past self’s choices, shaking his head slightly. Recalling the scene he witnessed at the end of time, during the final moments of the Void Realm devouring Mountains and Seas, two white points emerged. He was almost certain that after countless reincarnations, these two white points had likely gained an inkling that Mountains and Seas had been undergoing repeated cycles. They might not have known that Li Fan, through the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, was the instigator. But this did not prevent them from hiding and lying dormant until Mountains and Seas was reset.

"It's quite uncomfortable being parasitized within True Return." With True Return’s reset, Mountains and Seas returned to its original state. But these two existences were like blemishes. Every reset, they were still subtly imprinted.

"They definitely wouldn't be like me, retaining complete memories of the previous life. But they should have a similar intuition to mine."

"If both are like this, what about that New God?" A sense of worry suddenly arose in Li Fan's heart. However, after careful consideration, his worry gradually subsided.

"Having past intuition is not terrifying."

"What is truly terrifying is the power of a god."

"Returning to the present time, that New God is merely an ordinary Saint in the early days of Mountains and Seas."

"The battle for fragmented godhood had countless variables. Even if this era were to repeat itself, the victor might not necessarily be Him."

It had to be admitted that the New God, having absorbed nearly all the energy of Mountains and Seas, was indeed far superior to a Saint. Those purple and cyan dots were among the very few Saints who had survived to the end, yet they were easily crushed by the New God. Even powerful beings like the silver-white and pale white lights, who could maintain their intuition within True Return, were utterly defenseless before the New God and could only flee in disarray. The gap was so vast it was despair-inducing.

"In the entirety of Mountains and Seas, only the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood could pose a slight threat to the New God."

"I don't know if Fellow Daoist Shou Qiu can glean anything from his final killing move in the previous life." Shou Qiu Gong's strike using the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood definitely touched the New God. Even if it was far from causing damage, Li Fan believed that with Shou Qiu's comprehension, any contact would surely yield some harvest.

"The first time it was possible to make contact, the second, and even the third time..."

"Perhaps the power to contend with a god might be attainable!"

"However... that New God is not yet in its perfect state," Li Fan's gaze sharpened, thinking this. All things in the world originate from the god. Never mind Li Fan, even the silver-white and pale white lights had not yet returned to the god. Add to that the nourishment vortex, not fully absorbed by the god...

"The New God I saw in the previous life was merely a demigod."

"Compared to the 'True God' that Mountains and Seas once devoured, there is still a huge gap."

"It is likely still no match for the Star."

"Perhaps the New God itself knows this, which is why it would resort to such crude tactics as feigning death, drawing in the hidden elements to complete its true transformation."

"Unfortunately, it did not succeed."

"In that case, it was indeed a stroke of luck. A mere demigod nearly shook the True Return white mist. If the True God had appeared..."

"Even so, it is not something that ordinary Saints of Mountains and Seas or ordinary methods can contend with."

"At that time, I almost thought the True Return white mist would be torn apart."

In Li Fan's vision, the New God's merciless giant eyes reappeared. Even within contemplation, Li Fan's heart involuntarily skipped a beat. However, Li Fan was no longer the Li Fan who used to be terrified by a cat, easily scared into psychological trauma. Composing himself briefly, he banished the influence of the New God.

"True Return white mist..."

"Transformation of Truth and Falsehood."

With a thought, a branch appeared in Li Fan's palm. It was purely an object Li Fan had conjured using the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood. Holding it tightly, his divine sense enveloped it, carefully observing every detail. Then, Li Fan began to try and recall his glorious deeds from the past. Although they were still fleeting fragments like a rushing river, as Li Fan contemplated like this, he truly seemed to return to the past. His strength and confidence grew with each passing moment.

"I believe this branch should be more 'real'." As this thought arose, Li Fan keenly sensed that the branch in his hand had indeed become more 'real'! It wasn't just a feeling; it was reflected in the duration this imaginary object could persist.

"If it were purely based on my comprehension of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, this branch could last at most..."

"One thousand years without decay."

"But if I were to add the driving force of my past self..."

"It could last for ten thousand years without decay?" Li Fan was somewhat shocked. Simply by adding his past self's intent, the effect of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood had increased tenfold! This was a discovery Li Fan had made in the past life, during the critical moment when the New God was about to tear through the True Return white mist. Now that it was confirmed, his heart was still filled with excitement.

"Can this be called borrowing the power of my past self?" Li Fan well knew how powerful his past self had been. The Saints of Mountains and Seas, the gods of the Void Realm, even the Lone Star, could all be reset by a single thought. If Li Fan could borrow some of his past self's power, he would be able to navigate the battle for fragmented godhood with ease.

"Although... there are some side effects." A new kind of soreness struck from the depths of his soul. Li Fan's hand faltered, almost dropping the newly created branch.

"Power can be borrowed, but not beyond my tolerance limit."

"Otherwise..."

"The injury might be irreversible," Li Fan realized clearly.

"I need to rest well. But it is definitely worth it." The borrowed power from his past self would not disappear without a trace. Instead, it would deepen his understanding of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood and accelerate the recovery of his past memories.

After Li Fan rested for a while and looked back at the torrent of past memories, the flow of time seemed to slow down, allowing him to see more scenes within.

"The experiences of my past self are definitely a treasure trove comparable to Mountains and Seas itself."

"If utilized properly, I can quickly locate reliable allies for the Concentric Alliance."

"Coupled with insights into various Great Daos..."

However, Li Fan did not rashly delve into it. Only after hiding in the Xuanhuang Realm for a hundred years, until the swelling pain in his soul completely disappeared, did he take the next step. He skillfully opened the True Return panel and chose to inherit...

"Starfall Rhythm Law."

The moment he made his choice, Li Fan felt as if the entire sky of the Xuanhuang Realm had darkened. Not only the Xuanhuang Realm and Primordial, but the entire Mountains and Seas as well. Against the dim backdrop, a strange radiance permeated and pulsed, as if a heart was beating rhythmically, or like a gaze constantly sweeping across.

Chapter 1748: The Body Becomes the Void Realm Lord

The [Outline of Mountains and Seas Changes], as recorded in True Return, was the overarching data for all of Mountains and Seas.

The [Starfall Rhythm Law], however, was True Return's observation of the entity known as [Star] lurking behind the scenes.

In the final moments of every reincarnation, the Lone Star would descend, devouring everything, only for True Return to turn the tide and reverse it. This never changed.

However, did each reset by True Return completely influence the Star? Did it return to its starting point each time, or did its progress genuinely change? This remained unknown.

However, the silver glow hidden in the boundless seabed could retain some intuition; the Lone Star, it was safe to assume, would be even more profound.

"My past self, through countless reincarnation attempts, to what extent did the Lone Star change? It is truly worrying. This is likely why True Return specifically provided these two inheritance options."

"The Outline of Mountains and Seas Changes is the foundation for cultivation, while the Starfall Rhythm Law is more of a precautionary reminder."

In Li Fan's view, all the changes within Mountains and Seas, even the birth of a New God, were not to be feared. Only the Lone Star posed a genuine threat to him, who possessed the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood.

Now, True Return could still reverse everything. But if one day, True Return could no longer affect the Lone Star... that would be an irreversible catastrophe.

Amidst the swirling thoughts in his mind, Li Fan tried to glean something from the undulating starlight before him. Unlike the obvious changes in the Outline of Mountains and Seas, this record of the Star in True Return was filled with an indescribable strangeness.

As the starlight permeated his being, Li Fan faintly heard inexplicable whispers.

The sky of the Xuanhuang Realm seemed to come alive, opening countless yellow and black eyes. Li Fan naturally observed them. As he met the gaze of one of them, they seemed to discover Li Fan's existence.

Instantly, all the other eyes turned towards Li Fan. And on the sky, more and more eyes opened, densely packed, almost obscuring the heavens. All stared fixedly at Li Fan.

The rhythm of the Starfall pulses became increasingly erratic. The whispers in his ears began to be interspersed with tragic screams.

Li Fan found a sense of familiarity in these sounds. It was identical to the echoes from the Xuanhuang Mad Heavenly Dao, previously sealed by Su Bai and carried by Xu Ke.

Li Fan listened intently.

"Huh! It's you!"

"You look familiar!"

"How can a mere Dao Integration cultivator instinctively instill fear in me? Where does this feeling come from?"

"Damn it! Why did you harm me! Why did you appear here!"

"Ahhh, save me, please save me..."

"No, I... I'm not me anymore!"

...

Chaos, madness, strangeness, incomprehensible.

Li Fan frowned slightly, then suddenly realized something and withdrew from his contemplation of the Starfall Rhythm Law.

The starlight on the Xuanhuang Realm's backdrop vanished. But... the densely packed eyes on the sky did not disappear with it! They still stared at Li Fan, filled with crazed hatred!

"Hmm?" Li Fan felt a slight shock, not out of fear of the enraged Xuanhuang Realm. Even with his current Dao Integration cultivation, he could crush the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao with a single finger.

What startled him was that merely "seeing" the Starfall Rhythm during his contemplation could affect the reality of Mountains and Seas.

"The Star's records, upon being observed externally, can also distort and alter reality."

"This power..." Li Fan frowned, his gaze piercing through the Xuanhuang Realm to the entire Primordial Possibility.

Perhaps because the observation took place in the Xuanhuang Realm, the external Star's influence was significantly weaker than in the Xuanhuang Realm. But once it appeared, it did not disappear. Instead, like a terrifying plague, it rapidly spread.

The Primordial Possibility, already precarious under the threat of Dao Annihilation, now appeared like a fading photograph, becoming mottled and withered.

And in Li Fan's ears, the low whispers from the Xuanhuang Realm continued unabated.

"I will kill you! Kill kill kill kill kill!"

"Kill me quickly! Please kill me!"

"No! Don't listen to them! Save me, please! Father!"

"Mom, save me! I'm in so much pain! ..."

There were the desperate roars of men, the sorrowful cries of little girls, and the weak moans of little boys. A thousand voices converged, intertwining. It wasn't just meaningless madness; it was as if certain memories from past reincarnations had been imprinted.

"Noisy!" Facing these cacophonies, a cold glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. Disregarding past affections, he unleashed his divine sense, encompassing all infected areas in the Xuanhuang Realm and the Primordial Possibility. Even surrounding dozens of possibilities.

Then, the power of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood was unleashed. The wails of the Xuanhuang ceased abruptly, and Li Fan’s ears fell silent.

To his sight, the world restored its normal colors, as expected of Mountains and Seas. Void surrounded him, Dao Annihilation surged, yet Li Fan felt an unprecedented peace. Compared to the strangely shifting Starfall Rhythm, Dao Annihilation seemed almost charming.

The demise of dozens of possibilities was nothing more than a drop in the ocean for the vastness of Mountains and Seas. But within the Xuanji Ring, the Saints were present. Observing the entirety of Mountains and Seas, such a change could not escape their notice.

Fortunately, Li Fan, under the protection of Illusion is True, had temporarily hidden in other possibilities. The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood had left no trace; it was thorough.

Even the Gods' divine senses searched fruitlessly, finding no clues, and could only withdraw reluctantly.

"I never expected that merely reading the records of the Star would be so dangerous."

"Although I reacted in time and excised the Star's influence, however..."

"It is likely that its influence has not been completely eradicated. This life has seen new variables emerge." Li Fan frowned, calculating the extent of this variable. He could not pinpoint its location. He temporarily abandoned the thought.

"Starfall Rhythm..."

"It seems that to fully decipher True Return's records, a suitable time is still needed." He temporarily stopped trying to decipher the Starfall Rhythm Law and focused on restoring his cultivation. He naturally chose the Dao of Universe Cycle.

But the moment he began cultivating, Li Fan noticed an abnormality in his body.

"This feeling..." After a moment of contemplation and sensing, Li Fan let out a cold snort and ignored it for now, continuing his cultivation.

Ten years later.

The familiar sensation returned.

As long as Li Fan wished, he could take one step further and ascend to the Saint realm.

"In my previous life, it took me nearly three hundred years to cultivate from mortal to Universe Cycle Saint. In this life, it only took ten years?" He recalled that back then, even escaping the miasma when breaking through took a similar amount of time. Now, reaching Sainthood in ten years. This speed shocked even Li Fan, who had inherited his past memories.

"It's definitely not due to an improvement in my own talent."

"It's because..."

"I've been influenced by the Starfall Rhythm."

"Besides the Xuanhuang Realm and Primordial, I have also become 'diseased' in a sense?"

"No wonder I couldn't calculate the variable. It was because it was within me." Li Fan observed himself, but detected no signs of 'fading.' However, he was somewhat certain that he had been influenced by the Starfall Rhythm. He had unhesitatingly cut off the infected Xuanhuang Realm and other possibilities. But when the source of the infection was himself... Li Fan naturally wouldn't choose to act against himself.

"Interesting. An unprecedented experience." Li Fan wasn't panicked. He could sense that the Starfall Rhythm's influence was not particularly severe. The Lone Star's descent could be reversed by True Return. How much more so for a deviation caused by merely recording the Starfall Rhythm.

"The reason for the drastic improvement in my cultivation talent is, in a sense, because I have already become a member of the [Star] faction. However, I am still within Mountains and Seas."

"The stronger I become, the more beneficial it is for the Star to devour Mountains and Seas."

"It's as if the Star has planted a spy in Mountains and Seas."

"The enhancement of my cultivation talent is the assistance provided by the Star. Although it may not be intentional by the Star, it is a natural consequence of the change itself." Li Fan vaguely understood. Then he thought of the Dao Annihilation Void Realm, also an instrument of the Star.

"If that's the case..." Li Fan's thoughts shifted. He withdrew his intention to ascend to Sainthood. With a gentle step, he leaped into the Void Realm. Without any protective power, he plunged into the endless Dao Annihilation with his physical body alone.

Theoretically, in an instant, Li Fan would be swallowed by Dao Annihilation, leaving no trace and starting anew. However, a bizarre scene unfolded. The Dao Annihilation, capable of devouring mountains and consuming seas, seemed to encounter something terrifying the moment it touched Li Fan's body. Not only did it refrain from devouring, but it actively avoided him.

Waves of Dao Annihilation, like a million-strong army, surged towards him. But Li Fan walked among them as if strolling in a leisurely garden. Not a single wave dared to stop him or question him!

Li Fan’s guess was confirmed. It was all because of the faint aura of Starfall that clung to him.

"In that case, I cannot become a Saint in this life."

"As soon as I enter the sight of the Three Saints, they will likely join forces and kill me without question," Li Fan scoffed. This outcome was something Li Fan had never anticipated when inheriting the Starfall Rhythm Law.

"I still underestimated the power of the Star."

"I admit, the Star influence on me can be slowly cleansed by the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood. However, firstly, it is too troublesome. It’s better to start over."

"Secondly..." Li Fan, situated in the Void Realm, gazed towards Mountains and Seas.

"Having reincarnated countless times, this perspective is something I've never experienced before."

"Perhaps..." He couldn't help but think of the New God's birth in the previous life. Li Fan's thoughts churned, and a faint idea formed in his mind.

With a divine thought, the Dao Annihilation in the Void Realm stirred, creating waves billions of feet high. They fiercely surged towards Mountains and Seas. Like the emperor himself surveying his troops, the Dao Annihilation responded to Li Fan's command without resistance, as if extremely excited. Like soldiers before a battle seeing their emperor lead the charge, they unleashed a destructive force far greater than usual. Roaring, they crashed into Mountains and Seas.

Facing this sudden attack of Dao Annihilation, the Saints on the Other Shore were caught off guard. However, through years of defense, they had accumulated rich experience. The Xuanji Ring emanated waves of white light, protecting the entirety of Mountains and Seas. Despite Li Fan's enhancement, the Dao Annihilation could not achieve a qualitative change. For the moment, it was unable to overcome the steadfast Mountains and Seas.

"I can summon more Dao Annihilation power from other places. Even Void Realm avatars of Saints are not out of the question."

"However..." Li Fan, situated amidst the Dao Annihilation, narrowed his eyes, not acting rashly. Although he could now manipulate the power of Dao Annihilation, it was because, as an emissary of the Star, he bypassed the true controller of the Void Realm and directly commanded the Dao Annihilation soldiers on the battlefield.

However, this did not mean the true controller of the Void Realm had lost control over Dao Annihilation. For now, causing minor disturbances in a certain segment of Mountains and Seas was acceptable. It was a small force, and the true controller of the Void Realm might not notice. If he were to forcibly recruit forces from other regions, it might immediately draw the attention of the Void Realm. The current Li Fan was not ready to interact with it.

"The Starfall influence on me is not yet that strong."

"Let's wait a bit longer." The Void Realm was the vanguard of the Star. Before the Lone Star, the Void Realm had no power to resist. Even after toiling for the Star for a long time, its ultimate fate was to be devoured by the Star along with everything else.

But Li Fan was not the Star, merely a "deviant mutation" tinged with some Starfall aura. It might deceive Dao Annihilation, but it definitely wouldn't fool the true controller of the Void Realm. Of course, this was based on his current level of infection. If the changes in Li Fan progressed further... then it would be uncertain.

"My actions may seem reckless, but with the foundation of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood..."

"It's not as dangerous as it seems."

"As long as I can ensure that True Return can completely eliminate the Starfall influence..."

"It's not impossible to enter the dragon's den!"

"As for the degree of this change, it is up to me, and only me, to control." While regrettable, it was clear that he could not include Shou Qiu and Dao De in his alliance in this lifetime. Even with the Concentric Unity augmentation, Li Fan couldn't guarantee that Shou Qiu would willingly defect to the Star's side and become a "spy for Mountains and Seas." Shou Qiu's character and morality were too noble. Li Fan had experienced this firsthand. Forcing him into the Star's camp might even lead to internal conflict at a critical moment.

"In this life, let us be opponents." Li Fan looked at Shou Qiu, who sat cross-legged within the Xuanji Ring, and chuckled softly.

"Although I can now manipulate Dao Annihilation, the ultimate control still rests with the true controller of the Void Realm."

"But... there might be a way to counter it," Li Fan's eyes gleamed.

"Ink Kill!"

"Dao One Worm!" At his thought, two wriggling shadows appeared before Li Fan. The Void Realm tolerated no foreign entities, and Dao Annihilation devoured all. The moment Ink Kill and Dao One Worm appeared, they triggered an instinctive turmoil in Dao Annihilation. However, firstly, Ink Kill was vaguely of the same origin as Dao Annihilation. Secondly, with Li Fan’s presence, Dao Annihilation ultimately restrained itself and did not proceed with the act of devouring.

"Condense!" Li Fan gestured lightly, and Ink Kill and Dao One Worm merged into one. Their forms vanished simultaneously. In their place appeared countless wriggling black dots.

"Go!" Li Fan gestured again, and a small stream of Dao Annihilation power, like ferocious soldiers, rushed towards the newly formed Dao One Worms. The black dots instantly dwindled to less than a hundred. However, the remaining ones had endured the first wave of Dao Annihilation's assault.

Chapter 1749: Method Without Restraint Fully Deployed

Just like Mountains and Seas.

Although they barely endured the first wave of Dao Annihilation, the Dao One Worms were now extremely weak and could not withstand any further erosion. Fortunately, Li Fan was the controller of Dao Annihilation. With a slight turn of his will, he restrained the surging waves of Dao Annihilation, giving the dying Dao One Worms a chance to breathe.

Coupled with Li Fan's nourishment, the Dao One Worms soon thrived again. Then, Dao Annihilation surged once more. After a round of evolution, the Dao One Worms indeed showed slightly improved survival capabilities against the same scale of Dao Annihilation attack.

"But with this rate of growth..." Li Fan frowned slightly. "And it's still uncertain whether this increase is due to the Dao One Worms themselves becoming stronger or simply random chance."

So, Li Fan conducted further experiments. Within the Void Realm, Dao Annihilation surged, dividing the swarm of insects into a million equal parts. Then, it simultaneously launched an assault on these million swarms. Under Li Fan’s precise control, the strength of these Dao Annihilation attacks was just enough to almost annihilate the swarms, but not quite kill them completely.

Like waves crashing ashore, the once prosperous swarms were reduced to mere specks.

"Compared to before, there are increases and decreases. It seems to be mere chance, not that the Dao One Worms have truly strengthened in such a short time," Li Fan shook his head slightly.

This was only to be expected. The Dao One Worms, even when fused with Ink Kill, had not yet reached the Transcendent realm. How could they withstand Dao Annihilation, which could destroy Saints?

"However..."

"Through my efforts, perhaps the impossible can become possible."

"In Mountains and Seas, I can elevate mortals to Saints. In the Void Realm, I can also turn worms into dragons!"

Li Fan scooped up a tiny Dao Annihilation worm and, with his will like a knife, began to sculpt and modify it. As the patterns on its back were constantly refined, this Dao One Worm gradually revealed a different aura. It seemed to emit a special allure, provoking the nearby Dao Annihilation to surge forward again.

Fortunately, Li Fan forcefully suppressed the restless Dao Annihilation. He gazed at his masterpiece. The back of the Dao One Worm was covered in intricate lines, containing infinite Dao charm, resembling a replica of Mountains and Seas. Or rather, these lines were directly inspired by Li Fan’s imitation of the petrified Mountains and Seas he observed in his past life!

"Compared to the true Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas, it's still slightly inferior." Li Fan was somewhat dissatisfied and crushed the creation. He began to engrave anew.

"Previously, I only saw a fragment of Mountains and Seas. But the complete embodiment of all Mountains and Seas is within the [Outline of Mountains and Seas Changes]. With it as the master outline..."

In the past, Li Fan had directly achieved Sainthood of Mountains and Seas by embodying the shadow of Mountains and Seas. Theoretically, if the entire landscape of Mountains and Seas were engraved onto a single Dao One Worm, it might give birth to the first Dao One Worm at the Saint realm in Mountains and Seas.

However, after several attempts, Li Fan decisively gave up.

"A single Dao One Worm is too weak. It cannot bear the immeasurable Mountains and Seas. Even millions or tens of millions of swarms would be insufficient. More are needed."

With a shift in his thoughts, the Dao One Worm swarm began to multiply madly again. Li Fan even commanded his subordinates, the Dao Annihilation, to scour Mountains and Seas as nourishment to feed them.

After devouring several possibilities of Mountains and Seas, the scale of the Dao One Worm swarm finally reached a barely usable level.

"Hundreds of billions of units are the limit." The limit here refers not to the reproduction limit of the swarm, but to the number of Stone Tablets of Mountains and Seas Li Fan could meticulously carve simultaneously!

Li Fan's divine sense simultaneously covered hundreds of billions of Dao One Worm swarms, as if manifesting an equal number of arms, carving onto each swarm’s back. The patterns on each Dao One Worm were different, each depicting a corner of Mountains and Seas. But when combined...

They formed a magnificent, nearly complete landscape of Mountains and Seas!

Engraving the entire landscape of Mountains and Seas, even with the [Outline of Mountains and Seas Changes] as a guiding principle, was an extremely mentally taxing task. Every so often, Li Fan’s black hair would turn white. After his hair completely turned white, the signs of aging began to attack Li Fan’s skin. The engraving continued unabated, and Li Fan’s external appearance grew increasingly withered.

"Without achieving Sainthood, resistance to external influences is ultimately too weak."

But Li Fan paid it no mind, continuing to focus on carving the landscape of Mountains and Seas.

After an unknown period of time.

Suddenly, the Mountains and Seas before him emitted a brilliant light. Waves surged, causing the surrounding Daoists who were protecting Li Fan to tremble, nearly dissipating.

"Huh? Without me, Mountains and Seas has successfully reconnected?" Li Fan was somewhat surprised.

But looking at the [Dao One Mountains and Seas Map] nearing completion in his hands, Li Fan felt relieved.

"It took so long just to reconnect a segment of Mountains and Seas. To truly save Mountains and Seas from Dao Annihilation, who knows how long that will take?"

Without minding the Saints of Mountains and Seas who were celebrating the successful reconnection with renewed spirit, Li Fan coughed weakly and refocused on his own creation. As Mountains and Seas lit up again, and the Saints of Shou Qiu completed another reconnection, Li Fan was finally at the last brushstroke of completing the Dao One Mountains and Seas Map.

However, it was precisely this last stroke that Li Fan found he could not make. And at this moment, Li Fan had reached the end of his lifespan.

"Pouring all my efforts into one life, yet unable to complete it."

He looked at the newborn swarm of insects surrounded by Dao Annihilation before him. Billions of Dao One Worms gathered, carrying the continuous landscape of Mountains and Seas. Though called a swarm, they were essentially the shadow of Mountains and Seas. The aura they emitted was already very similar to Mountains and Seas itself, causing the surrounding Dao Annihilation to lose control and sporadically attack.

But compared to their initial weak state, they were now vastly different. Their imposing momentum had been established, and minor waves could no longer overthrow them. However, they were still far from Li Fan's ideal state.

Before completing the final touch, Li Fan had already reached the end of his lifespan in this life. Without forcing it, he silently chanted, "True Return!"

...

Anchored 1 year.

This time, Li Fan directly chose to inherit the unfinished [Dao One Mountains and Seas Map] from his previous life. With a thought, a meticulously crafted masterpiece appeared before Li Fan.

"A journey of a thousand miles begins with a single step. This final step is still difficult to take."
