Li Fan observed and meditated for a hundred years, repeatedly comparing it with the [Outline of Mountains and Seas Changes]. Ultimately, he still could not find the optimal moment to make the final stroke.

"I still need to learn from Mountains and Seas!"

Li Fan put away the [Dao One Mountains and Seas Map] and began to cultivate. After more than two hundred years, he once again reached the Saint realm of [Universe Cycle].

"Without the Star's favor, my cultivation speed is still faster than before," Li Fan thought to himself.

As a new Saint descended, the Saints of Mountains and Seas cast their gazes. However, Li Fan ignored them and leaped directly into the Void Realm, causing consternation. Li Fan’s actions were too swift; even the Three Saints couldn’t intervene in time. They could only watch as Li Fan vanished into the Void Realm, his whereabouts unknown.

"That... is the Dao of Universe Cycle. Although this path is extraordinary, entering the vast Void Realm alone is likely fraught with peril."

"What is the reason for this? It's as if they are trying to avoid us."

"What a pity. If only there was one more Saint to assist us, then the hope of reconnecting Mountains and Seas would be within reach."

The Saints deliberated amongst themselves. Ultimately, the Three Saints made the final decision: "Each has his own aspirations; there is no need to force it. Let him go."

The Saints remained unaware that Li Fan's journey through the Dao Annihilation, while not effortless, was not as perilous as they imagined. Compared to being surrounded and devoured by Dao Annihilation, the greater obstacle was the lack of direction and the inability to discern past from present.

In the past, with the Three Saints as guiding lights, they only needed to travel towards a predetermined goal. However, traveling alone now, without a guide, Li Fan had to find his own way. The Three Saints existed alongside Mountains and Seas throughout its entirety, thus they could always discern the correct direction in the Void Realm. But Li Fan was just Li Fan. His journey forward was not smooth.

Fortunately, he had the experience of reconnecting and repairing in previous lives. This dark path was one he had walked step by step himself. In some obscure way, there was a sense of familiarity.

He arrived at his destination safely, facing the mountains and seas before they were besieged by [Lock].

"When truth becomes falsehood, falsehood also becomes true!"

With a thought, the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood enveloped him, and his form dissolved into nothingness. Instantly, he bypassed [Lock]'s carefully woven net of devouring and entered Mountains and Seas.

The scene within was similar to ordinary Mountains and Seas. It bore some resemblance to the Xuanwu Net that once traversed the Xuanhuang Realm. Above the sky, intersecting lines were vaguely visible, with many gaps, as if parts had been directly devoured, revealing a strange rolling darkness. The entire Mountains and Seas was filled with [Lock]'s insatiable desire to devour, twisting the nature of sentient beings and even the very world itself.

"All things compete, heavens and men contend, but ultimately it benefits only the gluttonous maw of [Lock]."

"If there were no external intervention."

Li Fan coldly snorted. "Dao Annihilation..."

"Return!"

His gaze pierced through Mountains and Seas, past the layers of [Lock]'s net, reaching the depths of the Void Realm. Relying on the familiarity gained from immersing himself in Starfall in his previous life, Li Fan now used himself as bait, luring a large amount of Dao Annihilation from the Void Realm to this place!

It was important to note that at this time, Mountains and Seas was a place deemed important by the Void Realm, where the power of Dao Annihilation was exceptionally concentrated. Upon discovering a loophole, the Dao Annihilation naturally surged forward.

The Dao Annihilation, like a massive force, suddenly appeared in Mountains and Seas! [Lock] was stunned, unable to comprehend how the Void Realm had broken through its blockade and snatched food from under its jaws.

However, Li Fan's objective was not limited to this.

"After a long journey, trekking through mountains and rivers, would such a minor disturbance suffice?"

"The Life Meridians."

Li Fan's eyes narrowed, and he reached directly into Mountains and Seas, grabbing tens of thousands of sentient beings. These were not beings naturally born from Mountains and Seas, but products of Qiu Tianhui's Great Dao of Beings. With a gentle squeeze, the beings in his hand shattered, turning into specks of light. Li Fan infused them into the hidden Life Meridians of Mountains and Seas. Half towards the past, half towards the future.

In the previous previous life, the Saints of Mountains and Seas only sought to stimulate Mountains and Seas' instinctual resistance, hence the limited scale of Dao Annihilation invasion. But in this life, Li Fan acted without restraint. The light beams, transformed from tens of thousands of sentient beings, clearly indicated the path. The Dao Annihilation army advanced unimpeded!

Mountains and Seas plunged into darkness, instantly falling into turmoil. All sentient beings were annihilated, and most Saints fled in all directions. Only Shou Qiu continued to desperately try and resist. However, without Li Fan's Concentric Unity and the augmentation of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, Shou Qiu was merely an ordinary Saint. Faced with such a catastrophe, his efforts were but a drop in the ocean.

Li Fan did not concern himself with them, focusing his gaze on Mountains and Seas. "Three lifetimes of expenditure, will it succeed now?"

The Mountains and Seas invaded by Dao Annihilation also erupted with astonishing potential. Roaring sounds from within Mountains and Seas temporarily repelled the torrent of Dao Annihilation. And then...

The exact same scene as the New God's descent in the previous life appeared. Everything else within Mountains and Seas was shattered. Only the pure Mountains and Seas itself remained. The Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas reappeared!

Furthermore, because Li Fan's manipulation of Dao Annihilation in this life far surpassed previous attempts, and it invaded along the Life Meridians, the collapse of Mountains and Seas was exceptionally rapid. This caused the petrified Mountains and Seas to not be limited to the current segment. Instead, it spanned thirty-six consecutive segments of Mountains and Seas, spanning approximately twenty-five million years of history!

Even on the scale of Mountains and Seas' billions of years, this was no longer a negligible fraction, but equivalent to forcibly carving out a piece of flesh. Countless sentient beings were lost in this process.

And Li Fan, the instigator, remained indifferent, even mocking, "A drastic measure to cut off the rot. Impressive, impressive!"

"However, it suits my needs perfectly!"

The continuous Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas, spanning twenty-five million years, was far more detailed than what Li Fan had seen before. The boundlessness and infinitude of Mountains and Seas seemed to have gained a tangible form. Even observing from the Void Realm, there was a subtle pull, a sense of loss, as if being drawn into it. It was like a massive dike, standing before the Dao Annihilation of the Void Realm. Waves surged, but for the moment, they could not stir up any significant turmoil.

Li Fan no longer stopped himself from falling towards the Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas. Instead, he used this force to extend his divine sense, permeating every corner of the Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas. Every minute detail was clearly visible. Li Fan was immersed in it, his heart filled with yearning.

Compared to the [Outline of Mountains and Seas Changes], which contained all the data of Mountains and Seas, this Stone Tablet, evolved by Mountains and Seas itself, was more intricate and specific. "Knowing one can understand all. But with the boundlessness and infinitude of Mountains and Seas, understanding the 'one' is itself a boundless task."

Li Fan compared the patterns on the Stone Tablet with those recorded in the Outline of Changes and cross-referenced them with his own writings in the Dao One Mountains and Seas Map. New insights arose in his mind. That final stroke, which he had been unable to make, finally seemed possible.

"But..."

"Something still seems to be missing."

Li Fan mused, his divine sense continuing to roam within the Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas. Suddenly, at a seemingly insignificant 'point,' it paused.

"This is..."

Amidst the eradication of all things, on the Stone Tablet where only Mountains and Seas existed, there was still an 'external object.' Like a drop of ink falling on the stone tablet, it was out of place with its surroundings. Yet, it seemed to complement them, creating a harmonious balance. This was also why Li Fan's divine sense had overlooked its anomaly previously.

And this external object was not unfamiliar to Li Fan. It was the Boundless Mountains and Seas Monument!

"Even though Mountains and Seas has petrified, it remains here."

"Mountains and Seas are boundless and eternal. Life and death, all are thus determined."

Li Fan’s divine sense rapidly retracted from the twenty-five million years of Mountains and Seas, returning to human form and entering the Boundless Mountains and Seas Monument. Retracing the story, he inscribed a trace of his understanding of the Dao of Universe Cycle onto it. His divine sense then attached itself to this trace.

"Fortunately, I did not find any traces of myself left behind on this Boundless Mountains and Seas Monument. Otherwise, I would have been greatly alarmed."

"This Boundless Mountains and Seas Monument will be my final touch, adding the finishing stroke."

Observing the faint traces on the Boundless Mountains and Seas Monument, Li Fan's mind was enlightened. "Mountains are mountains, seas are seas. Even with shared fragmented godhood, they are ultimately independent entities, mutually dependent but not contaminating each other."

"But since the existence of this Boundless Mountains and Seas Monument..."

"Only then can Mountains and Seas be truly called [Mountains and Seas]."

Li Fan's eyes gradually brightened. Having understood everything, his mood was exceptionally joyful, and he couldn't help but laugh loudly.

However, his laughter was soon interrupted by roaring sounds from the outside.

"This is..."

"The torrent of godhood return?"

Li Fan's expression turned serious. While he was comprehending enlightenment on the Stone Tablet, the god fragmentation competition in this life had also concluded. Like a hundred rivers returning to the sea, all things derived from the god within Mountains and Seas now returned to the New God. The torrent was vast, crushing all else. Even the solidified, frozen Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas was propelled by this returning force, trembling towards the early days of Mountains and Seas.

If this were the first time he witnessed such a scene, Li Fan would undoubtedly have immediately activated True Return to flee in terror. But now, Li Fan watched calmly. Because the New God's descent in this life was entirely orchestrated by him, Li Fan no longer felt the fear he had experienced upon encountering a god for the first time.

"Gods..."

"Are nothing more than this."

"Malleable, can be shed."

"This is the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood..."

Li Fan savoring the myriad variables across his three lives. He summarized the conditions for the New God's emergence.

"It seems that the mere fall of [Lock] is not enough."

"The battle between [Lock] and the Saints was also a key factor."

"Why is this so?"

Although he did not know the specific reason now, he had mastered the method for stably creating the New God’s descent.

"However, considering the precedent of the silver light point, excessive repetition is not advisable."

"Otherwise, it might awaken its memories from when it was a god, or even subtly perceive the existence of True Return. And it cannot be eliminated by True Return's reset..."

"This is too dangerous for me."

"This life was necessary to perfect the Dao One Mountains and Seas Map."

Li Fan was contemplating when his thoughts suddenly halted. Because he noticed that the Boundless Mountains and Seas Monument, which had been flowing along with the Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas, suddenly stopped moving.

Chapter 1750: Li Fan's Record of Becoming a God

How does one become a god?

This question, without personally participating in the epic battle in the Primeval Immortal Realm, might never be answered accurately. Li Fan could only try to infer part of it based on the different outcomes caused by various variables.

"It seems that besides [Lock] being severely injured, there might be other factors."

Li Fan waited for a long time, but still did not hear the Three Saints utter the words, "The time for fragmented godhood has arrived." Choosing not to waste any more time, Li Fan decisively activated True Return. He still chose to inherit the [Dao One Mountains and Seas Map], which was just a brushstroke away from completion.

Temporarily halting his actions, Li Fan meticulously reviewed all the details of the life where the New God descended. "Could it be that besides [Lock] being severely injured, the Saints' mental intrusions and their battles with it were also a key factor?"

"Since the cause cannot be determined, it's best to replicate all variables as much as possible." With this thought, Li Fan summoned tens of Saints' spirits from Mountains and Seas. They would serve as pawns. The Saints who entered [Lock]'s net previously were, in order: Stealing Opportunity, Hundred Answers, Fang Cun, and Tai Wei. Li Fan followed. The first three had already left their marks in the Great Dao Return Hall, so creating and exerting an equivalent effect should not be difficult.

"The key lies with Emperor Tai Wei. Ordinary beings are hard-pressed to exude regal bearing." Li Fan's gaze swept over the chosen lucky individuals, selecting the most suitable vessel. Then, with a gentle breath, he infused it. The being was initially in a daze, but gradually, its temperament and demeanor underwent subtle changes. The beings gathered around it instinctively moved away, afraid to approach. Li Fan not only infused a phantom memory but, more importantly, a regal disposition.

Li Fan observed for a moment, still not satisfied, and shook his head slightly. "Although it possesses the demeanor of a Holy Emperor, it lacks the substance. It's not enough!"

In the life where the New God descended, Emperor Tai Wei, having comprehended the Great Dao of Beings, channeled his power into [Lock]'s net, consuming almost negligible energy. Therefore, for Li Fan to perfectly replicate the conditions for the New God’s birth, he had to create a Holy Emperor of comparable strength.

"With my understanding of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, I cannot yet create a Saint with a single thought. However..."

"I can transform my cultivation!"

"Dao of Universe Cycle, shed!"

A rather bizarre scene unfolded. The skin on Li Fan's body began to writhe as if being pulled and torn by an external force. Slowly, a figure detached from Li Fan. Faceless and formless, it drifted uneasily, yet emanating a vast aura of Sainthood. And Li Fan himself had regressed to the mortal realm!

Compared to a Saint, a mortal was like an ant in Mountains and Seas. Under normal circumstances, if Li Fan did this, he would immediately lose control of the Saint's guise upon shedding his cultivation. But Li Fan was different. The foundation of his strength lay mostly in the [Transformation of Truth and Falsehood]. Even as a mere mortal, he could still suppress the Saint's guise. Coupled with the fact that the Dao of Universe Cycle was already named in the Hall of Great Dao Return, these two factors made it impossible for Li Fan to lose control.

"It's not time to act yet. I'll wait until I cultivate to the Saint realm again." For his second cultivation, Li Fan chose the Dao of Profound牝ility. Li Fan's comprehension of the Dao of Universe Cycle was recorded on the Boundless Mountains and Seas Monument. His understanding of the Dao of Profound牝ility was naturally not as profound. But it only took him four hundred years to become a Saint again.

Repeatedly restarting and achieving enlightenment, the path to Sainthood, which was unattainable and difficult for other cultivators, had become as simple as eating and drinking for Li Fan. "In the future, creating Saints will also be within my grasp with a single thought."

Now a Profound牝ility Saint, Li Fan felt invigorated. Clad in the guise of the [Universe Cycle], he headed towards the Mountains and Seas sealed by [Lock]'s net. He still used Illusion is True to clear the path, silently infiltrating. Then, he successively released the fabricated "Stealing Opportunity," "Hundred Answers," and "Fang Cun." The [Lock]'s net underwent corresponding changes. Although not entirely identical to the life where the New God descended, the general trajectory remained the same.

"Next, it's your turn." Li Fan looked at the "Holy Emperor" phantom in his hand and smiled slightly, draping the Universe Cycle guise onto it.

Simultaneously achieving Sainthood, Li Fan also contended for ownership of the Dao of Universe Cycle in the Hall of Great Dao Return. Without a true owner, how could it contend with Li Fan? The Dao of Universe Cycle vanished. The guise also quickly fell from the Saint realm, retaining only profound cultivation but lacking Saint status. This aligned perfectly with the performance of Emperor Tai Wei when he crossed over into [Lock]'s net.

The "Holy Emperor" crafted by Li Fan had his actions pre-determined. He cultivated legions and forced [Lock] to reveal itself and change the rules. After the fabricated "Holy Emperor" turned to dust, Li Fan then made his grand entrance.

"Huh? You..." Even though Li Fan had hidden himself well, [Lock] instinctively sensed something was wrong. An inexplicable sense of crisis arose in its heart. "A mere ant from later generations could cause me such unease?"

[Lock] was shocked, but after all, it was one of the original Saints of Mountains and Seas, an ancient being who had survived the harsh environment of the Primeval Immortal Realm. Naturally, it could not be scared away by Li Fan directly. Another performance ensued. The outcome, as expected, was not in doubt. Li Fan showed no mercy, using the Dao of Stealing Opportunity to glean more fortune.

A chilling, eerie sensation lingered in its heart. The unease that had been deliberately suppressed by [Lock] earlier suddenly amplified a thousandfold. "A meticulously planned trap connected ring by ring." "Who is calculating me!" [Lock] roared inwardly.

For some reason, this scene evoked a sense of déjà vu. Once this thought arose, it could not be eliminated. What began as a seemingly insignificant snowflake had instantly turned into a roaring avalanche. Unease turned into terror. [Lock] even perceived visions of its own gruesome demise! "I will die?" "I will die!"

Overwhelmed by shock and disbelief, its heart filled with confusion, astonishment, and fear, [Lock] could no longer afford to linger. It fled in disarray.

"This time, did I overdo it again?" Li Fan keenly sensed the subtle changes in [Lock] at the final moment, his expression unreadable. His form flickered and blurred, and before the [Lock]'s net completely dissipated, he concealed himself.

The [Lock]'s net inexplicably receded, leaving the Saints of Mountains and Seas bewildered. However, they could find no reason and attributed it to the upheaval in the early days of Mountains and Seas. Li Fan hid, patiently awaiting the outcome. The appointed time arrived, yet there was no sign of the New God's descent. "Failed again?"

Li Fan frowned. Just as he was about to activate True Return to try again, his heart suddenly stirred. "Although [Lock] vaguely sensed something and became more cautious, it ultimately couldn't compensate for the damage to its origin." "The one destined to die will surely die." "It can only prolong its survival."

Li Fan's gaze seemed to pierce through the layers of Mountains and Seas and the Void Realm, reaching the very beginning of time. Li Fan suddenly gained some insight. He then resurfaced and waited for signs of the New God's descent. This time, he was not disappointed.

The sudden sensation of falling from the heavens struck. In many parts of Mountains and Seas, the Three Saints suddenly rose, their expressions extremely grave as they gazed towards the Primeval era. At the words, "The time for fragmented godhood has arrived," the Three Saints all took their own lives, their power converging towards the Primeval Immortal Realm. All that remained were the bewildered Saints and the chaotic Mountains and Seas.

"After waiting for so long, we have finally reached this moment!" Taking advantage of the turmoil in Mountains and Seas and the Void Realm, Li Fan casually tossed out millions of sentient beings. They were all "lucky ones" he had gathered during his journey against the current. He infused them into the Life Meridians of Mountains and Seas.

"Dao Annihilation, return!" Within Mountains and Seas, while starlight overflowed, Li Fan also pointed towards a spot in the vast Void Realm. Originally in a state of disarray, the Dao Annihilation forces, now guided by Li Fan, transformed into ferocious beasts smelling prey. Roaring and charging, they advanced unstoppably!

Mountains and Seas were instantly lost. Sentient beings were annihilated, and most Saints fled in all directions. Only Shou Qiu continued to desperately resist. However, without Li Fan's Concentric Unity and the augmentation of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, Shou Qiu was merely an ordinary Saint. Faced with such a catastrophe, his efforts were like a drop in the bucket.

Li Fan did not concern himself with them, focusing on Mountains and Seas. "The expenditure of three lifetimes, will it succeed now?" The life-devouring Mountains and Seas, invaded by Dao Annihilation, also unleashed astonishing potential. The rumbling sounds from within Mountains and Seas temporarily repelled the torrent of Dao Annihilation.

And then... The exact same scene as the New God's descent in the previous life appeared. All other things within Mountains and Seas were shattered. Only the pure Mountains and Seas itself remained. The Stone Tablet of Mountains and Seas reappeared!

Countless sentient beings were lost in this process.

Li Fan, the instigator, remained

expressionless, even managing a sarcastic remark: "A drastic measure to cut off the rot. Impressive, impressive!" "However, it suits my needs perfectly!"

Chapter 1751: New God Fighting in the Void

The Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet, as if knowing its fate was to be consumed by the New God ahead, remained fixed in the void, unmoved by the torrent of returning divinity.

"It can actually resist the tide of returning divinity…" Li Fan's gaze flickered as he scanned the tablet with his divine sense, searching for the reason for its steadfastness.

The remnants of Mountains and Seas flowed like a river towards the vortex of divine nourishment at the beginning of time. The Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet, however, stood like a stone mountain beside the river, unyielding. Li Fan, standing upon this mountain, watched the world collapse with a complex emotion.

"This stone tablet…" Li Fan mused, "It can gather Mountains and Seas, exist independently of them, and mirror the principles of Mountains and Seas. What exactly is its origin?" He suddenly recalled the scene he had perceived when he first encountered the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet. Outside of Mountains and Seas, in an obscure, unknown realm, a stone tablet seemed to have leaped from within Mountains and Seas, or perhaps descended into it from the outside. Mountains shook, waves surged, and Mountains and Seas merged, becoming boundless.

"Could it be, as the Three Saints said, a remnant of a god, or perhaps…" "One who stands shoulder to shoulder with gods?" As his thoughts spun, Li Fan made a decision. He would remain by the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet until the end of this life, observing how it fared during the descent of the New God and its subsequent return to the Star. "Perhaps, I can also use this Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet to further refine my [Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas]."

Li Fan's mind stirred, and a Daoist Worm instantly materialized in his hand. Even most Saints would struggle to leave a clear, distinct mark on the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet, let alone a mere Daoist Worm. As expected, it could not be accommodated by the stone tablet and instantly dissolved into wisps of ink, vanishing with the wind.

Next, Li Fan began to gradually increase the number of Daoist Worms. One, a hundred, a thousand, ten thousand… None could persist for more than a fleeting moment before perishing within the stone tablet. Only when the number reached ten billion did the Daoist Worm swarm, with the nascent Mountains and Seas diagram carved on their backs, manage to endure for a short while.

"There's hope…" Li Fan keenly sensed that during the brief moments the worm swarm struggled for survival, changes indeed occurred on the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet. However, as the worm swarm disappeared, so did the new etchings.

"Daoist Worms, carving Mountains and Seas, is a path in itself. Naturally, just as with other Daos, they can leave traces on the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet. Even more so, the one who leaves a mark on the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet, possesses the most accurate depiction of Mountains and Seas." Li Fan felt a sense of enlightenment.

He increased the number of worm swarms again. Billions upon billions of worms, painting a complete panorama of Mountains and Seas. Coupled with Li Fan's insight, the "boundless" stroke that completed the picture. The moment the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas took shape, the billions of Daoist Worms emitted a strange black light, coalescing into a single entity. It resembled an ink wash painting of Mountains and Seas, with undulating peaks and raging waves, all Great Daos revealed within. Possessing the true attributes of Mountains and Seas, it nearly broke free from Li Fan's control upon manifesting, drawn towards the vortex of returning divinity at the dawn of Mountains and Seas. Facing the suppression of the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet, this ink landscape flowed, its mountains trembling, its waves roaring, Mountains and Seas united, its form momentarily contending with the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet. Amidst the thunderous roars, the shadow of Mountains and Seas was slowly etched onto the stone tablet. The mission of the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet was boundlessness, as if it possessed a special connection to Mountains and Seas itself. As the depiction of Mountains and Seas within the Daoist Diagram grew more vibrant and realistic, the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet, which had been halted in the current of returning divinity, suddenly moved again, leaping into the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas! Without hesitation, it replaced the finishing stroke Li Fan had drawn based on his own comprehension. With a resounding boom! As if it were meant to be, the single stroke transformed, and within the Daoist Diagram, continuous changes erupted, as if a divine brush were constantly stroking ink, rewriting the very fabric of Mountains and Seas. Ink flowed like clouds, obscuring Mountains and Seas. As the ink diffused, Mountains and Seas gradually merged into one. Before the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet had entered the picture, Li Fan had not felt his own depiction of Mountains and Seas to be crude. But after the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet provided the finishing touch and replaced his work, the comparison revealed his own efforts to be mere imitation. This new Daoist Diagram, though just a painting, gave Li Fan the feeling of true Mountains and Seas.

"Not just the Dao of Mountains and Seas, but Mountains and Seas itself!" Li Fan, who had only intended to use the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet to correct his Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas, never expected the tablet itself to leap into the depiction. It was truly an unexpected joy! With the stone tablet's transformation, the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas reached perfection, no longer open to alteration.

"Mountains and Seas carved on the back of a Daoist Worm."

"Although it depicts the landscape of Mountains and Seas, in reality…"

"It is still a Daoist Worm."

Li Fan looked towards the void beyond the returning divinity tide, outside of Mountains and Seas. The ink-colored Mountains and Seas carved a path, parting the torrent. Li Fan plunged directly into the void. The Daoist Diagram, bearing a striking resemblance to Mountains and Seas, immediately drew the surrounding Dao Annihilation instinctively towards it. The ink surged, clashing and churning with the Dao Annihilation. After a fierce struggle, the Dao Annihilation finally recognized its opponent's true nature. It was, in essence, "brothers of the same origin"! Although this brother was a bit strangely shaped and weaker, the shared origin was undeniable. Thus, the great battle ceased. They did not merely coexist, but merged like fish and water, becoming one!

Witnessing this, Li Fan couldn't help but nod. "After the Daoist Worm merged with Ink Kill, it could already bear the power of Dao Annihilation, but its initial form was too weak to survive in Dao Annihilation, let alone be compatible with it."

"But after my modifications, integrating the Dao of Mountains and Seas, and with the finishing touch of the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet…"

"The current Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas, resembles Mountains and Seas in form, but its essence belongs to Dao Annihilation."

"It can merge into Dao Annihilation when advancing, and recreate the world of Mountains and Seas when retreating. Its utility is truly boundless!"

"With this diagram's protection, even without the power of True Spirit infusion, I can traverse the ancient void, disregarding the dangers of Dao Annihilation!"

"Of course…"

"It only resembles Mountains and Seas, it is not truly Mountains and Seas. It can deceive the armies of Dao Annihilation filling the void, but it cannot hide from the hidden master of the void. Even the Saintly avatars of the void realm could easily see through it. Traversing within requires caution."

Li Fan did not let temporary success cloud his judgment. He had not forgotten his original goal. The divinity's return to Mountains and Seas was nearing its end. However, the events that transpired had deviated slightly from his expectations. The New God born in this life had a completely different modus operandi from the one in his previous life. The New God of the previous life feigned death, luring out the hidden surviving Saints. But the New God born in this life was overt, sweeping across everywhere. With each breath, the vortex of divine nourishment spun faster, consuming everything. Gradually, besides the void, only the New God stood alone. Mountains and Seas perished, leaving no place to hide.

The blue, purple, and white lights, four points of brilliance, were forced to reveal themselves. The New God's gaze fell upon them. The cyan light point offered no resistance and was swallowed whole. The remaining three scattered like birds and beasts, but their flight speed visibly slowed. Ultimately, they all stopped and returned to the divinity.

"Perhaps it's due to the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet. While hiding within this Daoist Diagram, I was able to minimize the New God's influence."

"As long as I don't directly confront the New God, but observe from the shadows, it's difficult to be detected."

Only after the New God finished consuming Mountains and Seas did it stand in the void, motionless for a long time. It seemed to sense something was missing and was still searching for something. But Li Fan, hidden within the layers of Dao Annihilation, could not be easily found even with divine power.

The long-prepared void realm finally sounded the horn for battle against the New God. In the eyes of the void realm, Mountains and Seas, and the New God, were indistinguishable. They were merely different manifestations of the same power. Its mission was to annihilate everything and offer it to its greatest master. The New God's consumption of Mountains and Seas left it with only one remaining strategic objective, saving considerable effort. The final battle saw countless Dao Annihilation forces surge, unprecedentedly powerful. Currents intertwined like dragons, surrounding and strangling the New God!

As the concealing Dao Annihilation brothers dwindled in number, Li Fan's hidden Daoist Diagram also faced the risk of exposure. Li Fan even faintly sensed the presence of the void realm's master. He dared not act rashly, only seeking to remain hidden and await the outcome of the battle between the void realm and the New God.

The battle lasted only a moment before it exceeded Li Fan's observational scope. In the infinite darkness, the New God's reclusive figure flickered from time to time. Ripples churned, growing stronger wave after wave. Even with the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet's enhancement, the Daoist Diagram was repeatedly shaken and almost revealed. Fortunately, at the crucial moment of the fierce battle, neither the New God nor the void realm's master had the leisure to attend to anything else. Li Fan was thus able to continue his concealment.

Although he could not see, Li Fan focused his attention entirely, meticulously recording the battle between the New God and the void realm.

"In the future, by repeatedly studying this, the gains will be no less than observing Mountains and Seas."

Under the constant scouring of the ripples, the traces of Mountains and Seas on the Daoist Diagram gradually changed. Li Fan naturally noticed this. However, after some thought, Li Fan realized it might be a good thing and did not try to stop it. He allowed the battle's aftermath between the New God and the void realm to reshape the Daoist Diagram.

In the void, time flowed by. The New God that descended, compared to the dying Mountains and Seas, was clearly more vibrant. The two seemed locked in an endless struggle, with no clear victor. Under the constant tempering of the ripples, the Daoist Diagram gradually adapted to the aftermath of the great battle. Li Fan sat within the diagram like a meditating monk, engraving all the details of the battle in his heart. His mind gradually became devoid of joy or sorrow, tranquil and unperturbed. After an unknown period, even Li Fan, at the Saint realm, had streaks of silver white appearing in his hair.

The ripples echoing in the void finally began to weaken. At this moment, Li Fan's heart suddenly leaped. In the darkness, something seemed to be breaking free from its prison. This feeling was not unfamiliar to Li Fan. It was the [Star]! However, the descent of the Star he had witnessed before was the demise of Mountains and Seas, followed by the solitary Star's appearance. This time, however, as the New God gradually weakened, the cage imprisoning the solitary Star grew more fragile. The solitary Star seemed to be constantly bombarding it, its growing commotion announcing its imminent descent!

"It seems my predictions were accurate. Whether it be Mountains and Seas, or the New God, both ultimately cannot escape the fate of the solitary Star's descent." Li Fan grew even more cautious, dispelling all thoughts from his mind, ceasing to contemplate anything related to the [Star]. The outcome was predetermined; the New God's struggle was futile.

However, the demise of a god was not an instantaneous event. As Li Fan's hair turned completely white, absolute stillness descended upon the void. Pure death nurtured pure life. The void churned restlessly, the pounding of heartbeats intensifying. The solitary Star was about to descend upon the world. But for some reason, something seemed to be missing. It couldn't quite manifest?

Li Fan's mind, dormant for too long, remained blank. Until a peculiar fluctuation swept through all void, finally locking onto Li Fan's location. His divine sense then began to stir again. Just like the great vortex that nurtured the New God, a similar vortex, centered on Li Fan, faintly emerged in the void. However, it was not to nourish Li Fan, but to devour him! The Daoist Worm, after all, was not Dao Annihilation itself. As its disguise was ruthlessly torn away, it would face an impact several times fiercer than the Dao Annihilation it had encountered before. It was as if, during the battle to slaying gods, Dao Annihilation had also undergone some sublimation. Under the onslaught of Dao Annihilation, everything depicted on the Daoist Diagram seemed to be wiped away. The rich imagery quickly became thin and pale.

"This is the moment!" Li Fan remained calm and composed. The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood descended upon him instantaneously. Not rusty from prolonged disuse, it felt as natural as innate. The Illusion is True concealed his existence, and Li Fan, without mercy, tore apart the last vestiges of the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas. Countless Daoist Worms scattered in all directions under the tribulation of destruction, but in their disunity, they were quickly annihilated by Dao Annihilation. In the center of the Daoist Worms, the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet was once again exposed to the world.

The vortex of the void realm fell silent for a moment. The Star's movement also seemed to pause. Then, as if receiving a command, all the Dao Annihilation forces unexpectedly converged towards the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet, ignoring the fleeing Daoist Worms!

"This is…" Li Fan clearly felt the excitement emanating from Dao Annihilation. The reason for its surge was the will of the [Star].

"Why do I feel like…"

"It's as if the Star never devoured the Boundless Mountains and Seas?" Witnessing this, Li Fan suddenly experienced a peculiar sensation. The startling scene that followed confirmed his guess.

As Dao Annihilation impacted, the myriad Daoist principles inscribed on the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet became increasingly clear. Even figures began to vaguely appear. They were the Saints who had previously left their marks on the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet. There were beings from the primordial era, and the Three Saints. Li Fan even saw himself. Figures flew out, surrounding the tablet, while the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet gradually faded into the void. As if having completed its mission, it began to collapse inwards, shrinking to a single point, about to vanish completely.

At this moment, a ray of starlight pierced the darkness, locking onto this point.

Chapter 1752: The God Once Changed Mountains and Seas

Starlight descended, and all things bowed! Although the solitary Star did not truly descend, a single ray of its brilliance was enough to crush everything.

The Dao Annihilation of the void realm froze, as if witnessing their king, motionless. Swept by the starlight, it vanished without a trace.

The Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet, about to collapse and return, however, reshaped itself under this pure radiance. It was no longer a stone tablet, but… a severed finger!

This finger had existed for an unfathomable age, its appearance weathered as if by wind and frost, losing the original form of a "finger." It resembled a lone peak standing tall, defying the world. Yet, all who witnessed its existence, their minds were instantly enlightened. This was the Finger of a God. Or, more accurately, the Finger of a True God.

With a resounding boom! As this thought emerged, it was as if the fallen True God had truly crossed time and space, extending a finger to flatten everything.

The vortex of Dao Annihilation instantly shattered and dispersed. Even billions of fierce warriors were instantly crushed before the True God's finger.

Even with the augmentation of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, Li Fan felt his cultivation vanish, his Profound牝ility Dao dissipating like smoke, returning to the boundless primordial state. The solitary Star's ray of brilliance was twisted and broken. With the shackles removed, the True God's Finger instantly collapsed inwards, returning to nothingness.

Moments later, the starlight proliferated a thousandfold, filling Li Fan's vision. Having witnessed the descent of the solitary Star before, Li Fan remained calm, silently chanting in his heart. "True Return!"

At this moment, time seemed to reverse. The effusive starlight, as if encountering a strong wind, flowed backward. Despite its unwillingness, under the suppressive force of True Return's intangible hand, it was forced back to its origin.

The starlight receded, and darkness consumed everything.

After an unknown duration, or perhaps an instant, a ray of starlight reappeared, piercing the darkness like the dawn of a new sun. However, for some reason. The starlight only lasted for a moment before, as if sensing something, its brilliance mysteriously dimmed and vanished.

… Anchored for 1 year!

"The True God's Finger!" Li Fan, upon regaining consciousness, seemed still immersed in the moment the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet revealed its true form under the solitary Star's illumination. His eyes narrowed, and he mimicked the pose, pressing his finger towards the void. "Shatter Saints, break the void realm, crush starlight." "Truly a remnant of a True God."

Infused with the intent of the True God's Finger, even though Li Fan had just awakened and was in mortal form, with a gentle press of his finger, the entire Great Xuan Small World trembled. The heavens resounded with thunderous roars, as if breaking apart, with cracks appearing and spreading like a spiderweb. The Grand Array of Immortality Severance that sealed the Great Xuan Small World shattered instantly, allowing strands of spiritual energy to flow into it from the Xuanhuang Realm.

Not only that, but the profound finger force even penetrated outwards, reaching beyond the Xuanhuang Realm. Within the Immortal Ruins, the Dao-Enlightened Starving Immortal inexplicably felt a jolt in his heart and was about to open his eyes, but Li Fan forcefully pushed him back. As if his memory had been wiped clean, the Starving Immortal resumed his Dao enlightenment. And from beginning to end, the Starving Immortal remained completely unaware of being influenced by external forces.

"Where the finger force reaches, one can arbitrarily alter. Regardless of cultivation or realm." "This is merely an imitation of the intent." Li Fan retracted his hand, gazing intently at his fingertip. The intent of the True God had dissipated, leaving a completely ordinary mortal form. No one would have imagined that it could unleash such transcendent power.

"The various cultivation realms within Mountains and Seas are merely classifications established by us cultivators. In reality, they are all measured against Mountains and Seas. Those who can traverse Mountains and Seas are considered transcendent. Those who can stand shoulder to shoulder with Mountains and Seas are Saints." "However, everything within Mountains and Seas originates from the gods. When the True God's Finger falls, it determines the fate of Mountains and Seas. Borrowing its profoundness, it is naturally easy to distort and rewrite the beings within Mountains and Seas."

Li Fan, in his mortal form, displayed the True God's Finger without any discomfort. Li Fan vaguely sensed that this might be related to his long-term cultivation and comprehension of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood. "If it were anyone else, let alone a mortal, even a Saint would be unable to wield this divine ability so smoothly. But for me…" "Having been constantly influenced by the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, I have become somewhat different."

Li Fan savored the experience of manipulating the Starving Immortal's consciousness using the True God's Finger. While he only made him disregard external events and return to his Dao enlightenment state, he had effectively altered the cultivator's consciousness. Considering that the Starving Immortal, though not as formidable as Li Fan, was only a step away from the True Immortal realm, and yet was treated like a toy by a mortal. What if Li Fan regained his Saint cultivation? What if Li Fan's comprehension of the True God's Finger improved further? The outcome was truly unimaginable.

"If True Return resets Mountains and Seas with a single thought, then the True God's Finger possesses the potential to alter Mountains and Seas. In this regard, both are powers of the same magnitude. No wonder my cultivation of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood yielded such smooth comprehension of the True God's Finger." "But such a divine artifact…"

Li Fan frowned, trying to recall any traces of the True God's Finger from his past self's extensive reincarnation memories. Perhaps because Li Fan's past memories were too vast, the fragments he could recall were merely a tip of the iceberg. Or perhaps, in his previous lives, Li Fan was always struggling against the void realm in the final moments, and thus never noticed the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet hidden within Mountains and Seas. In any case, this was the first time Li Fan had truly encountered it.

Li Fan did not dwell on it further. "Having this divine ability at my disposal is undoubtedly fortunate for me now. With the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood and the True God's Finger combined…" "Even the Saints of the early days of Mountains and Seas would be no match for me."

Li Fan's heart swelled with ambition. However, recalling that in his previous life, the New God who descended seemed to be different, he instantly calmed down. "The two New Gods I encountered had vastly different styles. It can be concluded that the ones who attained godhood in the two lifetimes were not the same individuals. This means that the Saints of the early days of Mountains and Seas all possessed the capability to replace Mountains and Seas and become a New God; they only lacked a bit of luck." "They are indeed formidable. It's no wonder the Three Saints always remained so cautious whenever they mentioned the Saints of the early days of Mountains and Seas."

"We must not act rashly. We should proceed according to the original plan," Li Fan's excitement subsided. "With the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, I do not need to contend with them. The so-called fragmented godhood is ultimately a dead end."

Li Fan compared the various scenarios of the New God's descent across his lifetimes and his judgment was further solidified. "Mountains and Seas, and the New God, both cannot escape the pursuit of the Star. This has long been determined." "Mountains and Seas are boundless and merge together, forming the beginning of Dao Annihilation." "From the day they merged, the ultimate fate of Mountains and Seas was sealed…"

"However, this is hindsight. At the very beginning of Mountains and Seas, when they first merged, Mountains and Seas itself seemed unaware of its tragic future. It remained optimistic." "This is quite suspicious. Even the Saints of the early days of Mountains and Seas, who could foresee the dire catastrophe and chose the method of severing the future to escape the calamity, could not discern it. It makes no sense!"

Suddenly recalling his manipulation of the Starving Immortal's consciousness just now, an idea struck Li Fan. "The Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet, and the True God's Finger, not only caused Mountains and Seas to merge but also distorted and rewrote the concept of Mountains and Seas?"

Li Fan's heart trembled. "Perhaps the merging of Mountains and Seas was merely superficial. The true purpose of the True God's Finger was to alter the consciousness of Mountains and Seas and change its future trajectory."

Instantly, Li Fan thought of the three legends about the aftermath left by the gods. "It is rumored that when the gods were divided, the dying god left behind three posthumous arrangements." "Each with the power to overturn Mountains and Seas." "Previously, I speculated that the Star and True Return were among them." "However, I have now realized that True Return is my past self, obtained through supreme talent and the integration of all Saints' Daos, not a gift from the gods." "Now, it seems the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet is more likely one of the god's posthumous arrangements." "The key is, where did it go?"

Li Fan's mind stirred, and he chose to inherit the [Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas] created in his previous life. A splash-ink scroll appeared in Li Fan's hand. Compared to its initial creation, it had undergone significant changes. After countless years of the New God's battles with the void realm's reverberations, the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas now possessed a different profundity and rhythm. However… "The Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet is gone." "Only its shadow remains." "A faint trace…" "Even with True Return and the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, it cannot be fully replicated?"

This was the first time Li Fan had encountered something that True Return could not recreate. After all, even Mountains and Seas, and all the Saints, could be recreated with a single thought. If there was an object that could not be replicated… "Undoubtedly, it belongs to a realm beyond Mountains and Seas, the realm of gods."

Li Fan carefully examined the remnant of the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet. Even as a faint afterimage, it was still a thousand times more profound than Li Fan's own meticulous carvings. After prolonged observation, his insights grew like spring water from a mountain. Li Fan vaguely understood where the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet had gone after collapsing. "It did not go anywhere; it simply ceased to exist." "The Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet existed only to merge Mountains and Seas. If Mountains and Seas were no more, and its subordinate replacement, the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas, also disappeared, then the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet would naturally cease to manifest." "But if, in the void, Mountains and Seas were to reappear…" "Then the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet would descend again, like a brand on the bone, fixing its fate!" "So, the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet seen in each cycle of Mountains and Seas was not reset by True Return. Instead, it manifested on its own." "As for the myriad inscriptions upon it…"

Li Fan recalled the scene from his previous life, where the residual images of all Saints emerged from the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet during the Dao Annihilation's assault. "They were merely the inscriptions of the Saints' Daos, not the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet itself." "When it reappears, it naturally won't carry them." "The legacy of a True God is indeed extraordinary."

Li Fan looked up, his gaze seeming to pierce through the infinite possibilities of Mountains and Seas, reaching the location of the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet. "This single finger sealed all future possibilities of Mountains and Seas." "No matter how it struggles, no matter what variables arise, as long as Mountains and Seas itself exists, the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet will descend and fix its fate." "Coupled with the solitary Star that devours all in the end." "The fate of Mountains and Seas was truly sealed the moment the god was consumed." "No wonder, the outcome was irrelevant."

Li Fan then couldn't help but ponder, with such methods employed by the god, were three posthumous arrangements truly necessary? "Perhaps, for other purposes." "Either to restrain each other, to prevent failure. Or…" "To prepare for a future return."

The more Li Fan contemplated the True God's Finger, the more he realized the unfathomable nature of the True God in the past. His long-standing question resurfaced. "How did the god die?" "It was always the gods of Mountains and Seas who divided themselves, not Mountains and Seas slaying the god. Clearly, Mountains and Seas alone could not have been the opponent of that True God. Why did the god, the source of all power, perish?" The answer to this question might only be glimpsed at the very beginning of Mountains and Seas, during the division of the gods.

Li Fan did not trouble himself with it and proceeded with his plan. "With the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet as a foundation, my Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas can undoubtedly be considered a supreme treasure of Mountains and Seas." "Under normal circumstances, it can harmonize Dao Annihilation and Mountains and Seas. If I were to add my own True God's Finger enhancement…" "It would be effortless to trap and suppress all Saints with a single thought."

Having successfully crafted such a treasure, Li Fan had not forgotten his original objective, which was to… Become the Master of the Void Realm!

The Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas transformed into black and white robes, enveloping him as Li Fan sat in enlightenment. All the Daos within Mountains and Seas seemed within reach, for him to select. In reality, Li Fan was not touching the true Daos within Mountains and Seas, but merely a copy within the Daoist Diagram. Yet, its verisimilitude was so high that Li Fan could directly use it to achieve Sainthood! "It can greatly reduce the difficulty of achieving enlightenment, but it cannot serve as a foundation for increasing strength. To truly become a Saint of Mountains and Seas, one must still rely on the Daos within Mountains and Seas. However, the miraculous utility of the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas is already astonishing!" "True Spirit infusion solved the issue of SaintworthyMaturity. The Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas bypasses the requirements for enlightenment to become a Saint. Combined, as long as I wish, I can cultivate a sufficient reserve of Saints!" "Saints? They can be replaced at any time!"

As his thoughts churned, Li Fan's aura simultaneously surged. From mortal to Saint realm, Li Fan this time only took fifty-odd years! It was important to note that this was without the Star's favor, relying solely on Li Fan himself! The Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas draped over him, as if all of Mountains and Seas belonged solely to Li Fan. Cultivating and achieving enlightenment was as easy as eating and drinking.

On the day he became a Saint, concealed by the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas, even the Saints on the other shore did not perceive the emergence of another Saint within Mountains and Seas. Wrapped in rolling ink, Li Fan plunged directly into Dao Annihilation. Like ice melting into water, Li Fan, without using the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, but relying solely on the protection of the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas, completely blended into the surrounding Dao Annihilation environment.

But this was still not enough. Li Fan narrowed his eyes, recalling his inheritance of the [Starfall Rhythm Law]. The peculiar, heart-like rhythm of starlight reappeared, illuminating Li Fan's body. The surrounding Dao Annihilation seemed to sense something, instantly becoming turbulent and chaotic.

"Go!" Li Fan threw the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas in his hand into the surrounding submissive Dao Annihilation.

Chapter 1753: Mountain and Sea Great Thief Disciple

The void realm's Dao Annihilation, though bowing to Li Fan, was not truly subservient to him but to the starlight he wore. As an envoy of the [Star], he naturally possessed the authority to command the Dao Annihilation army. However, if the void realm's master were to appear, the Dao Annihilation would instantly lose control. Li Fan's goal in this life was to become the true [Master of the Void Realm].

"Let the Dao Annihilation change its name!" Li Fan revealed the starlight, firmly controlling the surrounding myriad Dao Annihilation forces. Then, he manipulated the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas, modifying them batch by batch. The ink-colored Mountains and Seas continuously churned, and with the rise and fall of the wind and waves, the intangible Dao Annihilation was gradually tainted with the aura of [Daoist One]. Before entering the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas, it was pure Dao Annihilation power, but after passing through, it was branded with the label of the "[Li Family Army]". These modified Dao Annihilation forces were absolutely loyal to Li Fan.

Although currently insignificant compared to the vast void realm, Li Fan believed that since change had begun, altering the landscape would be only a matter of time! The Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas acted like a vortex, slowly corroding the original Dao Annihilation. Yet, Li Fan still felt it was insufficient: "The speed of changing allegiances is still too slow…"

His gaze narrowed, looking towards the nearby Mountains and Seas. With a slight turn of his will, his subordinate Dao Annihilation, like a long spear, plunged directly into Mountains and Seas!

The Saints on the other shore were no strangers to Dao Annihilation. Under normal circumstances, even if the Dao Annihilation tide raged, the white light of the Xuanji Ring, guarded by the Saints, could temporarily resist it.

But this time…

The white light only held for a moment before shattering under the collision! Li Fan's elite forces penetrated deep into Mountains and Seas, descending upon it. Transforming into a world-destroying torrent, they instantly turned tens of thousands of possibilities into dust.

The Saints on the other shore were stunned by such an unexpected turn of events. Dao Annihilation ignoring the Xuanji Ring's defenses was unprecedented! The Saints' gazes turned towards the Three Saints. In Saint Gui Hai's eyes, myriad light images flashed, but they ultimately dissolved into chaos, unable to deduce the cause of this anomaly.

Saint Lian Shan, however, had already recalled his main body from the void realm. With his Lian Shan Staff, he intercepted the rampaging sword-like Dao Annihilation.

"Retreat!"

Among the Saints on the other shore, the only ones Li Fan truly respected were the Three Saints. With Lian Shan's main body having returned, and knowing his strength, Li Fan naturally chose not to confront him directly. One-third of his elite forces stayed behind to cover their retreat, while the main force withdrew rapidly. As swift as their arrival, their departure was even more decisive. In a short while, what seemed like a world-ending catastrophe vanished without a trace.

"Saint Lian Shan's mastery is indeed profound. He easily resolved the calamity of Dao Annihilation with a mere gesture," praised the Saints. Saint Lian Shan, however, vaguely sensed that something was amiss. "This surge of Dao Annihilation… came strangely." "Indeed. It might return soon. We must be vigilant."

…

In the void realm, although Saint Lian Shan's intervention resulted in the loss of some of Li Fan's elite forces, it was entirely worth it.

"Dao Annihilation devours Mountains and Seas, and the essence of divinity returns to the void realm, and back to the solitary Star."

"This should be the case. But then…" Li Fan stared intently at the twinkling lights slowly rising within the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas. The destination of these lights seemed predetermined. Even though Li Fan's subordinate Dao Annihilation had completed the world-destroying purge, they could not retain even a sliver. The brilliance flowed out of the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas, heading towards the unknown solitary Star above the void realm. No power could stop it.

"This is also why the void realm's master is destined to be a pitiful wage slave." "Dedicating immense effort to destroy Mountains and Seas, only to be unable to enjoy any of it, all for the solitary descending Star…" Li Fan's mind suddenly stirred as he recalled the scene of the solitary Star devouring everything.

"Perhaps, it is not that they cannot, but that they are unable." "The gods divided into Mountains and Seas, and upon the destruction of Mountains and Seas, everything returns to the gods." "Even if the void realm's master coveted it, they would be powerless."

"But…"

Within the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas, as Li Fan's will flowed, the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet suddenly emitted a faint, profound stream of light. Even though it was not the true Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet, but merely a fleeting shadow, the moment its brilliance manifested, the returning starlight seemed to instantly lose its direction. It became hesitant and uncertain.

"As expected…" Li Fan rejoiced at the sight. However, his joy did not last long. The illusory Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet, after all, could not contend with the influence of the true solitary Star. Ultimately, most of the essence of Mountains and Seas extracted through consumption was lost towards the solitary Star, vanishing without a trace.

Only about one in a million of the remainder was lured by Li Fan and lingered within the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas. Starlight descended, adhering to the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet, causing the illusory shadow to sharpen. Though the starlight only contained a few wisps of Mountains and Seas, Li Fan clearly felt the entire [Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas] become more substantial.

The pleasant surprises were not over. While Li Fan had managed to steal starlight by his own skill, the void realm's master, in turn, provided "rewards" for his subordinate Dao Annihilation's consumption of Mountains and Seas. A thought suddenly descended and retreated. It arrived abruptly, but Li Fan, with the dual blessings of Illusion is True and the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas, was not discovered.

Examining the changes, Li Fan found that the Dao Annihilation under his command had been affirmed by the void realm's master and had been promoted, becoming the "leader" of the myriad surrounding Dao Annihilation forces. "Able to mobilize more nearby Mountains and Seas Dao Annihilation power, and even, based on [Void Realm Memory], create Saints of Mountains and Seas! Although the quantity is currently limited to one, the potential is immense!"

From this change, Li Fan could vaguely discern the operational model of the void realm's Dao Annihilation. The void realm's master oversaw the grand scheme. The Dao Annihilation forces acted independently, carving up and devouring Mountains and Seas. Those who achieved success would be promoted, influencing and modifying surrounding Dao Annihilation forces according to effective invasion methods.

"As for the [Void Realm Memory]…" "It originates from that mysterious will of the void realm's master." "Although the Dao Annihilation that devoured Mountains and Seas could not hide its gains, during the process of erosion, all beings within Mountains and Seas, including Mountains and Seas itself and the Saints, were observed with extreme clarity. If there were sufficient power, recreating and evolving them would be within reach."

Li Fan felt faint figures emerging from his subordinate Dao Annihilation. They were, unmistakably, familiar Saints. "With my current control over Dao Annihilation, it's insufficient to create the Three Saints. However…" With a shift of thought, the Dao Annihilation churned, and shadows coalesced. Shou Qiu, cloaked in ink, materialized before him. Upon manifestation, he appeared slightly disoriented for a moment. But soon, he understood his situation and bowed to Li Fan. Fashioned by Li Fan's subordinate Dao Annihilation, he naturally acted entirely according to Li Fan's commands.

"Not merely an empty shell, but retaining some of the will and thoughts from his previous life." "But he is not the true Shou Qiu."

"But…" Li Fan, having been united with Shou Qiu in many instances and repeatedly inheriting his memories, being intimately familiar with Shou Qiu's ways, gathered all his knowledge. A point of light emerged from his fingertip and was pressed into the forehead of the ink-colored Shou Qiu.

Chapter 1754: Fluttering Play with Three Saints

The ink-colored Shou Qiu's face contorted in struggle. Becoming a tool of the void realm, contrary to his lifelong principles, caused an extremely violent shock to his mind. The reaction was so strong that it exceeded Li Fan's expectations.

"His thoughts conflict with his Dao; he cannot bear himself. He risks self-destruction!" Li Fan had not anticipated Shou Qiu's unwavering righteousness. Upon realizing his situation, he would rather choose self-annihilation than become a servant of the void realm.

But since he was under Li Fan's control, his life and death, his desires, were no longer his own to decide. With a thought, rolling Dao Annihilation surged forth, re-stitching the fragmented body of Shou Qiu. Then, Li Fan infused it with memories of his cycles of saving the world.

"To destroy the world is to save it; to kill life is to protect life. Daoist Shou Qiu, you misunderstand me deeply!" Li Fan sighed sorrowfully.

As expected, upon learning of Li Fan's past actions, Shou Qiu's struggles gradually weakened. However, he clearly still harbored reservations about his void realm persona and merely gazed at Li Fan without speaking.

"The solitary Star's descent is inevitable. Regardless of your stance or identity, Mountains and Seas cannot escape its doom."

"Whether destroyed by our hands or by the void realm, what fundamental difference is there?"

"Rather than be passively consumed by Dao Annihilation, it is better to become resources for us to deal with the void realm and the solitary Star."

"The phrase 'outcome is irrelevant,' Daoist friend, you still haven't truly grasped it!"

Facing Li Fan's words, Shou Qiu remained silent, but his contempt was evident. Li Fan paid it no mind and chuckled softly.

"Forget it, I know Daoist Shou Qiu would not collude with me."

"But, even if you don't approve of my methods, you should at least acknowledge my aspiration to save the world."

"The future of Mountains and Seas rests entirely on my shoulders. Without resorting to extreme measures, how can I find a glimmer of hope in impossibility?" Li Fan spoke with a sense of melancholy.

Shou Qiu's gaze shifted, his expression becoming more solemn.

"In this life, I intend to become the Master of the Void Realm."

"Since you are unwilling to accompany me, what difference does it make if I walk alone?"

"However…"

"I have an item I wish for Daoist friend to help me comprehend."

As Li Fan spoke, he slowly unfurled the [Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas]. The ink-colored Mountains and Seas churned, like a storm, appearing and disappearing, as if real.

Shou Qiu's eyes flashed with surprise upon first seeing it. Soon, his attention was drawn to the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet at the center of the Daoist Diagram.

"This is…"

"The True God's Finger." Li Fan's voice echoed softly.

Upon hearing these three words, even with Shou Qiu's composure, his ink-colored body trembled uncontrollably.

"When the divine finger fell, Mountains and Seas changed. This is the origin of the initial merging of Mountains and Seas."

"This Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas is merely a phantom I comprehended. Even so, it possesses the power to reshape the world!" Li Fan said, pointing a finger towards the ink-colored Shou Qiu.

It was as if, in an instant, he was facing the entire Mountains and Seas, or perhaps witnessing the True God outside of Mountains and Seas. The Daoist body of Shou Qiu uncontrollably surged.

The ink-colored Shou Qiu's expression subtly changed. The power of the True God's Finger was something he had never encountered before. Directly altering the origins of all things within Mountains and Seas was beyond mere description as "profound."

The fluctuations from Li Fan's fingertip, about to land on Shou Qiu's body, stopped just in time.

"I believe you can see that with this True God's Finger, even if you are unwilling, I can easily rewrite your will. However, we have, after all, fought side-by-side countless times…"

Perhaps it was the inherent reverence of cultivators of Mountains and Seas for the mysteries of the True God, or perhaps Li Fan's final words moved him. After a long period of silent contemplation, Shou Qiu finally nodded. While he would not assist in evil deeds, he would help Li Fan comprehend the secrets of the True God's Finger.

"Please, Daoist Shou Qiu, first comprehend the phantom of the True God's Finger I have left. When the true True God's Finger manifests in this life, that will be the crucial moment of comprehension."

The ink-colored Shou Qiu sat down, transforming into a speck of dust, floating beside the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet.

"As the saying goes, 'prevention is better than cure.' Daoist Shou Qiu, although you have agreed, I trust your character. However, this concerns the secrets of a True God…"

"To prevent any unforeseen circumstances, I need to take some precautions. Please do not mind, Daoist Shou Qiu."

As Li Fan spoke, wisps of ink emerged from the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas, like countless shackles, binding and restraining Shou Qiu. Shou Qiu chuckled, unconcerned, focusing his intent on the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet.

Li Fan bowed respectfully, and more ink continued to surge, completely isolating Shou Qiu from the outside world, save for the faint light of the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet penetrating inwards.

The smile on his face instantly vanished. Li Fan pondered inwardly, "My decision was correct. The reaction of the void realm avatar was so intense; how much more so for the true entity? If I had remained aligned with him, I might have been dragged into self-destruction."

"However, although I have finally persuaded him, he is merely an avatar. His comprehension ability naturally cannot match the true Shou Qiu." Li Fan's gaze flickered as he formulated a plan. "If the quality is insufficient, then increase the quantity."

Looking towards the distant Mountains and Seas, Li Fan's eyes were cold and calm. While a significant portion of Dao Annihilation power was used to shape Shou Qiu's void realm avatar, it did not affect Li Fan's progress in devouring Mountains and Seas. As a former Saint of Mountains and Seas, he was intimately familiar with his target. He even anticipated the actions of the Saints on the other shore. Using the same tactic as before.

While the Saints' main bodies were in Mountains and Seas, he strengthened himself. When the Saints' main bodies went to the void realm to attempt reunification, Li Fan dispatched his subordinate Dao Annihilation to devour Mountains and Seas to his heart's content.

The Dao Annihilation tide raged, on the verge of engulfing countless possibilities. At this moment, a staff, a shovel, and a club suddenly appeared, imprisoning the surging Dao Annihilation. The three formed a formation, their white radiance like a dike, preventing the Dao Annihilation from breaking through no matter how it churned.

The illusory figures of the Three Saints materialized within the white circle, their expressions grave as they looked at the imprisoned Dao Annihilation tide.

"This surge of Dao Annihilation seems different from before."

"The void realm has actually produced a second will?" The Three Saints deduced, arriving at an incredible conclusion.

Just as the Three Saints' expressions turned strange, the sealed Dao Annihilation seemed to come alive. It boiled, converged, and finally condensed into a phantom figure. It smiled sinisterly at the Three Saints, then suddenly exploded. The dark light penetrated instantly, piercing the Xuanji Ring's blockade. The trap, set by the Three Saints themselves with the Lian Shan Staff, Gui Hai Shovel, and Zhong Sheng Club, was treated as nothing by the opponent.

The white light persisted, seemingly unharmed by the explosion. However, the Dao Annihilation tide imprisoned within had vanished without a trace.

"This!" The illusory figures of the Three Saints flickered, revealing their inner turmoil. Saint Gui Hai exhausted his deductions but could not ascertain the origin of this newly born void realm will.

"The situation was already precarious, and now another variable has emerged…"

"Where did this variable come from?" The Three Saints' gazes interlocked, as if discussing something. Then, light and shadow shifted, and a Ruyi scepter appeared. It was condensed like autumn water, emitting a clear radiance that even the Three Saints' brilliance could not suppress. Clouds flowed around it, occasionally emitting deep black light, as if an eye were hidden within, observing all things. The handle's curve was natural, while the tail seemed to exist between reality and nothingness, like the meeting point of a hundred rivers merging into the sea, blending into one another.

Had Li Fan been present, seeing this Ruyi artifact, he would have instantly recognized it as Bai Xiao's creation, the [Ruyi Heart]. Yet, inexplicably, despite being crafted by Bai Xiao before his transcendence, the Three Saints treated it with extreme caution. Even when the Dao Annihilation army had arrived and was on the verge of devouring half of Mountains and Seas, the Three Saints had never been this solemn.

Facing the strange radiance on the surface of the [Ruyi Heart], the Three Saints instinctively closed their eyes.

"Let us use this item to investigate."

"We must proceed with caution."

Without any visible manipulation, the [Ruyi Heart] began to integrate into its surroundings from the tail, its acceleration multiplied a thousandfold. The wondrous Ruyi gradually vanished. The head of the [Ruyi Heart], with its hidden eye, suddenly opened, gazing towards the void realm.

Chapter 1755: Matters of the Void Realm

"The Three Saints are not to be underestimated. With just a glance, they perceived the anomaly and set up defenses."

"Fortunately, my plan was superior!" The gains from this encounter were naturally not as great as the first surprise attack, but they were sufficient to shape a second Shou Qiu avatar.

"The key is the reward from the void realm's will."

"The more Dao Annihilation I can mobilize, the faster it will be transformed by the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas. Master of the Void Realm??" Li Fan was deep in thought when a sense of extreme crisis, as if being spied upon, suddenly arose.

Without hesitation, Illusion is True enveloped him, simultaneously covering the Daoist Diagram of Mountains and Seas.

*Thump… thump… thump…*

Without Li Fan's will manipulating it, the void realm returned to its original silence. In the darkness, Li Fan felt as if he could hear his own heartbeat. It was a tremor originating from his body's instinct.

"This power is not weaker than facing the New God directly."

"What…" Li Fan dared not act rashly, forcibly suppressing all thoughts within his mind, hiding beneath the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood to observe further developments.

Within Dao Annihilation, ripples seemed to arise. Unbeknownst to their origin, they spread like ripples across the entire void realm in an instant. It was like a gaze sweeping across.

After a brief silence, the infinite Dao Annihilation of the void realm boiled forth, responding! Even when the solitary Star descended, consuming everything, the void realm's reaction was not this intense. It was as if it had encountered something extremely important to itself.

The Dao Annihilation, or perhaps the void realm's master, was using all means to pursue the source of the gaze. Li Fan could feel the unrestrained madness from his subordinate Dao Annihilation.

"The usually calm Master of the Void Realm is actually acting so erratically."

"They can temporarily abandon the mission of devouring Mountains and Seas, in pursuit of…"

"Their own ambition?" Li Fan gradually understood the void realm master's current obsession.

Just as cultivators of Xuanhuang, upon witnessing Scarlet Flame; transcendent powerhouses, upon encountering the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas; and Li Fan, upon encountering the True God's Finger. Despite differences in realm and strength, the pursuit of "advancement" and further potential was the same.

"Can the void realm, through this gaze, or more accurately, the source of the gaze, achieve a different kind of creation?" Li Fan's heart trembled.

The void realm master seemed to exist solely for the solitary Star's descent. After tirelessly devouring Mountains and Seas, even they could not escape their fate when the solitary Star broke free. The void realm master naturally knew this, but like Mountains and Seas' fate of returning to the Star, it was their inevitable end. Resistance was futile.

But what if… they could advance further? Even the New God born after the destruction of Mountains and Seas was no match for the void realm's Dao Annihilation. If they could advance further, wouldn't they possess the might of a True God?

How was this possible?!

"Could this gaze originate from a True God?"

"Just like the True God's Finger."

"The third posthumous arrangement left by the gods?"

"Why have I never seen it in my countless past lives?"

Instantly, Li Fan's thoughts raced. He immediately thought of its possible origin.

"I just escaped the encirclement of the Three Saints, and this gaze pursued me."

"Could it be…" The coincidence was too great, making Li Fan unable to dismiss the thought.

"Lian Shan, Gui Hai, Tai Yi!" A cold glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

But now, with the void realm's tides and the mysterious gaze intertwined, Li Fan dared not act rashly. He could only continue to hide beneath the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, awaiting further developments.

The void realm was boundless, yet the gaze seemed to encompass all. After searching fruitlessly, it gradually dissipated. The void realm master desperately tried to retain it, but the ripples were like sand slipping through fingers, impossible to grasp.

With the gaze gone, the boiling void realm returned to silence. Then, Li Fan felt a command from the void realm master. The Dao Annihilation instantly became agitated again, surging towards Mountains and Seas. Majestic and grand, it resembled a final assault. Mountains and Seas were momentarily in a precarious situation.

However, Li Fan frowned slightly. "Although the void realm holds the overall advantage, it should not be the time for a decisive battle yet."

"To prolong the battle line, continuously devouring Mountains and Seas, gradually weakening its strength, would allow for a final, decisive victory."

"Now, due to the appearance of that mysterious gaze, the void realm has become disorganized."

"Besides, I still pocketed some…"

"Could it be that in this life, Mountains and Seas will actually triumph over the void realm?" A seemingly unbelievable thought suddenly arose in Li Fan's mind.

Originally, Li Fan dismissed it as a joke and was about to shake his head and discard it. But it seemed to have triggered something, causing a sharp pain in Li Fan's mind, and a torrent of images flashed successively.

"After countless reincarnations, I have finally succeeded."
