"Mountains and Seas suppress Dao Annihilation, the void realm's will has collapsed, and the threat of Mountains and Seas' destruction is no more!" Joy was evident on his face. Li Fan and the Saints around him were celebrating this moment.

But for some reason, a sense of foreboding suddenly arose in his heart. The other Saints perceived nothing. Li Fan was the first to look up. A ray of starlight, from an unknown source, descended like snowflakes upon Mountains and Seas.

The jubilant Mountains and Seas gradually fell silent. Everyone stared fixedly at Li Fan with extremely strange eyes. A chill crept into Li Fan's heart, and immediately, he was attacked by everyone around him. Even the Mountains and Seas he had painstakingly saved turned against him.

Chapter 1756: The Starfall Devours the Mortal Body

"Shou Qiu!"

"Yongge!"

"Lian Shan!"

Starlight washed over Mountains and Seas, and once close comrades-in-arms had become his slaves.

Even though Li Fan shouted himself hoarse, trying to awaken their senses,

all was in vain. Their resolute eyes had long turned dark and indifferent.

No trace of struggle appeared on their faces, only distorted ferocity. They unleashed their divine abilities and techniques without reservation.

Even the surviving victors of Mountains and Seas let out roars, vowing to exterminate Li Fan.

Figures who had fought side-by-side with him before now surrounded him.

Those who had once fiercely protected Mountains and Seas now, without remembering their past, treated Li Fan as an enemy.

One moment, they were celebrating the successful salvation of Mountains and Seas, and the next, the situation had undergone such a drastic change.

Friends and kin were lost, and his efforts were in vain.

Under the eerie starlight, all living beings were twisted. Mountains and Seas were reborn, but they were no longer the Mountains and Seas of old.

Familiar things were instantly rewritten by the solitary Star. Li Fan's heart ached as if stabbed by a knife, and tears streamed down his face.

He was on the verge of despair.

Repeated failures were not frightening.

What was frightening was that after enduring thousands of calamities and countless reincarnations, it seemed that the disaster had finally been resolved.

But the descent of the solitary Star could still not be prevented.

First, hope was given, then despair was mercilessly cast down.

Li Fan's indomitable will was almost shattered.

He allowed the familiar Saints to attack him, piercing his body, and no longer resisted.

But in his final moments, witnessing the frenzied and terrifying state of Mountains and Seas under the starlight, Li Fan still forced himself to hold onto his will, using the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood to reverse everything.

"Hoo…"

Li Fan awoke from the boundless illusion.

This memory, unlike the fleeting fragments of the past, was incredibly real, as if he had personally experienced it in his previous life.

Li Fan found that a trace of undried tears still lingered at the corners of his eyes, apparently from immersing himself in the memories.

"It's not just emotions that are affected. Even…"

An unbearable pain spread from all over his body, as if the events of the Saints attacking him in the memory had truly happened in reality.

Even more astonishing to Li Fan was that specks of starlight began to emerge from various parts of his body, rustling and scratching.

It was as if a solitary Star had truly appeared above his head, shining down and locking onto Li Fan.

If the starlight inhaled from observing the Starfall Rhythm Law was one, then the scale of starlight gathered on Li Fan at this moment was a thousandfold.

And this was just the beginning.

The surrounding Dao Annihilation seemed to sense something and spontaneously surged towards Li Fan, like royalty greeting their king.

The feeling of being exposed to a certain gaze intensified, as if being roasted in a fierce fire, his entire body about to evaporate.

"When truth becomes falsehood, falsehood also becomes truth!"

Clearly aware of the Star's power, Li Fan, upon witnessing the abnormality in his body, decisively employed the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, attempting to suppress the influence of the starlight.

But before that, the corrosion brought by the solitary Star's strange light had already silently begun.

"When truth becomes truth, falsehood is also false!" Although his thoughts were based on the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, what Li Fan displayed was a distorted and incomplete imitation, having lost most of its essence, a four-unlike-anything divine ability!

The starlight did not fade; instead, it spread further.

"Slap!"

Suddenly, Li Fan's right hand slapped himself forcefully. It was not his intention, but his arm, controlled by the starlight, wanted to use this opportunity to further invade his head.

It was indeed successful.

Threads of starlight gradually appeared in Li Fan's left eye. Then, the eyeball seemed to be pulled out by an immense force, popping out of its socket.

With flesh and blood still connected, the starry eyeball turned halfway around and stared at Li Fan with a strange gaze.

In his own eyeball, Li Fan seemed to see a future where his entire body was soaked in starlight, becoming a servant of the solitary Star.

"Hmph!" Li Fan remained undaunted. Forcing himself to cheer up, he used the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood as his blade, severing the starlight eyeball from his flesh and blood.

However, the eyeball did not break its connection with Li Fan. With a flash of light, it returned to his eye socket.

Bang! Bang! Bang! Bang!

After a moment of silence, the starry eyeball began to violently collide inwards.

Blood gushed out like a spring.

"Damn it…"

It was not that he could not bear the pain; in countless past reincarnations, Li Fan had endured torments several times greater but had always managed to endure.

It was because, with the eyeball's continuous collisions, Li Fan's vision began to be gradually filled with starlight.

The erosion of the starlight accelerated further.

"Damn it, damn it, damn it!" Mad laughter erupted from Li Fan's mouth, but it was not his own intention; it was his mouth, which had mutated uncontrollably.

With each utterance, his mouth seemed to be torn wider. In a moment, Li Fan's entire jaw was ripped open.

He could no longer make any sound.

Silence followed. Li Fan's remaining upper lip constantly opened and closed.

At first, there was no sound. But slowly, murmuring sounds began to emanate from Li Fan's mouth.

The Dao Annihilation waves gradually rose, as if stirred by a strong wind, even the commotion rivaled that of the mysterious gaze scanning earlier. Spots of light burst forth from his body again, like festering sores.

Apart from his own sea of consciousness, Li Fan's body was completely lost.

The low murmurs emanating from his mouth not only affected Li Fan's body.

It also distorted Li Fan's memories.

For example, the [Starfall Rhythm Law] he had previously observed. Originally, Li Fan had only glanced at it superficially, but now, with the voice constantly echoing in his mind, Li Fan found the changes in the starlight to be slowly becoming clear and understandable.

So that's how it is, it's like this?

Li Fan almost became lost in it.

Fortunately, at the critical moment, the tragic sight of his former comrades distorted under the starlight flickered in his mind.

This startled Li Fan, temporarily pulling him away from his yearning for the starlight.

The temptation of the Star was like a shadow, closely following, and was about to drag Li Fan into the abyss again.

In this moment of crisis, Li Fan became calm as never before.

He abandoned the defense of most of his sea of consciousness, only guarding the core.

His thoughts raced: "The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood can absolutely reverse the trend of the solitary Star's descent. This is beyond doubt. The reason why I am now in such a miserable state, vulnerable to the erosion of starlight, is because my comprehension of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood has been distorted by the Star."

"The only way to survive…"

"Find the countermeasure, and restore my True Transformation of Truth and Falsehood to its original level!"

Li Fan resolutely transferred his last wisp of will into the Dao One Mountains and Seas Map floating quietly beside him.

Or, more accurately, onto the True God's Finger within the Mountains and Seas Map!

The Boundless Monument bore the imprints of all Saints, making it merely the Boundless Monument.

But when all later traces faded and it returned to its original form, the one who descended into the world was the True God's Finger!

Li Fan's spiritual sense hid within the Boundless Monument, and the starlight instinctively followed.

Amidst the starlight, the True God's Finger also appeared!

Although it was merely an illusionary phantom comprehended by Li Fan, it actually produced an inconceivable change when it collided with the starlight Li Fan had drawn!

Beside the Boundless Monument, Shou Qiu, who was meditating, was instantly swallowed without even time to struggle.

Chapter 1757: The Mystery of Mountains and Seas is Finally Solved

Starlight diffused.

An aura of dominance gradually emerged, and the True God's Finger, from 虚化实 (illusory to real), reappeared in the world! It seemed that to the starlight, this severed finger held an attraction far beyond that of Li Fan. All brilliance that met its gaze converged towards the True God's Finger. Even the light points engulfing most of Li Fan's body were abandoned without regret, disappearing directly into the starlight. Li Fan gradually regained control of his body but felt ill-at-ease, as if his every limb was stiff and out of sync. "After being immersed in starlight for only a moment, it feels like I've been away from the mortal world for ten thousand years." The extreme discomfort of his body, coupled with the corrosion of his thoughts, made him sluggish. However, spurred by his survival instinct, he did not forget his perilous situation. With a thought, the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood enveloped him, bringing an unparalleled sense of peace and stability amidst the storm. The corrosive feeling was expelled, and Li Fan's thoughts and abilities returned to their normal levels. He observed the changes unfolding before him.

There should only be one True God's Finger in the world. Thus, when the True God's Finger appeared under the starlight, the Boundless Tablet within the Mountains and Seas became turbulent. Its foundation vanished, leaving only the Dao marks of the Saints, unable to bear the destiny of the "Boundless Mountains and Seas." The Dao marks, like fragile branches, snapped inch by inch. The existing merged Mountains and Seas, at this moment, showed signs of separation!

Within the Xuanji Ring, due to the severe side effects of using "Ruyi Heart," the Three Saints closed their eyes, suppressing the Ruyi artifact once more. "Hmm?" At this moment, Saint Lian Shan was the first to sense the anomaly in the Mountains and Seas. Lian Shan represented all civilizations and beings who had attempted to bridge mountains and seas; their strength and foundation were built upon the fusion of mountains and seas. Now that mountains and seas were showing signs of separation, he was naturally the most affected. The mountains above, which were originally at his shoulder level, seemed to rise on their own, distancing themselves from the mortal world. Even though the Bridge of Lian Shan desperately extended, attempting to repair the rift, the speed of separation far surpassed Saint Lian Shan's ability to mend.

Hum, hum, hum… Once the gap exceeded a certain limit, a faint cracking sound emanated from between the mountains and seas. The sound echoed and reverberated. Mortal beings, unaware, perceived nothing. But all who had achieved True Immortal status felt a premonition, as if disaster had struck, their faces contorted in terror. Immortals stood above the mountains, connecting to the boundless sea. They possessed the supreme power of Immortals, wielding infinite divine abilities. But now, the bridge connecting the mountains above had collapsed with a bang. The countless Immortals on the bridge naturally could not escape the calamity and also plummeted downwards. Their cultivation realms and auras dropped at a visible rate. Saints, Transcendent beings, Nameless ones, True Immortals. Regardless of their realm, strength, or struggles, they could not escape. All plummeted to the mortal realm. How could mortals, now in mortal bodies, wield infinite power? Trapped in Dao Annihilation, unable to protect themselves, they perished instantly. Seeking refuge in the Mountains and Seas, they were instead engulfed by the boundless power of the Infinite Sea, becoming a part of the vast ocean.

With the disappearance of the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet, at this moment, 99.9% of cultivators above True Immortal realm in the Mountains and Seas perished. The remaining fortunate few, though still struggling, were destined for destruction. Because… the Mountains and Seas had awakened! Without the True God's Finger, the Mountains and Seas separated, reverting to their initial state of devouring the divine. The countless fallen cultivators within the Mountains and Seas transformed into nourishment, returning to the Mountains and Seas, allowing the once dying Mountains and Seas to regain some vitality, as if they had consumed a powerful tonic. While not returning to their peak state, they at least possessed the strength for a final desperate struggle.

More importantly, the will of the Mountains and Seas, twisted and rewritten by the True God's Finger, had returned to normal. The continuous mountain ranges stood tall and majestic. The boundless ocean reflected the myriad worlds. The two true wills representing the Mountains and Seas descended upon them. When the Mountains and Seas merged, they intertwined, chaotic and unclear, guided only by instinct. But now, separated into two, the mountains were solely mountains, the seas solely seas. Each independent will, upon separating from the other, became incredibly prosperous.

Thus, the Three Saints found themselves in different predicaments. Although the Three Saints were also affected by the anomaly, plummeting to the mortal realm, they survived for various reasons. As if sensing what was about to happen, Saint Lian Shan looked at the other two and sighed, "All feasts must eventually end…" Before his words were finished, Saint Lian Shan, not as a specific figure within the Mountains and Seas, but as all the differentiated parts, transformed into streaks of light and withdrew into the mountains above. Saint Gui Hai also responded with a soft sigh. Countless blue light points floated, surging into the boundless possibilities of the infinite sea. As for the last, Saint Tai Yi. Countless figures seemed to evaporate, disappearing. Tai Yi, and the Great Dao of Infinite Evolution it represented, all returned to the Mountains and Seas respectively! Mountains and Seas had once generated infinite Great Daos and countless beings, but now, all were reclaimed. Everything returned to its most primitive state! Just like at the beginning of the gods' division.

The anomaly occurring within the Mountains and Seas was already world-shattering. However, compared to the changes produced by the collision between starlight and the True God's Finger in the void, it seemed insignificant. As if it had found the key to breaking free, infinite starlight, centered on the True God's Finger, instantly permeated the surroundings. Compared to the solitary Star that descended before, the pervasive starlight now appeared softer. At the very least, the void realm could still exist under the starlight's illumination. At the very least, Li Fan could still barely maintain the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood state and continue observing. As the endless starlight initially manifested, Li Fan could faintly glimpse a blurry figure hidden behind the starlight for a moment. But as the starlight expanded a millionfold in an instant, Li Fan's vision was completely obscured. "Could it be my illusion?" Li Fan was filled with doubt. However, he soon had no time to ponder such questions.

The starlight spread endlessly from the depths of the void realm. As the central node of the Star's descent, the True God's Finger also seemed to feel the increasing brilliance around it, undergoing further changes. The change was not in the True God's Finger itself, but in its "posture." It was an extremely mysterious phenomenon; despite being merely a severed finger, it could perform various actions. The "Boundless Mountains and Seas," which Li Fan had seen before, distorted the will of the Mountains and Seas, causing them to merge. Now, the finger's transformation pointed towards the starlight filling the sky. In an instant, the brilliant starlight seemed to lose its color, transforming from dazzling brightness to a dull black and white. The entire void dimmed as a result. The starlight, no longer blazing, lost its sharpness, and its threat was greatly reduced. Looking up, Li Fan felt an intimation that, even without the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, he could now resist its influence. However, Li Fan did not rashly test it; the changes were truly beyond his expectations.

"What is happening? Why is the True God's Finger attacking the starlight?" "The solitary Star and the True God's Finger should both be remnants left by the gods, meant to merge the Mountains and Seas through the descent of the solitary Star?" The events unfolding before him completely contradicted Li Fan's assumptions, filling him with doubt while also subtly touching upon the truth about gods, Mountains and Seas, and the Star. "Since their identities and motivations deviate from their actual actions, let's re-evaluate." "Among the three, Mountains and Seas are the murderers of their divine fragments and the victims." "The True God's Finger…" "The faint ancient aura upon it, coupled with its ability to rewrite the will of Mountains and Seas, thus triggering their merger, and its power to dissipate the starlight, re-sealing the solitary Star… Such might and divine abilities can only be possessed by a True God." Li Fan first confirmed this point. "Finally, the Star." "What exactly is the Star?" At the end of every cycle, the solitary Star descends, devouring everything. It was evident that the Star seemed to be a contingency plan left by the True God, meant to allow for rebirth after being fragmented by the gods. The descent of the solitary Star leads to the destruction of Mountains and Seas, the annihilation of the void realm, and the rebirth of a New God. Li Fan had always believed this. But, was this truly the case? The scene of the True God's Finger turning against the starlight shattered this assumption. "The Star is not a god?" "Then what is the Star…?" There were no other known options. If the Star were not a god, then… The Star is Mountains and Seas. "The Star is Mountains and Seas! The Star is Mountains and Seas!" The moment this thought arose, Li Fan's body and mind trembled. The shock of such a drastic contrast almost prevented him from maintaining the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, and revealing himself amidst the battle between the True God's Finger and the starlight. "How could this be? How is this possible?" Li Fan forced himself to calm down. But a premonition had already arisen in his heart, making him know the conclusion of his deductions before even thinking them through.

In his mind, the infinite memories of his past self, like a breached dam, could no longer be suppressed. They exploded outwards. Countless figures flickered, countless past scenes burned like firewood, ultimately converging into an overwhelming sense of unyielding resentment and boundless rage born from despair. This was the final emotion of Li Fan's past self before making a decision, and the reason for the existence of the current Li Fan. "So that's how it is." Li Fan's expression became extremely peculiar. Gazing at the interaction before him, his cold nature acted like a stabilizing force, methodically sorting through all the resentment and anger. What his past self could not accept, Li Fan now viewed with indifference. "It's just, I feel a bit sorry for you." Li Fan let out a light sigh. With the support of his past memories, everything logically fell into place. Li Fan's heart was free of doubt. "If the Star is not the Star, then the Star is Mountains and Seas." "Mountains and Seas devouring themselves seems absurd, but if combined with their fated merger and the properties and actions set by the True God's Finger…" "Then everything can be explained."

"When time rewound to the moments after the True God's fall and the divine fragmentation of Mountains and Seas." Li Fan's vision was suddenly filled with a bizarre scene. In the darkness, two formless, ferocious entities seemed to be silently devouring something, greedily and with enjoyment. True God vanished, and two new gods were about to be born. But… Suddenly, a sense of fear spread from the heart of Mountains and Seas. After devouring part of the True God's body, they had also gained some of the True God's abilities. Thus, they could, to some extent, foresee future events. They saw that the True God had not completely vanished after death. As if the True God's solitary eye was still coldly watching them. As long as Mountains and Seas existed, the True God's Finger would appear. Mountains and Seas gradually merged, eventually returning to nothingness. Only pure energy remained. Upon this boundless and infinite warm bed, upon the corpses of Mountains and Seas, the True God would be reborn. The True God would return again. The remnants of the True God's body instantly became unappetizing. As newly born gods, Mountains and Seas naturally did not wish to suffer the same fate as their food. After foreseeing their own destruction, Mountains and Seas immediately deduced countless possibilities. But in all endings, there was no image of their survival. The True God's final strike before falling had annihilated all possibilities of reversal for Mountains and Seas. Mountains and Seas had no chance of winning. Just as they had newly transformed, they were about to embark on a path of destined destruction. How could these two newly born gods accept this? Even ants strive to survive, let alone divine beings? After completely devouring the True God's body, an unknown amount of time passed. Exhausting countless epochs, Mountains and Seas combined their efforts and deduced the only possible method of turning defeat into victory. "Since Mountains and Seas are doomed to perish, then…" "Let Mountains and Seas perish themselves." "Bury themselves completely, and then, before the True God's resurrection, conceive again." "This is your method of survival?" Li Fan's gaze seemed to pierce through the dark void, reaching the will behind it. In his mind, the scene of the solitary Star descending and devouring everything replayed. "The existence of the True God's Finger and its activation condition is the existence of Mountains and Seas." "With the invasion of the void realm's Dao Annihilation, if Mountains and Seas cease to exist, the True God's Finger will also vanish into nothingness, disappearing without a trace." "The only opposing opponent has finally disappeared. The Star, or the reborn Mountains and Seas, will immediately descend." "I want nothing but myself. Only I will remain, only I will be born, only I will win." "So the void realm's Dao Annihilation is merely a tool for Mountains and Seas to destroy themselves." "So it was all just a meticulously crafted play." "The beings of Mountains and Seas, Lian Shan, Gui Hai, Tai Yi. Shou Qiu, Dao De. They were all merely actors in the play." "As long as they followed the script and completed their designated roles, everything would be harmonious." "The True God perishes completely, the New Gods are without worry." "The grand play concludes, the New Gods ascend." "Perfect." "But regrettably…" Li Fan sighed. Not for any other reason, but for the lost "Li Fan" of the past. "An outsider to the play, who should not have existed." "Mountains and Seas self-destructing, in his eyes, was an incomparably terrifying catastrophe. Lives were perishing, and he wanted to save them from suffering." "Once is not enough, then a hundred times. If a hundred times is not enough, then a thousand, ten thousand times." "Countless times." "Finally, finally, finally…" "He turned the impossible into the possible, breaking the script written by [Mountains and Seas]." "Mountains and Seas finally won. But…" "As such, how can the script continue?"

Just as Mountains and Seas had foreseen. As long as Mountains and Seas existed, the True God's Finger would not perish. Without the void realm, without Dao Annihilation. Mountains and Seas merged, but did not disappear. Thus, Mountains and Seas became enraged. For Li Fan, the troublemaker, they finally revealed their sharp claws. For Mountains and Seas, countless cycles of reincarnation were but an instant. They did not care at all. But Li Fan actually shattered the script they had set. Therefore, Li Fan must die. Thus… Starlight spread across the Mountains and Seas, Saints drew their swords, and the Mountains and Seas regarded Li Fan as a mortal enemy who had destroyed their clan. At this moment, Li Fan truly understood why he had shed that tear then. It was not despair. But utter desolation. He no longer resisted, allowing what he had once protected to pierce his body. But fortunately, at the crucial moment, he changed his mind. And thus, the current Li Fan was born. Having understood the past, Li Fan felt no great anger. What Mountains and Seas did was understandable. If it were him, he would do the same. However… "What you can do, I can naturally do as well." Li Fan looked calmly at the scene before him. Mountains and Seas, the void realm, and the Star. He suddenly thought again. Even Mountains and Seas, after devouring the True God's corpse, could foresee their own demise. Could the fallen True God, when setting up the True God's Finger, truly not have anticipated the strategy of Mountains and Seas' golden cicada shedding its shell to escape? "Unless…" "An outsider arrives to break Mountains and Seas' plan." "This is the reason for reaching this point." In Li Fan's mind, a scene from long ago suddenly appeared. It was his life before transcending. Parents were present, children were complete. "Screw you!" "All of you, die!"

Chapter 1758: Stars Falling to the Mortal World

With Li Fan recalling most of his past memories, some long-standing doubts were finally resolved.

Since learning of the existence of his "past self," Li Fan had always been unable to understand how his true first self managed to cultivate successfully in the extremely perilous Xuanhuang Realm.

Li Fan had personally experienced it and naturally knew what a harsh path it was.

For a mere mortal, let alone cultivation, even surviving was an almost impossible feat.

Li Fan could only reach his current position step by step through "True Return," the countless reincarnation experiences of his past self, and the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood.

How could his initial self in the first life go so far?

If it were merely "extraordinary talent," the explanation would be too far-fetched.

Great Xuan, Xuanhuang, the Utter Darkness Star Sea, the High Wall.

Countless killing intents, hidden traps.

Without foreknowledge, even a cultivator with the highest talent would likely find it difficult to navigate the situation.

His first life ended in death, so how could he later encounter the Sage of Mountains and Seas' End and comprehend the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood?

"But if I were an outsider caught by a fallen True God to break the deadlock, then everything would be explainable."

"A True God's severed finger could rewrite and distort the will of Mountains and Seas, and dim the light of the Lone Star. Protecting a mortal to smoothly grow to the Saint realm would naturally be as easy as flipping a hand."

Looking at the words "Divine Blessing" on the True Return panel, before "The Pacifist Change" and "Illusion is True," Li Fan suddenly realized.

It turned out that nothing was exaggerated.

Divine Blessing was indeed divine blessing.

"With the True God's protection, coupled with my past self's supreme talent. Not only did it break the script written by Mountains and Seas, but it also grasped the method to indefinitely postpone the day Mountains and Seas become gods."

"But as I said before, a moment's delay can be achieved, but a lifetime's escape is difficult."

"Mountains and Seas fade, the Lone Star ascends to godhood. If this script is not changed, the final outcome will remain the same."

"Damn it!"

Li Fan's anger was naturally not because he lost his past parents and children.

In his past life as the Grand Tutor of the Great Xuan Realm, surrounded by wives and concubines and numerous children, he might have still enjoyed and cared about so-called familial affection.

But now, Li Fan grasped the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, personally burying and annihilating countless lives, and then restoring them with a single thought. In his view, his former parents and children were no different from other so-called beings.

As long as he wished, he could create his remembered relatives at any time.

When truth becomes falsehood, falsehood also becomes truth.

Truth and falsehood are indistinguishable.

The reason Li Fan was enraged was still because of himself.

It could only be because of himself.

No matter what, the "Li Fan" of the past was also Li Fan.

He was inexplicably dragged into working by a fallen True God.

Initially an outsider to the play, he was unknowingly drawn too deeply into it.

After struggling with all his might through countless reincarnations, he finally discovered that all his actions were a joke.

The past Li Fan was utterly dejected.

But the current Li Fan could only feel an irrepressible ferocity rising in his heart.

What of True Gods?

Did they ask for my opinion before bringing me here?

"What you couldn't do, I will do. The revenge you couldn't exact, I will exact."

"Mountains and Seas, the Star, the Gods..."

"Not a single one will escape!"

A fierce glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes, and boundless killing intent spread.

This killing intent was so strong that even the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood could not suppress it for the moment.

The True God's Finger, the dim starlight, and the divergence of Mountains and Seas all seemed to sense it at this moment.

Li Fan felt as if countless eyes were looking at him in unison.

He instantly calmed down.

The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood once again heavily concealed him.

Ferocity is only instinct, but caution is also instinct.

Although he made a vow of killing in a moment of impulsiveness,

Li Fan himself knew that with his current strength, self-preservation was sufficient. To kill gods...

He was far from qualified.

He used to think that as long as he comprehended the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood to a certain extent, everything would naturally be resolved. But all he knew now told him that this might not be the case.

"The past self could break the True God's script, and the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood had reached its peak. Yet, facing the descent of the New God at the end of the script, he was still helpless."

"The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood only reversed its existence to a time before its appearance and could not completely sever the possibility of the New God's descent."

"Killing gods..."

Li Fan thought of that question again.

Why did that True God fall?

He could foresee his own future, even seeing the method of breaking the deadlock with Mountains and Seas shedding its shell like a golden cicada, and bringing in an outsider to break the deadlock.

Yet, he could not avoid falling himself?

"If one can kill an old god, one can kill a new god. If the cause of the True God's death is found..."

Li Fan looked again at the True God's Finger standing in the Void Realm.

Suppressing the starlight seemed to be an instinctive act after being stimulated.

At this moment, the starlight dimmed, gradually disappearing. The True God's Finger then resumed its original mission.

Mountains and Seas are boundless!

The True God's Finger pierced into the separation of Mountains and Seas like a meteor.

Mountains and Seas, which had just recently completed their separation, seemed to be repeating their past fate.

Just then, two figures flew out from the mountains above and the infinite sea respectively, blocking the rapidly descending True God's Finger.

Li Fan naturally recognized these two figures with extreme familiarity.

"Lian Shan, Gui Hai?" Li Fan's pupils contracted as he observed from afar.

The appearance of the two sages had undergone earth-shattering changes compared to before.

Sage Lian Shan's appearance was gone. He only vaguely maintained a human form, but his face was covered with billions of inscriptions, each trace recording a civilization that had once existed in Mountains and Seas.

As for Sage Gui Hai, he seemed to be rooted in the infinite possibilities within the Infinite Sea. Billions of tentacles served as support, sending Gui Hai out of Mountains and Seas.

Lian Shan and Gui Hai, with expressionless faces and firm determination, blocked the rapidly descending True God's Finger.

Although the Three Saints were powerful, if Li Fan thought they could block the True God's Finger, he would never believe it.

But things developed beyond Li Fan's expectations.

A ray of light leaped out from Lian Shan and Gui Hai respectively.

Then, a final wisp of light came from Mountains and Seas itself.

The three lights merged, and a Ruyi Scepter instantly took shape!

"Ruyi Heart?"

The moment Li Fan saw this Ruyi Scepter, its name naturally appeared in his mind.

At the same time, he understood that it was this item that had been continuously searching for him in the Void Realm!

"It is indeed from the Three Saints."

"Using the Eye of God to counter the True God's Finger?" Li Fan thought at that moment.

When the Ruyi Heart appeared, it caused the same commotion as before.

The Void Realm fell into immense turmoil, with ripples uncontrollable. For a time, it even abandoned its mission of devouring Mountains and Seas and surged madly towards the Ruyi Heart.

And this time, Lian Shan and Gui Hai did not put away the Ruyi Scepter in time.

They simply let it lie in the center of the vortex of the storm.

Li Fan even faintly discerned that the two Saints seemed to be desperately manipulating the Ruyi Heart, making it be swallowed by the Void Realm.

"Mountains and Seas chose to turn into a Lone Star to break the deadlock."

"But at the same time, to deceive the True God's Finger, they had to act thoroughly. On the day the grand play began, Mountains and Seas would no longer be Mountains and Seas, but the Lone Star. Their identities would be completely transformed."

"The beings in the world depend on Mountains and Seas, merely as actors to complete the script. And the Void Realm's Annihilation is a prop to advance the plot."

"Because this play was so realistic, Mountains and Seas did not know their identity as actors. Therefore, under the erosion of Annihilation, they would still instinctively awaken their will to survive."

"Only when the script is broken and the performance stops will Mountains and Seas know their true identities. This is why Mountains and Seas betrayed me after defeating the Annihilation in the past."

"And now..."

Li Fan raised his head calmly and looked.

Starlight descended, blocked by the True God's Finger.

Mountains and Seas were about to merge again, continuing according to the predetermined script.

Although Li Fan had interfered and caused many variables,

it ultimately did not affect the outcome.

"Still within the script, so it means Mountains and Seas do not know their true identities."

Li Fan's eyes narrowed, and he concentrated his gaze towards the center where the Annihilation gathered, the location of the Ruyi Heart.

In this life, Mountains and Seas underwent an unprecedented process of merging, separating, and merging again.

The True God's Finger moved twice, evolving into a scene Li Fan had never encountered before.

The Annihilation surged like waves, constantly washing and eroding the Ruyi Heart.

The influence of the Ruyi Scepter gradually dimmed, and with it, in the dark and silent Void Realm, a thought seemed to be rapidly awakening.

The entire Void Realm came alive!

"It seems I only guessed half of it before."

"The Void Realm gains the Ruyi Heart and will indeed undergo transformation. Thus, the Void Realm's master's desire for it, even surpasses the mission of devouring Mountains and Seas."

"But the change is not further advancement, directly ascending to godhood. It is..."

"The Void Realm, as a tool to advance the plot, awakening, or rather, restoring its original consciousness!"

From the beginning of Mountains and Seas, the Void Realm had always been dark and silent. Now, it was no longer so.

The corrosive and destructive power originating from the Annihilation also gradually subsided.

If the Void Realm's Annihilation was an infinite army before, then now, billions of soldiers had returned to one person.

A distorted figure quietly appeared.

Looking at Mountains and Seas, a trace of hatred flashed in its eyes. But in the end, it still made a move, blocking the descending True God's Finger!

To be precise, it was delaying.

The True God's Finger was irresistible, but at this moment, it seemed to be trapped in a quagmire of infinite Annihilation.

Light continuously flashed, but it could not escape the scope of the Void Realm.

"He is..."

Li Fan felt a sense of familiarity from this figure.

It all stemmed from extreme anger and hatred towards the Lone Star.

"The Void Realm's Annihilation is a tool created by Mountains and Seas to advance the plot."

"But where did this tool come from..."

"After the division, besides Mountains and Seas, there should be nothing else in the world."

After temporarily blocking the True God's Finger, the figure of the Void Realm no longer paid attention to Mountains and Seas.

It then proudly flew towards the heavens.

Beyond the realm, the dim Lone Star!

Infinite ripples erupted from the figure of the Void Realm.

Each ripple was like a sharp blade, mercilessly tearing apart the fabric of reality and drama.

Layer after layer of dark curtains were being unveiled under this violent impact.

The originally dim starlight actually became brighter again.

"He is..."

"Pulling the Star into the script?"

Li Fan was overjoyed to have a potential ally with the same stance appear out of nowhere.

But he still chose to wait and see.

After all, the identity of the Void Realm figure was still unclear, and its appearance was extremely bizarre.

As the starlight beneath the heavens became brighter and brighter.

The True God's Finger, trapped in the Void Realm, also felt the presence of starlight again.

The target shifted from Mountains and Seas, directly towards the hidden Lone Star.

Li Fan finally understood: "If one hides outside the script, one might be able to deceive the True God's Finger. But if one enters the script, it is difficult to escape the True God's Finger's discernment!"

The figure of the Void Realm, spewing ripples, guided the starlight.

Unlike ordinary creatures that mutated upon contact with starlight, it became even more profound.

But it did not accept the starlight for its own use.

Instead, it guided it into the existing Mountains and Seas!

The streaks of starlight were not as domineering as the true descent of the Lone Star. Instead, they were more like the light scattered when Mountains and Seas defeated Annihilation in the past.

Witnessing such a familiar scene, Li Fan was instantly touched: "This means the script is broken, and the Lone Star has entered the game!"

With a single thought, the world changed.

A strange change occurred in Mountains and Seas as the starlight continued to be applied.

The figure of the Void Realm suffered the same fate as Li Fan in the past.

Starlight erosion, Mountains and Seas repeated.

Li Fan vaguely felt immense anger from the roaring mountains and seas and the blooming starlight.

"You know how to get angry too?"

Li Fan felt a sense of schadenfreude.

Compared to the past Li Fan, the figure of the Void Realm seemed to have foreseen the changes in its surroundings.

Especially the betrayal of Mountains and Seas.

Without mercy, it transformed into an endless surging tide, surrounding Mountains and Seas.

Devouring it as if venting.

As a tool used to devour Mountains and Seas, the strength of the Void Realm was already superior to Mountains and Seas.

And now, with the Ruyi Heart, it had become even more "complete." With its full power unleashed, the Void Realm was no longer something Mountains and Seas could resist.

Flowers wilted, all turning into nourishment for the figure of the Void Realm.

Li Fan looked at the figure standing in the desolate Mountains and Seas, the sense of familiarity growing stronger.

It was no longer due to hatred of the Lone Star, but...

It felt like déjà vu.

"Sun, Piao, Miao."

A strange light flashed in Li Fan's eyes, and he said, enunciating each word.

In reality, he was not entirely certain, but as the Void Realm figure intensified its devouring of Mountains and Seas, the figure became even more distinct.

Li Fan's premonition grew stronger.

"It's actually him? How is this possible?"

Li Fan suddenly thought of the previous question.

Mountains and Seas foresaw their own future and deduced the method of breaking the deadlock by shedding their shell like a golden cicada. They needed to create a tool to advance the plot.

But at that time, Mountains and Seas had just split.

Besides the devoured God and Mountains and Seas, there was nothing else in the world.

Where did the tool come from?

It couldn't be that they drew upon their own origin power to create a world-destroying tool, could it?

"No. At the beginning of Mountains and Seas' split, there were other beings."

"It was Sun Piaomiao who wrote the prophecy of Mountains and Seas!"

The prophecy of Mountains and Seas meticulously described various aspects of Mountains and Seas.

At the beginning of the notes, Mountains and Seas had not yet merged.

At the end of the notes, Mountains and Seas were nowhere to be seen, and under the Lone Star hanging high like the solitary eye of a god above Mountains and Seas, they stood atop Mountains and Seas.

"He who can resist Mountains and Seas before merging can also resist them after splitting. Time travelers would never simply stop progressing."

"And the last chapter of the notes..."

Li Fan suddenly thought of a question.

It was precisely because he had seen Sun Piaomiao's notes in the past, and seen the mention of the [Star] therein, that he subconsciously referred to the power transformed by Mountains and Seas as the Star.

In fact, it was merely a pure and absolute, domineering power that did not allow for any other elements.

The god that Mountains and Seas transformed into was the Star.

When the True God returned...

It was also the Star.

Li Fan suddenly froze.

"So, the last chapter of Sun Piaomiao's notes did not refer to events happening in the current Mountains and Seas. It referred to Mountains and Seas' own outcome seen through infinite deductions."

"Able to see the inner thoughts of Mountains and Seas..."

Li Fan seemed to see Mountains and Seas, who were struggling to find a tool to create a world-destroying device after splitting, suddenly discovering Sun Piaomiao, who was peeking into their inner thoughts at the beginning of their split.

Chapter 1759: Watch the True God Resurrect

Journeying upstream against the flow of Mountains and Seas, each step arduous, Li Fan arrived at the moment of their divine severance. He could now perceive the inner workings of Mountains and Seas.

Sun Piaomiao's power was undoubtedly immense.

Yet, ultimately, he could not contend with the most potent Mountains and Seas, fresh from their feast on the True God. His discovery was inevitable, and his fate clear.

Thus, Sun Piaomiao became a tool for Mountains and Seas to break their deadlock.

From behind the scenes of the Void Realm, he led the infinite Dao Annihilation, ultimately reducing Mountains and Seas to a Lone Star.

"Perhaps only Mountains and Seas themselves, with their intimate knowledge, could create the 'Dao Annihilation'."

"In reality, even without the Void Realm's Dao Annihilation, the True God's Finger alone would have inevitably forced Mountains and Seas to merge. However, given Mountains and Seas' initial scale, complete dissolution would have taken far too long. It was too long for Mountains and Seas to wait, fearing unforeseen changes."

"Hence, the calamity of the Void Realm's Dao Annihilation arose."

Witnessing Sun Piaomiao's relentless devouring of Mountains and Seas, Li Fan's mind raced with deductions.

"The 'Heart' was not what I thought of as the 'Eye of God,' but rather a fragment stripped from Mountains and Seas by Sun Piaomiao. After this part was lost, Sun Piaomiao was left with only a solitary will, obediently executing the Dao Annihilation's invasion plan."

"After all, Sun Piaomiao's power was already masterful. If he were to gain the status of the 'Void Realm Master'..."

"Even Mountains and Seas would likely have to show some deference."

"The scene before us is the best proof!"

Entangled vortexes of Dao Annihilation intertwined, completely burying and obscuring Mountains and Seas within.

Sun Piaomiao stood atop the great torrent.

Above him, the light intensified, countless starlight ascending.

Pulled forcefully into the script by Sun Piaomiao, Mountains and Seas were no longer untouchable.

Starlight rained down like sharp myriad swords, piercing downwards.

Sun Piaomiao, however, did not dodge. His face contorted with a ferocious madness.

While being pierced by countless starlight, he used his own body as a bridge, sending the True God's Finger into the continuous starlight of the heavens.

Mountains and Seas could deceive all beings in the world, perhaps even themselves.

Outside the script, they might have deceived the True God's Finger.

But now, having both fallen to the mortal realm, they could not escape the suppression of the True God's Finger.

Just as Mountains and Seas had predicted countless years ago.

In the endless brilliance, countless overlapping shadows seemed to exist.

A peculiar light gradually faded.

It was replaced by the image of Mountains and Seas merging, colliding, and shattering.

Endless continuous mountains, endlessly vast oceans.

The form of Mountains and Seas descended and manifested in the Void Realm.

There was only one true Mountains and Seas in the world.

As the true Mountains and Seas appeared, the fabricated Mountains and Seas instantly vanished, escaping the heavy encirclement of Dao Annihilation.

They merged with their lost main bodies, becoming one.

The momentum of Mountains and Seas surged, as if returning to their peak state after their divine severance. Amidst the roars of mountains and seas, they temporarily repelled the torrent of Dao Annihilation.

But…

This prosperity was merely an illusion.

The moment they returned to their original form, they began their fated "merger" once more.

Even after evading for countless ages, what was destined to come would eventually arrive.

Their end was predetermined annihilation.

This time, it was no longer a rehearsal of a script, but a true destruction that was about to befall Mountains and Seas.

Sun Piaomiao, the Void Realm Master, witnessed all this. As if his great revenge was achieved, he let out a mad, unrestrained laugh.

Then, without any pause, the Dao Annihilation army, obeying the supreme command, continued to swarm and devour.

Returning from behind the scenes to the forefront, although Mountains and Seas' plan had been thwarted, they were in their most powerful state.

And Sun Piaomiao, having pulled the Star into the mortal realm and consumed more than half of Mountains and Seas, was also in his most triumphant moment.

Both harbored irreconcilable grudges. The two clashed, seeking the other's death!

Compared to the scenes of Dao Annihilation and Mountains and Seas battling that Li Fan had witnessed in countless reincarnations, the battlefield now was even more magnificent and intense.

Every clash was comparable to the previous siege and blockade of Mountains and Seas' vital meridians by the Void Realm.

Both poured all their strength, seeking a swift victory, vowing to kill the enemy before them!

For Mountains and Seas, Sun Piaomiao, their mere tool, had not only betrayed them but also ruined their plan for godhood. He deserved to die.

For Sun Piaomiao, he, originally a benevolent physician saving lives, was forced to commit acts of mass destruction. Each act of devouring was no less than a torture. The calamity of Mountains and Seas, the script of billions of years, he was truly trapped in an infinite hell. This hatred was truly irreconcilable!

When enemies meet, their eyes are filled with fury.

Mountains and Seas and Dao Annihilation, disregarding their own consumption and future consequences.

Only seeking the death of the other!

*Boom boom boom!*

Mountains and Seas sank and fell into Dao Annihilation, causing heavy tremors and ripples.

Light and shadow currents roamed, Mountains and Seas transformed from void to substance, dispelling the boundless darkness.

It was as if the billions of years of conflict between Mountains and Seas and Dao Annihilation were compressed into a few short days.

Every moment's clash and fluctuation was incredibly violent.

Li Fan, concealed within the True Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, felt as if he were under a waterfall thousands of feet high, in a pool below. The sound of ten thousand giant drums striking simultaneously reverberated, echoing with a low hum. Each ripple was like a surging giant wave, possessing the power to overturn the world.

In such a terrifying battlefield, Li Fan's protective cloak of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood seemed like a thin straw cloak in a fierce storm, at risk of being blown away at any moment.

With Li Fan's current strength, without the protection of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, his fate would be instant death.

But he did not hastily revert to truth.

Firstly, during the most dangerous moments of the conflict, if he were to hastily revert to truth, it would undoubtedly attract the attention of both Mountains and Seas and Sun Piaomiao, increasing the risks.

Secondly…

Li Fan still wanted to witness the return of the fallen True God!

"Despite the intense fighting, it's merely a conflict between caged beasts."

"Regardless of who wins or loses, the final outcome remains the same."

"Since Mountains and Seas' plan to break the deadlock has failed, what awaits them now is the fate of returning to the True God."

"The increasingly frenzied attacks only indicate their helplessness."

Thinking this, Li Fan no longer felt the terrifying nature of the Void Realm's machinations.

This battle seemed to have no end.

However, during this process, Li Fan could keenly sense that the scale of Dao Annihilation and Mountains and Seas was constantly shrinking.

And above them…

Where Mountains and Seas had previously been detached and hidden, a terrifying existence seemed to be awakening.

The fierce battle lasted for an unknown duration, but ultimately, Mountains and Seas' foundation proved superior.

Driven by the impending fate of returning to godhood, the true Mountains and Seas unleashed numerous divine abilities that Li Fan had never witnessed before.

Pure imagery of Mountains and Seas, mountains supporting their might, seas signifying infinite expanse.

Even amidst their merging, numerous creations emerged.

A magnificent, indescribable mountain range rose from the sea, seemingly possessing the sharpness to suppress infinity.

Ocean tides surged, continuously rising, reaching upwards.

…

It could be seen that to cope with the impending return of the True God, Mountains and Seas had exhausted all possibilities and derived corresponding strategies, unleashing all their means.

Although he had experienced a segment of Mountains and Seas' life in reverse, and witnessed the process of Mountains and Seas' existence from beginning to end as the Void Realm Master,

Sun Piaomiao was gradually losing ground amidst the infinite transformations of the newly evolved Mountains and Seas.

Finally, he vanished, consumed by the infinite images of Mountains and Seas.

All remnants were destroyed. The victors, the Saints, should have been ecstatic.

But in reality, Li Fan could sense a trace of fear from the current Mountains and Seas.

When Sun Piaomiao was present, Mountains and Seas could still suppress their inner fear through endless combat.

But now, with their only enemy gone,

Mountains and Seas had to face the fallen True God.

Just as they had done before, Mountains and Seas still refused to give up, attempting various methods of salvation.

Trying to prevent their fated merger.

But now, Mountains and Seas were not the same as their initial separated state.

Having undergone several instances of devouring, they were now purely Mountains and Seas.

There were no other beings, no scapegoats.

Mountains and Seas ultimately could not escape their own predetermined fate.

This time, it was not a rehearsal, but the destruction that was truly about to befall Mountains and Seas.

Sun Piaomiao, the Void Realm Master, witnessed all this. As if his great revenge was fulfilled, he let out a mad, unrestrained laugh.

Then, without any pause, the Dao Annihilation army, obeying the supreme command, continued to swarm and devour.

Returning from behind the scenes to the forefront, although Mountains and Seas' plan had been thwarted, they were in their most powerful state.

And Sun Piaomiao, having pulled the Star into the mortal realm and consumed more than half of Mountains and Seas, was also in his most triumphant moment.

Both harbored irreconcilable grudges. The two clashed, seeking the other's death!

Compared to the scenes of Dao Annihilation and Mountains and Seas battling that Li Fan had witnessed in countless reincarnations, the battlefield now was even more magnificent and intense.

Every clash was comparable to the previous siege and blockade of Mountains and Seas' vital meridians by the Void Realm.

Both poured all their strength, seeking a swift victory, vowing to kill the enemy before them!

For Mountains and Seas, Sun Piaomiao, their mere tool, had not only betrayed them but also ruined their plan for godhood. He deserved to die.

For Sun Piaomiao, he, originally a benevolent physician saving lives, was forced to commit acts of mass destruction. Each act of devouring was no less than a torture. The calamity of Mountains and Seas, the script of billions of years, he was truly trapped in an infinite hell. This hatred was truly irreconcilable!

When enemies meet, their eyes are filled with fury.

Mountains and Seas and Dao Annihilation, disregarding their own consumption and future consequences.

Only seeking the death of the other!

*Boom boom boom!*

Mountains and Seas sank and fell into Dao Annihilation, causing heavy tremors and ripples.

Light and shadow currents roamed, Mountains and Seas transformed from void to substance, dispelling the boundless darkness.

It was as if the billions of years of conflict between Mountains and Seas and Dao Annihilation were compressed into a few short days.

Every moment's clash and fluctuation was incredibly violent.

Li Fan, concealed within the True Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, felt as if he were under a waterfall thousands of feet high, in a pool below. The sound of ten thousand giant drums striking simultaneously reverberated, echoing with a low hum. Each ripple was like a surging giant wave, possessing the power to overturn the world.

In such a terrifying battlefield, Li Fan's protective cloak of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood seemed like a thin straw cloak in a fierce storm, at risk of being blown away at any moment.

With Li Fan's current strength, without the protection of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, his fate would be instant death.

But he did not hastily revert to truth.

Firstly, during the most dangerous moments of the conflict, if he were to hastily revert to truth, it would undoubtedly attract the attention of both Mountains and Seas and Sun Piaomiao, increasing the risks.

Secondly…

Li Fan still wanted to witness the return of the fallen True God!

"The conflict, although fierce, is merely a fight between caged beasts."

"Regardless of who wins or loses, the final outcome remains the same."

"Since Mountains and Seas' plan to break the deadlock has failed, what awaits them now is the fate of returning to the True God."

"The increasingly frenzied attacks only indicate their helplessness."

Thinking this, Li Fan no longer felt the terrifying nature of the Void Realm's machinations.

This battle seemed to have no end.

However, during this process, Li Fan could keenly sense that the scale of Dao Annihilation and Mountains and Seas was constantly shrinking.

And above them…

Where Mountains and Seas had previously been detached and hidden, a terrifying existence seemed to be awakening.

The fierce battle lasted for an unknown duration, but ultimately, Mountains and Seas' foundation proved superior.

Driven by the impending fate of returning to godhood, the true Mountains and Seas unleashed numerous divine abilities that Li Fan had never witnessed before.

Pure imagery of Mountains and Seas, mountains supporting their might, seas signifying infinite expanse.

Even amidst their merging, numerous creations emerged.

A magnificent, indescribable mountain range rose from the sea, seemingly possessing the sharpness to suppress infinity.

Ocean tides surged, continuously rising, reaching upwards.

…

It could be seen that to cope with the impending return of the True God, Mountains and Seas had exhausted all possibilities and derived corresponding strategies, unleashing all their means.

Although he had experienced a segment of Mountains and Seas' life in reverse, and witnessed the process of Mountains and Seas' existence from beginning to end as the Void Realm Master,

Sun Piaomiao was gradually losing ground amidst the infinite transformations of the newly evolved Mountains and Seas.

Finally, he vanished, consumed by the infinite images of Mountains and Seas.

All remnants were destroyed. The victors, the Saints, should have been ecstatic.

But in reality, Li Fan could sense a trace of fear from the current Mountains and Seas.

When Sun Piaomiao was present, Mountains and Seas could still suppress their inner fear through endless combat.

Chapter 1760: The Shadows of the Gods

"In my previous life, faced with the imminent descent of the True God, I lost everything except for the [Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood]."

"However…"

"It's not a big problem."

Li Fan looked at the True Return panel. Like the first time he opened it, the characters did not all appear at once, but popped out one by one. They appeared and then disintegrated, all the complex content disappearing, leaving only a few lines of text.

Name: Li Fan.

Dao Paths: Truth, Falsehood.

Great Dao Return:

...

Under the Dao Paths, the words Truth and Falsehood flickered unsternly, as if these two words alone encompassed all laws and all things in the world. The Great Dao Return Hall, which had initially taken shape, was now empty. All the Daos previously captured, such as the First Profound牝ility and the Second Universe Cycle, had vanished. At the end of his previous life, in order to verify the origin of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, Li Fan had held on until the very last moment. The divine power devoured all things. Even True Return was dismembered and separated. The functions of the various Daos that once originated from the Saints, as well as the various Daos in the Great Dao Return Hall, were all swallowed by the resurrecting True God. True Return now consisted only of Li Fan and the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. However, for the current Li Fan, possessing Truth and Falsehood meant possessing everything. All else was unimportant.

"Falsehood is Truth!"

Li Fan stared at the flickering characters before him, recalling the two solitary beams of light that had enveloped him at the end of his previous life, and his understanding of the various Daos in the Great Dao Return Hall. With a thought, he conjured existence from nothingness. Lines of colorful characters were born in the void, written out of thin air. The First Profound牝ility, the Second Universe Cycle… As well as the Daos of the Saints on the other shore, all were listed. The Great Dao Hall, previously blank, instantly became filled with myriad Daos, shining brightly. It was no different from what Li Fan had possessed before. However, it did not exceed the original limit of existence.

Li Fan then contemplated the [Dao One Mountains and Seas Map]. Unfortunately, amidst the churning clouds of the Dao One, although the Mountains and Seas Map had generally taken shape, it could not perfectly replicate the strongest state of the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet. Seated within the Mountains and Seas Map was the True God's Finger, even more ethereal and indistinct than before. If one did not observe closely, its existence would be hard to detect.

"The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood is built upon my understanding of all things. Through continuous reincarnation, my mastery of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas is sufficient to manifest it with a single thought."

"But…"

"The True God's Finger is different."

The scene of the True God's imminent resurrection, filled with starlight, resurfaced in Li Fan's mind. "Even after witnessing the divine, it is difficult to comprehend the divine."

"With my reincarnated experiences, deciphering the divine is still far from sufficient."

"But perhaps my past self could."

With a thought, the True Return inheritance option, which had been suppressed for a long time, finally appeared. It skipped all previous options and went straight to the last line. A completely new option that had never appeared before.

"[The Pantheon]."

Li Fan stared intently at these three words but hesitated to choose. For some unknown reason, a chilling sensation arose, unceasingly.

"The Pantheon. What does this mean?"

Li Fan already knew that True Return was the sum of his past countless reincarnation memories, experiences, the Daos of the Saints, and the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood.

"[The Pantheon] represents my past self's insights after witnessing the resurrecting True God. But why is it called the Pantheon?"

Li Fan couldn't help but recall the legends of the Creator God he had heard before. "The powerful Creator God defeated his peers and extracted their power to evolve all beings in the world…"

"The only source of this record comes from Sun Piao Miao's notes."

"The Prophecy of Mountains and Seas, and other records, all matched the Mountains and Seas I observed. Only this one concerning the Creator God remains confusing."

Li Fan's expression was uncertain, and he did not choose the inheritance directly. Instead, after cultivating back to the Saint realm, at least possessing a certain degree of self-preservation, he reopened it.

As if starlight returned to the earth, a profound darkness enveloped everything, devouring it. Xuanhuang, Primordial, Mountains and Seas, all vanished. In absolute nothingness, Li Fan vaguely sensed that there seemed to be some indescribable existences around him. They were beyond Li Fan's scope of understanding and observation, thus invisible and unknowable. But he could perceive the drastic changes occurring in the darkness. Without any warning, one of the unknowable existences suddenly disappeared. As if it were suddenly devoured. Next, a second, then a third. The original "Pantheon," it seemed, was reduced to only the last remaining existence.

This scene matched what Sun Piao Miao had recorded. Li Fan suddenly had an epiphany: "Sun Piao Miao likely glimpsed this scene from Mountains and Seas' thoughts at the beginning of their fragmentation and creation, hence writing the prophecy of the Creator God slaying other gods."

"But…"

Li Fan frowned slightly, feeling something was amiss. "At this time, Mountains and Seas did not exist. How could Mountains and Seas know of this scene?"

The boundless darkness did not recede. It continuously surrounded Li Fan. Li Fan suppressed all doubts in his heart, waiting for the next development. It took longer than the time it took for all the "gods" to disappear. Suddenly, a faint light appeared, illuminating this unknowable world. It allowed Li Fan to glimpse blurry images hidden within the darkness. Multiple figures overlapped and merged into one. It was as if they were devouring, chewing, and also integrating and sublimating. The many became one, the one contained all. However, within this, disharmony was quietly brewing. Li Fan seemed to see two images attempting to break free from it. Compared to the other unknowable and invisible existences, these two figures were quite familiar.

"Mountains, Seas!"

Li Fan's heart trembled violently. At this moment, the light in the void suddenly intensified. The darkness was dispelled, and Li Fan returned to reality.

Compared to observing the Outline of Mountains and Seas Changes and the Starfall Rhythm Law, this so-called "[The Pantheon]" did not bring any special impact. It was as if he had experienced a dream, and upon exiting it, Li Fan quickly emerged from its influence.

"This does not mean that the True God is weaker than Mountains and Seas or the Star."

"Rather…"

"The experience and memories of my past self have finally reached their limit in this scenario. His insights and my insights are essentially the same and cannot generate anything more meaningful. Only such inexplicable images can be produced."

"The legacy of my past self has finally been exhausted."

Li Fan did not find this day unexpected. In fact, he had already achieved what his past self could not: he understood the truth of Mountains and Seas and the Star, and witnessed the scene of the resurrecting True God's imminent descent.

"The path ahead must be walked by myself."

The moment this thought arose in Li Fan's mind, another version of himself seemed to appear before his eyes. He smiled faintly, then his form completely shattered, turning into countless rays of starlight that surged towards Li Fan.

All his past memories, like a surging flood, all rushed towards Li Fan. If before he could only partially review them, now it was a complete inheritance. After sitting in meditation for a long time, Li Fan finally digested all the memories of his past self. In addition to the countless reincarnation experiences, there were also insights into the various Great Daos of Mountains and Seas.

"This is the foundation for the operation of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, the fundamental reason why True Return can be achieved."

Although these were Li Fan's own memories and insights, Li Fan now felt a sense of disconnect during the inheritance. "My past self was me, and yet not me."

"The Li Fan of the past truly perished. Only to such an extent of severance could a completely different possibility of breaking the deadlock be born."

Li Fan's heart was enlightened. Although he could not directly convert all the divine abilities and cultivation of his past self, such a gift was equivalent to a direct enlightenment. Li Fan's understanding of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas and the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood increased exponentially with every passing moment. From another perspective, it was as if Li Fan and True Return were gradually merging. They would gradually become indistinguishable.

"The day the fusion is complete will be the day True Return perishes."

"But it can also be said that True Return has not perished."

"Because I am True Return, and True Return is me."

Li Fan's heart was utterly calm, and he looked up towards the beginning of Mountains and Seas. "The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is merely a means of self-preservation. To truly break the deadlock, one must still seek a method to slay gods."

"The [Pantheon] I glimpsed was too vague. At the time of Mountains and Seas' fragmentation, there should have been more clues."

"Let's proceed according to the original plan, moving against the current towards the beginning of Mountains and Seas."

"Billions of years of time, even with my current cultivation, it is an extremely long journey. Let's take it slowly."

"By the time I arrive…"

"Perhaps the fusion and absorption of True Return will be largely complete."

Li Fan's thoughts gradually flowed, and his form transformed into a thread, disappearing into the void realm. The void realm was vast, fraught not only with the danger of Dao Annihilation but also the peril of distinguishing past from present. This was the greatest obstacle for ordinary Saints attempting to traverse against the current. Li Fan did not know how Sun Piao Miao managed to reach the beginning of Mountains and Seas step by step. But for him, traversing against the current was no longer difficult. With the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood enveloping him, Dao Annihilation could not harm him in the slightest. His past experiences and memories, countless cycles of saving the world, every corner of Mountains and Seas, and even the void realm, Li Fan had personally traversed. For others, it was a place where past and present were indistinguishable, but for Li Fan, everywhere felt deeply familiar. He walked as if strolling through a garden.

Without any hesitation, Li Fan traversed onward, ignoring the conflict between Mountains and Seas and Dao Annihilation, his only focus being the potential whereabouts of Sun Piao Miao and the couple Qiu Tianhui. He did discover traces left by Sun Piao Miao, further verifying his past traversal. However, strangely, the couple Qiu Tianhui seemed to have vanished from Mountains and Seas as if evaporated.

"Only their vital meridians remain, but their figures are nowhere to be found."

"From the end of Mountains and Seas to the beginning, what exactly are they seeking?"

As Qiu XinHui's creation, she could faintly sense the existence of Li Fan's True Return. Perhaps the couple Qiu Tianhui had also sensed it.

"The plan to reconnect Mountains and Seas… is completely useless for saving the world. They must know this."

Li Fan pondered as he traveled against the current, as if a passerby of Mountains and Seas, traversing its entirety without leaving a trace. After an unknown period, until…

With one step forward, reality seemed to spin, and the scene of towering mountains and flowing seas vanished. In an instant, he found himself in a vast, desolate world.

"Primeval Immortal Realm."

A sharp gleam flashed in Li Fan's eyes. This was the initial stage of Mountains and Seas' merger, even containing the attempts of Mountains and Seas to resist their fate. However, it was interfered with by the True God's Finger, causing the realm to be destroyed.

"Only the Saints within, who vaguely sensed something, managed to achieve temporary peace by severing their future."

"The Primeval Saints…"

"Hmph, they are all just cowards."

In his countless past cycles, Li Fan had indeed interacted with these Primeval Saints, but none could become his allies. "Unable to achieve godhood, unable to save the world, they could only hide in this realm and fight amongst themselves."

Although Li Fan disdained them, he did not underestimate them. The Primeval Immortal Realm seemed isolated from Mountains and Seas, its time stagnant. No matter how long the Saints fought amongst themselves, only those who could survive in this place possessed the potential for godhood; they only lacked an opportunity. Li Fan's previous two witnessing of different New Gods' births were the best proof.

Li Fan looked towards the sky, attempting to gaze further into the ancient past, but it was as if something was blocking his view, preventing him from seeing clearly. He tried to move forward, to go against the current, but it was like getting stuck in mud, unable to move.

"This is why, despite the gathering of Saints in the Primeval Immortal Realm, the matter of contending for godhood has been delayed for so long."

"Before the Primeval Immortal Realm was the time of Mountains and Seas' fragmentation."

"Mountains and Seas naturally would not allow their creations to interfere with them. Thus, they established this divine-mortal boundary."

"Severing space-time, cutting off karma."

Li Fan reached out, attempting to break through the divine-mortal boundary using the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood. But the moment he moved, the eyes of all the Saints in the Primeval Immortal Realm simultaneously turned towards him!

In the next instant, various divine abilities and techniques rained down like a storm.

"There are the Three Saints of Lian Shan, and an old acquaintance, [Suo]."

"Hmm, and [Hua], [Ding], [Liu]…"

Ripples of light and shadow emanated before Li Fan, blocking all harm. Although he ignored the attacks of the Saints, Li Fan felt his energy being rapidly depleted. His protective Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood also began to tremble.

Frowning slightly, Li Fan's form flickered and faded, disappearing from their sight. Although a few divine senses could still track him, Li Fan evaded their sight after several consecutive shifts.

"Firstly, the divine-mortal boundary is a restriction set by Mountains and Seas and cannot be easily broken."

"Secondly, all the Saints are eyeing him greedily. Any attempt to step forward, regardless of potential success, will be met with a united attack. The fewer opponents for godhood, the greater the chance of becoming a god."

"The opportunity for godhood has arrived. What are the conditions to break the stalemate?" Li Fan, in hiding, deduced rapidly based on his experiences in past lives of creating gods.

"The Saints have been locked in a struggle for years, forming a strange balance."

"No one can overcome the other, and no one can advance further."

"It's like a stagnant pool."

"When still, there is no change. At such times, a pebble is needed to smash into it."

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. His form flickered again, and he stealthily appeared beside [Suo]. Suo had been 'plucked' by Li Fan several times and had his name recorded in the Great Dao Return Hall. Naturally, he could not escape Li Fan's search.

Countless tentacle-like black shadows writhed and moved. The moment they sensed Li Fan, they coiled like a net, entangling him.

Chapter 1761: The Holy Spirits All Get Caught in the Net

Without any wasted words, the moment Suo sensed Li Fan, he unleashed all his divine abilities.

It was as if he had left the Primeval Immortal Realm and entered the vast net that Suo had woven for who knows how many years.

Countless thin threads and shadows intertwined horizontally and vertically. Upon them lay decaying bones, and billions of resentful souls. All wailed at the top of their lungs, surging towards Li Fan in unison. Innumerable hands reached out, seeking to drag Li Fan into their midst.

Those whose remnants survived Suo's devouring were naturally not weak. In later eons of Mountains and Seas, they might possess transcendent strength capable of crossing the Heavenly River of Annihilation. But in this Primeval Immortal Realm, they were merely dishes on the plates of the Saints.

With billions of transcendent souls charging simultaneously, even the Saints of the Primeval Immortal Realm would falter for a moment.

Li Fan, within the net, froze on the spot. Facing the attacks of countless resentful souls, he neither dodged nor resisted, seemingly having given up.

Suo, however, was not pleased but surprised.

Clearly, the prey was no longer struggling, yet he felt a sense of danger, as if he himself had been locked onto.

Suo's net's countless tendrils continued to entangle Li Fan.

But the master of the net had already silently escaped.

Li Fan did not rush to pursue. With his name recorded in the Hall of True Return, Suo and the Mountains and Seas Void Realm had nowhere to flee.

"This net is excellent; it can be used by me."

A cold light flashed in Li Fan's eyes. Where each part of the net contacted Suo's resentful souls, a face appeared.

Grinning menacingly, they, in turn, devoured them without mercy.

In an instant, the guest became the host.

Suo, who had woven the net with his lifelong efforts, instantly seemed poised to change its master.

A stream of light flashed, and wherever its hazy radiance reached, Suo's claws and teeth, all transformed into Li Fan's subordinates.

In a moment, Li Fan controlled more than half of Suo's net.

And at this moment, Suo actually returned!

“You actually know the Great Dao of [Suo]?”

“No wonder you could so easily accept the net I wove.”

Suo’s ethereal voice came from all directions, making it impossible to pinpoint his location.

Upon hearing the voice of the original master, countless resentful souls within Suo’s net first felt an instinctual fear, and then a sign of breaking free from Li Fan’s control.

“Ignorant and greedy junior! My creation, how can it be so easily stolen?”

Li Fan flipped his hand, suppressing the anomaly in the net, and squinted outwards, but Suo’s trace was already gone.

However, he keenly sensed that a crisis was imminent.

“This is…”

Li Fan, within the net, trembled violently.

A familiar feeling, from the resentful souls in the net and from Li Fan’s own heart, emerged.

It was as if they were currently within another, even larger, net!

“So that’s how it is. This net floating on the surface was merely a trap.”

Compared to the net of bait, the threads of the true net were formless and intangible.

But in an instant, they tightly bound the prey within the net.

Outside the darkness, an eye resembling a rising red sun slowly appeared.

Utterly cold, it stared at Li Fan.

Like looking at prey that was certain to be captured.

From countless directions, a pulling force came. It tightened with each passing moment, making it extremely difficult to break free.

The bait net, occupied by Li Fan, was easily torn to shreds.

And Li Fan, within the net, seemed doomed.

If Li Fan were an ordinary Saint, in such a predicament, he would indeed be in danger of perishing.

But…

Compared to the terrifying scene of the lone star descending and devouring everything, Suo’s display of power was completely lacking in deterrence.

“No matter how many nets you weave, it will be of no avail.”

“The damned must die eventually.”

Firmly ensnared by the invisible net, Li Fan’s expression remained as calm as ever.

Taking a step forward, he actually ignored all restraints of the threads and walked out of the net out of thin air.

“Trying to escape?”

Li Fan’s eyes narrowed, and he lightly stepped on the ground.
