Like ripples spreading, an identical, copied net of Suo emerged from Li Fan’s toes.

Its scale rapidly expanded, then enshrouded the original net.

Li Fan reached out with his hand, and grasping in the void, pulled.

A figure, battered and bruised, was dragged out by him.

Countless threads, like flying dragons, instantly wrapped him tightly.

“How is this possible!”

Even when captured by Li Fan, Suo was still filled with disbelief. Rack his brains as he might, he could not fathom how Li Fan had reversed the situation so swiftly.

Li Fan naturally would not explain to him.

With a slender finger, he pressed down from a distance.

The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood was instantly activated.

It was not a direct obliteration of [Suo]'s existence, but rather, while feigning it, he absorbed and comprehended [Suo]'s Dao path.

On the Hall of True Return, the characters representing Suo gradually became clearer.

And in reality, the radiance condensed on Suo’s body grew dimmer and dimmer.

The Dao paths of the Saints in the Primeval Immortal Realm were all derived from the Great Dao that stood shoulder-to-shoulder with Mountains and Seas, remnants not fully assimilated by the fragmented consciousness of Mountains and Seas.

Even with the amplification of Li Fan’s past self’s memories and experiences, it was not something that could be fully mastered in a short time.

Fortunately, this world was self-contained, and the flow of time held no significant meaning.

Suo was also deeply bound within the net, unable to move or struggle.

He could only let Li Fan absorb and comprehend him.

After an unknown period, the light-like shadow that condensed on Suo's body completely dimmed. The Primeval Saint revealed his true form before Li Fan.

A spider’s body with a human face, but its tendrils resembled human arms.

Countless tiny eyes on his body stared intently at Li Fan.

The hatred in their eyes was bone-deep.

Li Fan looked at one of Suo’s eyeballs.

It vanished silently, like a crushed flame.

As Li Fan’s gaze shifted, the eyes on Suo’s body, which had been closed, slowly diminished.

They were extinguished at a steady and resolute pace.

At first, Suo could still maintain a glare of defiance.

But when only over ninety eyeballs remained, Suo’s body trembled slightly.

He finally averted his gaze.

“Even an ant strives to survive, let alone a Saint of Mountains and Seas?”

“Bowing to me is not shameful.”

Li Fan did not mock him but said calmly.

“You have two choices. First, perish here and now. Leaving no trace in Mountains and Seas.”

“Second…”

“The spirits within the net, though they have lost their freedom, may yet have a chance to turn the tables in the future.”

“Spirits within the net?” Upon hearing Li Fan’s words, Suo first showed a slight astonishment.

Then he saw the net that had captured him suddenly reveal its true form.

Compared to the invisible net he had meticulously woven, this replica crafted by Li Fan was resplendent and dazzling, with myriad colors.

It was as if the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas were contained within, full of infinite vitality.

Suo clearly understood that this was not his illusion.

But rather, this net truly seemed to carry the weight of Mountains and Seas!

Only now did Suo comprehend the insurmountable chasm that lay between him and Li Fan.

“Although their strength is both at the Saint realm, his foundation…”

“But where did it come from?”

In the Primeval Immortal Realm, all opponents were intimately familiar with each other.

There was no one like Li Fan.

As he pondered, a sense of emptiness from all parts of his body interrupted Suo’s thoughts.

“I am willing to become a spirit within the net!” Suo said repeatedly.

The sense of oppression vanished.

A moment later, Suo only felt his vision blur as he entered a magnificent and boundless palace.

Vast and endless, its scope unknown.

Within, myriad Daos stood, walking in the high heavens.

Like bricks and tiles, they formed this ineffable palace together.

With Suo’s understanding, facing this scene, he almost felt lost.

However, driven by an instinctual urge, he flew towards his intended destination.

[Suo].

His heart was immensely calm; all previous calculations had vanished. The moment he saw the flashing characters ahead, Suo understood this was where his lifelong cultivation of the Great Dao resided.

With a thought, he drifted into it.

The moment Suo returned to his position, a light streaked from heaven to earth.

And then, he completely concealed himself.

…

Suo opened his eyes again.

It was as if what he had just experienced was merely a nightmare.

“Hmm?”

He was stunned and quickly checked his condition.

“Nothing is missing, and my Great Dao is not damaged in the slightest.”

“Could it have been a delusion?”

Suo furrowed his brow, and at that moment, he suddenly sensed a figure standing behind him.

He wanted to turn and look back but couldn't move!

Only then did Suo fully understand that what he had just experienced was not an illusion.

After such a dramatic turn of events, Suo could only reluctantly accept the fact.

“Although it seems I have recovered my full strength, my life and death are entirely in this person's hands. Every action can be controlled by him.”

Suo could not discern the specific method of control, but he instinctively understood that if he tried to break free from his restraints,

he would instantly perish.

In other words, Suo's current existence was maintained under Li Fan’s control.

If the connection of control disappeared, then Suo would also vanish into nothingness.

“This kind of method…”

Suo’s thoughts churned like a tide, but he heard Li Fan’s faint voice transmit,

“Do your best to wreak havoc in the Primeval Immortal Realm.”

Before the words even fell, Suo felt himself returned to the Primeval Immortal Realm.

The heavens and earth were still vast, but Suo was no longer the same Suo as before.

He quickly invigorated his spirits and, as per Li Fan’s instructions, began his actions.

The word “wreak havoc” seemed simple.

But when preceded by “do your best,” its meaning changed drastically.

Suo dared not delay, first targeting his decades-long plan for [The Tower].

The Dao of The Tower was “all things are ordered, with clear hierarchies.”

The Tower sat at the highest level, while all other Great Daos were below it, suppressed by it.

Suo and The Tower had always been at odds.

Years ago, when Suo was at a critical juncture of attaining Sainthood, The Tower had launched a surprise attack, attempting to suppress Suo.

Fortunately, Suo had some luck and managed to evade calamity.

However, he was also suppressed by a wisp of his own origin in The Tower.

Since then, whenever he encountered The Tower, he was unknowingly at a disadvantage, naturally restrained. But this also allowed him to faintly know of The Tower’s existence.

For many years, Suo had tried various methods and schemes against The Tower.

But he had never succeeded.

Now that he had fallen under someone else’s control, his life and death were no longer his to decide, so he might as well go all out!

Suo deliberately created the appearance of being severely injured, hoping to lure The Tower into a trap.

The Tower, by suppressing and sealing a wisp of Suo's origin, should have been able to detect Suo's severely injured state immediately.

But after surviving in the Primeval Immortal Realm for many years, all Saints were extremely cautious.

This degree of injury was not enough to make The Tower act rashly.

With great resolve, Suo directly severed one-third of his origin.

And deliberately created a massive disturbance.

A shattered net appeared in the sky of the Primeval Immortal Realm.

Suo’s voice echoed: “If there is a chance to turn things around, I will make you repay me a thousandfold!”

His tone, filled with utter hatred, was far from an act.

And the Saints clearly sensed Suo’s severe injuries.

Thus, they began to stir.

Just as Suo had deduced, The Tower was the first to attack him.

By using the sealed wisp of his origin, The Tower successfully locked onto the location of the severely injured Suo.

Threads, like heavenly pillars, descended from above.

Sealing the heavens and locking the earth, suppressing everything within.

This was the same method used to deal with Li Fan earlier. The visible Suo net was merely a trap to lure the enemy.

The real killing blow was another, unseen net that Suo had painstakingly woven for countless years.

The net covering the sky and earth, leaping out from the void, ensnared The Tower, which was penetrating the heavens and earth.

The one who was originally suppressed became a hunter with a covetous gaze.

But The Tower showed no sign of panic.

“Your petty tricks, in this magnificent world, who doesn’t know them?”

“To use this to fight, truly laughable!”

“You are best suited to hiding in the darkness forever. Once you step into the light, it's a dead end!”

The Tower's mocking voice echoed throughout the Primeval Immortal Realm.

Although Suo's net had already ensnared The Tower, The Tower’s radiance flowed, and its form suddenly became identical to the surrounding net.

As if it were already a part of Suo’s net, Suo could devour external things, but it could not devour itself.

An immeasurable suction force emanated from within The Tower, and the meticulously woven net uncontrollably fell towards The Tower.

“What The Tower took before was merely a wisp of origin. After all these years, it has researched to such an extent that it can almost pass off as real, forcibly impersonating me!”

“I have been scheming against it all along, and has it not been scheming against me as well?”

Before his consciousness faded, Suo had a moment of realization.

But towards the impending demise, Suo was unexpectedly not very fearful.

“Rather than always being controlled by others, it is better to disappear completely and be truly free.”

“As for you…”

A ferocious thought flashed in Suo’s mind.

The vast net instantly disintegrated, its form no longer intact, transforming into pure energy that erupted forth.

Darkness engulfed Suo.

…

“Hmm?”

After an unknown duration, Suo woke up again from the darkness.

“What happened? I’m still alive?”

Suo was a little stunned, not understanding why, he quickly checked his condition.

He had returned to his full strength.

“Was what just happened a delusion?”

But soon, Suo dismissed his guess.

Because at this moment, within the Primeval Immortal Realm, chaos had already begun to manifest.

Although The Tower had successfully devoured Suo, Suo's final desperate blow had also left The Tower with severe injuries.

Two Saints, one dead and one injured.

It was like the opportunity had arrived for the boundary between the divine and mortal worlds to open, and the Saints were all developing their own intentions.

“I’m dead. But how am I alive again?”

Just as Suo was puzzled, Li Fan’s voice sounded again behind him.

“Well done.”

“But it’s still far from enough.”

Chapter 1762: All Saints Break the Seal and Fight

Starlight diffused.

An aura of dominance gradually emerged, and the True God's Finger, from illusory to real, reappeared in the world!

It seemed that to the starlight, this severed finger held an attraction far beyond that of Li Fan. All brilliance that met its gaze converged towards the True God's Finger. Even the light points engulfing most of Li Fan's body were abandoned without regret, disappearing directly into the starlight.

Li Fan gradually regained control of his body but felt ill-at-ease, as if his every limb was stiff and out of sync. "After being immersed in starlight for only a moment, it feels like I've been away from the mortal world for ten thousand years."

The extreme discomfort of his body, coupled with the corrosion of his thoughts, made him sluggish. However, spurred by his survival instinct, he did not forget his perilous situation. With a thought, the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood enveloped him, bringing an unparalleled sense of peace and stability amidst the storm. The corrosive feeling was expelled, and Li Fan's thoughts and abilities returned to their normal levels. He observed the changes unfolding before him.

There should only be one True God's Finger in the world.

Thus, when the True God's Finger appeared under the starlight, the Boundless Tablet within the Mountains and Seas became turbulent. Its foundation vanished, leaving only the Dao marks of the Saints, unable to bear the destiny of the "Boundless Mountains and Seas." The Dao marks, like fragile branches, snapped inch by inch. The existing merged Mountains and Seas, at this moment, showed signs of separation!

Within the Xuanji Ring, due to the severe side effects of using "Ruyi Heart," the Three Saints closed their eyes, suppressing the Ruyi artifact once more. "Hmm?"

At this moment, Saint Lian Shan was the first to sense the anomaly in the Mountains and Seas. Lian Shan represented all civilizations and beings who had attempted to bridge mountains and seas; their strength and foundation were built upon the fusion of mountains and seas. Now that mountains and seas were showing signs of separation, he was naturally the most affected.

The mountains above, which were originally at his shoulder level, seemed to rise on their own, distancing themselves from the mortal world. Even though the Bridge of Lian Shan desperately extended, attempting to repair the rift, the speed of separation far surpassed Saint Lian Shan's ability to mend.

Hum, hum, hum…

Once the gap exceeded a certain limit, a faint cracking sound emanated from between the mountains and seas. The sound echoed and reverberated. Mortal beings, unaware, perceived nothing. But all who had achieved True Immortal status felt a premonition, as if disaster had struck, their faces contorted in terror.

Immortals stood above the mountains, connecting to the boundless sea. They possessed the supreme power of Immortals, wielding infinite divine abilities. But now, the bridge connecting the mountains above had collapsed with a bang. The countless Immortals on the bridge naturally could not escape the calamity and also plummeted downwards. Their cultivation realms and auras dropped at a visible rate. Saints, Transcendent beings, Nameless ones, True Immortals. Regardless of their realm, strength, or struggles, they could not escape. All plummeted to the mortal realm.

How could mortals, now in mortal bodies, wield infinite power? Trapped in Dao Annihilation, unable to protect themselves, they perished instantly. Seeking refuge in the Mountains and Seas, they were instead engulfed by the boundless power of the Infinite Sea, becoming a part of the vast ocean.

With the disappearance of the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet, at this moment, 99.9% of cultivators above True Immortal realm in the Mountains and Seas perished. The remaining fortunate few, though still struggling, were destined for destruction.

Because… the Mountains and Seas had awakened! Without the True God's Finger, the Mountains and Seas separated, reverting to their initial state of devouring the divine. The countless fallen cultivators within the Mountains and Seas transformed into nourishment, returning to the Mountains and Seas, allowing the once dying Mountains and Seas to regain some vitality, as if they had consumed a powerful tonic. While not returning to their peak state, they at least possessed the strength for a final desperate struggle.

More importantly, the will of the Mountains and Seas, twisted and rewritten by the True God's Finger, had returned to normal. The continuous mountain ranges stood tall and majestic. The boundless ocean reflected the myriad worlds. The two true wills representing the Mountains and Seas descended upon them.

When the Mountains and Seas merged, they intertwined, chaotic and unclear, guided only by instinct.

But now, separated into two, the mountains were solely mountains, the seas solely seas. Each independent will, upon separating from the other, became incredibly prosperous.

Thus, the Three Saints found themselves in different predicaments. Although the Three Saints were also affected by the anomaly, plummeting to the mortal realm, they survived for various reasons.

As if sensing what was about to happen, Saint Lian Shan looked at the other two and sighed, "All feasts must eventually end…" Before his words were finished, Saint Lian Shan, not as a specific figure within the Mountains and Seas, but as all the differentiated parts, transformed into streaks of light and withdrew into the mountains above.

Saint Gui Hai also responded with a soft sigh. Countless blue light points floated, surging into the boundless possibilities of the infinite sea.

As for the last, Saint Tai Yi. Countless figures seemed to evaporate, disappearing. Tai Yi, and the Great Dao of Infinite Evolution it represented, all returned to the Mountains and Seas respectively!

Mountains and Seas had once generated infinite Great Daos and countless beings, but now, all were reclaimed. Everything returned to its most primitive state! Just like at the beginning of the gods' division.

The anomaly occurring within the Mountains and Seas was already world-shattering. However, compared to the changes produced by the collision between starlight and the True God's Finger in the void, it seemed insignificant.

As if it had found the key to breaking free, infinite starlight, centered on the True God's Finger, instantly permeated the surroundings. Compared to the solitary Star that descended before, the pervasive starlight now appeared softer. At the very least, the void realm could still exist under the starlight's illumination. At the very least, Li Fan could still barely maintain the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood state and continue observing.

As the endless starlight initially manifested, Li Fan could faintly glimpse a blurry figure hidden behind the starlight for a moment. But as the starlight expanded a millionfold in an instant, Li Fan's vision was completely obscured. "Could it be my illusion?" Li Fan was filled with doubt. However, he soon had no time to ponder such questions.

The starlight spread endlessly from the depths of the void realm. As the central node of the Star's descent, the True God's Finger also seemed to feel the increasing brilliance around it, undergoing further changes.

The change was not in the True God's Finger itself, but in its "posture." It was an extremely mysterious phenomenon; despite being merely a severed finger, it could perform various actions. The "Boundless Mountains and Seas," which Li Fan had seen before, distorted the will of the Mountains and Seas, causing them to merge. Now, the finger's transformation pointed towards the starlight filling the sky.

In an instant, the brilliant starlight seemed to lose its color, transforming from dazzling brightness to a dull black and white. The entire void dimmed as a result. The starlight, no longer blazing, lost its sharpness, and its threat was greatly reduced. Looking up, Li Fan felt an intimation that, even without the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, he could now resist its influence. However, Li Fan did not rashly test it; the changes were truly beyond his expectations.

"What is happening? Why is the True God's Finger attacking the starlight?"

"The solitary Star and the True God's Finger should both be remnants left by the gods, meant to merge the Mountains and Seas through the descent of the solitary Star?"

The events unfolding before him completely contradicted Li Fan's assumptions, filling him with doubt while also subtly touching upon the truth about gods, Mountains and Seas, and the Star.

"Since their identities and motivations deviate from their actual actions, let's re-evaluate." "Among the three, Mountains and Seas are the murderers of their divine fragments and the victims." "The True God's Finger…" "The faint ancient aura upon it, coupled with its ability to rewrite the will of Mountains and Seas, thus triggering their merger, and its power to dissipate the starlight, re-sealing the solitary Star… Such might and divine abilities can only be possessed by a True God." Li Fan first confirmed this point. "Finally, the Star." "What exactly is the Star?" At the end of every cycle, the solitary Star descends, devouring everything. It was evident that the Star seemed to be a contingency plan left by the True God, meant to allow for rebirth after being fragmented by the gods. The descent of the solitary Star leads to the destruction of Mountains and Seas, the annihilation of the void realm, and the rebirth of a New God. Li Fan had always believed this. But, was this truly the case? The scene of the True God's Finger turning against the starlight shattered this assumption.

"The Star is not a god?" "Then what is the Star…?" There were no other known options. If the Star were not a god, then… The Star is Mountains and Seas. "The Star is Mountains and Seas! The Star is Mountains and Seas!"

The moment this thought arose, Li Fan's body and mind trembled. The shock of such a drastic contrast almost prevented him from maintaining the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, and revealing himself amidst the battle between the True God's Finger and the starlight. "How could this be? How is this possible?"

Li Fan forced himself to calm down. But a premonition had already arisen in his heart, making him know the conclusion of his deductions before even thinking them through. In his mind, the infinite memories of his past self, like a breached dam, could no longer be suppressed. They exploded outwards. Countless figures flickered, countless past scenes burned like firewood, ultimately converging into an overwhelming sense of unyielding resentment and boundless rage born from despair. This was the final emotion of Li Fan's past self before making a decision, and the reason for the existence of the current Li Fan.

"So that's how it is." Li Fan's expression became extremely peculiar. Gazing at the interaction before him, his cold nature acted like a stabilizing force, methodically sorting through all the resentment and anger. What his past self could not accept, Li Fan now viewed with indifference. "It's just, I feel a bit sorry for you." Li Fan let out a light sigh. With the support of his past memories, everything logically fell into place. Li Fan's heart was free of doubt.

"If the Star is not the Star, then the Star is Mountains and Seas." "Mountains and Seas devouring themselves seems absurd, but if combined with their fated merger and the properties and actions set by the True God's Finger…" "Then everything can be explained."

"When time rewound to the moments after the True God's fall and the divine fragmentation of Mountains and Seas." Li Fan's vision was suddenly filled with a bizarre scene. In the darkness, two formless, ferocious entities seemed to be silently devouring something, greedily and with enjoyment. True God vanished, and two new gods were about to be born. But… Suddenly, a sense of fear spread from the heart of Mountains and Seas. After devouring part of the True God's body, they had also gained some of the True God's abilities. Thus, they could, to some extent, foresee future events. They saw that the True God had not completely vanished after death. As if the True God's solitary eye was still coldly watching them. As long as Mountains and Seas existed, the True God's Finger would appear. Mountains and Seas gradually merged, eventually returning to nothingness. Only pure energy remained. Upon this boundless and infinite warm bed, upon the corpses of Mountains and Seas, the True God would be reborn. The True God would return again.

The remnants of the True God's body instantly became unappetizing. As newly born gods, Mountains and Seas naturally did not wish to suffer the same fate as their food. After foreseeing their own destruction, Mountains and Seas immediately deduced countless possibilities. But in all endings, there was no image of their survival. The True God's final strike before falling had annihilated all possibilities of reversal for Mountains and Seas. Mountains and Seas had no chance of winning. Just as they had newly transformed, they were about to embark on a path of destined destruction. How could these two newly born gods accept this? Even ants strive to survive, let alone divine beings? After completely devouring the True God's body, an unknown amount of time passed. Exhausting countless epochs, Mountains and Seas combined their efforts and deduced the only possible method of turning defeat into victory.

"Since Mountains and Seas are doomed to perish, then…" "Let Mountains and Seas perish themselves." "Bury themselves completely, and then, before the True God's resurrection, conceive again."

"This is your method of survival?" Li Fan's gaze seemed to pierce through the dark void, reaching the will behind it. In his mind, the scene of the solitary Star descending and devouring everything replayed.

"The existence of the True God's Finger and its activation condition is the existence of Mountains and Seas." "With the invasion of the void realm's Dao Annihilation, if Mountains and Seas cease to exist, the True God's Finger will also vanish into nothingness, disappearing without a trace." "The only opposing opponent has finally disappeared. The Star, or the reborn Mountains and Seas, will immediately descend." "I want nothing but myself. Only I will remain, only I will be born, only I will win." "So the void realm's Dao Annihilation is merely a tool for Mountains and Seas to destroy themselves." "So it was all just a meticulously crafted play." "The beings of Mountains and Seas, Lian Shan, Gui Hai, Tai Yi. Shou Qiu, Dao De. They were all merely actors in the play." "As long as they followed the script and completed their designated roles, everything would be harmonious." "The True God perishes completely, the New Gods are without worry." "The grand play concludes, the New Gods ascend." "Perfect."

"But regrettably…" Li Fan sighed. Not for any other reason, but for the lost "Li Fan" of the past. "An outsider to the play, who should not have existed." "Mountains and Seas self-destructing, in his eyes, was an incomparably terrifying catastrophe. Lives were perishing, and he wanted to save them from suffering." "Once is not enough, then a hundred times. If a hundred times is not enough, then a thousand, ten thousand times." "Countless times." "Finally, finally, finally…" "He turned the impossible into the possible, breaking the script written by Mountains and Seas." "Mountains and Seas finally won. But…" "As such, how can the script continue?"

Just as Mountains and Seas had foreseen. As long as Mountains and Seas existed, the True God's Finger would not perish. Without the void realm, without Dao Annihilation. Mountains and Seas merged, but did not disappear. Thus, Mountains and Seas became enraged. For Li Fan, the troublemaker, they finally revealed their sharp claws. For Mountains and Seas, countless cycles of reincarnation were but an instant. They did not care at all. But Li Fan actually shattered the script they had set. Therefore, Li Fan must die.

Thus… Starlight spread across the Mountains and Seas, Saints drew their swords, and the Mountains and Seas regarded Li Fan as a mortal enemy who had destroyed their clan. At this moment, Li Fan truly understood why he had shed that tear then. It was not despair. But utter desolation. He no longer resisted, allowing what he had once protected to pierce his body. But fortunately, at the crucial moment, he changed his mind. And thus, the current Li Fan was born. Having understood the past, Li Fan felt no great anger. What Mountains and Seas did was understandable. If it were him, he would do the same.

However… "What you can do, I can naturally do as well." Li Fan looked calmly at the scene before him. Mountains and Seas, the void realm, and the Star. He suddenly thought again. Even Mountains and Seas, after devouring the True God's corpse, could foresee their own demise. Could the fallen True God, when setting up the True God's Finger, truly not have anticipated the strategy of Mountains and Seas' golden cicada shedding its shell to escape? "Unless…" "An outsider arrives to break Mountains and Seas' plan." "This is the reason for reaching this point."

In Li Fan's mind, a scene from long ago suddenly appeared. It was his life before transcending. Parents were present, children were complete. "Screw you!" "All of you, die!"

Chapter 1763: The Primordial Spirit of Shan Hai Begins

Clad in the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood like a veil, Li Fan concealed himself and the net of captured spirits he bore. Nevertheless, the instant he stepped into this splintered divine realm, Li Fan sensed two gazes sweep over him. The Mountains and Seas, momentarily pausing their feast, focused their attention elsewhere after their fruitless search, turning their energy back to devouring the True God.

Li Fan held his breath, concealed. "This place seems like a boundless void, with no sight of Mountains and Seas, nor the True God," he mused. "No past, no future." Li Fan did not act rashly, choosing instead to carefully observe his current surroundings. It was as if this was a self-contained space-time. The moment Li Fan crossed the boundary between mortal and divine, he had become separated from the subsequent fate of Mountains and Seas, trapped in the present.

"The fragmentation of Mountains and Seas into divine entities was not a fleeting moment," Li Fan realized. "Given the True God's immense scale, for Mountains and Seas to devour and digest it would naturally take an exceedingly long time."

"No… that's not right." A thought struck Li Fan. He temporarily shifted his focus away from the colossal entities in the void, concentrating on the space-time itself. "This place actually has no concept of 'time's passage.' What determines its existence is the state of 'Mountains and Seas' unfinished devouring of the True God.' This means that as long as one is here, it is a moment when Mountains and Seas have not yet completed their task. When they do, they will naturally evolve into the later Mountains and Seas and the Primordial Immortal Realm, and this space-time will naturally dissipate."

"Although there is no concept of time passing, it does not mean I can stay here forever," Li Fan continued his deduction. "Entering this place means one has already become involved in the struggle for divine essence. In this conflict where one consumes the other's strength, if one does nothing and completely loses the qualification to compete, they will be expelled from this space-time." Li Fan vaguely felt as if he had landed upon the enormous corpse of the fallen True God, officially entering a gluttonous feast for divine fragments.

"From the perspective of Mountains and Seas, they are still in a state of indecision regarding their divine fragmentation. All future possibilities have yet to unfold." "But from the perspective of us who defy destiny, everything is already set in stone." "A stagnant, infinitely repeating moment of divine fragmentation…" Li Fan dimly perceived that the True God's corpse was like a cage, trapping Mountains and Seas, or any entity that dared to covet the True God's remains, within this place. "Transcending space-time, one is conceptually anchored here, becoming a prisoner participating in the divine fragmentation struggle. Meaning, no one who enters this place can truly escape."

In the complete darkness, Li Fan seemed to see the fallen True God's corpse, standing indifferently, observing all. "Though I have come here, I have no intention of competing for divine essence. I am only here to glimpse the secret of the True God's demise." "But first, I need to truly see the True God's corpse."

The existence of the True God surpassed Li Fan's current comprehension. Hence, his eyes could not see, nor his ears hear. "You shall be my eyes and ears, to fully comprehend the secrets of the True God." "If any among you achieve enlightenment, perhaps they can use divine power to tear apart this net of restraint and regain freedom." Li Fan smiled as he addressed the twenty-eight Saints within the net.

Even though he knew the probability of success was close to zero, a flicker of hope still resided deep within the Saints' hearts. Competing with Mountains and Seas for divine essence was a long-held dream of all Saints in the Primordial Immortal Realm. However, due to the boundary between the divine and mortal realms, they were all trapped within the Primordial Immortal Realm, unable to advance even half a step. Through years of exploration, the Saints had reached a consensus: only by using the body of a Saint could the limits of Mountains and Seas be broken, allowing them to enter the moment of divine fragmentation. Now, Li Fan had brought them all here through his own efforts. The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood was indeed beyond imagination.

"However, if one can gain divine might…" "The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood will also be subservient!" Since Li Fan had given them the opportunity to fully comprehend, why would they refuse? The twenty-eight Saints, at this moment, cast aside all thoughts of life and death and dedicated themselves to comprehending the dark void before them.

Those who could become Saints, especially in the Primordial Immortal Realm, were undoubtedly the most top-tier talents of Mountains and Seas. The gods and the later Mountains and Seas shared commonalities. As the Saints observed, this dark space gradually brightened. With every inch of darkness that receded, the "divine might" that Li Fan sensed intensified. Mountains and Seas raged, but for the moment, they could not subdue them.

The Mountains and Seas trembled slightly, and a sound echoed once more. In the void, it was as if an unknown existence was falling and descending. *Pfft…* As if crushing an insect, twenty-eight bright lights were instantly extinguished in one place. "What was that just now…" The Saints were bewildered, but Li Fan, hidden in the shadows, saw it clearly. "This is the true power of a god." "Just like the True God's Finger." "Mountains and Seas devoured the True God, and indeed gained something."

Through this action of Mountains and Seas, Li Fan's vision of the True God's body became clearer. The closer one got to the divinity, the further they seemed to be from all worldly things. Li Fan felt as if he were leaping from the sea and ascending the mountains, the clamor below on the mountains and in the sea receding into the distance. Only the True God above and the sparse Mountains and Seas beside him remained. Li Fan no longer cared about the rapidly extinguishing lights afar; he ascended upwards with apparent slowness but actual swiftness. The surroundings he saw and the ground he felt occasionally gave him a sense of inexplicable familiarity.

"All laws, all things, originate from the gods." "Mountains and Seas are like this, and the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is also like this." "Using the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood to reverse the universe is, in fact, also the self-transformation of the gods…" When all twenty-eight streams of starlight were extinguished, the Mountains and Seas, finally regaining their senses, seemed to have finally sensed Li Fan's presence. The mountains beneath his feet trembled and shook constantly. The sea wind roared, attempting to blow Li Fan off.

"When truth becomes falsehood, falsehood also becomes truth!" Clad in a straw cloak, Li Fan ignored the winds and rains between Mountains and Seas. He walked leisurely, ascending step by step. As he climbed higher, even the mountains and the vast sea began to recede from him. All that remained in sight were a few solitary mountain peaks, and a corner of the sea visible in the distance. But ultimately, they could no longer affect Li Fan. The appearance of the True God above became clearer and clearer. Every step Li Fan took required greater effort.

"Mountains and Seas, the gods…" All the experiences from his past reincarnations swirled into a vortex in his mind, constantly echoing. It seemed that everything could find its reflection in the True God's body. Using his past memories and experiences as points, he gradually depicted the formless and intangible god. When Li Fan could no longer take a single step forward, the god finally appeared above him. Li Fan's body and soul seemed frozen at that moment, all cognitive activity ceasing. Fortunately, the True God had already perished, leaving only its remains.

After an unknown amount of time, Li Fan's thoughts, which had been frozen, slowly began to move again. "This… is this a god?" It was vastly different from what he had imagined. There was no majestic presence of a god, looking down upon all. Only a vast expanse of lifelessness stretched above. Li Fan's mental freeze was not due to the oppressive aura of the god but due to the repercussions of the True God's death. "Before seeing the True God's complete form, one vaguely sensed its omnipresent divine might." "But now, having seen the True God's face…" "The god is no longer a god. Void and lifelessness fill the expanse." Li Fan frowned slightly. The True God's body was indeed immensely vast, encompassing all. All knowledge, all principles, seemed to find answers within the boundless dark clouds above. But one fact was unavoidable: the True God had perished.

"Why did the True God perish?" "Perhaps only by becoming a god can one find the answer." At this moment, Li Fan seemed to have a revelation. He slightly opened his mouth, and the boundless dark clouds above began to slowly rotate, being absorbed by Li Fan. In a few breaths, the data equivalent to Li Fan's past experiences was forcibly poured into his mind, far exceeding his capacity for assimilation. The normal response would be to, like Mountains and Seas, slowly devour and digest over an immeasurably long period. But Li Fan chose a different path.

"Then, Truth becomes Falsehood…" All that was gained from the gods instantly became ethereal and illusory. Without the weight of application, it still existed, and could be accessed if one wished to read it. Feeling a lightness in his body, Li Fan accelerated his devouring pace. "To devour all of the True God’s essence is to inherit the True God's complete power." "But what I seek is not to become a god. It is to possess the gaze of a god…" Precisely because he had personally witnessed the birth of a New God in the past, Li Fan would not be easily tempted. His will was incomparably firm, he swallowed everything whole, taking all of the True God's remnants into himself. He didn't seek to digest them, only to completely absorb them.

Li Fan might have maintained his composure, but his rivals, Mountains and Seas, were thrown into extreme fury. Mountains and Seas sensed that Li Fan's devouring speed far exceeded their own. If this continued, the one to become a god would undoubtedly be Li Fan. Thus, Mountains and Seas made a desperate gamble. The mountains beneath their feet collapsed. The distant seas vanished. Beneath the True God's dark clouds, two similar dark clouds, noticeably smaller than the True God's body, suddenly appeared beside Li Fan. They began to press in and surround him, squeezing towards Li Fan.

Li Fan's heart remained undisturbed, treating them as mere True God remnants to be devoured along with the rest. He had not expected… the outcome to be surprisingly good. It seemed that Mountains and Seas, and the True God's body, had no fundamental difference in texture? The only difference was that the two dark clouds representing Mountains and Seas were filled with frenzied resentment. Not just the marks of having their bodies taken, but also countless indescribable hatreds far more ancient than Mountains and Seas themselves. Compared to the corrosive power of Mountains and Seas, these resentful emotions were even more troublesome. Even with Li Fan's current state of mind, his expression occasionally contorted. In his mind, countless new personalities seemed to emerge, seeking to replace Li Fan. Li Fan’s original self, looking at the versions of himself appearing one after another, felt a strange sensation, as if it were similar to the initial birth of Mountains and Seas. Further associating this with the dark clouds of Mountains and Seas resembling the fallen True God's remains, Li Fan had a sudden realization: "Mountains and Seas originally separated from the True God." "But their consciousness originated from… other gods who were devoured by the True God in the past?"

In Li Fan's mind, a scene appeared of gods of the past, feuding and perishing. Just as he was about to deduce further, he was interrupted by the countless new versions of himself emerging in his mind. Li Fan's eyes flashed with ferocity. "Coincidentally, let's have a taste of them all together, exactly what do they taste like!" His will, like a vortex, swept through them indiscriminately, devouring them all. Even though they all bore his likeness, they were all swallowed.

With a flash of light, wherever its hazy radiance reached, Suo's claws and teeth were all transformed into Li Fan's subordinates. In an instant, Li Fan controlled more than half of Suo's net. And at this moment, Suo actually returned!

“You actually know the Great Dao of [Suo]?”

“No wonder you could so easily accept the net I wove.”

Suo’s ethereal voice came from all directions, making it impossible to pinpoint his location. Upon hearing the voice of the original master, countless resentful souls within Suo’s net first felt an instinctual fear, and then a sign of breaking free from Li Fan’s control.

“Ignorant and greedy junior! My creation, how can it be so easily stolen?”

Li Fan flipped his hand, suppressing the anomaly in the net, and squinted outwards, but Suo’s trace was already gone. However, he keenly sensed that a crisis was imminent.

“This is…”

Li Fan, within the net, trembled violently. A familiar feeling, from the resentful souls in the net and from Li Fan’s own heart, emerged. It was as if they were currently within another, even larger, net!

“So that’s how it is. This net floating on the surface was merely a trap.” Compared to the net of bait, the threads of the true net were formless and intangible. But in an instant, they tightly bound the prey within the net. Outside the darkness, an eye resembling a rising red sun slowly appeared. Utterly cold, it stared at Li Fan. Like looking at prey that was certain to be captured. From countless directions, a pulling force came. It tightened with each passing moment, making it extremely difficult to break free. The bait net, occupied by Li Fan, was easily torn to shreds. And Li Fan, within the net, seemed doomed.

If Li Fan were an ordinary Saint, in such a predicament, he would indeed be in danger of perishing. But… Compared to the terrifying scene of the lone star descending and devouring everything, Suo’s display of power was completely lacking in deterrence.

“No matter how many nets you weave, it will be of no avail.”

“The damned must die eventually.”

Firmly ensnared by the invisible net, Li Fan’s expression remained as calm as ever. Taking a step forward, he actually ignored all restraints of the threads and walked out of the net out of thin air.

“Trying to escape?”

Li Fan’s eyes narrowed, and he lightly stepped on the ground. Like ripples spreading, an identical, copied net of Suo emerged from Li Fan’s toes. Its scale rapidly expanded, then enshrouded the original net. Li Fan reached out with his hand, and grasping in the void, pulled. A figure, battered and bruised, was dragged out by him. Countless threads, like flying dragons, instantly wrapped him tightly.

“How is this possible!”

Even when captured by Li Fan, Suo was still filled with disbelief. Rack his brains as he might, he could not fathom how Li Fan had reversed the situation so swiftly. Li Fan naturally would not explain to him. With a slender finger, he pressed down from a distance. The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood was instantly activated. It was not a direct obliteration of [Suo]'s existence, but rather, while feigning it, he absorbed and comprehended [Suo]'s Dao path. On the Hall of True Return, the characters representing Suo gradually became clearer. And in reality, the radiance condensed on Suo’s body grew dimmer and dimmer.

The Dao paths of the Saints in the Primordial Immortal Realm were all derived from the Great Dao that stood shoulder-to-shoulder with Mountains and Seas, remnants not fully assimilated by the fragmented consciousness of Mountains and Seas. Even with the amplification of Li Fan’s past self’s memories and experiences, it was not something that could be fully mastered in a short time. Fortunately, this world was self-contained, and the flow of time held no significant meaning. Suo was also deeply bound within the net, unable to move or struggle. He could only let Li Fan absorb and comprehend him.

After an unknown period, the light-like shadow that condensed on Suo's body completely dimmed. The Primeval Saint revealed his true form before Li Fan. A spider’s body with a human face, but its tendrils resembled human arms. Countless tiny eyes on his body stared intently at Li Fan. The hatred in their eyes was bone-deep. Li Fan looked at one of Suo’s eyeballs. It vanished silently, like a crushed flame. As Li Fan’s gaze shifted, the eyes on Suo’s body, which had been closed, slowly diminished. They were extinguished at a steady and resolute pace. At first, Suo could still maintain a glare of defiance. But when only over ninety eyeballs remained, Suo’s body trembled slightly. He finally averted his gaze.

“Even an ant strives to survive, let alone a Saint of Mountains and Seas?”

“Bowing to me is not shameful.” Li Fan did not mock him but said calmly. “You have two choices. First, perish here and now. Leaving no trace in Mountains and Seas.” “Second…” “The spirits within the net, though they have lost their freedom, may yet have a chance to turn the tables in the future.” “Spirits within the net?” Upon hearing Li Fan’s words, Suo first showed a slight astonishment. Then he saw the net that had captured him suddenly reveal its true form. Compared to the invisible net he had meticulously woven, this replica crafted by Li Fan was resplendent and dazzling, with myriad colors. It was as if the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas were contained within, full of infinite vitality. Suo clearly understood that this was not his illusion. But rather, this net truly seemed to carry the weight of Mountains and Seas! Only now did Suo comprehend the insurmountable chasm that lay between him and Li Fan. “Although their strength is both at the Saint realm, his foundation…” “But where did it come from?” In the Primordial Immortal Realm, all opponents were intimately familiar with each other. There was no one like Li Fan. As he pondered, a sense of emptiness from all parts of his body interrupted Suo’s thoughts.

“I am willing to become a spirit within the net!” Suo said repeatedly. The sense of oppression vanished. A moment later, Suo only felt his vision blur as he entered a magnificent and boundless palace. Vast and endless, its scope unknown. Within, myriad Daos stood, walking in the high heavens. Like bricks and tiles, they formed this ineffable palace together. With Suo’s understanding, facing this scene, he almost felt lost. However, driven by an instinctual urge, he flew towards his intended destination. [Suo]. His heart was immensely calm; all previous calculations had vanished. The moment he saw the flashing characters ahead, Suo understood this was where his lifelong cultivation of the Great Dao resided. With a thought, he drifted into it. The moment Suo returned to his position, a light streaked from heaven to earth. And then, he completely concealed himself.

…

Suo opened his eyes again. It was as if what he had just experienced was merely a nightmare. “Hmm?” He was stunned and quickly checked his condition. “Nothing is missing, and my Great Dao is not damaged in the slightest.” “Could it have been a delusion?” Suo furrowed his brow, and at that moment, he suddenly sensed a figure standing behind him. He wanted to turn and look back but couldn't move! Only then did Suo fully understand that what he had just experienced was not an illusion. After such a dramatic turn of events, Suo could only reluctantly accept the fact. “Although it seems I have recovered my full strength, my life and death are entirely in this person's hands. Every action can be controlled by him.” Suo could not discern the specific method of control, but he instinctively understood that if he tried to break free from his restraints, he would instantly perish. In other words, Suo's current existence was maintained under Li Fan’s control. If the connection of control disappeared, then Suo would also vanish into nothingness. “This kind of method…” Suo’s thoughts churned like a tide, but he heard Li Fan’s faint voice transmit, “Do your best to wreak havoc in the Primordial Immortal Realm.” Before the words even fell, Suo felt himself returned to the Primordial Immortal Realm. The heavens and earth were still vast, but Suo was no longer the same Suo as before. He quickly invigorated his spirits and, as per Li Fan’s instructions, began his actions. The word “wreak havoc” seemed simple. But when preceded by “do your best,” its meaning changed drastically. Suo dared not delay, first targeting his decades-long plan for [The Tower]. The Dao of The Tower was “all things are ordered, with clear hierarchies.” The Tower sat at the highest level, while all other Great Daos were below it, suppressed by it. Suo and The Tower had always been at odds. Years ago, when Suo was at a critical juncture of attaining Sainthood, The Tower had launched a surprise attack, attempting to suppress Suo. Fortunately, Suo had some luck and managed to evade calamity. However, he was also suppressed by a wisp of his own origin in The Tower. Since then, whenever he encountered The Tower, he was unknowingly at a disadvantage, naturally restrained. But this also allowed him to faintly know of The Tower’s existence. For many years, Suo had tried various methods and schemes against The Tower. But he had never succeeded. Now that he had fallen under someone else’s control, his life and death were no longer his to decide, so he might as well go all out!

Suo deliberately created the appearance of being severely injured, hoping to lure The Tower into a trap. The Tower, by suppressing and sealing a wisp of Suo's origin, should have been able to detect Suo's severely injured state immediately. But after surviving in the Primordial Immortal Realm for many years, all Saints were extremely cautious. This degree of injury was not enough to make The Tower act rashly. With great resolve, Suo directly severed one-third of his origin. And deliberately created a massive disturbance. A shattered net appeared in the sky of the Primordial Immortal Realm. Suo’s voice echoed: “If there is a chance to turn things around, I will make you repay me a thousandfold!” His tone, filled with utter hatred, was far from an act. And the Saints clearly sensed Suo’s severe injuries. Thus, they began to stir. Just as Suo had deduced, The Tower was the first to attack him. By using the sealed wisp of his origin, The Tower successfully locked onto the location of the severely injured Suo. Threads, like heavenly pillars, descended from above. Sealing the heavens and locking the earth, suppressing everything within. This was the same method used to deal with Li Fan earlier. The visible Suo net was merely a trap to lure the enemy. The real killing blow was another, unseen net that Suo had painstakingly woven for countless years. The net covering the sky and earth, leaping out from the void, ensnared The Tower, which was penetrating the heavens and earth. The one who was originally suppressed became a hunter with a covetous gaze. But The Tower showed no sign of panic. “Your petty tricks, in this magnificent world, who doesn’t know them?” “To use this to fight, truly laughable!” “You are best suited to hiding in the darkness forever. Once you step into the light, it's a dead end!” The Tower's mocking voice echoed throughout the Primordial Immortal Realm. Although Suo's net had already ensnared The Tower, The Tower’s radiance flowed, and its form suddenly became identical to the surrounding net. As if it were already a part of Suo’s net, Suo could devour external things, but it could not devour itself. An immeasurable suction force emanated from within The Tower, and the meticulously woven net uncontrollably fell towards The Tower. “What The Tower took before was merely a wisp of origin. After all these years, it has researched to such an extent that it can almost pass off as real, forcibly impersonating me!” “I have been scheming against it all along, and has it not been scheming against me as well?” Before his consciousness faded, Suo had a moment of realization. But towards the impending demise, Suo was unexpectedly not very fearful. “Rather than always being controlled by others, it is better to disappear completely and be truly free.” “As for you…” A ferocious thought flashed in Suo’s mind. The vast net instantly disintegrated, its form no longer intact, transforming into pure energy that erupted forth. Darkness engulfed Suo.

…

“Hmm?” After an unknown duration, Suo woke up again from the darkness. “What happened? I’m still alive?” Suo was a little stunned, not understanding why. He quickly checked his condition. “Nothing is missing, and my Great Dao is not damaged in the slightest.” “Was what just happened a delusion?” But soon, Suo dismissed his guess. Because at this moment, within the Primordial Immortal Realm, chaos had already begun to manifest. Although The Tower had successfully devoured Suo, Suo's final desperate blow had also left The Tower with severe injuries. Two Saints, one dead and one injured. It was like the opportunity had arrived for the boundary between the divine and mortal worlds to open, and the Saints were all developing their own intentions. “I’m dead. But how am I alive again?” Just as Suo was puzzled, Li Fan’s voice sounded again behind him. “Well done.” “But it’s still far from enough.”

Chapter 1764: A Peerless Treasure

Traveling against the flow of Mountains and Seas, each step arduous, reaching the time of Mountains and Seas' fragmentation, and being able to perceive the inner thoughts of Mountains and Seas. Sun Piao Miao's strength was undoubtedly immense. However, he was ultimately no match for the strongest Mountains and Seas, who had just consumed the True God. His discovery by them meant his fate was sealed. Thus, Sun Piao Miao was crafted into a tool for Mountains and Seas' plan to break the deadlock. The master of the void realm, leading infinite Dao Annihilation, completely destroyed Mountains and Seas, returning them to the solitary Star.

"Perhaps only Mountains and Seas themselves, with their deep understanding of themselves, could create Dao Annihilation."

"In fact, even without the existence of the void realm's Dao Annihilation, with the True God's Finger suppressing it, Mountains and Seas were already fated to merge. However, with Mountains and Seas' initial scale, complete dissolution would take too long. So long that Mountains and Seas could not wait, fearing unforeseen variables."

"Thus, the calamity of the void realm's Dao Annihilation arose."

Witnessing the scene of Sun Piao Miao devouring Mountains and Seas, Li Fan's mind rapidly deduced.

"Ruyi Heart was not, as I assumed, the 'eye of a god,' but a part stripped from Sun Piao Miao by Mountains and Seas. With this part missing, Sun Piao Miao was left with only a singular will, obediently carrying out the plan of Dao Annihilation's invasion."

"After all, Sun Piao Miao's strength was already extraordinary. If he possessed the identity of the void realm's master as well…"

"Even Mountains and Seas would have to yield somewhat."

"The scene before us is the best proof!"

Heavy Dao Annihilation vortexes intertwined, completely burying and obscuring Mountains and Seas within. Sun Piao Miao stood above the surging tide. Above him, the ever-brighter starlight rose in countless sparks. Mountains and Seas, forcibly pulled into the script by Sun Piao Miao, were no longer untouchable. Starlight rained down like a million sharp swords, piercing downwards. Sun Piao Miao, however, did not dodge. His face contorted with manic ferocity. Simultaneously being ravaged by countless starlight, he acted as a bridge, sending the True God's Finger into the continuous starlight above.

Mountains and Seas could deceive all beings, even themselves. Outside the script, they might have deceived the True God's Finger. But now, they had both fallen into the mortal realm. They could no longer escape the suppression of the True God's Finger. Just as Mountains and Seas had foreseen countless years ago.

Amidst the boundless radiance, it seemed billions of shadows overlapped each other. Strange lights gradually faded, replaced by the image of Mountains and Seas merging, colliding, and shattering. Infinite continuous mountain ranges, vast boundless oceans. The appearance of Mountains and Seas manifested in the void realm.

There was only one Mountains and Seas in the world. As the true Mountains and Seas appeared, the fabricated actor Mountains and Seas instantly vanished, escaping the surroundings of heavy Dao Annihilation. They merged with their lost main body. The momentum of Mountains and Seas strengthened, as if returning to their peak state after fragmentation. Amidst the roaring mountains and crashing waves, the Dao Annihilation tide was temporarily repelled.

But… Prosperity was merely an illusion. The moment they reverted to their original form, they began their so-called "merger" fate again. Even if they escaped for countless epochs, what was to come, would come. They were destined for annihilation. This time, it was no longer a rehearsal script but a true destructive calamity about to befall Mountains and Seas.

The master of the void realm, Sun Piao Miao, witnessed this, as if his long-cherished revenge had been achieved, and he let out a wild laugh. Without any pause, the Dao Annihilation army continued its frenzied consumption under his command. Returning from behind the scenes to the forefront, although Mountains and Seas' plan was thwarted, they were in their most prosperous state. And Sun Piao Miao, by pulling the Star into the mortal realm and devouring most of Mountains and Seas, was also at the peak of his ambition. Both harbored an irreconcilable hatred, and their conflict was life and death!

Compared to the scenes of Dao Annihilation and Mountains and Seas fighting in Li Fan's countless past cycles, the current battlefield was far grander and more intense. Every clash was comparable to the previous encounter where the void realm besieged and attacked the life meridians of Mountains and Seas. Both sides went all out, seeking a swift victory, determined to kill their enemies.

For Mountains and Seas, Sun Piao Miao, a mere tool, had not only betrayed them but also ruined their plan for ascending to godhood—a crime punishable by death. For Sun Piao Miao, he was originally a benevolent physician, yet he was forced to commit acts of mass destruction. Each act of devouring was equivalent to a brutal torture. The calamity of Mountains and Seas, a script spanning epochs, made him truly endure an infernal purgatory. This hatred was irreconcilable.

Enemies meeting with furious eyes. Mountains and Seas and Dao Annihilation, disregarding their own consumption and future gains, sought only the death of the other!

Boom boom boom! Mountains and Seas sank, falling into Dao Annihilation, stirring up surging ripples. Light and shadow flowed, Mountains and Seas solidified from illusion, dispelling the boundless darkness. It was as if the eons of struggle between Mountains and Seas and Dao Annihilation were compressed into a few days. Every moment of collision was incredibly intense.

Li Fan felt as if he were beneath a thousand-zhang waterfall, in a pool below. Ten million giant drums beat simultaneously, their deafening sound filling the air. The collision was accompanied by a low, resounding hum. Ripples like surging giant waves, each possessing the power to overturn the world. In the face of such a terrifying battle, Li Fan’s protective Transformation of Truth and Falsehood was like a thin straw cape in a torrential storm, at risk of being blown away at any moment.

With Li Fan's current strength, without the protection of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, his fate would be instant death. But he did not rashly activate True Return. Firstly, during the most dangerous moments of the battle, if he were to rashly return, he would undoubtedly attract the attention of both Mountains and Seas and Sun Piao Miao, increasing the risk. Secondly… Li Fan still wanted to witness the return of the fallen True God!

"Don't be fooled by the fierce fighting; it's just a fight between caged beasts."

"Regardless of who wins or loses, the final outcome remains unchanged."

"Since Mountains and Seas' plan to break the deadlock has failed, the only thing awaiting them is the destiny of returning to the True God."

"The current escalating offense only indicates their impotent rage."

Thinking this, Li Fan no longer felt the terrifying nature of the so-called mastermind behind Mountains and Seas. This battle seemed endless. However, Li Fan could keenly perceive that the scale of Dao Annihilation and Mountains and Seas was continuously shrinking. And above them… Where Mountains and Seas had been hiding, untouched, something terrifying seemed to be awakening.

The battle continued for an unknown duration, but ultimately, the profundity of Mountains and Seas prevailed. Stimulated by the imminent fate of returning to divinity, the true Mountains and Seas unleashed numerous divine abilities that Li Fan had never seen before. Pure imagery of Mountains and Seas, mountains supporting their posture, seas extending infinitely, and within their fusion, various wondrous creations emerged. A magnificent and indescribable mountain range rose from the sea, possessing an aura of suppressing the infinite. The sea tides surged, rising endlessly, turning the world upside down. It was evident that to counter the impending return of True God, Mountains and Seas had exhausted every possible method and employed every tactic.

Despite traversing Mountains and Seas against the current, and witnessing the process of Mountains and Seas from existence to non-existence as the master of the void realm for the second time, Sun Piao Miao was gradually overwhelmed by the infinite changes evolved by the new Mountains and Seas. Ultimately, he vanished, consumed by the infinite imprints of Mountains and Seas. With the rest annihilated, the victorious Saints should have been jubilant. However, Li Fan clearly sensed a trace of fear from the current Mountains and Seas. When Sun Piao Miao was present, Mountains and Seas could still suppress their inner fear through endless combat. But now, with their only enemy gone, Mountains and Seas had to face the fallen True God!

Just as they had done before, Mountains and Seas still refused to give up, attempting various methods of salvation. They tried to prevent their fated merger. But the current Mountains and Seas were no longer the fragmented Mountains and Seas of the beginning. They were now pure Mountains and Seas after several instances of devouring. Without any other beings, without scapegoats, Mountains and Seas could not avoid their own fate. Another hundred billion years passed. Mountains and Seas, from their peak, gradually declined, and then merged and perished again.

Outside the Mountains and Seas, a point of light gradually appeared, just as Sun Piao Miao had prophesied in his texts regarding the solitary Star, like a god's eye. It hung high above, gazing down upon the Mountains and Seas with majesty. Mountains and Seas trembled because of it. In their final moments, they still tried to struggle, but it was all in vain.

The moment Mountains and Seas finally perished… Li Fan, who had been observing everything, suddenly felt as if he had taken the place of the former Mountains and Seas. He directly faced the True God's gaze! Li Fan could clearly feel that the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, which served as his protective charm, was creaking under the True God's pressure, as if it might shatter at any moment. It seemed that everything previously devoured by the True God had now returned to the fallen True God. Although the starlight still maintained a glimmer, its power intensified relentlessly. The weight Li Fan bore on his shoulders grew heavier.

Even the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood could no longer fully protect him; his body gradually turned into dust, drifting towards the solitary point in the heavens. Only the tenacious Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood stubbornly endured. Until this moment, Li Fan had not activated True Return, all to verify a conjecture: did the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood truly belong to the True God? Based on the currently known information, everything in the world originated from the fallen True God. If the True God were to resurrect, they would reclaim all that was once theirs. If the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood was indeed a part of the True God, then undoubtedly, it would also return to the light above as the True God's resurrection process progressed.

Li Fan maintained his form while observing the changes in the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. Mountains and Seas had perished, yet the True God had not descended immediately. It was as if they were only a hair's breadth away from resurrection, their radiance growing ever brighter. The brilliant light frantically searched, attempting to find Li Fan's hidden trace. Dazzling and filling his vision. The stronger the brilliance, the more intense the pressure and the allure it exerted on Li Fan. Finally, with a crisp snapping sound. The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood collapsed.

Li Fan had been waiting for this moment. As it collapsed, Li Fan caught a glimpse of the disintegration of True Return. Built upon the twin pillars of Truth is Falsehood and Falsehood is Truth, with several other Daos as filler, the magnificent hall of the Great Dao had crumbled. All the previously captured Daos, such as the First Profound Qi and the Second Universe Cycle, had vanished. Only the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood remained, stubbornly holding on. But even between Truth and Falsehood, there were differences. Falsehood is Truth clearly resisted less than Truth is Falsehood. In this critical situation, Truth is Falsehood was desperately supporting Falsehood is Truth, maintaining the integrity of True Return.

"So, it is as I initially suspected. All laws and all things originate from the gods."

Witnessing this, Li Fan sighed deeply in his heart. The connection between Truth and Falsehood was about to be severed by the True God's tearing force, and Li Fan dared not hesitate any longer. He called out to True Return in his heart. A ray of light erupted sequentially from Truth is Falsehood and Falsehood is Truth. Its brilliance was dazzling, its intent fierce. At this moment, it seemed to surpass the divine radiance from above.

Truth is Falsehood acted like an invisible hand, wiping away the starlight. Falsehood is Truth acted like a divine brush, reshaping the perished Mountains and Seas. In an instant, ten billion years passed. The world, which had become empty due to the True God's resurrection, was once again filled with life. Li Fan returned to the anchored time of 1 year.

Having escaped from the True God's grasp multiple times, Li Fan was no longer afraid or regretful. Instead, he had gradually become accustomed to it. With a calm expression, he reviewed the events of his previous life.

"The fallen True God, and the Star formed after Mountains and Seas successfully laid their plans, were actually different."

"Of course, if I hadn't been a variable, then Mountains and Seas, after completing their plans, might have truly succeeded in their ascension, becoming God."

"But, because I possessed True Return, hoarding the True God's Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. This caused Mountains and Seas to transform and ascend to the Star, but not fully become God."

"I previously confused the Star with God because both the Star and God possessed overwhelming and indomitable power. Their strength far surpassed the beings of Mountains and Seas, and once they appeared, sentient beings had no power to resist."

"It was fundamentally impossible to distinguish the difference between the Star and God."

"Perhaps, throughout the entirety of Mountains and Seas, only I know the difference."

"The only missing element is Truth and Falsehood."

At this thought, Li Fan couldn't help but think of Emperor Tian Luo from the Primeval Immortal Realm. Previously, he thought that Emperor Tian Luo leading the Immortal Realm to vanish without a trace might have been a successful transcendence of Mountains and Seas. But now, facing the Star and the descending True God, he finally understood. Everything was part of Mountains and Seas' predetermined script; how could one possibly escape Mountains and Seas?

Outside the script of Mountains and Seas, the waiting, watchful true Mountains and Seas.

"Perhaps, the moment they escaped, they would be destroyed and returned to the script of Mountains and Seas."

"The only thing Emperor Tian Luo could do…"

"Was to ensure that the nutrients derived from himself and the Immortal Realm after their destruction were collected by the primordial beings as much as possible."

"This might be the reason why the survivors' talents improved after the destruction of the Primeval Immortal Realm."

Li Fan shook his head slightly: "The cage built by the phrase 'the outcome is irrelevant' is not so easily escaped."

"Even with my countless reincarnations, combining the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, and understanding all the hidden truths…"

"In such a short time, I still cannot find a way to break the deadlock."

Li Fan frowned slightly, feeling truly at a loss. How could he slay the gods? Using his own methods, creating countless Saints to attack them? Faced with the True God's brilliance, the Saints' fate would be to dissolve like ice and snow.

"They originated from the True God, so how can they contend with the True God?"

"The fate of Mountains and Seas has already proven this."

"The fall of a god…"

Li Fan's gaze drifted towards the time before the Xuanhuang Realm, towards the beginning of time.

"Perhaps, like Sun Piao Miao, only by going back to the time of divine fragmentation can the mystery of the True God's fall be glimpsed."

"Only then might the secret be revealed."

Chapter 1765: Punish God Transformation

"In my previous life, faced with the imminent descent of the True God, I lost everything except for the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood."

"However…"

"It's not a big problem."

Li Fan looked at the True Return panel. Like the first time he opened it, the characters did not all appear at once, but popped out one by one. They appeared and then disintegrated, all the complex content disappearing, leaving only a few lines of text.

Name: Li Fan.

Dao Paths: Truth, Falsehood.

Great Dao Return:

...

Under the Dao Paths, the words Truth and Falsehood flickered unsternly, as if these two words alone encompassed all laws and all things in the world. The Great Dao Return Hall, which had initially taken shape, was now empty. All the Daos previously captured, such as the First Profound Qi and the Second Universe Cycle, had vanished. At the end of his previous life, in order to verify the origin of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, Li Fan had held on until the very last moment. The divine power devoured all things. Even True Return was dismembered and separated. The functions of the various Daos that once originated from the Saints, as well as the various Daos in the Great Dao Return Hall, were all swallowed by the resurrecting True God. True Return now consisted only of Li Fan and the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. However, for the current Li Fan, possessing Truth and Falsehood meant possessing everything. All else was unimportant.

"Falsehood is Truth!"

Li Fan stared at the flickering characters before him, recalling the two solitary beams of light that had enveloped him at the end of his previous life, and his understanding of the various Daos in the Great Dao Return Hall. With a thought, he conjured existence from nothingness. Lines of colorful characters were born in the void, written out of thin air. The First Profound Qi, the Second Universe Cycle… As well as the Daos of the Saints on the other shore, all were listed. The Great Dao Hall, previously blank, instantly became filled with myriad Daos, shining brightly. It was no different from what Li Fan had possessed before.

However, it did not exceed the original limit of existence.

Li Fan then contemplated the Dao One Mountains and Seas Map. Unfortunately, amidst the churning clouds of the Dao One, although the Mountains and Seas Map had generally taken shape, it could not perfectly replicate the strongest state of the Boundless Mountains and Seas Tablet. Seated within the Mountains and Seas Map was the True God's Finger, even more ethereal and indistinct than before. If one did not observe closely, its existence would be hard to detect.

"The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood is built upon my understanding of all things. Through continuous reincarnation, my mastery of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas is sufficient to manifest it with a single thought."

"But…"

"The True God's Finger is different."

The scene of the True God's imminent resurrection, filled with starlight, resurfaced in Li Fan's mind.

"Even after witnessing the divine, it is difficult to comprehend the divine."

"With my reincarnated experiences, deciphering the divine is still far from sufficient."

"But perhaps my past self could."

With a thought, the True Return inheritance option, which had been suppressed for a long time, finally appeared. It skipped all previous options and went straight to the last line. A completely new option that had never appeared before.

"[The Pantheon]."

Li Fan stared intently at these three words but hesitated to choose. For some unknown reason, a chilling sensation arose, unceasingly.

"The Pantheon. What does this mean?"

Li Fan already knew that True Return was the sum of his past countless reincarnation memories, experiences, the Daos of the Saints, and the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood.

"[The Pantheon] represents my past self's insights after witnessing the resurrecting True God. But why is it called the Pantheon?"

Li Fan couldn't help but recall the legends of the Creator God he had heard before.

"The powerful Creator God defeated his peers and extracted their power to evolve all beings in the world…"

"The only source of this record comes from Sun Piao Miao's notes."

"The Prophecy of Mountains and Seas, and other records, all matched the Mountains and Seas I observed. Only this one concerning the Creator God remains confusing."

Li Fan's expression was uncertain, and he did not choose the inheritance directly. Instead, after cultivating back to the Saint realm, at least possessing a certain degree of self-preservation, he reopened it.

As if starlight returned to the earth, a profound darkness enveloped everything, devouring it. Xuanhuang, Primordial, Mountains and Seas, all vanished.

In absolute nothingness, Li Fan vaguely sensed that there seemed to be some indescribable existences around him. They were beyond Li Fan's scope of understanding and observation, thus invisible and unknowable. But he could perceive the drastic changes occurring in the darkness.

Without any warning, one of the unknowable existences suddenly disappeared. As if it were suddenly devoured.

Next, a second, then a third. The original "Pantheon," it seemed, was reduced to only the last remaining existence.

This scene matched what Sun Piao Miao had recorded.

Li Fan suddenly had an epiphany: "Sun Piao Miao likely glimpsed this scene from Mountains and Seas' thoughts at the beginning of their fragmentation and creation, hence writing the prophecy of the Creator God slaying other gods."

"But…"

Li Fan frowned slightly, feeling something was amiss.

"At this time, Mountains and Seas did not exist. How could Mountains and Seas know of this scene?"

The boundless darkness did not recede. It continuously surrounded Li Fan. Li Fan suppressed all doubts in his heart, waiting for the next development.

It took longer than the time it took for all the "gods" to disappear. Suddenly, a faint light appeared, illuminating this unknowable world. It allowed Li Fan to glimpse blurry images hidden within the darkness. Multiple figures overlapped and merged into one. It was as if they were devouring, chewing, and also integrating and sublimating. The many became one, the one contained all.

However, within this, disharmony was quietly brewing. Li Fan seemed to see two images attempting to break free from it. Compared to the other unknowable and invisible existences, these two figures were quite familiar.

"Mountains, Seas!"

Li Fan's heart trembled violently. At this moment, the light in the void suddenly intensified. The darkness was dispelled, and Li Fan returned to reality.

Compared to observing the Outline of Mountains and Seas Changes and the Starfall Rhythm Law, this so-called "[The Pantheon]" did not bring any special impact. It was as if he had experienced a dream, and upon exiting it, Li Fan quickly emerged from its influence.

"This does not mean that the True God is weaker than Mountains and Seas or the Star."

"Rather…"

"The experience and memories of my past self have finally reached their limit in this scenario. His insights and my insights are essentially the same and cannot generate anything more meaningful. Only such inexplicable images can be produced."

"The legacy of my past self has finally been exhausted."

Li Fan did not find this day unexpected. In fact, he had already achieved what his past self could not: he understood the truth of Mountains and Seas and the Star, and witnessed the scene of the resurrecting True God's imminent descent.

"The path ahead must be walked by myself."

The moment this thought arose in Li Fan's mind, another version of himself seemed to appear before his eyes. He smiled faintly, then his form completely shattered, turning into countless rays of starlight that surged towards Li Fan.

All his past memories, like a surging flood, all rushed towards Li Fan. If before he could only partially review them, now it was a complete inheritance.

After sitting in meditation for a long time, Li Fan finally digested all the memories of his past self. In addition to the countless reincarnation experiences, there were also insights into the various Great Daos of Mountains and Seas.

"This is the foundation for the operation of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, the fundamental reason why True Return can be achieved."

Although these were Li Fan's own memories and insights, Li Fan now felt a sense of disconnect during the inheritance.

"My past self was me, and yet not me."
