"The Li Fan of the past truly perished. Only to such an extent of severance could a completely different possibility of breaking the deadlock be born."

Li Fan's heart was enlightened. Although he could not directly convert all the divine abilities and cultivation of his past self, such a gift was equivalent to a direct enlightenment. Li Fan's understanding of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas and the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood increased exponentially with every passing moment.

From another perspective, it was as if Li Fan and True Return were gradually merging. They would gradually become indistinguishable.

"The day the fusion is complete will be the day True Return perishes."

"But it can also be said that True Return has not perished."

"Because I am True Return, and True Return is me."

Li Fan's heart was utterly calm, and he looked up towards the beginning of Mountains and Seas.

"The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is merely a means of self-preservation. To truly break the deadlock, one must still seek a method to slay gods."

"The [Pantheon] I glimpsed was too vague. At the time of Mountains and Seas' fragmentation, there should have been more clues."

"Let's proceed according to the original plan, moving against the current towards the beginning of Mountains and Seas."

"Billions of years of time, even with my current cultivation, it is an extremely long journey. Let's take it slowly."

"By the time I arrive…"

"Perhaps the fusion and absorption of True Return will be largely complete."

Li Fan's thoughts gradually flowed, and his form transformed into a thread, disappearing into the void realm. The void realm was vast, fraught not only with the danger of Dao Annihilation but also the peril of distinguishing past from present. This was the greatest obstacle for ordinary Saints attempting to traverse against the current.

Li Fan did not know how Sun Piao Miao managed to reach the beginning of Mountains and Seas step by step. But for him, traversing against the current was no longer difficult. With the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood enveloping him, Dao Annihilation could not harm him in the slightest. His past experiences and memories, countless cycles of saving the world, every corner of Mountains and Seas, and even the void realm, Li Fan had personally traversed. For others, it was a place where past and present were indistinguishable, but for Li Fan, everywhere felt deeply familiar. He walked as if strolling through a garden.

Without any hesitation, Li Fan traversed onward, ignoring the conflict between Mountains and Seas and Dao Annihilation, his only focus being the potential whereabouts of Sun Piao Miao and the couple Qiu Tianhui. He did discover traces left by Sun Piao Miao, further verifying his past traversal. However, strangely, the couple Qiu Tianhui seemed to have vanished from Mountains and Seas as if evaporated.

"Only their vital meridians remain, but their figures are nowhere to be found."

"From the end of Mountains and Seas to the beginning, what exactly are they seeking?"

As Qiu XinHui's creation, she could faintly sense the existence of Li Fan's True Return. Perhaps the couple Qiu Tianhui had also sensed it.

"The plan to reconnect Mountains and Seas… is completely useless for saving the world. They must know this."

Li Fan pondered as he traveled against the current, as if a passerby of Mountains and Seas, traversing its entirety without leaving a trace. After an unknown period, until…

With one step forward, reality seemed to spin, and the scene of towering mountains and flowing seas vanished. In an instant, he found himself in a vast, desolate world.

"Primeval Immortal Realm."

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. This was the initial stage of Mountains and Seas' merger, even containing the attempts of Mountains and Seas to resist their fate. However, it was interfered with by the True God's Finger, causing the realm to be destroyed.

"Only the Saints within, who vaguely sensed something, managed to achieve temporary peace by severing their future."

"The Primeval Saints…"

"Hmph, they are all just cowards."

In his countless past cycles, Li Fan had indeed interacted with these Primeval Saints, but none could become his allies.

"Unable to achieve godhood, unable to save the world, they could only hide in this realm and fight amongst themselves."

Although Li Fan disdained them, he did not underestimate them. The Primeval Immortal Realm seemed isolated from Mountains and Seas, its time stagnant. No matter how long the Saints fought amongst themselves, only those who could survive in this place possessed the potential for godhood; they only lacked an opportunity. Li Fan's previous two witnessing of different New Gods' births were the best proof.

Li Fan looked towards the sky, attempting to gaze further into the ancient past, but it was as if something was blocking his view, preventing him from seeing clearly. He tried to move forward, to go against the current, but it was like getting stuck in mud, unable to move.

"This is why, despite the gathering of Saints in the Primeval Immortal Realm, the matter of contending for godhood has been delayed for so long."

"Before the Primeval Immortal Realm was the time of Mountains and Seas' fragmentation."

"Mountains and Seas naturally would not allow their creations to interfere with them. Thus, they established this divine-mortal boundary."

"Severing space-time, cutting off karma."

Li Fan reached out, attempting to break through the divine-mortal boundary using the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood. But the moment he moved, the eyes of all the Saints in the Primeval Immortal Realm simultaneously turned towards him! In the next instant, various divine abilities and techniques rained down like a storm.

"There are the Three Saints of Lian Shan, and an old acquaintance, Suo."

"Hmm, and Hua, Ding, Liu…"

Ripples of light and shadow emanated before Li Fan, blocking all harm. Although he ignored the attacks of the Saints, Li Fan felt his energy being rapidly depleted. His protective Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood also began to tremble.

Frowning slightly, Li Fan's form flickered and faded, disappearing from their sight. Although a few divine senses could still track him, Li Fan evaded their sight after several consecutive shifts.

"Firstly, the divine-mortal boundary is a restriction set by Mountains and Seas and cannot be easily broken."

"Secondly, all the Saints are eyeing him greedily. Any attempt to step forward, regardless of potential success, will be met with a united attack. The fewer opponents for godhood, the greater the chance of becoming a god."

"The opportunity for godhood has arrived. What are the conditions to break the stalemate?"

Li Fan, in hiding, deduced rapidly based on his experiences in past lives of creating gods.

"The Saints have been locked in a struggle for years, forming a strange balance."

"No one can overcome the other, and no one can advance further."

"It's like a stagnant pool."

"When still, there is no change. At such times, a pebble is needed to smash into it."

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. His form flickered again, and he stealthily appeared beside Suo. Suo had been 'plucked' by Li Fan several times and had his name recorded in the Great Dao Return Hall. Naturally, he could not escape Li Fan's search. Countless tentacle-like black shadows writhed and moved. The moment they sensed Li Fan, they coiled like a net, entangling him.

Chapter 1766: Good Intentions Change

Countless God Slayers, variants of the original, naturally could not possess the same "True Return" ability as the original. Their reset power was confined to a single possibility, with a limit of a hundred uses.

Even with such strict limitations, under normal circumstances, it would be enough for a God Slayer variant to successfully cultivate to the Transcendent realm.

After leaping out of their initial possibilities, the "True Return" they carried would "upgrade." The reset would not be limited to a single possibility but would encompass a certain range around themselves.

Furthermore, if they encountered a Mountain and Sea Saint far stronger than themselves, the effective range of "True Return" would further shrink.

There was also another point... if two God Slayer variants were too close to each other, their "True Return" would both become void. Simultaneously, they would sense each other.

The only way to restore the "True Return" function was to kill the other party and plunder their creation.

The victor lives, and their "True Return" function is restored, even advancing their understanding of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood by devouring the opponent's "True Return."

The loser dies, but not entirely. Under the protection of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, they would return to the world of Li Fan's original body, the "God Slayer Variant."

Their memories and experiences would feed back to the main body, and then, guided by "True Return," with all memories erased, they would re-enter the cycle of Mountains and Seas!

This cycle repeated until the destruction of Mountains and Seas.

It was not a quick process to forge the God-slaying variables. In fact, even Li Fan himself did not know the extent of accumulation required to successfully slay gods before he acted. But he understood that this was the only way.

Thus, he acted without hesitation.

As time passed, ripples began to form in the peaceful Mountains and Seas. The countless variants created based on Li Fan's original template generally had ordinary cultivation aptitudes.

However, compared to the main body, their starting circumstances were generally much better. Even if their first life's cultivation was unsuccessful, after numerous reincarnations, they could basically embark on the path of cultivation with their foresight.

They could even ascend to True Immortal.

Deploying variants generally did not consume more than thirty lifetimes. However, from True Immortal to Transcendent was like a chasm that blocked almost all variants.

Nearly 90% of the variants, even after ninety reincarnations, could not find a way to transcend.

This situation was precisely the opposite of Li Fan's main body's cultivation path.

The Great Xuan, Xuanhuang, the Darkest Star Sea, the High Wall – countless killing intents and hidden traps everywhere. Without foresight, even a cultivator with exceptional talent would struggle to break through.

His first self died early, so how could he have possibly met the late Saints of Mountains and Seas and comprehended the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood?

"But if I were an outsider 'pulled' by the fallen True God to break the stalemate, then everything would make sense."

"The True God's severed finger could distort the will of Mountains and Seas and dim the solitary Star's brilliance. Protecting a mortal to smoothly reach the Saint realm was naturally effortless."

Looking at the words "Divine Blessing" on the True Return panel, before "Courageous Transformation" and "Illusion is True," Li Fan had a sudden realization.

It turned out everything was not exaggerated. Divine Blessing was truly divine blessing.

"Divine blessing, coupled with the supreme talent of my past self. Not only did it break the script written by Mountains and Seas, but it also allowed me to possess the method to indefinitely postpone the New God's ascension."

"But as I said before, I can delay the Star for a while, but not for a lifetime."

"Mountains and Seas fade, the solitary Star ascends the divine throne. If this script remains unchanged, the outcome will be the same."

"Damn it!" Li Fan's rage wasn't because he had lost his past parents and children. In his past life as a Grand Tutor in the Xuanhuang Realm, with numerous wives and children, he might have still cherished familial bonds.

But now, Li Fan, possessing the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, had personally orchestrated the demise and restoration of countless lives with a single thought. In his view, his past parents and children were no different from other beings. If he wished, he could create his remembered family at any time.

When truth becomes falsehood, falsehood also becomes truth. True or false, there was no difference.

Li Fan's rage stemmed from himself. It could only be about himself. No matter what, that "Li Fan" from the past was still Li Fan.

Unceremoniously brought here by a fallen True God to work. He was originally an outsider to the play, but unknowingly became too deeply involved. He struggled desperately through countless cycles, only to realize it was all a joke.

The past Li Fan was utterly despairing. The current Li Fan, however, felt an uncontrollable surge of malevolence.

What about True Gods? Did they ask for my opinion when they brought me here?

"What you cannot do, I will do. The revenge you cannot enact, I will enact."

"Mountains and Seas, Star, Gods…"

"None of you will escape!"

A ferocious glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes, his boundless killing intent spreading outward. This killing intent was so intense that even the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood could not suppress it for the moment.

The True God's Finger, the dim starlight, and the fragmented Mountains and Seas all seemed to sense something at this moment. Li Fan felt as if countless eyes were simultaneously looking at him.

He calmed down instantly. The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood heavily concealed him once more. While ferocity was instinctual, caution and discretion were also instinctual.

Although he had uttered a vow of vengeance in a moment of impulse, Li Fan himself knew that with his current strength, self-preservation was possible, but slaying gods… was far from it.

Previously, he believed that by comprehending the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood to a certain degree, anything could be easily resolved. But knowing everything now told him that it might not be the case.

"My past self could break the True God's script, and had perfected the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood. Yet, faced with the final descent of the New God, he was still helpless."

"The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood could only shift its existence back to before its appearance, but could not completely sever the possibility of the New God's descent."

"Slaying Gods…" Li Fan couldn't help but ponder that question again. Why did that True God perish? He could foresee his own future, even foresee the strategy of Mountains and Seas shedding its golden cicada to escape and bringing in an outsider to break the stalemate. Yet, he couldn't avoid his own demise?

"If the old god could be slain, then the new god could also be slain. If only the reason for the True God's death could be found…"

Li Fan looked again at the True God's Finger standing tall in the void realm. The suppression of starlight seemed to be an instinctive reaction after being stimulated. Now, with the starlight dimming and gradually fading, the True God's Finger returned to its original mission.

Boundless Mountains and Seas!

The True God's Finger, like a shooting star, pierced into the separation between Mountains and Seas. The Mountains and Seas, having just completed their separation, seemed destined to repeat their past fate.

At this moment, two figures flew out from the mountains above and the infinite sea, intercepting the rapidly descending True God's Finger.

Li Fan, naturally familiar with these two figures, recognized their identities at a glance.

"Lian Shan? Gui Hai?"

Li Fan's pupils constricted as he observed from afar. The appearances of the two Saints had undergone a radical transformation compared to before.

Saint Lian Shan's form was no longer distinct. He only vaguely maintained a humanoid shape, but his face bore billions of etchings, each trace recording the history of a former civilization within Mountains and Seas.

Saint Gui Hai, on the other hand, seemed to be rooted within the infinite possibilities of the infinite sea. Billions of tentacles supported him, sending Gui Hai out of the Mountains and Seas.

Lian Shan and Gui Hai, their faces expressionless and resolute, stood before the rapidly descending True God's Finger. Although the Three Saints were powerful, Li Fan absolutely did not believe they could block the True God's Finger.

But things developed beyond Li Fan's expectations.

From Lian Shan and Gui Hai, three streams of light leaped out. Then, a final wisp of brilliance came from the Mountains and Seas themselves. The three lights merged, and a Ruyi scepter instantly took shape.

"Ruyi Heart?"

The moment he saw this Ruyi artifact, the name "Ruyi Heart" naturally appeared in Li Fan's mind. He also understood that it was this artifact that had been constantly searching for him in the void realm!

"As expected, it originated from the Three Saints."

"Using the eyes of a god to counter the True God's Finger?" Li Fan thought this instantly.

The appearance of the Ruyi Heart caused a commotion identical to before. The void realm was thrown into boundless turmoil, with ripples unceasingly emerging. For a time, it even abandoned its mission of devouring Mountains and Seas, surging towards the Ruyi Heart.

This time, Lian Shan and Gui Hai did not retrieve the Ruyi artifact in time. They merely allowed it to lie quietly in the center of the vortex. Li Fan could even vaguely sense that the two Saints seemed to be desperately manipulating the Ruyi Heart, guiding it towards being consumed by the void realm.

"Mountains and Seas, to break the True God's Finger's plan, chose to transform into the solitary Star."

"But at the same time, to deceive the True God's Finger, they had to 'act' thoroughly. On the day the grand play began, Mountains and Seas were no longer Mountains and Seas, but the solitary Star. Their identities were completely transformed."

"The beings of the world depend on Mountains and Seas, merely as actors to fulfill the script. The void realm's Dao Annihilation is the prop to drive the plot forward."

"Because this play was so convincing, Mountains and Seas did not know their own roles. Thus, under the erosion of Dao Annihilation, they would instinctively awaken their will to survive."

"Only when the script is broken and the performance is halted will Mountains and Seas truly know their identities. This is also why Mountains and Seas betrayed me after defeating Dao Annihilation in the past."

"And now…"

Li Fan looked up indifferently. Starlight descended, blocked by the True God's Finger. Mountains and Seas were about to merge again, following the predetermined script. Although Li Fan had interfered, causing many variables, the final outcome remained unchanged.

"Still within the script, meaning Mountains and Seas do not know their true identities."

Li Fan's eyes narrowed sharply, focusing on the Ruyi Heart at the center of the converging Dao Annihilation. In this life, Mountains and Seas underwent an unprecedented process of merging, separation, and re-merging. The True God's Finger shifted twice, creating a scenario Li Fan had never encountered.

Dao Annihilation surged like waves, constantly eroding and corroding the Ruyi Heart. The Ruyi Heart's influence gradually dimmed. Subsequently, in the dark and silent void, a consciousness seemed to be rapidly awakening.

The entire void realm, which had been dark and silent from the beginning of Mountains and Seas, was no longer so. The destructive power of Dao Annihilation, which had been eroding and destroying, gradually subsided.

If before the Dao Annihilation forces of the void realm were like an army of countless soldiers, now, billions of soldiers had returned to one person. A distorted figure quietly emerged.

Looking at Mountains and Seas, a trace of hatred flashed in its eyes. But ultimately, it still intervened, blocking the descending True God's Finger! To be precise, it was delaying it.

The True God's Finger was unstoppable, but at this moment, it seemed to be trapped in a mire of infinite Dao Annihilation. Its light continuously flashed, yet it could never escape the void realm's confines.

"He is…" Li Fan felt a sense of familiarity from this figure. It stemmed from an intense hatred and anger towards the solitary Star.

"The void realm's Dao Annihilation is a tool created by Mountains and Seas to advance the plot."

"But where did this tool originate from…"

"After the divine fragmentation, besides Mountains and Seas, there should be nothing else in the world."

The void realm figure, after temporarily holding back the True God's Finger, ignored the Mountains and Seas. Then, it arrogantly flew towards the heavens, beyond the boundary, towards the dim solitary Star!

Infinite ripples erupted from the void realm figure, each like a sharp blade, fiercely tearing through the veil between reality and drama. Layer by layer, the black curtains were peeled back under this intense collision. The originally dim starlight actually seemed to brighten somewhat.

"He is…"

"Pulling the Star into the play?" Li Fan was pleasantly surprised to have a potential ally with a similar stance. However, he chose to observe passively first. After all, the identity of the void realm figure was still unknown, and its appearance was extremely bizarre.

As the starlight under the heavens grew brighter, the True God's Finger, trapped in the void realm figure's grasp, once again felt the presence of starlight. The target shifted from Mountains and Seas, directly towards the hidden solitary Star.

Li Fan finally understood: "If one hides outside the script, one might deceive the True God's Finger. But if one enters the script, it becomes difficult to escape the True God's Finger's discernment!"

The void realm figure, exhaling and inhaling ripples, guided the starlight. Unlike ordinary beings who mutated upon contact with starlight, it became even more profound.

But it did not absorb the starlight for its own use. Instead, it channeled it into the existing Mountains and Seas! The streams of starlight were not as overbearing as the true descent of the solitary Star. Instead, they resembled the scattered light when the Mountains and Seas had previously defeated Dao Annihilation.

Witnessing such a familiar scene, Li Fan was deeply moved: "This is the script being broken, the solitary Star entering the game!"

In a single thought, the world changed. A bizarre transformation, with the constant smearing of starlight, occurred within the Mountains and Seas. The void realm figure suffered the same treatment as Li Fan had in the past. Starlight erosion, Mountains and Seas repeatedly fell.

Li Fan vaguely sensed intense anger emanating from the howling winds and roaring waves and starlight.

"You know how to get angry too?" Li Fan felt a hint of schadenfreude.

Compared to the past Li Fan, the void realm figure seemed to have anticipated the surrounding changes. Especially the betrayal of Mountains and Seas.

Without hesitation, it transformed into an endless, surging tide, encircling the Mountains and Seas. Devouring them in a fit of rage.

As a tool used to devour Mountains and Seas, the void realm’s strength was already superior to Mountains and Seas. Now, having obtained the Ruyi Heart and become "complete," the void realm, acting with impunity, was no longer something Mountains and Seas could resist.

Like a wilting flower, all were transformed into nourishment for the void realm figure.

Li Fan watched the figure standing amidst the withered Mountains and Seas, the sense of familiarity growing stronger. It wasn't due to their shared hatred for the solitary Star, but rather… a sense of déjà vu.

"Sun, Piao, Miao."

A strange light flashed in Li Fan's eyes as he spoke Sun Piao Miao's name word by word. Although not entirely certain in his heart, as the void realm figure intensified its devouring of Mountains and Seas, its form became increasingly distinct. Li Fan's premonition grew stronger.

"It's really him? How is this possible?" Li Fan suddenly recalled the question from before. Mountains and Seas foresaw their future and deduced a method to break the stalemate by shedding their golden cicada, thus needing to create a prop to drive the plot.

But at that time, Mountains and Seas had just fragmented. Besides the devoured True God, and Mountains and Seas, there was nothing else. Where did the tool come from? They couldn't possibly have drawn upon their own origins to create a world-destroying tool, could they?

"No. At the beginning of Mountains and Seas' fragmentation, other beings existed."

"That was Sun Piao Miao, who wrote the prophecy of Mountains and Seas!"

The prophecy of Mountains and Seas meticulously described various aspects of Mountains and Seas. At the beginning of the notes, Mountains and Seas had not yet merged. At the end of the notes, Mountains and Seas were no more, and because of the solitary Star hanging high like a god's solitary eye, standing above Mountains and Seas.

"One who can resist the state before Mountains and Seas merged can also resist the state of Mountains and Seas' fragmentation. A time traveler would never abruptly stop progressing."

"And the last chapter of the notes…"

Li Fan suddenly thought of a question. It was precisely because he had seen Sun Piao Miao's notes before, seen the mention of the Star within, that he subconsciously called the power transformed by Mountains and Seas as the Star. In fact, it was merely a pure, exclusive, and overbearing power.

The god formed by Mountains and Seas was the Star. The True God's return… was also the Star.

Li Fan was suddenly stunned.

"So, the last chapter of Sun Piao Miao's notes did not refer to the events happening in the current Mountains and Seas. Instead, it referred to the outcome Mountains and Seas foresaw in their endless deductions."

"One who can perceive the inner thoughts of Mountains and Seas…"

Li Fan seemed to see Mountains and Seas, agonizing over the lack of a world-destroying tool, suddenly discover Sun Piao Miao, who was peeking into their inner thoughts at the beginning of Mountains and Seas' fragmentation.

Chapter 1767: The God-Becoming Guest

Zhang Fan, caught between indecision, did not notice Xuanyuan Hong’s shift in expression. He was indeed a little shocked by the sudden revelation of the truth behind the annihilation of Mountains and Seas. However, by nature, and with the supreme treasure "True Return" by his side, staying in this small space forever was truly unwilling. After all, he was not like the senior Angler, who seemed content to sit and fish for a lifetime.

"Let me think again, let me think again," Zhang Fan was unsure of his decision for a while.

Xuanyuan Hong did not urge him, but it seemed he had already foreseen Zhang Fan's final decision. In this world, time seemed to have stopped. The Angler and the newly captured stone slab, one large and one small figure, were always seated and fishing. Xuanyuan Hong spent most of his time with his Dao Companion, occasionally checking on Zhang Fan. As for the other seniors Xuanyuan Hong mentioned, Zhang Fan did not find them. He assumed they did not wish to be disturbed.

There were living beings in this place, but they had extremely long lifespans, with no signs of aging before the destruction of Mountains and Seas. This world itself seemed to possess life, its size and scale growing daily. Resources were inexhaustible. In a sense, it could indeed be called a paradise. There should be no reason to find fault. But… Ten years passed, a hundred years passed, and Zhang Fan still could not adapt. Even though he lived a carefree life every day, he always felt constrained.

Eight hundred years later, Zhang Fan finally couldn't stand it. He came before Xuanyuan Hong, his expression solemn.

"It seems you've made up your mind," Xuanyuan Hong said with emotion, having anticipated his arrival.

Zhang Fan nodded.

"You must think carefully. Once you leave here, you won't have another chance to return," Xuanyuan Hong said very solemnly.

Zhang Fan could not truly grasp the meaning of his words. After eight hundred years of confinement, and now freed, his heart was like a wild horse that had broken free from its reins, eager to gallop.

"My mind is made up. I will never regret it."

"Alright," Xuanyuan Hong sighed softly.

"When do you depart?" he asked again.

"Now," Zhang Fan said in a deep voice. "I fear that if I linger any longer, my will might wane, and I won't have this resolve." He explained.

"Very well. Then I shall escort you on your final journey. The road ahead is difficult, and I cannot help you further."

Accompanied by Xuanyuan Hong, Zhang Fan walked out of that illusory sky. Once again feeling the immense pressure of Dao Annihilation, a primal fear arose in Zhang Fan's heart. But at the same time, he felt a sense of absolute freedom, like a fish leaping in a boundless sea and a bird soaring in the high heavens. He just wanted to let out a wild roar to vent his exhilaration.

Xuanyuan Hong let Zhang Fan express his emotions freely. At their farewell, he handed Zhang Fan a jade pendant.

"If you encounter a life-threatening crisis, this jade pendant can shield you from one calamity."

"However, it can only withstand one instance."

"As for where you go from here, it is all up to your own destiny."

Zhang Fan thanked him profusely and bid farewell to Xuanyuan Hong. Crossing the Dao Annihilation, he walked on the waves within Mountains and Seas. As for where he came from, along with Xuanyuan Hong, it suddenly vanished into the depths of Mountains and Seas.

Within that world, Xuanyuan Hong, the Angler, the Everlasting Guest, and three other figures all looked up simultaneously. Their gaze swept towards the world of the "God Slayer Transformation" where Li Fan's true body resided, and the "True Return" figure. Although they couldn't pinpoint the exact location, they had locked onto the general area.

Zhang Fan had been in this realm for thousands of years. Although his true origins were not fully understood, a general outline was known. "Actually, Brother Zhang is quite a good person. It's a pity that there will never be another Zhang Fan to come here."

"After all, it is the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. To break through the blockade and descend from the void realm in an instant is not something to be ashamed of. Fortunately, I have already perfected this realm's defenses, and no more pawns will enter."

"Unless that person comes in person."

"Senior Broken Formation, you have worked hard," Xuanyuan Hong said.

The gaze of Broken Formation, however, never left the direction of the "God Slayer Transformation." After a long silence, he said with a hint of loss, "In the past, it seems I fought alongside him. Alas, now I have lost my courage." Saying so, he produced a wine gourd and drank it down.

"In the past, we believed that the continuation of Mountains and Seas was the natural order. Not only you, but who among us hasn't fought to save the world?"

"But in reality, reincarnation is the true destiny of this realm. Those who try to break reincarnation are the anomalies. Broken Formation, haven't you seen through this yet?"

A voice came, and Broken Formation merely snorted and took another swig.

"Forgotten Wisdom Old Man, you talk too much."

"Knowing is one thing, accepting it is another."

"Besides, when we built this sanctuary together, we never agreed that we couldn't break out!"

...At this moment, the atmosphere turned cold.

"Ha, they took the bait!" It was the Angler's cheer that broke the stalemate. After toying with the hooked fish for a bit, he casually tossed it back into the Mountains and Seas fishery. The Angler stopped fishing and stood up. He joined the group of old friends.

All eyes instantly focused on him.

"The unchanging is momentary. The changing is eternal."

"Our abode here is merely waiting for the opportune moment. If it's possible, we'll act. If not, we'll continue to rest. Why argue?" the Angler said calmly.

"One must know that there are more than just us hiding in Mountains and Seas, waiting for the true variable," the Angler's gaze seemed to pierce through the undercurrents of the Mountains and Seas fishery, reaching all corners of Mountains and Seas.

"Our combined strength is probably less than even one of theirs," he chuckled self-deprecatingly.

Xuanyuan Hong repeatedly said, "Senior Angler is too modest. Although all Saints are equal except for the True God, you were all once beings who had [Become Gods]. If we were to truly fight, none of us would fear anyone."

"Become Gods…"

These words seemed to stir ancient memories in everyone present, plunging them back into silence.

"At the beginning of time, in the Primordial Era, the Saints fought incessantly, all for the sake of seizing the creation of Mountains and Seas and achieving Sainthood."

"We lost ourselves in that pursuit, just like we did back then."

"No amount of persuasion was useful. Only after truly becoming a god and experiencing everything can one understand."

"Except for you, young Xuanyuan." The Angler walked to a visually pleasing spot in the heavens and earth and sat down again. He grabbed the stone slab, which had been utterly stunned by overhearing this shocking secret, and began fishing again.

Xuanyuan Hong gave a wry smile, "Compared to you seniors, I merely have self-awareness."

"Countless cycles of reincarnation, the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. Perhaps this time, there will be a variable. Let fate take its course. We cannot resist it anyway."

"However, this time, I feel it might truly be different."

After a period of discussion, the Saints dispersed, hiding themselves in the world.

"It's just a pity about Brother Zhang."

"He was indeed a good person. I wonder if we will ever meet again," Xuan Tianwang sighed.

…

Zhang Fan, who had traveled far away from this realm, was naturally unaware of all this. He had gradually recovered from the initial excitement of his departure. Although he wouldn't admit it, he was already starting to regret his decision. The peril and boundlessness of Dao Annihilation had far exceeded his expectations. Seeing it was one thing; experiencing it firsthand was another. Simply finding another potential place to live had drained almost all of Zhang Fan's strength.

"If Dao Annihilation within Mountains and Seas is already this dangerous, how much more perilous is the void realm outside Mountains and Seas?" Zhang Fan's heart became increasingly terrified. But there was no turning back. Zhang Fan could no longer find the path he came from and could only push forward.

"Fortunately, 'True Return' still has over ninety uses left."

Just as Zhang Fan was feeling fortunate, his expression suddenly changed drastically.

"Someone else nearby also possesses 'True Return'? And I can't use it temporarily?"

"What does this mean?" At this moment, Zhang Fan was under even greater impact than when he first saw the truth of Mountains and Seas' annihilation. From his birth, possessing the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, he had always believed himself to be the protagonist, the chosen one. Thus, even if his cheat was discovered, he could still remain unharmed. Unexpectedly, shortly after leaving the beginner's village, he encountered someone with the same template as himself.

"What exactly is going on?" Zhang Fan was both shocked and angry. But before he could ponder, the surrounding possibilities had already erupted into flames. Under the searing flames that could scorch the heavens and destroy the earth, Zhang Fan was forced to reveal himself.

"Fellow Daoist, wait…" Zhang Fan still wanted to discuss their similar predicaments with the other party. However, the person who also carried "True Return" had no intention of communicating with him. Not only did the offensive not cease, but it intensified. The surrounding flames possessed the power to incinerate the heavens and extinguish the earth. Even the waves of Dao Annihilation were temporarily suppressed by the inferno.

Zhang Fan tried to escape, but no matter how he tried, he could not break free from the fiery blockade. "They truly intend to kill me!" Zhang Fan finally realized. In this moment of life and death, a cold glint flashed in his eyes.

"In that case, don't blame me!" Having lived in a protected world for many years, without worries of life and death, his cultivation and combat skills had become complacent. But after all, there were too many powerful beings around him. Zhang Fan's occasional inquiries had yielded him opportunities and fortunes that others could hardly attain in a lifetime.

"The bait is willing!" Zhang Fan narrowed his eyes, his gaze seeming to pierce through the sea of flames, finding the person hidden behind the scenes. Using his hand as a fishing rod, he gently cast it.

The rod landed, and a catch! As if by pure reason, Lin Fan, who had scattered the sea of flames, was captured by Zhang Fan. His face was filled with shock. Instinctively wanting to struggle, he found himself completely immobilized, as if bound by countless fishing lines.

The enemy was instantly captured. Just as Zhang Fan was about to kill him, he hesitated. After all, he had never killed anyone in his life. Moreover, the opponent not only shared a similar fate but also had a faint resonance in spirit.

"We must have some connection." Zhang Fan pondered inwardly. Just as he was hesitating, a gust of wind seemed to pass before him. The captured Lin Fan, as if burned to ashes by the fierce flames, turned into bits of flying ash. Zhang Fan was shocked. Before he could react, a wisp of black flame struck him directly in the center of his eyebrows.

"I'm going to perish here?" In Zhang Fan's mind, scenes of the past flashed by. He felt regret, a sense of loss, and anger towards this sneak attacker. Just as the black flame was about to incinerate Zhang Fan's soul, a green light flickered, blocking all harm.

"Brother Xuanyuan!" Zhang Fan instantly reacted. The one who saved his life was the jade pendant Xuanyuan Hong had given him before he left. He had thought that with "True Return" in hand, he would never need to use this treasure. He never expected that halfway through his journey, it would be triggered. Knowing that he would not get a second chance, Zhang Fan gritted his teeth.

"Life and Death Split!" As the words fell, Zhang Fan seemed to split into two. One was filled with death energy, like a zombie that had slept for ten thousand years. The other was brimming with life force, like an ancient green wood. The death avatar slashed its own head fiercely. As the head was severed, the distant Lin Fan also let out a scream simultaneously. His head was inexplicably cut off as well. It wasn't just the physical body. Even their souls and wills were separated by this linked strike. It fell into Zhang Fan's hands.

"Die!" Zhang Fan no longer hesitated. The death avatar pointed a finger at the center of its severed head. Its body shattered into pieces, taking the formidable enemy Lin Fan with it. The demise of the death avatar did not affect Zhang Fan's actual survival. The boundless green life force nourished him, allowing him to quickly recover from his injuries. The psychological impact of this battle far surpassed that on his body and soul. However, there was a gain.

"True Return" could be activated again, temporarily averting danger. And… "I can feel that the True Return power of the opponent has been absorbed by me." Zhang Fan closed his eyes, sensing the growth of a strange energy within him.

"Senior Angler mentioned more than once that True Return is actually the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood."

"I also privately asked Brother Xuanyuan. It seems only I can comprehend and practice this Dao. Even someone as talented as him cannot grasp it at all."

"Now, another person has appeared."

"And there are far more than just one."

After killing Lin Fan, Zhang Fan also intercepted some of his memories. Before encountering him, Lin Fan had already encountered three other individuals who also possessed "True Return." Lin Fan had defeated them all, but ultimately fell to him.

"This person's secondary cultivation is the Great Dao of Blazing Silence Fire…"

"Mediocre." Zhang Fan frowned slightly, then relaxed. According to Lin Fan's memories, this Dao was already among the highest-ranking in Mountains and Seas, something ordinary cultivators could never attain in their lifetime.

"I already vaguely knew that Senior Angler's identity was extraordinary, but I never imagined it might be even more extraordinary than I thought…" Only now did the belated Zhang Fan begin to understand what Xuanyuan Hong meant by "you can never go back." But after a moment of regret, Zhang Fan's will quickly strengthened.

"Compared to eternal peace, it is this kind of killing and plunder…"

"More suits me." Even though this battle yielded no substantial gains, Zhang Fan felt an indescribable excitement from the depths of his heart.

"Let me see how many more people like me are there in this vast Mountains and Seas!"

"I will kill whoever I meet, until…"

"I find the mastermind behind this!" Even though Zhang Fan didn't understand, he was likely caught in a vast conspiracy. He wanted to break free, he wanted revenge!

Chapter 1768: Slaying the Lord of Fate

To have ambitions is good, but things don't always go as smoothly as one might think.

Those who can rise from obscurity with "True Return" are all extraordinary individuals.

Zhang Fan's ability to successfully defeat Lin Fan relied on his divine abilities, but victory in a life-or-death struggle is determined by more than just divine abilities.

Since the one encounter where he was accidentally let go, the ultimate techniques he learned from the protected world had spread throughout Mountains and Seas.

Now, everyone knew he possessed divine abilities like "The Bait is Willing," "Life and Death Separation," and "Heavenly Fortune Devourer."

From afar, they were already on guard, and he often faced attacks from multiple individuals.

In contrast, Zhang Fan was often unaware of the other Heaven-Sent Children and was at a disadvantage.

"Damn it, I should have been more ruthless back then!"

Recalling this, Zhang Fan was filled with regret.

However, he couldn't completely blame himself.

Who knew that the person named Zhou Fan was 99.9% similar to him?

Even at close range, he could vaguely sense each other's thoughts, as if they were the same person.

When the other party's soul was almost extinguished, Zhang Fan also felt as if he had experienced it.

Terribly shocked, he felt a flicker of sympathy for himself and hesitated.

Zhang Fan's mind was shaken, and his killing move faltered.

Zhou Fan seized the moment of his daze and broke free, escaping at lightning speed.

"You wait! I will definitely get revenge for this!"

The resentful voice of the other party still echoed in his ears.

At that time, Zhang Fan never imagined how much trouble this fleeing figure would cause him.

"Fortunately, I still have a trump card, "Reincarnation Annihilation," which I've never used before. It might serve as a last resort for a desperate struggle."

"However, no matter how strong it is, it can't withstand such a war of attrition. I can only hide for now."

"But hiding forever isn't a solution. Sooner or later, others will find out."

Illusory and stealthy techniques were effective against other cultivators, but for these Heaven-Sent Children with the same "True Return," they were practically useless.

Heaven-Sent Children was the general term for all cultivators who possessed "True Return."

It was unclear who first coined the term, but with the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood in hand, they could indeed be called children of destiny.

Everyone was satisfied with this term and got used to it.

When two Heaven-Sent Children met, even from a great distance, their "True Return" and soul's similarity would allow them to sense each other immediately.

What made Zhang Fan even more frustrated was that Zhou Fan, through unknown means, seemed to have directly marked him as "Zhang Fan" among all the Heaven-Sent Children.

Whenever other Heaven-Sent Children encountered him, even if they had never met or heard of Zhang Fan before, all of Zhang Fan's information would spontaneously appear in their minds after a moment.

Moreover, this public announcement of information seemed to be shared and constantly updated.

Initially, Zhang Fan didn't realize this.

In a deathmatch, his divine abilities "The Bait is Willing" and "Life and Death Separation" were repeatedly deciphered by the opponent, and he gradually fell into a disadvantage.

Then, he used "Heavenly Fortune Devourer" for the first time to turn the tide and kill the opponent.

Zhang Fan was sure that he had thoroughly destroyed the corpse and cleaned up the surrounding possibilities, leaving no witnesses.

However, when he encountered other Heaven-Sent Children later, they were all prepared for "Heavenly Fortune Devourer."

They carried filthy items with them and used methods to defile their own luck, thus countering Zhang Fan's divine ability.

This caused Zhang Fan to suffer greatly, and his injuries had not yet recovered.

He could only temporarily hide in an ordinary mortal possibility to absorb the luck of living beings and slowly recover.

"This public announcement of information must be Zhou Fan's doing."

"This kind of cognition only exists among Heaven-Sent Children; it doesn't affect other cultivators."

Zhang Fan had confirmed this through extensive soul searching.

"It's likely that he used some similar characteristic of ours. This characteristic might be the fundamental reason why we all carry True Return, and it might even be related to the entire conspiracy behind the scenes..."

Realizing this, Zhang Fan was shocked to discover how little he understood himself.

"Where did True Return come from? Where did I come from?"

Zhang Fan forgot his former ambitions and the dangers lurking outside.

He was immersed in his heart, seeking the answer to this question.

To see the heart and awaken the nature, to observe oneself.

This might be extremely difficult for others, but for Zhang Fan, it was inexplicably easy.

Zhang Fan vaguely sensed that it might be related to his time living in the protected world.

"There, heaven and earth grew infinitely, and all beings had no worries of aging, likely blessed by the Great Dao of Longevity."

"Moreover, I lived there for a long time and encountered almost no conflict or killing. It was likely that some kind of great Dao power subtly changed and nourished the disposition of all things."

Although he hadn't been away for long in reality, after experiencing life-and-death battles consecutively, Zhang Fan had already undergone a transformation.

Looking back at the things he had taken for granted, he now realized something was amiss.

The longing for the newbie village existed only in his mind for a moment.

Zhang Fan's thoughts sank deep, as if facing his own soul.

It was smooth and transparent, as if it encompassed all wonders of the world, yet it seemed to have no fundamental difference from the countless beings in Mountains and Seas.

"Where is the connection?"

Zhang Fan tried to examine himself from an outsider's perspective.

In an instant, it was as if he split into two.

One returned to his own body, while the other floated out, observing from a distance.

Slowly, Zhang Fan's heart dawned with understanding.

"Those who are ordinary, Zhang Fan, all belong to you."

"I, who am extraordinary, all belong to me."

As he spoke these inexplicable words, it was as if a transparent white light floated out from the observing him and returned to the body of the meditating "Zhang Fan."

In that instant, Zhang Fan seemed to escape the fate of a Heaven-Sent Child, able to observe himself from an "outsider's" perspective.

A thin thread, or countless threads representing destiny, extended from himself, connecting to countless different corners of Mountains and Seas.

And outside of Mountains and Seas...

In that unknowable place, all the threads converged in one spot!

Boom!

The observation lasted only for a moment before Zhang Fan was dragged back by a strong attraction from within his original body.

He spat out a mouthful of blood.

Foolishly moving his origin soul, this injury was far more severe than Zhang Fan had estimated.

He almost lost his Transcendent realm and fell to the Nameless realm.

Fortunately, it was all worth it.

In that fleeting glance, Zhang Fan not only saw a way to avoid "Omniscience" but also glimpsed the mastermind controlling all the Heaven-Sent Children!

"Unfortunately, I only know how to avoid the 'Omniscience' but not how to use this divine ability. Otherwise, I could directly publicize the mastermind's location, and everyone could go and kill him..."

Zhang Fan's expression shifted constantly.

He didn't realize that his thoughts had suddenly frozen.

A blurry figure crossed infinite time and space, descending before him.

It was "True Return"!

As the manipulator of Li Fan's plan, all the God Slayer Variants were under its control.

All actions, even thoughts, could not escape its perception.

Therefore, the moment Zhang Fan showed signs of losing control, it took action.

True Return did not expect to be able to see through the connection between the God Slayer Variants so quickly.

The power that caused Zhang Fan to deviate from himself seemed to linger in the air.

True Return gazed for a moment, then understood.

"Slaying the Fate Master."

It then looked towards the place where the God-Seer guests were located.

Without causing any ripples, the God-Seer guests and their created protected worlds quietly disappeared from Mountains and Seas ahead of schedule.

Then, True Return looked at the frozen Zhang Fan, hesitating for a moment.

Although this God Slayer Variant seemed to have lost control, who could guarantee that this was not also within the expected variables?

As True Return hesitated, Li Fan's voice suddenly appeared.

"Since it is a variable, it has a reason to exist."

"Let's see how far he can go."

The voice echoed, and True Return's figure had already disappeared, returning.

...

"Wouldn't it be faster if we all went together to capture the mastermind?"

Zhang Fan's thoughts resumed flowing.

He had not noticed True Return's arrival or his near-death experience from beginning to end.

After recovering slightly from his injuries, Zhang Fan began to recall the divine ability he had just comprehended to avoid the influence of "Omniscience."

"That feeling should originate from the butcher who occasionally handled the catches for the Old Fisherman."

The Old Fisherman of Mountains and Seas did not release all the fish he caught.

In very rare cases, he would encounter treasures he was satisfied with and keep them, like that stone tablet.

Before taking them away, he would often hand them over to a scruffy butcher.

Only after the butcher's decisive action would the Old Fisherman confidently store his treasures.

"This is too obvious; it's not an ordinary cultivator. Yet, before this, I had never noticed him and instinctively ignored him."

"Such power..."

Zhang Fan secretly marveled.

As the image of the butcher appeared in his mind, his feeling towards that path became even stronger.

The clean, decisive blade light flickered in Zhang Fan's mind.

Slowly, he also swung a knife through the air.

It was as if a single strand of hair fell off in response.

Then, thousands, tens of thousands, like snowflakes falling, descended.

Simultaneously, countless bloodstains appeared on Zhang Fan's body, the price for severing the connection of the Heaven-Sent Children.

But Zhang Fan was overjoyed instead of alarmed, a smile uncontrollable on his lips.

"The Fate Slaying Blade, a good name!"

Severing the shackles, eradicating destiny.

With a single strike, the bonds were broken.

The effect of "Omniscience" slowly disappeared.

The dark clouds that had lingered in Zhang Fan's mind for a long time finally dispersed.

An unprecedented sense of security enveloped him.

Zhang Fan fell into a deep sleep.

When he woke up, he was still alive, and his injuries had fully recovered.

"If there's a chance, I must go back and thank those seniors properly."

Zhang Fan mused.

He knew very well that the reason he could escape the fate of a Heaven-Sent Child was not because he was special, but entirely due to the subtle care he received from great beings like the Old Fisherman and Xuan Yuanhong during his time in the protected world.

"I wonder what their cultivation realms are?"

"Could they all be so-called Saints of Mountains and Seas?"

Zhang Fan pondered as he continued to sever all remaining connections.

When only one last thread remained, the Fate Slaying Blade hesitated, unable to fall.

The blade's light flickered, and Zhang Fan felt an indescribable fear, as if severing the thread meant his own death.

After hesitating for a long time, Zhang Fan finally chose to trust his intuition and did not force the action.

"It's not time yet."

"Perhaps when I prove myself as a Saint, I can truly wield this blade."

Zhang Fan seemed to have an epiphany.

"Speaking of which, am I truly exceptionally talented? This 'Fate Slaying Blade' divine ability is profound and mysterious, yet I comprehended it so smoothly, and it feels more natural to use. As for other divine abilities..."

Zhang Fan couldn't understand it no matter how hard he thought, so he could only attribute it to the hidden guidance of the great beings.

He would never have imagined that all the God-Seer guests, including the Old Fisherman, had now been erased by "True Return."

All the Great Daos had temporarily become masterless.

As the only one in Mountains and Seas currently connected to these Great Daos, he naturally benefited greatly from their inheritance, making comprehension exceptionally smooth.

Zhang Fan didn't think that much.

His current priority was to find Zhou Fan and exact revenge.

"Now, it's my turn to hide in the shadows. I hope you don't get caught too easily."

Zhang Fan squinted, a cold glint flashing in his eyes.

Zhou Fan's "Omniscience" divine ability had truly caused him a lot of trouble.

If he didn't get revenge, wouldn't that be inhumane?

Soon, Zhang Fan left the mortal realm where he was recuperating and began searching for Zhou Fan's whereabouts in secret.

However, Zhou Fan was indeed cautious.

Relying on the mutual sensing of "True Return," Zhang Fan had already eliminated nearly a hundred Heaven-Sent Children, but he still hadn't found Zhou Fan's trace.

The number of Heaven-Sent Children had drastically reduced in a short period, and everyone had realized something was wrong.

They all stopped acting ostentatiously and went into hiding.

This caused Zhang Fan's revenge journey to suffer another setback.

The turbulent Mountains and Seas unexpectedly fell into an eerie calm.

After painstakingly finding another Heaven-Sent Child and killing him, Zhang Fan was suddenly shocked.

"Strange, the number of disappearances in such a short time is too large."

"It doesn't add up..."

"Could it be that besides me, someone else is also hunting Heaven-Sent Children?"

His heart skipped a beat, as if confirming this guess.

Zhang Fan's expression turned serious.

"Who could it be?"

He didn't find this surprising.

After all, the number of Heaven-Sent Children appearing in such a short period was too large.

They attacked each other, disregarding the other cultivators in Mountains and Seas.

Moreover, all Heaven-Sent Children possessed the "True Return" treasure, so it was inevitable that they would be coveted.

"Those with the strength and motive should be the Saints of Mountains and Seas."

Once upon a time, Zhang Fan had wanted to cross the Dao Annihilation to visit the so-called Shore and the Holy Dynasty to admire the demeanor of the Saints.

Now, he had to avoid them at all costs.

"I am strong enough now. With divine abilities in hand, I can treat Transcendent cultivators like ants. However, I am not strong enough. Even though I haven't truly fought with a Saint, I know that I am no match for a Saint at this moment. Breaking through in a short time is hopeless. To protect myself, I still need to rely on the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood!"

After this period of killing, the "True Return" that Zhang Fan had absorbed and accumulated was quite substantial.

Chapter 1769: Abandoning the True Return

"True Return..." The more Zhang Fan comprehended it, the more unsettled he felt. He was amazed by the infinite mysteries of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, but he also felt a slight pang of sadness that it did not truly belong to him. It was like standing before an unparalleled beauty but only being able to admire her from afar.

As he felt a sense of loss, Zhang Fan's heart suddenly stirred: "However, who possesses the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is still unknown. Even if that mastermind views us as chess pieces, they still gave us the opportunity to interact with True Return."

"There is no wall in the world that cannot be dug through..." Zhang Fan quickly regained his spirits and dedicated himself to comprehending the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood. He was already on the verge of breaking free, and he realized that while direct plunder from other Heaven-Sent Children was one method of strengthening himself, self-comprehension was equally important, and perhaps even more "reliable."

With this belief, Zhang Fan entered a long period of secluded cultivation. Regardless of the treacherous storms raging outside, he remained steadfast in his pursuit of enlightenment.

Time flew by. The chess pieces scattered across Mountains and Seas by Li Fan gradually perished in silence. From their initial glorious presence across Mountains and Seas to the current mere handful clinging to survival, the change was surprisingly rapid. The fundamental reason was that "True Return" in a single time and place could not be called "True Return." Without the game-changing power to reset the entire Mountains and Seas in an instant, the countless powerful cultivators in Mountains and Seas had too many ways to deal with "True Return." It seemed like a slight numerical difference, but it was an essential distinction.

When Zhang Fan awoke from his deep slumber, he immediately recognized this point. He felt ashamed of his past arrogance and ignorance: "Indeed, a newborn calf is not afraid of a tiger. I thought having the advantage of True Return meant I could go anywhere in Mountains and Seas. In reality, even a Saint realm cultivator could probably break the protection of True Return and suppress it directly."

"And how many Saints are there in Mountains and Seas! If they joined forces..."

With a thought, Zhang Fan recited the seven words: "When truth becomes falsehood, falsehood also becomes truth!" As if from the perspective of "True Return," he saw through the entire Mountains and Seas, gaining a general understanding of the scattered Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood throughout.

"In the time I was in seclusion, the number of them has dwindled so much."

"No... there are still a large number gathered in one place!" Zhang Fan's expression changed. He didn't dare to look directly but could only sense it. While he was terrified, he also felt a sense of pity. So many Heaven-Sent Children gathered together in the past, what a lively scene. He had even thought of gathering them all to expose the mastermind. Now, it seemed...

"Having the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is indeed a rare treasure, but it brings disaster. The risks faced are truly terrifying. With the Saints watching covetously, ordinary Heaven-Sent Children have no good way to escape."

Thinking of this, Zhang Fan's resolve from his recent seclusion grew even stronger. That was... He wanted to abandon the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood and instead comprehend other paths that truly belonged to him!

This decision, even in Zhang Fan's own opinion, was incredibly unreasonable. A supreme Great Dao was within reach, yet he chose to abandon it for lesser paths? It was utter folly. But Zhang Fan knew he had reasons to do so.

"Because 'True Return' ultimately does not belong to me!"

Zhang Fan sighed again. After a long period of secluded cultivation, no matter how hard he tried to grasp it, the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood did not seem any closer. It also did not distance itself. Instead, it remained tantalizingly out of reach, as if it had been predetermined. After countless failures, Zhang Fan finally decided to give up.

"He who knows himself is wise."

"Giving up one mountain does not mean losing all the mountains in the world. Perhaps I can find the mountain that truly belongs to me..." Zhang Fan tried to convince himself.

Although he had officially decided to abandon comprehending the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, it did not prevent him from continuing to use "True Return" as a "convenient tool."

"Perhaps a 'True Return' in a single time and place cannot completely turn the tide, but releasing it in a life-or-death crisis will always cause some interference."

"Moreover, all Saints believe that the biggest trump card of the Heaven-Sent Children is True Return. Perhaps this is my opportunity..." Zhang Fan's eyes flickered.

With a breath, a wooden fishing rod materialized in his hand. Simultaneously, a silver vortex appeared between his brows, and he seemed to hear the slow sound of a whetstone grinding. During his seclusion, although he did not actively seek to comprehend these paths, they actively gravitated towards him, strengthening their connection with Zhang Fan invisibly. He felt as if he had returned to that protected place, living comfortably with the Old Fisherman, Xuan Yuanhong, and others. He had desperately sought something but failed. Now, without seeking, blessings arrived. This was also one of the main reasons for Zhang Fan's change in perspective.

Zhang Fan was not dull. He had already vaguely guessed the reason for these Great Daos' changes. "It's probably because of me that they perished." He felt no great sorrow in his heart, only a sense of wistful regret. However, he quickly cast aside all emotions and began to comprehend the Great Daos entangled with his own being.

"Apart from the Great Dao of Longevity, which is not with me."

"All others are gathering towards me spontaneously??"

"Fate Slaying, Fishing, Formation Breaking, Forgetfulness, Marvelous Fortune, Paper Folding."

Zhang Fan found all these mysterious Great Daos not obscure or difficult, but familiar and intimate. "Perhaps compared to the complete Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, they are far inferior." "But compared to the incomplete True Return..." "They are actually stronger!" "Better one bird in hand than ten in the bush!"

Zhang Fan gritted his teeth and finally made his decision. In an instant, it was as if his obsession was severed. Zhang Fan felt completely relaxed. The complex emotions he had previously felt towards "True Return" completely vanished, leaving only a sense of acceptance of fate. "If you are in my hand, I will treat you as a convenient tool. If you are gone..." "Then consider the tool broken."

Zhang Fan smiled faintly. Although he had spent years trying to comprehend the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, only to decide to switch paths, it wasn't a waste of time. Zhang Fan vaguely sensed that the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood shared many similarities with the Great Daos of Fate Slaying, Fishing, and others entangled with him. "Or rather, the relationship between the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood and all the Great Daos of Mountains and Seas is similar. It's like the foundation of Mountains and Seas. Comprehending the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood first, then comprehending other Great Daos, can yield twice the result with half the effort. Conversely, if one fully grasms all other Great Daos of Mountains and Seas, then the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood will also become more proficient."

Zhang Fan mused, and then entered seclusion again. Originally, the various Great Daos on him were separate. But as time passed, Fishing, Fate Slaying, Marvelous Fortune, Paper Folding, and others began to fuse together. The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood acted as their fusion agent, causing these Great Daos, which once belonged to the God-Seer Guests of Mountains and Seas, to all converge upon Zhang Fan.

As multiple Great Daos fused, especially those from Mountains and Seas, the process required an extremely long time, measured by the lifespan of Mountains and Seas. Zhang Fan seemed to have fallen into a deep slumber. And the Marvelous Fortune of Mountains and Seas also seemed to be at play. Zhang Fan sat there quietly, comprehending his Daos. In the long passage of time, vast consciousnesses swept over him but never discovered Zhang Fan's trace.

After an unknown period, all of Zhang Fan's aura was retracted, and he seemed to have vanished from Mountains and Seas. The lifespan of Mountains and Seas was also nearing its end. Marvelous Fortune could no longer protect his current possibility, and Dao Annihilation descended like a whale. However, the Dao Annihilation that could devour Mountains and Seas had no effect on Zhang Fan. The dark waves churned, passing through him without leaving a trace.

However, sensing the anomaly around him, Zhang Fan finally woke up leisurely. "Hmm? How long did I sleep?" Zhang Fan was somewhat surprised, but after sensing his current realm, all emotions vanished. "I've already become a Saint?"

Zhang Fan felt a strange sense of bewilderment as he felt his current state. The seemingly endless Mountains and Seas he saw in the past no longer appeared majestic and imposing in his vision. He could bear them on his shoulders, standing shoulder to shoulder with them. "Mountains and Seas are nothing more than this."

Zhang Fan couldn't help but think this. The breakthrough from Transcendent to Saint realm should have been a world-shattering event. However, for Zhang Fan, it happened so silently and naturally, as if it were a matter of course, without any movement or even a fluctuation in his aura. He had become a Saint. To be honest, Zhang Fan felt a sense of disappointment for not experiencing the thrilling moment of becoming a Saint.

"Fortunately, I've finally completed this step."

"Now, I have enough strength. I no longer need to fear anyone in Mountains and Seas."

Originally, Zhang Fan thought he would first confront the mastermind in the place he had sensed, but after realizing the near-extinction of the Heaven-Sent Children and the great convergence of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood nearby, he changed his mind. "Someone has to seek justice for you." "I, the one who survived, will do it."

Zhang Fan took a light step and walked towards the depths of Mountains and Seas. The Saints were gathered there, but all their attention was focused on a certain spot. They did not react at all to Zhang Fan's quiet arrival.

Zhang Fan's gaze followed theirs. A towering tree stood in the void. Countless figures hung upside down from it, like ripening fruit. The faint or strong auras of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood emanating from them undoubtedly revealed their identities. Heaven-Sent Children! Zhang Fan also recognized many familiar people among the countless figures, including Zhou Fan, who had used the "Omniscience" divine ability and caused him so much trouble. However, it was countless years ago, and the resentment in Zhang Fan's heart had long since faded. There was no hatred, only deep sorrow for his fellow Heaven-Sent Children.

Although they still possessed "True Return" and seemed to have the power to start anew at any time, all the Heaven-Sent Children had fallen into a powerful illusion. This was a net woven by the Saints of Mountains and Seas, influencing and distorting the perceptions of the Heaven-Sent Children. The worlds they experienced were not real. The "True Return" they thought they had activated had, in fact, not been activated at all.

"The Saints are doing this..." "Trying to use the bodies of the Heaven-Sent Children to comprehend the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood?"

Zhang Fan initially thought so. But he soon realized something was wrong. No one knew the unfathomable nature of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood better than he did. Even by borrowing the experiences and sensations of the Heaven-Sent Children, they could not comprehend "Truth" or "Falsehood" at all. Zhang Fan was certain that any attempt to comprehend "True Return" would be futile.

"Except for the Lord of True Return, no one else in this world can truly comprehend and control the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood."

"After all these years, with the talents of the Saints, they couldn't have failed to realize this. So, they are..."

What happened next answered Zhang Fan's question. Mountains and Seas entered their end times, Dao Annihilation raged and churned relentlessly. But the Saints were not panicked at all. From the tree hanging with Heaven-Sent Children, faint fluctuations gradually emanated. Zhang Fan was naturally familiar with this.

"True Return?!" he exclaimed in shock. A faint light surged, and the Mountains and Seas, which had been swallowed by Dao Annihilation, reappeared as if returning. It was as if Mountains and Seas had been reset. But the colossal tree hanging with countless Heaven-Sent Children remained. The Saints were still there. The Mountains and Seas, which should have been destroyed, welcomed a glimmer of life due to this reset.

"But what is the point of doing this?" Zhang Fan was somewhat confused.

"As long as they are alive, there is meaning," a voice said.

The gazes of all the Saints turned towards Zhang Fan. "Who are you?"

Zhang Fan looked at the young man who appeared before him, filled with wariness. "Qiu Xin Hui," the young man simply said. Then he asked, "Are you here to avenge them?"

His motive was exposed, but Zhang Fan did not admit it, only snorted coldly, "I am here to liberate them!" Although Zhang Fan felt that with his current strength, he could contend with any Saint, he still felt a sense of crisis from this young man. Therefore, he did not act immediately but chose to observe the situation. For some reason, Qiu Xin Hui's words gave him a strange sense of familiarity.

"Liberation..." Qiu Xin Hui smiled again. He repeated, "As long as they are alive, there is meaning. Do you think... 'they' truly want to be liberated?"

Fearing that he might not be able to out-argue the other party, Zhang Fan narrowed his eyes, "Whether they want it or not, I decide!" "What, are you going to stop me?"

Facing the Saints present, Zhang Fan felt neither fear nor excitement. He felt a strange sense of exhilaration. His life had been too boring. He had barely left the nascent stage before being suppressed by great beings like the Old Fisherman, forced to stay obediently in the newbie village. After finally emerging, although he experienced a brief period of fighting, most of his subsequent days were spent in hiding and seclusion. Experientially, his life had not even reached a hundred years. It could be said to be very plain. Now that he had finally achieved success in his cultivation and had the strength to contend with the Saints of Mountains and Seas, why would he miss such an opportunity? This was also why he had to come here first. His heart was restless. In his vision, blades of light were already appearing above the Saints' heads.

Just then, a pale dot suddenly appeared in his vision. The light of the Fate Slaying Blade dimmed completely. Zhang Fan's heart suddenly lurched, but he felt a hand rest on his shoulder. "Let's talk things through properly, no need to hurt our camaraderie." "After all, our goal is the same."

Although the other party did not explicitly state it, Zhang Fan knew who "our goal" referred to. The mastermind who created countless "Heaven-Sent Children."

Chapter 1770: True Departure Hidden

"Who are you?"

The hand resting on his shoulder was ice-cold, freezing even his life force. Even though Zhang Fan instantly protected himself with the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, he could not escape the dissipation of his vitality. Although he had reached the Saint realm, Zhang Fan had rarely engaged in combat throughout his life. Thus, in this first battle after becoming a Saint, he suffered a slight disadvantage. Fortunately, although he had not proven his Dao with "Longevity," he had benefited greatly from it. The gentle power of longevity, like a clear stream in spring, resisted the complete descent of the ice.

Zhang Fan, who had gradually recovered from the surprise attack, his face turned cold, his gaze like a blade, instantly locking onto the target. Even though he didn't know the other party's identity or name, as long as they were within his senses, the Fate Slaying Blade could strike! And not just one.

A slender, jade-like hand appeared out of thin air, gently gripping the Fate Slaying Blade. Then, like folding white paper, the Fate Slaying Blade split into two, then eight. In just a breath, rain-like blades fell menacingly!

"Who are you!?"

"Who are you!?"

"Who are you!?"

These were questions and doubts. They inquired about the other party's identity and questioned their existence. The sound echoed like thunder, constantly reverberating and striking down, aiming to obliterate the other party.

Folding Paper fused with Fate Slaying, Forgetfulness fused with Truth and Falsehood. The moment Zhang Fan saw that pale dot, he instinctively knew the other party was powerful. Thus, he unleashed all his divine abilities as a sign of respect!

The pale dot let out a muffled groan, and the hand on Zhang Fan's shoulder disappeared. However, the radiant light it emitted remained bright and stable, completely unaffected by Zhang Fan's various Great Daos! Although all his divine abilities accurately locked onto the target, for some reason, they did not exert their intended effect.

"This feeling, the protection of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood?"

Zhang Fan was instantly shocked. But a moment later, he realized the difference. "It's not that it's unaffected, but rather, he seems to have experienced and endured all these divine abilities countless times before. He's already accustomed to it, so he receives them as if he hasn't!"

Zhang Fan vaguely felt that the strength of this pale dot might be even more unfathomable than he had imagined. Therefore, after forcing it back, he did not rashly attack again. The pale light gradually dimmed, revealing its true appearance. A simple, lean middle-aged man.

"I am Zhen Shi Yin," the man said, cupping his hands and smiling faintly.

"Zhen Shi Yin?" The moment these three words appeared in his mind, Zhang Fan felt his comprehension of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood subtly stirred, as if this lean middle-aged man was somehow related to "True Return."

Zhen Shi Yin looked no different from an ordinary person, but just by standing there, he exuded a subtle pressure on Zhang Fan. Zhang Fan calmly retreated a slight distance, feigning ignorance, and asked, "May I ask what you mean by the 'mastermind' you mentioned earlier?"

Zhen Shi Yin did not expose Zhang Fan's pretense of ignorance but directly stated, "The mastermind behind this chaos in the Star Sea is naturally the Lord of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood."

"As for you, and them..."

"You are merely his creations, his avatars."

"Avatars? Avatars..." Zhang Fan was stunned. "Avatars? So that's how it is." He then seemed to awaken from a dream, understanding everything. It was like the saying, "You cannot see the true face of Mount Lu, only because you are on the mountain yourself." Zhang Fan had vaguely glimpsed the potential mastermind and even managed to break free from his predetermined fate and comprehend various extraordinary Daos of Mountains and Seas to reach the Saint realm. However, he had always instinctively believed that the true mastermind was someone else, and subconsciously ignored the possibility that he himself was an avatar.

Now, Zhang Fan finally reacted. Perhaps it was due to the subtle influence of the Old Fisherman of Mountains and Seas, Xuan Yuanhong, and others. "It is precisely because I have always firmly believed that I am an independent being, not an avatar of someone else, that I was able to successfully inherit everyone's Daos and cultivate to become a Saint. If the thought of being someone else's avatar had ever crossed my mind, even for a moment, the path to becoming a Saint would have been cut off."

Zhang Fan, who was beginning to understand, felt a sense of relief. "Fellow Daoist, you likely already know that Mountains and Seas are in an endless cycle."

"Birth, destruction, endless reincarnation."

"The matter of truth and falsehood is inherently illusory."

"However, in countless experiences, this scene is truly the first time." Zhen Shi Yin pointed to the great tree standing in the void and said. "It is fortunate that this is the case; otherwise, we would not have the chance to observe the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood so closely."

Zhen Shi Yin's words carried a clear emotional fluctuation. Zhang Fan had only vaguely speculated about the cycle of Mountains and Seas. Now that it was confirmed by Zhen Shi Yin, he was not particularly surprised. His main focus was still on the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, so he asked, "Did you gain anything?"

Zhen Shi Yin smiled again, "If you can't see it, how can you gain anything?" "The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood only favors one person. Even if we try every method, we cannot touch it or comprehend it. Although I had this premonition before, only now have I truly given up hope."

"Then, in the recent small-scale reset of Mountains and Seas, why were you able to remain?" This was the only thing Zhang Fan could not understand.

"Our continued existence is not due to our own strength, but thanks to the merits of these countless Heaven-Sent Children," Zhen Shi Yin did not conceal anything. "Although we ourselves cannot comprehend or manipulate the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, we can affect and distort the thoughts of the Heaven-Sent Children, making them willingly apply the power of Truth and Falsehood to us." "Of course, in their dreams, they may not truly realize what they are doing."

Zhang Fan remained silent, looking again at the great tree built by countless "avatars" of himself. Zhen Shi Yin seemed to see through Zhang Fan's thoughts and suddenly suggested, "It is not impossible to free them. In fact, you could even be the one to personally end all of this."

Zhang Fan's heart stirred upon hearing this but he did not respond immediately. "The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is invisible and intangible. Although we can use it to some extent by borrowing from the Heaven-Sent Children, it has no practical significance. Conversely, if we can gain an ally who can turn the tide with this, it would be a worthwhile exchange."

Zhen Shi Yin's expression was calm, but his tone was sincere. "So, what is your goal?" Zhang Fan looked at him and asked.

"To seize the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood and regain divinity." Zhen Shi Yin only spoke eight words.
