Zhang Fan, however, fell into deep thought. After a long while, Zhang Fan finally voiced his doubts, "What is the difference between the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood being with me or with a god? It's all still the destruction of Mountains and Seas and reincarnation."

Zhen Shi Yin's gaze was distant. "Perhaps the past and present are indistinguishable. But the future..." He remained silent for a while, as if contemplating something. Only when he had finally determined his deduction did Zhen Shi Yin continue, "When the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood is with a god, the destruction of Mountains and Seas is not true destruction. Death is the beginning of life, and life is the beginning of death. Endless reincarnation, endless future."

"But if the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood is with him..." Zhen Shi Yin did not look at Zhang Fan. Instead, he looked up towards the approximate location of Li Fan's original body's cultivation world, "God Slayer Variant," outside the boundless Mountains and Seas, "Mountains and Seas will be completely destroyed, reincarnation will cease, and all will return to one person."

"This is the outcome we foresee."

Zhang Fan was deeply shaken by these words. "Reincarnation will cease, all returning to one person?" These eight words seemed to possess infinite power. Even though he was actually in the position of being subsumed, Zhang Fan couldn't help but be slightly dazed. But he quickly sobered up and asked in disbelief, "How can he achieve such a feat?"

Zhen Shi Yin nodded, "These countless split Heaven-Sent Children are the best proof. Although it's only just beginning to show, if we don't stop it..."

"Our only fate is destruction."

"Destruction..." Hearing this, Zhang Fan suddenly thought of the Old Fisherman, Xuan Yuanhong, and others who had mysteriously disappeared because of him. From this, he could glimpse the true modus operandi of "him" and began to believe him.

Zhang Fan then frowned and asked, "What kind of person is he? Since you know about the cycle of Mountains and Seas, you should be very familiar with him."

Zhen Shi Yin denied Zhang Fan's guess, "The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood governs the cycle of Mountains and Seas. Everything in Mountains and Seas is destined to be reset."

"Even the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is no exception!"

"Although we have some minor cultivation, how can we escape such a fate? It's just that due to too many cycles, a very small number of us can faintly sense something." "For example, we have a 'hunch' about past events, as if we have experienced them before. This premonition is weakest at the beginning of the reset of Mountains and Seas. Only as Mountains and Seas evolve and the sensation accumulates can we recall more. Therefore, even though I know about the cycle of Mountains and Seas now, after the reset, I will still lose all my awareness and repeat my past foolish actions..." Zhen Shi Yin said self-deprecatingly. "Even I am like this, let alone them." He was referring to the Saints who were still observing and comprehending under the great tree.

Hearing the tone of surprise in his words, Zhang Fan's expression became solemn, "May I ask, fellow Daoist, what is your realm?"

"We are all Saints. However, unlike most of them, I have achieved a 'Divine Body'." "You can call me a 'God-Conqueror Guest'."

God. Such a majestic and heavy word was spoken by Zhen Shi Yin so lightly and indifferently. Zhang Fan naturally knew that everything in Mountains and Seas originated from the fallen True God and understood the weight of the word "God." Thinking that the cultivator before him had once achieved the fruit of divinity, the invisible pressure he felt from him seemed to increase.

"Strictly speaking, it's not a true divinity," Zhen Shi Yin said with a sigh, as if sensing Zhang Fan's thoughts, and explained. "The cycle of Mountains and Seas should not have produced 'God-Conqueror Guests'."

"When the old god falls, Mountains and Seas appear. When Mountains and Seas perish, new gods emerge."

"It has always been new gods replacing old gods."

"Once divinity is achieved, it is eternal. Either you exist in the name of a god, or you perish and disappear."

"As for the so-called 'God-Conqueror Guests'..."

"They are the Saints of Mountains and Seas who, against the flow of time, plundered the creation of the old god during the fragmentation of Mountains and Seas. But they were then reset by the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood."

"Although they returned to the mortal realm, they had, for a time, existed in the name of a god, becoming subtly different from other beings in Mountains and Seas."

"But only subtly."

Zhen Shi Yin's lengthy explanation detailed the "God-Conqueror Guests." "Only God-Conqueror Guests can know the truth within the cycle of Mountains and Seas. If that's the case, then the Old Fisherman and Xuan Yuanhong... they might all be 'God-Conqueror Guests'?"

Zhang Fan, having understood the cause and effect, thought of his past close interactions with the God-Conqueror Guests and even took them for granted. The pressure he felt from Zhen Shi Yin suddenly diminished. As he breathed a sigh of relief, he was even more astonished by the power of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. Even though he had "possessed" it before and it was still with him, Zhang Fan felt that the power of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood was beyond his imagination.

Suddenly, he recalled a sentence Zhen Shi Yin had said earlier and felt something was amiss. "Fellow Daoist just mentioned that everything in Mountains and Seas is subject to reset, even the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. If that's the case..." Zhang Fan frowned. "Theoretically, shouldn't he also be reset along with it? How could he..."

Zhen Shi Yin's single sentence made Zhang Fan's words stop abruptly, and his doubts vanished: "That is because he is an 'outsider'."

"So that's how it is, so that's how it is." Zhang Fan muttered repeatedly.

Zhen Shi Yin's tone was distant. "In the past, at the end of Mountains and Seas, a group of God-Conqueror Guests who had regained most of their awareness gathered and discussed the source of the reset."

"But they could never figure it out."

"After all, we all possess divine bodies, yet we are repeatedly reset."

"Everything in the world originates from the god. Yet gods can be reset by the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. This seems entirely illogical."

"Then, as Mountains and Seas were destroyed again, we suddenly realized."

"'Truth and Falsehood' is a supreme power that even gods cannot escape."

"Although it originates from the True God's body, the True God himself is also affected by it."

"We speculate that this might be the True God's innate divine ability, and the fundamental origin of the cycle of Mountains and Seas."

"Even if they perish, they can reappear from the void through the Great Dao of 'Truth and Falsehood' and return to their original state. Immortal, indestructible, eternal—this is 'God'."

Through Zhen Shi Yin's descriptions, Zhang Fan seemed to vaguely glimpse the majesty of the True God who had given birth to everything in Mountains and Seas. But soon, the tone shifted drastically.

"If the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood resides within the god, then everything is easy to say."

"But..."

"For some reason, 'Truth and Falsehood' has fallen into the hands of an outsider."

"The divine authority has been usurped. Because it originated from the outside, it can avoid the fate of reset. The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood in his hands has an influence that surpasses that of 'God'."

Zhang Fan vaguely sensed a hint of fear in Zhen Shi Yin's words. "With just a single thought, he can reverse everything we know and return to the beginning. He can carry the memories of the past, while you remain ignorant."

"How can we possibly contend with such an opponent?"

"Throughout countless cycles, we could not see hope for breaking the deadlock. Until..."

"Your appearance."

Chapter 1771: Outer Body Vision

Outside Observation

"As for me..." Zhang Fan remained noncommittal, unfazed by Zhen Shi Yin's effusive praise.

In a sense, his stance was fundamentally aligned with Zhen Shi Yin's, and indeed with all beings in the Mountains and Seas. Mountains and Seas annihilated, reincarnation ceased, all returning to one. The actions of this Lord of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, performed in pursuit of enlightenment, were truly staggering.

Whether driven by self-preservation or the promptings of conscience, cultivators in the Mountains and Seas ought to unite and stop him.

That is, of course, assuming... Zhen Shi Yin's words were the whole truth. At Zhang Fan's current level, even without knowing the full story, he could intuitively judge the veracity of Zhen Shi Yin's statements.

"Zhen Shi Yin isn't lying," Zhang Fan mused. "But that doesn't mean he's telling the whole story."

Zhang Fan had his own deductions. It was simple: if everything were as Zhen Shi Yin claimed, then the Old Fisherman and Xuan Yuanhong would surely have stood with Zhen Shi Yin. But they hadn't; instead, they had merely created a protected world and quietly hidden themselves away.

Zhang Fan's decision, from beginning to end, remained unchanged. He would personally face the mastermind behind the scenes and demand an explanation!

However, in front of Zhen Shi Yin, Zhang Fan did not reveal his true intentions. Instead, he shook his head and said, "I am merely a clone, one of countless scattered chess pieces. If this Lord of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is truly as terrifying as you say, what role can I play? Even if we join forces and successfully kill him, don't you worry that I might become the new Lord of Truth and Falsehood, rendering all our efforts in vain?"

"Our current goal is already at the limit of our capabilities. Why would we seek further trouble by aiming for infinity? Besides... I don't think you would do that." Zhen Shi Yin looked at Zhang Fan intently. "Of all the Heaven-Sent Children, you are the only one willing to abandon the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. If I hadn't noticed this, we wouldn't be having this conversation."

Zhang Fan scoffed, "Then I'm afraid I will have to disappoint you. The reason I abandoned it was because I couldn't obtain it. Frankly, if the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood truly appeared before me, allowing me to grasp it, I would undoubtedly choose it without hesitation..."

Before Zhang Fan could finish speaking, Zhen Shi Yin interrupted, "But you have already abandoned it."

"Even a good horse doesn't eat its old grass, let alone the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood! Since you have actively chosen to abandon it, then even if one day the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood becomes masterless, it will certainly not choose someone who actively abandoned it..." Zhen Shi Yin said with utmost confidence. "At least, not in this lifetime."

Zhang Fan opened his mouth, speechless for a moment. Finally, he simply said, "This is likely just your speculation, Fellow Daoist?"

In truth, Zhang Fan already had a clear understanding. Zhen Shi Yin had chosen to cooperate with him entirely because he saw Zhang Fan as a clone of the Lord of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood and someone who couldn't inherit the "True Return." As for the chances of success? They had no other choice.

Since that was the case, Zhang Fan no longer stood on ceremony. "Since we've said all that, any further politeness would be an insult to you, Fellow Daoist." He gestured towards the great tree. "This tree is yours. From now on, let us form an alliance and work together to reclaim the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood."

As he spoke, the Saints of the Mountains and Seas, engrossed in their enlightenment, all turned their gazes towards Zhang Fan. Beneath their placid exteriors, a flicker of malice could be detected. Zhang Fan, however, remained unfazed, awaiting Zhen Shi Yin's decision.

There was little hesitation. It was clear Zhen Shi Yin held significant influence among the Saints. Despite his inner reluctance, the Saints meditating on the Great Dao made way, allowing Zhang Fan to approach the great tree from which countless Heaven-Sent Children hung like fruit.

"Aren't you afraid I'll go back on my word? You agreed so easily." To be honest, Zhang Fan was somewhat surprised by Zhen Shi Yin's decisiveness.

"We have no choice, and neither do you." Zhen Shi Yin stated.

Zhang Fan fell silent, finding no retort. With a sigh, he slowly opened his mouth. Using the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood as his hand, he gently brushed the fruits hanging from the great tree. A gentle breeze seemed to sweep across the remnants of the Mountains and Seas. Countless Heaven-Sent Children swayed with the wind, and then, one by one, they fell and vanished.

Simultaneously, Zhang Fan's aura grew increasingly ethereal. Although Zhang Fan had decided to abandon comprehending the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood upon becoming a Saint, he had not given up the idea of using it as a handy tool. Just like Zhen Shi Yin and the surviving Saints of the Mountains and Seas in this lifetime, but as a clone of the Lord of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, Zhang Fan could personally wield the power of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood.

As each fruit fell, the entire great tree withered. Its leaves turned yellow and fluttered away. Its branches snapped, falling into the void and turning to dust. Correspondingly... the lives of the observing Saints also began to wither, like flowers one by one. Facing death, the Saints showed little fear. They simply gazed at the scattered Truth and Falsehood in the void, calmly awaiting their fate.

"This..." Zhang Fan had not expected this tree to be sustained by the lives of the Saints. This also explained why the Saints had been able to maintain their forms during the previous reset of the Mountains and Seas. Although Zhang Fan had not killed the Saints, they died because of his single thought. After all, he had spent most of his life in secluded cultivation, and the only time he interacted with others was in an atmosphere of goodwill. Zhang Fan's heart was understandably shaken.

"It's nothing, just dying once more."

"Blessed by the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, although they may not be like me now, with eyes that can see through reincarnation. Still, they understood their fate, which is why they could face death so calmly."

"Whether our plan succeeds or fails, they will reappear with the reset of the Mountains and Seas," Zhen Shi Yin said softly, standing beside Zhang Fan. In fact, Zhang Fan's shock lasted only a few moments. His attention quickly shifted to the incoming Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. Originally originating from billions of Heaven-Sent Children, it now flowed like a gentle stream into Zhang Fan's mouth.

His vision gradually brightened. The desolate, apocalyptic Mountains and Seas were no longer shrouded in darkness; everything seemed to follow a discernible pattern. A scroll depicting all that once was in the Mountains and Seas appeared before Zhang Fan's eyes. However, as the Dao Annihilation encroached, the scenes within the scroll slowly became transparent. To ordinary mortals, the Mountains and Seas had vanished. But to the holder of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, merely by re-infusing power, the Mountains and Seas would reappear!

"This is the 'Outline of Mountains and Seas Changes'," Zhang Fan murmured, deeply fascinated by this wondrous sight.

This was not all. Outside the scroll of the Mountains and Seas, there seemed to be a figure, the 'scroll holder', standing tall. Everything within the scroll – its birth, death, and transformations – was under this person's control. After memorizing every detail within the scroll of the Mountains and Seas, Zhang Fan strained his gaze, attempting to pierce through the scroll's blockade and look at the scroll holder.

This act of transgression caused the scroll of the Mountains and Seas to tremble violently. The Mountains and Seas within his sight surged upwards, attempting to obscure Zhang Fan's prying eyes. Zhang Fan, wielding his mastery over the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, suppressed all these disturbances. His goal remained unchanged: to see the scroll holder beyond the scroll.

The clash between these two powers rent the scroll of the Mountains and Seas, shattering it inch by inch. Correspondingly, Zhang Fan's divine soul also seemed to develop countless tiny cracks, teetering on the brink of collapse. This was not mere injury, but a backlash from the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, causing his very foundation of existence to erode.

The Great Daos of Longevity and Forgetfulness worked desperately to repair the cracks in Zhang Fan's soul. Although their efforts were like throwing a bucket of water onto a burning house, they bought him precious time to continue his observation. Zhang Fan's gaze finally broke through the obstruction of the Mountains and Seas imagery, allowing him to see the scroll holder.

*Boom! Boom! Boom!* As if his soul had suffered a violent impact, all phenomena of the Mountains and Seas, and even the surrounding void's Dao Annihilation, faded into the background, becoming insignificant and disappearing from his sight. Even myriad Great Daos, including the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, seemed like mere passing clouds. In Zhang Fan's eyes, only one person remained.

At this moment, he saw himself. And... another looming phantom hovering above him.

The world of the God Slayer Incarnation.

As Zhang Fan, through the channel of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, managed to glimpse Li Fan. Li Fan, too, using the other's gaze, observed himself from an external perspective for the first time. Consequently, he also noticed the phantom perpetually present above his head.

Despite having stripped away all experiences and memories since his reincarnation, leaving only his purest original state as a traveler. Something unknown inexplicably remained above his head!

For some reason, Li Fan, upon witnessing this sudden sight, was not particularly surprised. Everything was as he had predicted. Indeed, if he had no contingency plan, it would have been inexplicable. "I only wonder if this phantom originated from my past self. Or... the fallen True God?"

The encounter between Li Fan and Zhang Fan lasted only a fleeting moment. After the "External Observation" vanished, Li Fan could no longer perceive the phantom that had always been above his head. It was as if it had never existed; even with the aid of the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, he could not recall it in his mind. Even the memory of this phantom's existence was slowly fading.

After attempting to halt this process and failing, Li Fan decided to seize the last few moments to deduce the phantom's origin as much as possible. He immediately ruled out his past self's involvement.

"My current understanding of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is nearly at its peak in the Mountains and Seas. Compared to my past self, I wouldn't be much weaker. I don't believe he possessed the power to achieve this level."

"Existing within the body without knowledge or sensation, invisible, unknowable, unmemorable."

"Beyond the Mountains and Seas, outside the realm of cognition."

"A phantom of the True God..." In an instant, Li Fan reached a conclusion. "Based on the knowledge I already have."

"This world exists within endless reincarnation. Even True Gods cannot live forever. As eons pass, new consciousnesses will differentiate within them. Whether this consciousness originates from swallowed gods or is a new evolution, in short, the old god falls, and the new god descends. This is destined."

"To say 'fallen,' it's more accurate to say 'returned.' Because... 'God' seems to be singular. Once divinity is achieved, one is a god. Reincarnation continues, and now, with the fragmentation of the Mountains and Seas, things have changed."

"The Mountains and Seas are merely two diverging intentions before the new god's evolution. Their sole purpose is a transition between the True God's fall and resurrection." "But they foresaw their own inevitable demise. Unwilling, they attempted to alter their fate." "They conceived a grand play, deceiving the heavens, transforming into the Star. If the play was perfectly executed, they would have replaced the god that was supposed to appear, becoming the new god..."

As he reached this point, Li Fan's thoughts slightly paused. The phantom of the True God was disappearing faster now; he needed to speed up his progress. "Gods are singular. But who becomes god doesn't seem to be unique. On the original list of gods, the Mountains and Seas were not included. But they forcefully altered it..."

"The True God's power is infinite, capable of knowing the past, present, and future. Thus, just before falling, foreseeing future changes, He brought me from outside reality, making me a player outside the game to break this stalemate."

"But..." A cold glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. "Is that all?" "From the god's perspective, He should have seen everything that happened after I successfully shattered the Mountains and Seas' grand play."

"As Zhen Shi Yin and the others said."

"The Mountains and Seas are destroyed, reincarnation ceases, all returning to me."

"..."

"This is not the result the True God desired."

"Sacrificing Himself just to break the endless reincarnation of this world and make me, an outsider, ascend?"

"Do Gods possess such kindness?" Li Fan snorted coldly, dismissing this possibility.

"But that True God did so without hesitation."

"It's only because... He was absolutely convinced that I could shatter the Mountains and Seas' play and destroy the nascent Star. But ultimately, could not slay a god."

"The god can see the future, foreseeing all possibilities. Exhausting all options, He did not foresee me successfully slaying a god. That's why He did it."

"Dragging me in to work for Him, and then wanting me to be a scapegoat..."

"That's truly excessive." Li Fan calmed his anger, the initial fury upon discovering the truth replaced by a wry smile. However, beneath the smile, Li Fan's gaze was colder than ever.

"The only reason for the ultimate outcome is this phantom above my head?" In the remaining time, Li Fan did his best to deduce a countermeasure. The ink faded, and the phantom disappeared. Li Fan's expression showed a moment of bewilderment.

"It seems..."

"I've forgotten something extremely important." Feeling an inexplicable tremor in his heart, Li Fan mused.

"Do you have any insights?" He looked at the True Return phantom standing beside him. The True Return phantom had no subjective consciousness; it only reacted mechanically. To answer Li Fan's question, illusory lights flickered, attempting to trace back. But ultimately, nothing was found.

Li Fan's expression did not change much. "Sometimes, the absence of an answer is the answer itself."

"I have stood at the pinnacle of this world, yet something like this still causes such a strange change..."

"Only [God]."

"Remembering it or not makes no difference."

Chapter 1772: False Universe Exists

The False Universe's Existence

"So, let me see who the final victor will be." Facing the seemingly inescapable fate determined by the True God of this world, Li Fan's will remained unshaken. As his thoughts flowed, billions of rays of light, like countless stars, appeared around him. These were the thoughts, feelings, and insights of his clones that he had previously deployed. It was as if he had personally experienced countless cycles of reincarnation in the Mountains and Seas, with each Great Dao cultivated being different. It was as if a divine brush were constantly painting, transforming the once somewhat empty Hall of the Great Dao into a more sacred and solemn space, restoring its original appearance in the Mountains and Seas. The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, or the True Return phantom, standing in the Hall of the Great Dao, also became more substantial, its blurry facial features faintly visible. It bore striking resemblance to Li Fan, yet incorporated the characteristics of countless "Heaven-Sent Children."

Even more astonishing was Li Fan's own transformation. "I am just myself. Even after countless ages in this cycle of reincarnation, I will not change one bit." The myriad rays of starlight surrounded Li Fan, illuminating his body. Yet, Li Fan himself remained unchanged. The starlight, like a torch, allowed Li Fan to perceive himself in the void's darkness.

"This Hall of the Great Dao is resplendent, perhaps capable of easily suppressing all beings in the Mountains and Seas. But before that True God, it is utterly useless."

"All Great Daos and all laws in the Mountains and Seas originate from the True God. No matter how high one cultivates, one cannot escape the tribulation of returning to the god. If there are exceptions... perhaps it is [Truth and Falsehood]."

"[Truth and Falsehood] is akin to a god's innate divine ability, allowing a god to exist eternally through endless reincarnation. Thus, all things in this world, even gods, cannot escape Truth and Falsehood."

"In other words, gods can be regarded as the true possessors of [True Return]. However, compared to me, an outsider, they cannot retain their memories through repeated returns."

"Even with this characteristic, using the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood to slay gods is still impossible."

"Zhang Fan and Zhen Shi Yin both believe I am the Lord of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. In reality, only [God] is eligible to be called the Lord of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood. A god without the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is not a true god, merely a God-Conqueror Guest born by accident."

"[True Return] and True Gods cannot coexist in this world simultaneously. If I can prevent [True Return] from returning to the god, I can actually stop the True God's descent. But alas..."

"I cannot do it." Li Fan couldn't help but recall the last moments of the Mountains and Seas in every cycle. All things returning to the god was the fated end of the world. With the trend set, even [Truth and Falsehood] could not escape it.

"It seems, as I deduced before, that only I can slay gods. It's just that previously, I didn't have a concrete plan for how to slay gods. But now..." Li Fan lowered his gaze to the "Zhang Fan" remaining in the ravaged Mountains and Seas. "Perhaps, this is the path to breaking the deadlock."

...

"Any discoveries?" Zhen Shi Yin's voice came from beside him, startling Zhang Fan from his momentary daze. The instant their gazes met and he saw the looming phantom, Zhang Fan's mind had become lost, as if falling into a dream. He seemed to have experienced countless bizarre events, but upon waking, all were completely forgotten. Only the two overlapping figures, like inescapable specters, flashed intermittently before Zhang Fan's eyes, sending chills down his spine. He truthfully recounted the scene he had witnessed, and Zhen Shi Yin fell into deep thought. However, time was running out for the Mountains and Seas. The Tree of Truth and Falsehood had withered, and the tide of Dao Annihilation was once again raging. The Mountains and Seas collapsed, and the apocalypse returned. This time, there would be no chance to turn back. All things in the world were inevitably falling towards their predetermined end.

Zhen Shi Yin seemed to have made up his mind. "It's time to have a talk with some old friends."

"Follow me." A pale light enveloped Zhang Fan, instantly traversing the shattered Mountains and Seas. They arrived at a peculiar place. The deepest part of the Infinite Sea, the very foundation of the Mountains and Seas' construction. If the Mountains and Seas had visible growth rings, this would be the innermost circle. Ancient, primordial energy flowed freely. But by this point, even the fundamental logic of the Mountains and Seas was beginning to collapse. Yet, here, a silver light stood out. Zhen Shi Yin led Zhang Fan, flying rapidly into the silver light.

At this moment, Zhang Fan felt as if he had returned to the protected world of the Old Fisherman and other God-Conqueror Guests. The oppressive feeling of the god's return vanished instantly. Zhang Fan attempted to observe this world, but found that even with his current strength,

Chapter 1773: Cicada Concealment

Cicada's Concealment

"Zhen Shi Yin, False Universe Existence! You two owe me a life!"

"If it could truly be born, the imprint would be completed. With this imprint, my eternal void world could also develop its own Transformation of Truth and Falsehood, thus escaping the cycle of endless reincarnation. We are all going to die anyway."

As False Universe Existence pondered, he had already made up his mind. "I will buy you a little more time. Whether you succeed or not..." Without finishing his sentence, silver light surged and shot out beyond the heavens. Although the eternal world appeared to have stabilized once more, Zhen Shi Yin and Zhang Fan knew that its foundation was lost. It would not be long before its complete destruction.

"The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood returns to the True God."

"And I, this Heaven-Sent Child, this clone, will also return..."

"Into his body."

"This is the so-called inescapable fate!"

Zhang Fan finally understood why his last stroke could never be completed. "It seems that even he has not fully grasped the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood. As a clone, I naturally cannot surpass the main body."

In Zhang Fan's long-held beliefs, his main body, the mastermind behind everything, must have possessed unfathomable power, perhaps capable of contending with a True God. Although he had never given up on confronting the main body, he had never dared to underestimate him. He never expected that after a lifetime of cultivation, he could now stand on equal footing with him? This was an idea Zhang Fan had never entertained, never even dared to imagine.

In that instant of realization, an uncontrollable ambition began to sprout in his heart. "Who is true, who is false? Who leads, who follows?"

"It remains to be seen!"

Zhang Fan knew that his main body must be waiting for him outside this eternal world. After this place shattered, before returning to the True God, he would first absorb him. "But this is precisely my only chance of survival!"

The brush that painted the scroll of Truth and Falsehood inexplicably appeared and then quietly fell, landing heavily on Zhen Shi Yin. Zhen Shi Yin's face showed a trace of surprise. He didn't understand how Zhang Fan could have changed so drastically in an instant.

"You still have a chance to start over, but I may not."

Seeing that Zhen Shi Yin could still maintain his form under the touch of his True Painting, only slightly trembling, Zhang Fan was inwardly alarmed. He did not press further, but with a flash of light, he transmitted all his newfound understanding to him.

Zhen Shi Yin's gaze shifted from Zhang Fan to the void outside the eternal world. After contemplating something unknown, he genuinely gave up resisting. His form dimmed, his light gradually faded, finally transforming into a silent white spot that slowly fell into Zhang Fan's palm.

Zhang Fan remained silent for a moment, then bowed respectfully towards the place where Zhen Shi Yin had fallen. Without hesitation, he absorbed the silent white spot into himself. Though Zhen Shi Yin's demise was not true death, his sacrifice of a lifetime to give Zhang Fan a sliver of chance to fight for survival was a debt of immense gratitude.

Zhang Fan seized the last moment, savoring the taste of the silent radiance left by Zhen Shi Yin. "Death is merely an illusion."

"The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, while beyond Senior's sight and knowledge, he attempted to depict the creation of Truth and Falsehood through the imagery of life and death."

"The result was like a blind man touching an elephant, grasping only a part. But it genuinely held a trace of the essence of Truth and Falsehood."

"A great supplement!"

As if struck by inspiration, Zhang Fan furiously wrote on the scroll of Truth and Falsehood, adding another half-stroke. Then he looked at this eternal void world. He could sense that False Universe Existence had already perished. Just as False Universe Existence had said, although this world could exist independently of the Mountains and Seas, it was ultimately just void, its foundation entirely reliant on False Universe Existence's cultivation. Facing the might of the descending True God, it had no chance of resistance. It was no longer merely shaking; it was on the verge of complete collapse.

Zhang Fan made his stroke, extinguishing this world before it was destroyed. "The living ride on the void, outside the false."

The scroll of Truth and Falsehood, painstakingly painted by his own hand, was instantly consumed by flames, transforming into a blazing inferno that only he could see. The eternal void world ceased to exist, and Zhang Fan plunged into the final moments of returning to the god.

A ferocious voice repeatedly roared "True Return!" But due to the presence of others' phantoms, the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood could not be activated. Each time True Return was about to be initiated, a faint voice would interject, interrupting the process.

Only the God-Conqueror Guests of the Mountains and Seas could retain some faint memories through the constant resets of the Mountains and Seas. In this lifetime, through his interactions with the God-Conqueror Guests from various paths, Zhang Fan confirmed that his main body had never intersected with the God-Conqueror Guests during his past reincarnations. All possibilities within the Mountains and Seas, the paths he took, the events he experienced – the main body might have gone through them all. Only the affairs of the God-Conqueror Guests were exceptions. Therefore, they could be used to distinguish Zhang Fan from the main body.

Undeniably, with the main body's control over the clone, this peculiarity could not last long. A clone, after all, was just a clone, destined from its creation to be unable to resist. Under normal circumstances, these phantoms of God-Conqueror Guests could at best prolong Zhang Fan's life for a moment. They could not change anything. But now... In the final moments of returning to the god, this fleeting opportunity was enough to reverse everything.

"As long as True Return can be achieved, there is still a possibility. If we fall into the True God, we are doomed, with no chance to try again!"

Anger and panic. The main body's pathetic display was all witnessed by Zhang Fan. He met its gaze with cold indifference. "It is precisely because I do not want to die that I will fight with my life!"

Starlight scattered, as if leaping into the world. The high-hanging Star, at this moment, was like a great sun, standing alone. Zhang Fan finally uttered the two words that the main body had shouted countless times before. With no other intentions obstructing him, after a brief pause, the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood descended upon this realm. The scattered starlight dimmed, as if an invisible giant hand had grasped the sun in the sky and was dragging it down, step by step, with irresistible force.

A miraculous scene appeared before Zhang Fan's eyes. It was as if time had reversed, and all the overflowing brilliant starlight slowly returned to the star. Deep darkness surged forth again. This cold, silent stillness, compared to the divine brilliance, was unexpectedly more reassuring. This time was truly too perilous. It was only a hair's breadth away from the True God's final descent. Erasing the impending True God and performing True Return took longer than all previous instances combined. But ultimately, it was successful. The taut string in Zhang Fan's mind finally relaxed. He let out a long sigh of relief.

He gazed one last time at the fading form of the True God, filled with pride, "I can defy fate and challenge the main body. From now on, I can shatter the Star and slay gods!"

"You just wait!"

As if sensing Zhang Fan's thoughts, the fading starlight flared one last time before disappearing into invisibility. Rolling darkness immediately followed, engulfing Zhang Fan's consciousness.

Chapter 1774: Good Development

Good Will Progress

Three years later.

"The battle with the main body was even more brutal than I imagined."

"Fine, let's wait until I've completely washed away the True God's influence." Putting aside all other thoughts, Zhang Fan fell into a deep sleep. It took another ten years for him to fully recover. During this time, Zhang Fan also secretly acted to slow down Auntie's aging process. Although this slightly delayed his own recovery, Zhang Fan felt it was worthwhile.

To make his cultivation path appear more reasonable, immediately after recovering, Zhang Fan used his unfathomable True Void energy to alter the environment of the Xuanhuang Realm.

"Mortals here cannot cultivate because of the Immortal-Mortal Barrier."

"Obstructions should simply disappear." With a single thought of Truth and Falsehood, the Transmission of Law and the Heavenly Physician were directly erased from this world by Zhang Fan, as if they had never existed. Without the suppression of the Transmission of Law defying the natural order, the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao gradually returned to its normal flow amidst constant roars. He then cast a glance and destroyed the Immortal Extinguishing Array that sealed the Great Xuan Minor World.

Strange, it was scorching hot not long ago." Zhang Fan nodded in agreement. Without anyone actively spreading cultivation techniques, as long as there was spiritual energy, cultivators would naturally emerge.

Half a month later, the first Qi Refining cultivator was born in the Great Xuan Minor World. The matter of cultivation spread like wildfire.

"Cultivation... according to them, does this mean I can cultivate too?" In the room, Bai Shuyue exclaimed in disbelief, feeling the spiritual energy flowing clearly within her body. "What about you, Fan'er?" A moment later, Bai Shuyue asked with great concern. "Don't worry, Auntie, I also feel the spiritual energy in this world," Zhang Fan replied with a smile. Bai Shuyue breathed a sigh of relief. "Heaven bless us, ancestors bless us!" With the path of cultivation opened, the two left the Great Xuan and entered the Xuanhuang Realm, seeking further possibilities. With Zhang Fan's covert protection, there were naturally no risks. "This world is actually so vast." Bai Shuyue, upon learning the truth of the Mountains and Seas, was stunned into silence. True Immortal, Nameless, Transcendent. "For Auntie, the Mountains and Seas are still too dangerous. Only the protected world would be safer." Looking at Bai Shuyue's face, Zhang Fan thought to himself. In the profound void, a soft sound of surprise seemed to echo. Like a stone stirring a thousand ripples, the Saints of the Mountains and Seas, even when faced with [Truth and Falsehood], were moved. Just as Li Fan was certain that his past self had truly perished and disappeared, becoming True Return, the current Zhang Fan was also utterly convinced that it was his own desperate struggle in the face of death that had successfully overthrown the main body, not a scheme orchestrated by the main body. However, looking at the thoughtful expressions of the God-Conqueror Guests present, Zhang Fan's expression changed rapidly several times.
