Therefore, Zhang Fan directly released his divine sense, allowing all the God-Conqueror Guests to examine him. Under unity of purpose, he had nothing to fear. The matter was of great importance, and the Old Fisherman and others dared not be negligent. They meticulously examined him. Once, twice. After a long while, everyone withdrew their divine senses. "A perfect union, without flaws. It seems we were overthinking," Fate Slayer Master said. "Under the end of the god's return, without the enhancement of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, that so-called Lord of True Return has no advantage. Either outcome is possible. A clone overthrowing the main body is indeed feasible." ... After discussing amongst themselves, they found no flaws. "However, given that the Lord of True Return has an advantage that we cannot compare to. Through countless reincarnations, he has managed to retain his memories. Perhaps there are some methods we are unaware of. It's wise to remain vigilant." Although they said this, they had no particularly effective way to intervene in the struggle between the clone and the main body. All they could do was offer a warning. Setting aside this matter, they then discussed the main topic. Now that the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood was on their side, they had the potential to subvert the True God. Coupled with Zhang Fan, an outsider, even the God-Conqueror Guests, who had always preferred inaction, felt their ambitions stirring. "I will certainly not repeat the story of the past, devouring all the Mountains and Seas and slaying the gods." "But how can we prevent falling back into reincarnation while preserving the Mountains and Seas?"

Chapter 1775: Traces of the Dao

Cicada Hides

"False Universe Existence's eternal void world can serve as a backup plan. In the previous life, I didn't succeed in imprinting the traces of [Truth and Falsehood]. This time, after devouring the main body, my comprehension has greatly improved, with a qualitative leap. Perhaps we can try again," Xuan Yuanhong said first.

"How about you becoming a god?" Fate Slayer Master's words were startling.

"Even if you obtain the creation of Truth and Falsehood, becoming a savior will not be easy. You still need to patiently cultivate for several more lifetimes, observing all kinds of changes," the Old Fisherman was not so optimistic.

...

Although they were united in purpose, they still held different opinions on this matter among the God-Conqueror Guests. Zhang Fan merely listened, refraining from offering his opinion readily.

"Regardless, we must first visit Senior Zhen Shi Yin and Senior False Universe Existence."

Zhang Fan, entrusting Bai Shuyue's safety to this place, then, with the help of the Old Fisherman and others, found Zhen Shi Yin, who was hiding in the Mountains and Seas.

It had to be said that Zhen Shi Yin's hiding place was indeed extremely secret. Even though Zhang Fan knew of his existence, he searched the entire Mountains and Seas but could not find any trace of Zhen Shi Yin. Even when he invoked the Great Dao he comprehended, Zhen Shi Yin still remained hidden.

It was only after the God-Conqueror Guests conducted a dragnet search themselves that he was found.

"Such a grand mobilization, I fear you harbor ill intentions." Zhen Shi Yin stared at the group who had suddenly barged in.

Zhang Fan said helplessly, "Fellow Daoist, you might not believe me, but I've come to repay a debt of gratitude."

"Repay a debt?" Zhen Shi Yin sneered. "You understand the [Hidden] Dao I comprehended, likely obtained from killing me in the previous life. No wonder I had a vague impression of you. This time, you've gathered so many helpers..."

Zhen Shi Yin's eyes flashed with ferocity.

"Stop the nonsense and fight! Although you have numbers on your side, I, Zhen Shi Yin, am not afraid of you!"

Facing Zhen Shi Yin's misunderstanding, Zhang Fan simply replied, "You use [Hidden] as your brush, attempting to depict [Truth and Falsehood], yet you have always been unable to achieve it. Now that the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is within reach, don't you want to try?"

"Hmm?"

Thus, under the unity of purpose, the misunderstanding was resolved. Zhen Shi Yin was overjoyed, completely changed from his previous demeanor.

"Good, good, good! I never imagined you actually succeeded!"

"The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood is truly wondrous!" The deathly pale light that occasionally flashed on his body grew deeper. Through Zhang Fan's vision, he finally glimpsed the ultimate creation he had been desperately seeking.

Zhen Shi Yin, who was already at the pinnacle of the Mountains and Seas, his cultivation and strength advanced by leaps and bounds in a short period.

In fact, after glimpsing Truth and Falsehood, all the God-Conqueror Guests gained something. However, their connection to Truth and Falsehood was far less intimate than Zhen Shi Yin's. Hence, their gains were also significantly less.

After seeing Zhen Shi Yin, the last step was to find False Universe Existence.

"I wonder if his world has left any traces."

Soon, their doubts were resolved. Led by Zhen Shi Yin, upon returning to the eternal void world, Zhang Fan immediately sensed a faint, familiar feeling.

False Universe Existence stood at the center of the world, staring at a trace that should not have existed, his expression solemn.

"It's not completely preserved, perhaps only a faint residual trace. But..."

"It's definitely a good start!" Everyone was overjoyed, as if they had seen hope.

After another round of unity of purpose, False Universe Existence's doubts finally vanished. He was even more excited than the other God-Conqueror Guests.

"With one, all can be obtained. If the traces were complete, this eternal world might truly give birth to its own [Truth and Falsehood]!"

Finally, they found Empty Daoist, and an unprecedented scene of harmony and joy unfolded in the Mountains and Seas.

Relying on their unity of purpose, everyone assisted Zhang Fan in painting the scroll of [Truth and Falsehood], attempting to etch the traces of Truth and Falsehood.

Simultaneously, the God-Conqueror Guests discussed how to facilitate Zhang Fan's ascension to godhood.

"In the long cycles of reincarnation, we have all defeated the Mountains and Seas and attained godhood."

"However, according to the main body's memories, the [Star] we faced after becoming gods was not the truly fallen True God, but the actual Mountains and Seas."

"In other words, although we call ourselves God-Conqueror Guests, we were merely pseudo-gods."

"However, it is possible that Fellow Daoist Zhang Fan can achieve true [Godhood]."

...

This was the best plan derived from their collective discussion. How to reverse the cycle of all things returning to the god? Even though they had reached the pinnacle of existence and pooled their wisdom, they could not find an answer.

"Only by becoming a True God might there be a solution."

"The only issue is, after becoming a god... will I still be myself?"

Zhang Fan's gaze swept across everyone. Although his inherited memories from the main body were somewhat incomplete, the fear of the god's return in his heart was extremely clear.

"Therefore, this step must be taken with extreme caution."

"After all, what happens after becoming a god... no one in this world knows."

"We are merely insignificant consciousnesses, living within a link in the long chain of endless reincarnation."

He did not rush to make a decision. Since this lifetime had just begun, there was ample time for preparation.

The painting of the scroll of Truth and Falsehood proceeded more smoothly than Zhang Fan had anticipated. Perhaps it was due to his transformation after the battle with the main body, which resulted in a qualitative leap. He easily accomplished what he, and even his main body, could not do in the previous life.

In the eternal void world, an immeasurable scroll flickered past, appearing within the world yet seemingly encompassing the entire world. It only appeared for an instant before vanishing. But everyone saw it clearly.

"This world is no longer void." False Universe Existence wept with joy. Under the influence of unity of purpose, the other God-Conqueror Guests were also deeply moved.

"The most urgent task now is to find a way to delay the arrival of the end."

"To allow [Truth and Falsehood] to be born from these traces."

Zhang Fan nodded. "Although the traces of Truth and Falsehood have been formed, they are ultimately just imprints and are still subject to the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood."

"With each reset, the traces will likely be significantly weakened. Only by nurturing genuine [Truth and Falsehood] from this place, using Truth and Falsehood against Truth and Falsehood,"

"Can we leave an unchanging constant amidst repeated resets."

"Besides me, an outsider, another unchanging constant."

Zhang Fan repeated the words. Since a consensus had been reached, it was time for the God-Conqueror Guests to showcase their individual abilities.

"We have been in hiding for so long; it's time to move around a bit." Fate Slayer Master spoke first.

"I will go to the Primeval Immortal Realm first and forcibly sever their thoughts. If we want to extend the existence of the Mountains and Seas as much as possible, the first priority is to reunite the Mountains and Seas and perform internal consolidation. Only at the Saint realm can one traverse and reunite. The Saints of the Primeval Immortal Realm can serve as assistance."

For some unknown reason, the usually lazy Old Fisherman's eyes flashed with excitement. He stood up abruptly and said, "I'll accompany you. Hehehe, it's been a long time since I've had a good fight; I'm itching for one."

If only Fate Slayer Master, a single God-Conqueror Guest, had acted, there might have been some complications. But with the addition of the Old Fisherman... Even with the numerous Saints in the Primeval Immortal Realm, they would be no match.

This point was deeply believed by everyone present. After all, only after becoming a god would one truly understand the vast chasm between [God] and [Mortal]. Although they were merely God-Conqueror Guests, the experience of becoming gods had already changed them, enough to crush other Saints of the Mountains and Seas. Not to mention, they now had the advantage of [Truth and Falsehood].

In the Primeval Immortal Realm. All things flourished, but dark currents surged secretly. After countless years of conflict, this realm had reached a delicate and eerie balance. All Saints lay hidden, waiting for variables to emerge, seeking the opportunity to attain godhood.

However, the appearance of Fate Slayer Master and the Old Fisherman attracted no attention.

The Old Fisherman surveyed his surroundings, his eyes filled with emotion. "I haven't been to this region in a long time."

"Back then, I was so foolish and obsessed."

Fate Slayer Master, however, showed little emotion, his tone chilling. "It's better to awaken them early; it's a good thing for them."

"Let's begin."

The moment Fate Slayer Master finished speaking, all Saints in this realm, no matter where they were hidden or in what form, were horrified to discover that a blade existing between virtual and real, truth and falsehood, had quietly appeared above their heads. It had no physical form, yet could not be removed by any means. The blade hanging above their heads made them feel as if their lives were hanging by a thread.

"Who?" Most Saints were inwardly enraged, attempting to find the owner behind the blade's silhouette. Some, sensing an anomaly, tried to flee this realm and escape to the Mountains and Seas.

However, the moment they tried to leave the Primeval Immortal Realm, their vision went black. Then, they found themselves in an unknown place.

"Stay put for now." A calm voice echoed from above, carrying an undeniable authority.

"This voice is..."

"The Old Fisherman of the Mountains and Seas?"

"His power is terrifyingly immense?" The Saints were filled with dread, and their confusion was palpable. Locking onto all the Saints in an instant, capturing them with a single thought. What realm was this? They were so powerful, why didn't they participate in the competition for godhood?

As they pondered this, figures were continuously thrown down from above. They were all individuals known to the Primeval Immortal Realm. The Saints were even more astonished.

Packing up the Primeval Immortal Realm did not take much time.

"Alas, boring. I thought they would at least put up some resistance," Fate Slayer Master sighed.

"I can release them all, and you can try again. No need for the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood," the Old Fisherman suggested with a smile.

"Let's forget it. Too much trouble." Fate Slayer Master shrugged. Then, he suddenly sighed again. "The Transformation of Truth and Falsehood is truly profound and mysterious. But ultimately, it does not belong to us. I fear that in the next life, without unity of purpose and the aid of Truth and Falsehood, it might be difficult to adapt, and greed might arise."

"Like how we once yearned for godhood. Although we knew it was unattainable, our obsession remained unyielding."

"If such a thing were to happen..."

"Please stop me," Fate Slayer Master said earnestly.

"Me too," the Old Fisherman replied, his smile gone.

A moment later.

"It has been a long time since I've had such a bountiful harvest. Time for a drink!" The Old Fisherman produced a gourd, drank deeply, and casually tossed it to Fate Slayer Master. Fate Slayer Master accepted it without complaint and drank it down heartily. Then, the two glanced at the now silent Primeval Immortal Realm and quietly returned.

The Saints were released. Although they regained their freedom, the blades still hovered above their heads, and they did not act foolishly.

"Becoming a god is an illusory pursuit; do not engage in futile efforts."

"Of course, I know persuasion is futile. Therefore, I have placed a blade above your heads."

"Please assist in reuniting the Mountains and Seas. When the Mountains and Seas are rebuilt, I will grant you your freedom." Fate Slayer Master said coldly. Though his words were polite, even using the word "please," the Saints clearly felt the blade above their heads sharpen and move closer. Although they didn't dare to agree, they all nodded in assent.

"However, the Mountains and Seas are vast and endless; reuniting them..."

"Even with our efforts, it might be like a drop in the ocean." Towering Dragon said solemnly.

"Don't worry, you only need to lead the way." It was Zhang Fan who spoke.

With a single thought, hundreds, even thousands, of illusions diverged from Zhang Fan. "I will use True Spirit Infusion to continuously shape Saints for the Mountains and Seas. You will lead, and the newly formed Saints will assist. With everyone's combined efforts, even though the Mountains and Seas are currently fragmented, reuniting them will not take long."

"True Spirit Infusion? Shaping Saints?" The Saints of the Primeval Immortal Realm were all profoundly shaken. The familiar Mountains and Seas of the past, shattered in an instant. They suddenly realized that the truth of the Mountains and Seas might be far more profound than they had imagined. The situation was dire, and their strength was insufficient. Despite their unwillingness, with the threat of the blade above their heads, the Saints could only comply.

Reuniting the Mountains and Seas was undoubtedly a tedious and arduous task. Even with the strength of the Primeval Saints and the continuous influx of reinforcements, the Saints were still physically and mentally exhausted by the long process of rebuilding the Mountains and Seas. However, after the blade above their heads mercilessly beheaded [Suo] for attempting to escape this fate, the remaining Saints all became obedient. They had no choice but to continue.

Suo did not perish. With a flash of the Fate Slaying Blade, Suo lost his Dao path, falling from the Saint realm. However, he was forcibly infused with True Spirit, granted a different Dao path, and sent back to the grand task of reuniting the Mountains and Seas. However, at this point, his situation was far less comfortable than before. Like all the other continuously shaped Saints, he had to physically exert himself, traversing the void realm, and acting as a bridge to construct the path for reuniting the Mountains and Seas. The Primeval Saints, on the other hand, only needed to oversee the overall situation and intervene at critical moments to ensure everything proceeded smoothly. The difference between these two roles, though perhaps not significant in the short term, became immense as time accumulated. Suo's drastically different circumstances effectively extinguished any thoughts of escape among the Primeval Saints. Although the project of reuniting the Mountains and Seas was long, fortunately, under the current circumstances, it was not without end. If they endured, they would eventually achieve freedom when the Mountains and Seas were reunited. With the realm and strength of [Fate Slayer Master] and [Old Fisherman] as [God-Conqueror Guests], they would not possibly deceive them.

"Fellow Daoist Fan's method is indeed ingenious. I originally thought supervising and suppressing them would be quite troublesome."

"I didn't expect the Saints to be so compliant; it saved us a lot of effort," Forgetfulness Elder sighed in admiration.

"However..." The God-Conqueror Guests looked at the eternal void world. The birth of Truth and Falsehood seemed to be still far off.

"If the Mountains and Seas are successfully reunited, and new Truth and Falsehood does not arrive, then what?" Zhang Fan's expression was calm, his gaze deep.

"Then, I can only trouble the Saints of the Mountains and Seas further."

Chapter 1776: Divine Taste

The shattering of the Mountains and Seas, followed by their return to the Star, was predestined, an inescapable outcome. Even if all the Saints joined forces, they could only alter the situation temporarily. What the God-Conqueror Guests desired was merely to delay the inevitable. Besides creating enough time for the Eternal Void World to nurture the traces of the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, they also needed to find a fundamental method to resist the impending return of divinity.

Though the lifespan of the Mountains and Seas was vast, it seemed insufficient. From the dawn of the Mountains and Seas to the end of time, a continuous period of one hundred and sixty billion years had passed. The number of Mountains and Seas fragments, fractured by the erosion of Dao Annihilation, numbered in the millions. The reunification of even a single segment of the Mountains and Seas was a monumental undertaking that required the combined efforts of numerous Saints. Yet, what initially seemed impossibly distant progressed with unexpected speed. Countless clones of Zhang Fan, wielding the divine ability of True Spirit Infusion, resolved the supply issues for the Saints in the void realm. The God-Conqueror Guests and the Saints of the Primordial Era collectively managed the overall situation. Over one hundred billion years, the shattered Mountains and Seas were slowly repaired, bit by bit. Even the Saints who participated in the entire process found it incredible when they looked back.

"Before, I scoffed at the idea of reunifying the Mountains and Seas. Now, it doesn't seem so difficult!"

"All the Saints uniting, putting aside all their disputes – this was almost an impossible feat. I am curious, what exactly are those God-Conqueror Guests plotting together?"

"Forget it; no need to dwell on it. It only brings unnecessary trouble. I'm tired after such a long time. Once the reunification is complete, I want to rest well."

"Soon, very soon."

Under the expectant gaze of all, the final rift in the Mountains and Seas was repaired. As the Saints were finally freed, a faint sense of confusion welled up in their hearts. For so long, their goal had been the reunification of the Mountains and Seas; it had almost become an ingrained habit. Now that the task was complete, the Saints found themselves momentarily lost, unsure of what to do next.

The God-Conqueror Guests fulfilled their promise. The Fate Slaying Blade hovering above their heads gradually vanished, and the threat was gone. However, the God-Conqueror Guests themselves seemed to have evaporated from the Mountains and Seas, disappearing without a trace. Some Saints, bored and disillusioned, sought quiet places in the Mountains and Seas to seclude themselves. Others, yearning for the power of the God-Conqueror Guests, greedily returned to the Primordial Immortal Realm. Some, accustomed to interacting with the beings of the Mountains and Seas during the reunification process, transformed into mortals and hid among them.

In the Eternal World, it was no longer an empty void. Instead, a magnificent, sacred hall stood at its center. The hall was boundless, seemingly forming its own realm. Within the infinite expanse, countless Great Daos were arranged in orderly fashion. The God-Conqueror Guests inspected the Hall of Great Daos, nodding frequently.

"The Dao paths of the Saints of the Mountains and Seas have all been incorporated within."

"With the Mountains and Seas now intact, this state should last for one hundred billion years. After one hundred billion years, Dao Annihilation will arise again, and the Mountains and Seas will shatter and reform." Broken Formation Master spoke slowly, seemingly foreseeing the dark tide that had been pushed back beyond the Mountains and Seas.

Zhang Fan then added, "By then, I will use the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood to erase all the Saints, and then, using this Hall of Great Daos, reconstruct a new batch of Saints. This way, another cycle of reunification for the Mountains and Seas can begin."

Xuan Yuanhong sighed softly, "After all, we made a promise to them. If we force them away again, it will inevitably lead to conflict. Although it's a simple matter, I fear they won't be as dedicated to reunification the next time."

"It's better to simply create them anew through Truth and Falsehood." None of the God-Conqueror Guests disagreed, clearly thinking along the same lines. Having understood the principles of Truth and Falsehood for countless years, their ways of thinking had subtly changed without them realizing it. They themselves might have noticed this at some point, but with their mastery over Truth and Falsehood, it was difficult to view other beings as equals. Furthermore, the majority of the God-Conqueror Guests' energy was still focused on dealing with the inevitable end of the gods. They paid little attention to minor details.

"The traces of Truth and Falsehood have already nurtured two-thirds of the way. However, the slower the evolution proceeds, the longer it will take to fully form. Perhaps more time is still needed, perhaps three times as long."

"It's fine; it's merely three more reincarnations. We have already grasped the origins of all the Saints. With the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood, we can create a new batch of Saints for reunification at any time. The only concern is the Mountains and Seas themselves."

An image of the vast and boundless Mountains and Seas instantly appeared before the God-Conqueror Guests. Through the reunification, the Saints' footprints had covered every inch of the Mountains and Seas. The Saints themselves were their eyes. As the true creators of the current Mountains and Seas, nearly every inch of the Mountains and Seas was under the control of those present.

"The return of the Mountains and Seas to divinity is destiny, an unstoppable fate."

"Although we have forcefully reversed it, each time a new birth and destruction occurs, the momentum will only grow stronger."

"Even doubling each time."

"Until... Dao Annihilation appears, and the Mountains and Seas are instantly wiped out."

"Leaving us no time to slowly reunify."

"Therefore, the time we have left is truly not much."

Under the gaze of the God-Conqueror Guests, the image of the Mountains and Seas transformed several times. Then, a solitary Star hung high, towering above the Mountains and Seas.

"Fellow Daoist Fan, are your preparations complete?"

"The current Great Daos within the Mountains and Seas are already fully understood. I can replace the Mountains and Seas at any time and ascend to the position of a new god. The Star formed by the Mountains and Seas behind the scenes is no match for me. The only concern remains the god." Zhang Fan said indifferently.

"Therefore, we still need to wait for the birth of the traces of Truth and Falsehood." The God-Conqueror Guests nodded slightly. Over the years, as Zhang Fan's strength grew, he had gradually begun to detach himself from the initial "unity of purpose." Even though Zhang Fan intended to share with the God-Conqueror Guests, as he drew closer to becoming a god, he would inadvertently disappear from their shared consciousness. Thus, there were unspoken parts in Zhang Fan's words. Theoretically, the stronger one's cultivation and the more thorough their preparations, the greater their confidence in slaying gods. However, the reality was the exact opposite. Zhang Fan had deduced the aftermath of his actions after destroying the Star countless times, but the result was always "nothingness." No victory, no defeat. It was as if after completing the destruction of the Star, he simply vanished into thin air. Such a bizarre outcome left Zhang Fan perplexed. In his current state, he was arguably the closest being to godhood in the entire Mountains and Seas. Therefore, he understood the power of gods more and more clearly.

"It's still not enough." A fleeting sense of powerlessness arose in Zhang Fan's heart, though he quickly suppressed it. He now understood why his original self had scattered countless clones throughout the Mountains and Seas in search of a way to break the deadlock. It was because he had exhausted all his resources and found nothing.

"But I am different from him." Zhang Fan extinguished all extraneous thoughts. "What he cannot achieve, I may still be able to!"

"Slaying gods..." Zhang Fan's gaze swept across the illusory image of the Mountains and Seas, as if witnessing the true Mountains and Seas, and made a silent decision in his heart.

Chapter 1777: True and False

The moment all the starlight was devoured, all external images and sounds vanished. True, pure darkness and silence enveloped Zhang Fan completely. Apart from Zhang Fan, there was nothing else. Even the concept of time ceased to exist.

After a long period of dead silence, faint murmuring sounds began to echo in Zhang Fan's ears, like thunder against the extreme quietness of his surroundings.

"This is..." Zhang Fan found the voice strangely familiar, but could not recall it for a moment. Although only an instant had passed since the return of all things to divinity, it felt like an eternity had passed in Zhang Fan's eyes. Even his memories began to decay and blur. Instinctively, he tried to listen carefully.

It was like a sudden cicada's chirp, followed by a chorus of thousands. What was mere whispering one moment became a grand, magnificent symphony the next.

"Xuan Yuanhong, Fate Slayer Master, Old Fisherman..." Familiar yet strange names surfaced in Zhang Fan's mind, causing him to hesitate. Zhang Fan no longer remembered who these people were. But their desperate shouts, seeming incredibly urgent, were telling Zhang Fan something. Sensing their emotions, Zhang Fan tried to calm himself, to exclude the influence of other distracting sounds. But it was to no avail. Soon, these familiar voices were drowned out by the incoming tide. New voices began to emerge. Both familiar and strange. So familiar that Zhang Fan could instantly recall their names, but so strange that his mind held no memory of them. Zhang Fan had a vague premonition that something was wrong.

"Am I... decaying?" In this moment, Zhang Fan was filled with profound confusion and bewilderment. He suddenly recalled his goal: to slay gods. His ambition from years ago was still vivid. After proudly devouring the Mountains and Seas and annihilating the Star, his realm, strength, and state of mind had all reached their peak. He was fully prepared to face the rumored fallen True God. But he never imagined... No True God appeared. Instead, he was met with endless solitude and darkness. For an instant, then an eternity.

His body and consciousness began to decay and wither. And within him, all that he had previously consumed began to resurvive. This was entirely different from what he had expected. As if deceived, a surge of malevolence erupted in Zhang Fan's heart.

"Get out!" "Get out!" he roared in extreme anger. But even he couldn't hear his own voice. The dark void remained eternally unchanged, like cold seawater silently engulfing Zhang Fan.

In this instant, Zhang Fan felt the bone-chilling cold within this darkness. He felt himself suddenly becoming weak, the ground he relied on for survival rapidly disappearing. Instinctively, he tried to gasp for air, but he could not reverse this trend. The sounds in his ears grew louder and louder, like dark clouds obscuring the sky.

Zhang Fan felt like a dying behemoth, lying on the ground, devoid of all strength, unable to struggle, letting the scorching sun bake him, his body decay, and insects feast upon him.

"I am dying." This realization flashed through his mind. Then, immense unwillingness surged within Zhang Fan. "I worked tirelessly, growing from an insignificant clone step by step to this point. I devoured my original body, consumed the Mountains and Seas, destroyed the solitary Star. I nearly attained godhood!" "How could I be dying so meaninglessly?"

Zhang Fan angrily waved his hand, trying to drive away the insects swarming around his body. But as he raised his arm, it also became a breeding ground for insects. Not only did the situation not improve, but the surrounding voices grew even louder, like a roaring flood. Despite his millions of grievances, Zhang Fan felt his own existence becoming increasingly fragile, drawing closer to death.

In a daze, he seemed to hear a terrifying chewing sound. It was as if a colossal being in the darkness was silently consuming him. Compared to the minuscule insects, its feeding was slow and elegant, seemingly savoring the fall of this "new god" with a hint of mockery, quietly appreciating it.

Like being doused with a basin of ice water in winter, Zhang Fan's boundless rage instantly extinguished, leaving only fear. At this moment, no thought of resistance arose in his mind. The only thing that remained was the desperate struggle to escape its maw. But its feeding was unquestionable, an inescapable destiny. Zhang Fan could only watch in absolute clarity as every inch of his body was gnawed, crushed, swallowed, and then digested. All that he had consumed was lost in this invisible digestion. Ultimately, only Zhang Fan himself remained. In the next moment, even Zhang Fan himself was about to be completely consumed.

With no external restraints or burdens, Zhang Fan suddenly felt a resurgence of hope for survival. He had forgotten many things, virtually everything. But one thing he remembered: "Truth..." "Truth and Falsehood..." Like a flickering lamp in the darkness, even if wavering, it briefly illuminated Zhang Fan's lost thoughts. "The traces of... Truth and Falsehood?"

He vaguely recalled that in a certain world, [Truth and Falsehood] was about to be born. It was only a hair's breadth away from completion but could never succeed due to its location within the Mountains and Seas. In the process of proving his Dao, Zhang Fan had not devoured that world. He had merely allowed it to change. "It's still there!"

As if seeing hope, Zhang Fan's remaining essence was ignited by the flames. He struggled to open his eyes, trying to find the only possible refuge in the boundless darkness. "It's there!" His memories resurfaced, and Zhang Fan quickly located his target. An Eternal World was floating silently, as if it had been there since its inception. Unchanged through the ages. The silent feeding in the darkness regarded him as nothing, as if he were a final lifeline.

Zhang Fan's remaining divine sense resisted the devouring force from outside and quickly reached the Eternal World. Although it was only a small corner, it brought Zhang Fan an unprecedented sense of security. All external threats vanished instantly, and Zhang Fan managed to survive.

The darkness receded, and time regained its meaning. Zhang Fan gradually regained his composure. The experience he had just endured was like a nightmare. Even now, Zhang Fan could not fully comprehend what had happened. But the familiar aura of [Truth and Falsehood] emanating from this Eternal World brought him a sense of peace. His rationality gradually returned. "It actually succeeded in nurturing?" This was the first normal thought that arose in Zhang Fan's mind.

Chapter 1778: New Ship

"Incredible..." Casting aside the myriad bizarre events outside, Zhang Fan carefully contemplated the nascent [Truth and Falsehood] before him.

Like looking in a mirror, Zhang Fan observed the [Truth and Falsehood] of this world, and found it indistinguishable from the [Truth and Falsehood] he had always controlled.

"No difference in strength, no distinction in superiority or inferiority, no order of precedence."

"Since it is Truth and Falsehood, it is Truth and Falsehood."

As if discovering a peerless treasure, Zhang Fan's divine sense became lost, and only after a long while did he regain his senses.

Simultaneously, countless questions and curiosities arose in his mind.

"If there is no difference between the two [Truth and Falsehood]..."

Zhang Fan's heart stirred, and he reached out, attempting to incorporate this nascent [Truth and Falsehood] into his grasp.

But something unexpected happened. Though he could perceive the Truth and Falsehood, the nascent Truth and Falsehood appeared like reflections in a mirror or flowers in water to him; he could not touch it.

"Though it is Truth and Falsehood, it is not the Truth and Falsehood I control."

After several failed attempts, Zhang Fan pondered, no longer continuing his attempt to grasp it.

He then sat down on the spot, trying to comprehend the nascent supreme Dao principles of this Eternal World from scratch.

Moments later, he frowned. In the very first instant of his attempt, he felt immense resistance within his body, which even shook the foundation of his existence.

He could indeed comprehend and cultivate the nascent Truth and Falsehood, but the price was separation and severance from the Truth and Falsehood he currently controlled.

"Can the two not coexist...?"

A faint sense of regret flickered through Zhang Fan's mind. Although this was within his expectations, he couldn't help but feel a trace of regret.

"Having the ultimate treasure before me, yet only able to gaze from afar."

Fortunately, he quickly adjusted his mindset and shifted his gaze outward, towards the darkness beyond the world.

In the darkness, he could vaguely sense the colossal entity descending. Though formless and shapeless, and separated by a world, Zhang Fan still felt an overwhelming pressure that was impossible to resist.

"The divine body has appeared."

"Only lacking Truth and Falsehood, and a True God will descend."

"And this True God was nurtured from my own body, or rather, from my decaying body."

As his gaze delved deeper into the darkness of time, the pressure Zhang Fan felt multiplied exponentially. He had to shift his gaze away.

"The resurgence of the True God is unstoppable."

The Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood within his body began to stir, as if wanting to leave his body and return to the True God's sanctuary, its rightful place.

Zhang Fan sighed inwardly, knowing that his attempt in this lifetime had failed.

Seizing the last moments while the Truth and Falsehood could still maintain stability, he analyzed the reasons for the current situation as much as possible.

"Devouring the Mountains and Seas, annihilating the solitary Star. Everything went smoothly, until..."

"The moment after becoming a god."

Like the God-Conqueror Guests who had appeared in the Mountains and Seas before, Zhang Fan in this lifetime could indeed be called a [god]. But he too could not escape the fate of demise.

Zhang Fan meticulously recalled the events of that time. Just before the Truth and Falsehood was about to completely detach, he arrived at an answer.

"It was not because the fallen True God reappeared, causing my downfall. Rather, it was because I was gradually decaying and on the verge of death that the True God within me began to gestate."

"My death was the cause, the appearance of the True God, the effect."

"That boundless darkness seems to solidify and corrupt even the will of a god. Even with my divine body, I could barely survive?"

Zhang Fan's mind was in turmoil, the Great Dao of Truth and Falsehood was about to completely detach.

At this critical juncture, Zhang Fan silently chanted [True Return]!

A ray of light ignited from Zhang Fan, illuminating the surrounding darkness.

In that instant, he seemed to witness the complete form of a god, as if making eye contact with the fallen True God.

Then he saw the divine body, under the light of True Return, melt away like ice and snow, returning to its origin.

The Mountains and Seas reappeared, anchored at year 1!

"Fan'er..."

Ignoring Bai Shuyue's call, Zhang Fan used True Truth and Falsehood to revert his cultivation to the Saint realm.

His figure shot like lightning towards False Universe Existence's location.

He had to confirm whether the nascent Truth and Falsehood, nurtured by the combined efforts of all the Saints of the Mountains and Seas in the previous life, still existed.

This point was crucial.

False Universe Existence's created Eternal Void World was independent of the Mountains and Seas. Without directly involving himself, even Zhang Fan could not glimpse its changes.

Fortunately, he was familiar with the path; after a short while, he arrived.

"Truth and Falsehood are still here!"

An indescribable sense of excitement surged through Zhang Fan's heart. This was the only thing besides himself that had survived the True Return reset.

"If the nascent Truth and Falsehood were still in the Mountains and Seas, it would likely not have escaped the True Return reset, just like that divine body."

"Gods, and even Truth and Falsehood itself, cannot escape the changes of Truth and Falsehood."

"However, after nurturing the nascent Truth and Falsehood in this Eternal Void World, it has seemingly become completely independent of the Mountains and Seas. They exist in parallel, not interfering with each other. Their reset will not affect me in the slightest."

The lingering unease in his heart from being consumed by darkness and the True God was dispelled by this discovery.

This time, Zhang Fan truly saw hope for breaking the cycle of fate.

"Who is it?"

Because of the significant fluctuations in his emotions, False Universe Existence finally discovered the uninvited intruder at this moment.

"Hahahahaha!"

Zhang Fan did not reply, merely laughing heartily.

Just as False Universe Existence was about to take action, scenes flashed through his mind.

"Fellow Daoist Fan...?"

Driven by instinct, he inexplicably uttered this name.

They had spent too much time together in the previous life, united in purpose. Thus, even after the reset of the Mountains and Seas, the God-Conqueror Guests still retained memories of each other.

Soon, the God-Conqueror Guests met again. In this Eternal Void World.

"Unity of purpose!"

Zhang Fan said solemnly, and the Saints finally saw the nascent [Truth and Falsehood] in their midst.

"No... Incredible! The supreme Great Dao has truly been nurtured in the world I created! No wonder I felt something was amiss from the beginning of this life, yet could never pinpoint it."

False Universe Existence trembled uncontrollably with extreme excitement.

"It can withstand the True Return reset. It can basically be concluded that this world has truly achieved independence. It could potentially serve as a veritable Ark of Salvation."

The Old Fisherman, usually so calm, was no longer so.

Amidst the collective excitement, Zhang Fan posed a series of questions.

"The nascent Truth and Falsehood can escape the reset of the Mountains and Seas. As for the beings within it... further verification is needed."

"But first, there is a crucial question. Will the beings hiding in this world reappear in the Mountains and Seas after the True Return reset?"

"If so, wouldn't there be two existences simultaneously?"

"And if not..."

"Wouldn't that mean the absence of gods?"

Zhang Fan's questions brought the God-Conqueror Guests back to a sobering reality. Apart from the Mountains and Seas, the existence of another world's creation was unprecedented.

No one knew the answers to these questions; only practice could reveal the truth.

False Universe Existence volunteered, "This time, I will remain here and observe the changes before and after the True Return."

Zhang Fan deliberately reminded him, "There may be unknown risks."

False Universe Existence said dismissively, "Witnessing the birth of Truth and Falsehood is already enough. Even if I die immediately, I will have no regrets."

Zhen Shi Yin then smiled, "Since he is not afraid, I will accompany him. It would be a waste of our cultivation if we didn't personally experience the act of reversing the fate of the Mountains and Seas."

Zhang Fan nodded, wasting no more time. After leaving the world with the God-Conqueror Guests, he immediately initiated the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood again.

Opening his eyes, he found himself back in the Xuanhuang Realm.

To verify what had happened, Zhang Fan rushed back to the Eternal Void World without delay.

"Why have we returned?"

False Universe Existence, who was meditating at the center of the world, was initially stunned, then exclaimed as if realizing something, "We have already initiated a True Return?"

Beside him, Zhen Shi Yin also revealed a joyous expression.

Chapter 1779: The Light

Zhen Shi Yin and False Universe Existence were still in the state they were in during the previous life, before the reset of the Mountains and Seas. This was sufficient proof that this Eternal Void World could truly exist independently and was unaffected by True Return.

"Are... we still here?" Amidst the joy, Zhen Shi Yin's expression became somewhat peculiar as he looked at Zhang Fan and asked, "Within the Mountains and Seas, there are still 'Zhen Shi Yin' and 'False Universe Existence,' but they are no longer you."

From his journey here, Zhang Fan had already sensed two different Eternal Void Worlds outside the Mountains and Seas. However, one of them did not involve the Transformation of Truth and Falsehood; it was merely a sanctuary created by False Universe Existence. The other was the place he was currently in, nurtured by the combined efforts of countless Saints and forged through the passage of infinite time and Zhang Fan's relentless sculpting with his understanding of Truth and Falsehood, thus giving birth to a new Ark.

Receiving the answer, Zhen Shi Yin's expression became complicated. "We are now like objects bound by True Return in the past. Independent of the Mountains and Seas, and unable to see each other. Otherwise, only one of us could remain."

False Universe Existence, on the other hand, seemed nonchalant. "I am me, and he is not me. Being in the new Ark, the life and death of others has nothing to do with us."

"Since the achievement has been verified, I will go and notify the Old Fisherman and the others. After countless cycles of reincarnation, we finally see hope for escaping our fate," Zhang Fan said emotionally.

"Does this world have a carrying capacity? Furthermore, we God-Conqueror Guests originated from the Mountains and Seas. If too many of us flood in, causing the Ark to fall into a vortex and be doomed..." False Universe Existence actually showed a hint of worry, as if he were gaining something.

Zhang Fan simply smiled, "We'll know after we try."

Shortly after, the Old Fisherman, Fate Slayer Master, and the others arrived. Upon learning of the birth of the new Ark, they were all deeply moved. After countless attempts to save the Mountains and Seas and ultimately failing, choosing to withdraw and protect themselves seemed like the more intelligent choice. This Eternal World was boundless, originally created by False Universe Existence to imitate the Mountains and Seas and nurture Truth and Falsehood. Especially now that his own Truth and Falsehood had truly been born, in a sense, it could be considered another Mountains and Seas. The God-Conqueror Guests gathered together, and their presence did not cause any burden. Eternal peace, surrounded by void.

Soon, the group began to discuss plans for evacuation.

"Should we... take some others with us?" Xuan Yuanhong asked hesitantly, but ultimately spoke. All the God-Conqueror Guests looked at Zhang Fan. If the new Ark needed a navigator, it could only be Zhang Fan. The God-Conqueror Guests were actually indifferent; the most important thing was to consider Zhang Fan's opinion.

Bai Shuyue's face flashed in his mind for a moment. Zhang Fan pondered for a while, then finally nodded, "We can bring them selectively, regardless of their realm. Also..."

"I won't be going."

This statement caused everyone to be stunned. "However, this world still needs a helmsman." Saying this, a faint figure floated out from Zhang Fan's body. It bore some resemblance to Zhang Fan but had no cultivation aura. It was derived from Zhang Fan's inspiration from his original 'master' who had countless clones. "He will leave with you in my place."

"As for me..." Zhang Fan remained silent, merely shaking his head slightly.

"Fellow Daoist, are you worried that if you leave the Mountains and Seas, you might not be able to use True Return to go back to the beginning?" Zhen Shi Yin asked, seeing this.

Zhang Fan smiled confidently, "With a single thought of Truth and Falsehood, regardless of the original time, place, or state. If I am on the new Ark and initiate True Return, the Mountains and Seas will vanish from their original location, and reappear outside the new Ark."

Upon hearing this, all the God-Conqueror Guests looked perplexed. "If that's the case, why doesn't Fellow Daoist Fan come with us?"

"There is one matter that still needs verification. Don't worry, as long as he is here, it's as if I am here." Zhang Fan pointed to his clone.

Seeing that Zhang Fan's mind was made up, the God-Conqueror Guests no longer insisted. As he said, they "selectively" brought some beings, whether familiar or potentially promising, into the new Ark. The originally empty and silent world became much more lively with these additions. And with the God-Conqueror Guests remodeling it, there was no need to worry about survival issues.

Zhang Fan watched everything unfold, then subtly glanced at his clone. "Let's call him... Little Fan."

"He is my clone, naturally understanding Truth and Falsehood. Although he appears merely mortal now, he, like me, possesses the ability to reverse and reset with a single thought."

"The initial anchor point is the moment the new Ark departs from the Mountains and Seas."

"I hope they can hold on for a little longer." A peculiar expression flashed in Zhang Fan's eyes. Although everything was ready, the new Ark could not leave the Mountains and Seas for now. Because in everyone's perception, whether it was the Mountains and Seas or the Void Realm, they were all once parts of the True God. Even with the new Ark as their tool, they could not escape this limitation.

"Only when the Mountains and Seas are completely gone and the True God is about to return is the moment we can escape." Little Fan said solemnly, his tone and demeanor indistinguishable from the original Zhang Fan.

The God-Conqueror Guests nodded, all expressing understanding. They had experienced countless cycles of reincarnation; waiting a little longer was nothing.

This time, Zhang Fan once again played the role of the Mountains and Seas' undertaker. Devouring mountains and seas, destroying the solitary Star, facing the True God. Everything was done with practiced ease. From the initial shock and tumultuous emotions, to this, his second time, Zhang Fan had become somewhat numb and accustomed to it.

The boundless darkness enveloped Zhang Fan once more. It was as if apart from him, nothing else existed in the world. In this instant, time seemed to come to a standstill, or perhaps it flowed a thousand to ten times faster. This was a power that could corrupt even a divine body. Perhaps only the fallen [True God] could resist it. Zhang Fan, after all, had only devoured the divine body and inherited the Truth and Falsehood; he had not possessed the [god's] will. Thus, he could only watch helplessly as his body slowly withered and rotted in the darkness.

But...

As if sensing a strange aura upon himself in this moment, Zhang Fan looked towards a certain point in the darkness. He faintly sensed that there, a new Ark carrying his clone and numerous beings was located. Compared to Zhang Fan, who had now become a [god], the new Ark was undoubtedly minuscule. But for some reason, the existence of the new Ark could illuminate the darkness like a candle, repelling the corrosive power within.

"As expected." Zhang Fan slowly regained his consciousness, attempting to find a way to survive safely in this darkness. However...

In the darkness, a gust of wind seemed to blow. The only candle in the world flickered precariously. Zhang Fan faintly seemed to see the God-Conqueror Guests struggling to save it. But ultimately, the light extinguished. Without the candle's illumination, coldness, silence, and decay once again enveloped Zhang Fan. He seemed to have reached the end of his rope, but Zhang Fan did not immediately initiate True Return. Instead, he was waiting for something.

As expected, he was not disappointed. Moments later, a flickering flame ignited once more in the darkness. It was... Little Fan's Transformation of Truth and Falsehood!
